function inferLocation(x){const s=((x?.location||x?.name||x?.address||x?.area||'')+'').toLowerCase();if(s.includes('bintaro')||s.includes('tangerang'))return 'Tangerang Selatan';if(s.includes('bandung'))return 'Bandung';if(s.includes('jakarta'))return 'Jakarta';return 'Bandung'}
function parsePeriod(period){const dates=String(period||'').match(/\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}/g)||[];return {startDate:dates[0]||todayISO(),endDate:dates[1]||addDays(todayISO(),365)}}
function normalizeMasterData(data){
 data.hubs=(data.hubs||deep(DEMO.hubs)).map((x,i)=>{const d=DEMO.hubs.find(v=>v.id===x.id)||{};const parts=String(x.hours||'').match(/(\d{2}:\d{2}).*?(\d{2}:\d{2})/);return {...x,location:x.location||inferLocation(x),latitude:x.latitude??d.latitude??'',longitude:x.longitude??d.longitude??'',openTime:x.openTime||(parts?.[1]||'08:00'),closeTime:x.closeTime||(parts?.[2]||'17:00'),is24Hours:x.is24Hours??String(x.hours||'').includes('24'),hours:x.is24Hours||String(x.hours||'').includes('24')?'24 Hours':`${x.openTime||(parts?.[1]||'08:00')} - ${x.closeTime||(parts?.[2]||'17:00')}`}});
 const firstLocation=data.hubs[0]?.location||'Bandung',firstPool=data.hubs[0]?.name||'Hub A Bandung';
 data.carriers=(data.carriers||deep(DEMO.carriers)).map(x=>({...x,type:x.type==='Contracted Carrier'?'3PL':x.type,location:x.location||inferLocation(x)||firstLocation,slaHours:Number(x.slaHours||String(x.sla||'24').match(/\d+/)?.[0]||24),sla:`${Number(x.slaHours||String(x.sla||'24').match(/\d+/)?.[0]||24)} Hours`}));
 data.contracts=(data.contracts||deep(DEMO.contracts)).map(x=>{const p=parsePeriod(x.period);return {...x,startDate:x.startDate||p.startDate,endDate:x.endDate||p.endDate,location:x.location||firstLocation}});
 data.vehicles=(data.vehicles||deep(DEMO.vehicles)).map(x=>({...x,pool:x.pool||firstPool,stnkExpiry:x.stnkExpiry||x.expiry||addDays(todayISO(),365),kirExpiry:x.kirExpiry||x.expiry||addDays(todayISO(),365),requiredSim:Array.isArray(x.requiredSim)?x.requiredSim:(x.requiredSim?[x.requiredSim]:['B1']),expiry:x.expiry||x.stnkExpiry||x.kirExpiry}));
 data.maintenanceTasks=Array.isArray(data.maintenanceTasks)?data.maintenanceTasks:deep(DEMO.maintenanceTasks);
 data.mobileUsers=Array.isArray(data.mobileUsers)?data.mobileUsers:deep(DEMO.mobileUsers);
 data.drivers=(data.drivers||deep(DEMO.drivers)).map(x=>({...x,carrier:x.carrier||data.carriers[0]?.name||'',pool:x.pool||firstPool,username:x.username||data.mobileUsers[0]||''}));
 data.routes=(data.routes||deep(DEMO.routes)).map(x=>{const parts=String(x.window||'').match(/(\d{2}:\d{2}).*?(\d{2}:\d{2})/);const toll=Number(x.tollCost||0),fuel=Number(x.fuelCost||0),parking=Number(x.parkingCost||0),other=Number(x.otherCost||0);return {...x,averageSpeed:Number(x.averageSpeed||40),openTime:x.openTime||(parts?.[1]||'08:00'),closeTime:x.closeTime||(parts?.[2]||'17:00'),tollCost:toll,fuelCost:fuel,parkingCost:parking,otherCost:other,totalCost:Number(x.totalCost||toll+fuel+parking+other)}});
 return data;
}

function loadDB(){try{const d=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(KEY));if(!d||!d.hubs)return deep(DEMO);const merged=Object.assign(deep(DEMO),d);merged.mceasyConfig=Object.assign({},deep(DEMO.mceasyConfig),d.mceasyConfig||{});['syncLogs','addressMappings','productMappings','fleetMappings','statusMappings','fleetOrders','costRecords'].forEach(k=>{if(!Array.isArray(merged[k]))merged[k]=deep(DEMO[k])});return merged}catch(e){return deep(DEMO)}}
function saveDB(){try{localStorage.setItem(KEY,JSON.stringify(db))}catch(e){console.warn('Local storage is unavailable; demo continues in memory.')}}
function resetDemo(){if(!confirm('Reset seluruh data prototype ke kondisi awal?'))return;db=deep(DEMO);saveDB();selectedDocs.clear();renderAll();toast('Demo data berhasil di-reset')}
function toast(msg){const el=document.getElementById('toast');el.textContent=msg;el.classList.add('show');clearTimeout(el._t);el._t=setTimeout(()=>el.classList.remove('show'),2300)}
function statusBadge(s){const c={Active:'b-green',Available:'b-green',Completed:'b-green','Successfully Delivered':'b-green',Planned:'b-blue','Ready to Dispatch':'b-blue',Draft:'b-gray',Reserved:'b-orange',Assigned:'b-orange',Loading:'b-orange','In Transit':'b-purple','On Going':'b-blue','At Risk':'b-orange',Delayed:'b-red',Exception:'b-red',Maintenance:'b-red',Inactive:'b-gray',Expired:'b-red','Expiring Soon':'b-orange',Valid:'b-green',Scheduled:'b-blue','In Progress':'b-orange',Cancelled:'b-gray','Need Planning':'b-orange','Partially Delivered':'b-orange','Failed Delivery':'b-red',Synced:'b-green',Valid:'b-green',Posted:'b-green',Paid:'b-green',Approved:'b-blue',Connected:'b-green',Confirm:'b-gray',Dijadwalkan:'b-blue',Dijalankan:'b-purple','OTW Tujuan':'b-purple',Unloading:'b-orange',Delivered:'b-green',Pending:'b-orange',Failed:'b-red','Invalid Coordinate':'b-red',Incomplete:'b-orange'}[s]||'b-gray';return `<span class="badge ${c}">${esc(s)}</span>`}
function closeModal(){document.getElementById('modalMask').classList.remove('open')}

 Pickup:['A','A Umum'],

 CDD:['B1','B1 Umum','B2','B2 Umum'],

const masterCfg={
 hubs:{title:'Hub',id:'id',prefix:'HUB'},carriers:{title:'Carrier',id:'id',prefix:'CAR'},contracts:{title:'Contract',id:'id',prefix:'CTR'},vehicles:{title:'Vehicle',id:'id',prefix:'VEH'},maintenanceTasks:{title:'Maintenance Task',id:'id',prefix:'MNT'},drivers:{title:'Driver',id:'id',prefix:'DRV'},routes:{title:'Route / Lane',id:'id',prefix:'LANE'}
};
function nextMasterId(type,prefix,digits=3){const re=new RegExp('^'+prefix+'-(\\d+)$','i'),nums=(db[type]||[]).map(x=>String(x.id||'').match(re)).filter(Boolean).map(m=>Number(m[1]));return `${prefix}-${String((nums.length?Math.max(...nums):0)+1).padStart(digits,'0')}`}
function activeHubNames(){return db.hubs.filter(x=>x.status==='Active').map(x=>x.name)}
function activeLocations(){return [...new Set(db.hubs.filter(x=>x.status==='Active').map(x=>x.location).filter(Boolean))]}
function activeCarrierNames(){return db.carriers.filter(x=>x.status==='Active').map(x=>x.name)}
function activeLaneIds(){return db.routes.filter(x=>x.status==='Active').map(x=>x.id)}
function withCurrent(options,current){const a=[...new Set((options||[]).filter(Boolean))];if(current&&!a.includes(current))a.unshift(current);return a}
function optionMarkup(options,value,placeholder='Select option'){return `<option value="">${esc(placeholder)}</option>`+withCurrent(options,value).map(o=>`<option value="${esc(o)}" ${String(o)===String(value)?'selected':''}>${esc(o)}</option>`).join('')}
function idField(isNew,label){return isNew?[]:[{k:'id',l:label,readonly:true,disabled:true}]}
function masterFields(type,obj={},isNew=false){
 const locations=activeLocations(),hubs=activeHubNames(),carriers=activeCarrierNames(),lanes=activeLaneIds();

 if(type==='carriers')return [...idField(isNew,'Carrier Code'),
  {k:'name',l:'Carrier Name'},{k:'type',l:'Carrier Type',t:'select',o:['Internal Fleet','3PL']},{k:'location',l:'Location',t:'select',o:locations,help:'Sumber data dari Location di Hub Management.'},{k:'slaHours',l:'SLA Time (hours)',t:'number',min:1},{k:'status',l:'Status',t:'select',o:['Active','Inactive']}];
 if(type==='contracts')return [...idField(isNew,'Contract Number'),
  {k:'carrier',l:'Carrier',t:'select',o:carriers},{k:'location',l:'Location',t:'select',o:locations,help:'Sumber data dari Location di Hub Management.'},{k:'startDate',l:'Effective Start',t:'date',onchange:'refreshContractStatus()'},{k:'endDate',l:'Effective End',t:'date',onchange:'refreshContractStatus()'},{k:'lane',l:'Lane',t:'select',o:lanes},{k:'vehicleType',l:'Vehicle Type',t:'select',o:['Any',...VEHICLE_TYPES]},{k:'rate',l:'Rate Type',t:'select',o:['Flat Trip','Base + /kg','Per km','Per drop']},{k:'baseRate',l:'Base Rate',t:'number',min:0},{k:'status',l:'Contract Status',t:'computed',readonly:true,help:'Otomatis berdasarkan tanggal efektif dan tidak dapat diubah manual.'}];
 if(type==='vehicles')return [...idField(isNew,'Vehicle ID'),
  {k:'plate',l:'Plate Number',t:'plate',full:true},{k:'carrier',l:'Carrier',t:'select',o:carriers},{k:'type',l:'Vehicle Type',t:'select',o:VEHICLE_TYPES,onchange:'refreshVehicleSimOptions()'},{k:'weight',l:'Weight Capacity (kg)',t:'number',min:1},{k:'volume',l:'Volume Capacity (m³)',t:'number',min:.1,step:'0.1'},{k:'pool',l:'Base Pool',t:'select',o:hubs},{k:'requiredSim',l:'Allowed / Required SIM Type',t:'checkboxgroup',full:true,help:'Pilihan SIM menyesuaikan Vehicle Type.'},{k:'stnkExpiry',l:'STNK Expiry',t:'date'},{k:'kirExpiry',l:'KIR Expiry',t:'date'},{k:'status',l:'Vehicle Status',t:'select',o:['Available','Reserved','Assigned','Loading','In Transit','Returning','Maintenance','Inactive']}];
 if(type==='drivers')return [...idField(isNew,'Driver ID'),
  {k:'name',l:'Driver Name'},{k:'phone',l:'Phone'},{k:'sim',l:'SIM Type',t:'select',o:SIM_TYPES},{k:'expiry',l:'SIM Expiry',t:'date'},{k:'carrier',l:'Courier / Carrier',t:'select',o:carriers},{k:'pool',l:'Base Pool',t:'select',o:hubs},{k:'username',l:'Mobile Username',help:'Free text dan harus unik.'},{k:'status',l:'Status',t:'select',o:['Available','Assigned','On Trip','Returning','Resting','Leave','Inactive']}];
 if(type==='routes')return [...idField(isNew,'Lane ID'),
  {k:'origin',l:'Origin',t:'select',o:hubs,onchange:'refreshRouteCalculation()'},{k:'destination',l:'Destination',t:'select',o:hubs,onchange:'refreshRouteCalculation()'},{k:'averageSpeed',l:'Planning Average Speed',t:'select',o:['20','30','40','50','60','80'],onchange:'refreshRouteCalculation()',suffix:' km/h'},{k:'distance',l:'Distance (km)',t:'computed',readonly:true},{k:'duration',l:'Planned Duration',t:'computed',readonly:true},{k:'serviceWindow',l:'Service Window',t:'serviceWindow',full:true},{k:'tollCost',l:'Toll Cost',t:'number',min:0,oninput:'refreshRouteCalculation()'},{k:'fuelCost',l:'Fuel Cost',t:'number',min:0,oninput:'refreshRouteCalculation()'},{k:'parkingCost',l:'Parking Cost',t:'number',min:0,oninput:'refreshRouteCalculation()'},{k:'otherCost',l:'Other Cost',t:'number',min:0,oninput:'refreshRouteCalculation()'},{k:'totalCost',l:'Total Estimated Cost',t:'computed',readonly:true},{k:'status',l:'Status',t:'select',o:['Active','Inactive']}];
 return [];
}
function parsePlate(plate){const p=String(plate||'').trim().toUpperCase().split(/\s+/);return {prefix:p[0]||'',number:p[1]||'',suffix:p.slice(2).join('')||''}}
function fieldHTML(f,v,obj,readonly=false){const ro=readonly||f.readonly,dis=readonly||f.disabled,cls=f.full?'field full':'field';let x='';
 if(f.t==='select')x=`<select class="select" id="mf-${f.k}" ${dis?'disabled':''} ${f.onchange?`onchange="${f.onchange}"`:''}>${optionMarkup(f.o,v,'Select '+f.l)}</select>`;
 else if(f.t==='textarea')x=`<textarea class="textarea" id="mf-${f.k}" ${ro?'readonly':''} ${dis?'disabled':''}>${esc(v||'')}</textarea>`;
 else if(f.t==='plate'){const p=parsePlate(obj.plate);x=`<div class="plate-inputs"><input class="input" id="mf-platePrefix" maxlength="2" placeholder="B" value="${esc(p.prefix)}" ${dis?'disabled':''} oninput="this.value=this.value.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z]/g,'')"><input class="input plate-number" id="mf-plateNumber" inputmode="numeric" maxlength="4" placeholder="1234" value="${esc(p.number)}" ${dis?'disabled':''} oninput="this.value=this.value.replace(/\\D/g,'')"><input class="input" id="mf-plateSuffix" maxlength="3" placeholder="OZ" value="${esc(p.suffix)}" ${dis?'disabled':''} oninput="this.value=this.value.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z]/g,'')"></div>`;}
 else if(f.t==='checkboxgroup')x=`<div class="checkbox-group" id="mf-${f.k}" data-selected="${esc(JSON.stringify(Array.isArray(v)?v:[]))}" data-readonly="${dis?'1':'0'}"></div>`;
 else if(f.t==='operatingHours')x=`<div class="check-row" style="margin-bottom:8px"><input type="checkbox" id="mf-is24Hours" ${obj.is24Hours?'checked':''} ${dis?'disabled':''} onchange="toggleHubHours()"><label for="mf-is24Hours">Open 24 Hours</label></div><div class="time-pair"><input class="input" id="mf-openTime" type="time" value="${esc(obj.openTime||'08:00')}" ${dis||obj.is24Hours?'disabled':''}><span class="time-separator">to</span><input class="input" id="mf-closeTime" type="time" value="${esc(obj.closeTime||'17:00')}" ${dis||obj.is24Hours?'disabled':''}></div>`;
 else if(f.t==='serviceWindow')x=`<div class="time-pair"><input class="input" id="mf-openTime" type="time" value="${esc(obj.openTime||'08:00')}" ${dis?'disabled':''}><span class="time-separator">to</span><input class="input" id="mf-closeTime" type="time" value="${esc(obj.closeTime||'17:00')}" ${dis?'disabled':''}></div>`;
 else if(f.t==='computed'){if(f.k==='status')x=`<div class="readonly-value" id="mf-${f.k}">${statusBadge(contractAutoStatus(obj))}</div>`;else {const val=f.k==='totalCost'?fmtIDR(obj.totalCost||0):(v??'');x=`<input class="input" id="mf-${f.k}" value="${esc(val)}" disabled>`;}}
 else {const inputType=f.t||'text';x=`<input class="input" id="mf-${f.k}" type="${inputType}" value="${esc(v??'')}" ${f.min!==undefined?`min="${f.min}"`:''} ${f.step?`step="${f.step}"`:''} ${ro?'readonly':''} ${dis?'disabled':''} ${f.oninput?`oninput="${f.oninput}"`:''} ${f.onchange?`onchange="${f.onchange}"`:''}>`;}
 return `<div class="${cls}"><label>${esc(f.l)}</label>${x}${f.help?`<small>${esc(f.help)}</small>`:''}</div>`;
}
function toggleHubHours(){const checked=document.getElementById('mf-is24Hours')?.checked;['mf-openTime','mf-closeTime'].forEach(id=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.disabled=checked})}
function refreshVehicleSimOptions(){const box=document.getElementById('mf-requiredSim');if(!box)return;const current=[...box.querySelectorAll('input:checked')].map(x=>x.value),initial=(()=>{try{return JSON.parse(box.dataset.selected||'[]')}catch(e){return []}})(),selected=box.dataset.initialized?current:initial,type=document.getElementById('mf-type')?.value||'',options=VEHICLE_SIM_MAP[type]||SIM_TYPES,disabled=box.dataset.readonly==='1';box.innerHTML=options.map(o=>`<label class="checkbox-option"><input type="checkbox" value="${esc(o)}" ${selected.includes(o)?'checked':''} ${disabled?'disabled':''}>${esc(o)}</label>`).join('')||'<span class="muted">Select Vehicle Type first.</span>';box.dataset.initialized='1'}
function contractAutoStatus(x){if(!x?.startDate||!x?.endDate)return 'Draft';const now=isoDate(todayISO()),start=isoDate(x.startDate),end=isoDate(x.endDate),days=Math.ceil((end-now)/86400000);if(now<start)return 'Draft';if(now>end)return 'Expired';if(days<=30)return 'Expiring Soon';return 'Active'}
function refreshContractStatus(){const el=document.getElementById('mf-status');if(!el)return;el.innerHTML=statusBadge(contractAutoStatus({startDate:document.getElementById('mf-startDate')?.value,endDate:document.getElementById('mf-endDate')?.value}))}
function expiryInfo(date){if(!date)return {status:'No Date',days:null};const d=isoDate(date),today=isoDate(todayISO()),days=Math.ceil((d-today)/86400000);return {status:days<0?'Expired':days<=30?'Expiring Soon':'Valid',days}}
function expiryHTML(date){const e=expiryInfo(date),note=e.days===null?'':e.days<0?`${Math.abs(e.days)} day(s) overdue`:`${e.days} day(s) remaining`;return `<div class="expiry-stack"><span class="date">${esc(date||'-')}</span>${statusBadge(e.status)}<span class="muted">${esc(note)}</span></div>`}
function haversineKm(a,b){if(!a||!b)return 0;const toRad=v=>Number(v)*Math.PI/180;if([a.latitude,a.longitude,b.latitude,b.longitude].some(v=>v===''||v===null||v===undefined||Number.isNaN(Number(v))))return 0;const R=6371,dLat=toRad(Number(b.latitude)-Number(a.latitude)),dLon=toRad(Number(b.longitude)-Number(a.longitude)),lat1=toRad(a.latitude),lat2=toRad(b.latitude);const h=Math.sin(dLat/2)**2+Math.cos(lat1)*Math.cos(lat2)*Math.sin(dLon/2)**2;return Math.round((2*R*Math.asin(Math.sqrt(h)))*10)/10}
function durationText(distance,speed){const mins=Math.max(1,Math.round(Number(distance||0)/Math.max(1,Number(speed||40))*60));const h=Math.floor(mins/60),m=mins%60;return h?`${h} hr${m?` ${m} min`:''}`:`${m} min`}
function refreshRouteCalculation(){const origin=document.getElementById('mf-origin')?.value,destination=document.getElementById('mf-destination')?.value,a=db.hubs.find(x=>x.name===origin),b=db.hubs.find(x=>x.name===destination),distance=a&&b&&origin!==destination?haversineKm(a,b):0,speed=Number(document.getElementById('mf-averageSpeed')?.value||40),duration=distance?durationText(distance,speed):'';const distEl=document.getElementById('mf-distance'),durEl=document.getElementById('mf-duration');if(distEl)distEl.value=distance||'';if(durEl)durEl.value=duration;const total=['tollCost','fuelCost','parkingCost','otherCost'].reduce((s,k)=>s+Number(document.getElementById('mf-'+k)?.value||0),0),totalEl=document.getElementById('mf-totalCost');if(totalEl)totalEl.value=fmtIDR(total)}
function openMasterForm(type,index=null,view=false){const cfg=masterCfg[type],isNew=index===null,obj=isNew?{}:{...db[type][index]};if(type==='contracts'&&isNew){obj.startDate=todayISO();obj.endDate=addDays(todayISO(),365);obj.status=contractAutoStatus(obj)}if(type==='routes'&&isNew){obj.averageSpeed=40;obj.openTime='08:00';obj.closeTime='17:00';obj.tollCost=0;obj.fuelCost=0;obj.parkingCost=0;obj.otherCost=0;obj.totalCost=0}if(type==='hubs'&&isNew){obj.openTime='08:00';obj.closeTime='17:00';obj.is24Hours=false}if(type==='vehicles'&&isNew){obj.type='CDD';obj.requiredSim=[]}const fields=masterFields(type,obj,isNew),body=`<div class="form-grid">${fields.map(f=>fieldHTML(f,obj[f.k],obj,view)).join('')}</div>`;let foot=`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`;if(!view)foot+=`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveMaster('${type}',${isNew?'null':index})">${isNew?'Create':'Save Changes'}</button>`;openModal((view?'Detail ':'')+cfg.title,body,foot);if(type==='routes')setTimeout(refreshRouteCalculation,0);if(type==='hubs')setTimeout(toggleHubHours,0);if(type==='vehicles')setTimeout(refreshVehicleSimOptions,0)}
function readField(f){if(['computed','operatingHours','serviceWindow','plate'].includes(f.t))return undefined;const el=document.getElementById('mf-'+f.k);if(!el)return undefined;if(f.t==='checkboxgroup')return [...el.querySelectorAll('input:checked')].map(o=>o.value);if(f.t==='number')return Number(el.value);return el.value.trim()}
function saveMaster(type,index){const isNew=index===null,fields=masterFields(type,isNew?{}:db[type][index],isNew),obj=isNew?{}:{...db[type][index]};for(const f of fields){const val=readField(f);if(val!==undefined)obj[f.k]=val;if(!['computed','operatingHours','serviceWindow','plate','checkboxgroup'].includes(f.t)&&!f.readonly&&!f.disabled&&(val===''||val===null||val===undefined)){toast(f.l+' wajib diisi');return}if(f.t==='checkboxgroup'&&(!val||!val.length)){toast('Pilih minimal satu tipe SIM');return}}
 if(isNew)obj.id=nextMasterId(type,masterCfg[type].prefix);
 if(type==='hubs'){obj.is24Hours=!!document.getElementById('mf-is24Hours')?.checked;obj.openTime=document.getElementById('mf-openTime')?.value||'00:00';obj.closeTime=document.getElementById('mf-closeTime')?.value||'23:59';obj.hours=obj.is24Hours?'24 Hours':`${obj.openTime} - ${obj.closeTime}`;if(Number.isNaN(obj.latitude)||Number.isNaN(obj.longitude)){toast('Latitude dan Longitude tidak valid');return}}
 if(type==='carriers')obj.sla=`${obj.slaHours} Hours`;
 if(type==='contracts'){if(obj.endDate<obj.startDate){toast('Effective End tidak boleh sebelum Effective Start');return}obj.period=`${obj.startDate} to ${obj.endDate}`;obj.status=contractAutoStatus(obj)}
 if(type==='vehicles'){const prefix=document.getElementById('mf-platePrefix')?.value.trim().toUpperCase(),number=document.getElementById('mf-plateNumber')?.value.trim(),suffix=document.getElementById('mf-plateSuffix')?.value.trim().toUpperCase();if(!prefix||!number||!suffix){toast('Lengkapi huruf depan, angka, dan huruf belakang Plate Number');return}if(!/^[A-Z]{1,2}$/.test(prefix)||!/^\d{1,4}$/.test(number)||!/^[A-Z]{1,3}$/.test(suffix)){toast('Format Plate Number tidak valid');return}obj.plate=`${prefix} ${number} ${suffix}`;obj.expiry=[obj.stnkExpiry,obj.kirExpiry].sort()[0];if(db.vehicles.some((x,i)=>i!==index&&x.plate.toLowerCase()===obj.plate.toLowerCase())){toast('Plate Number harus unik');return}}
 if(type==='drivers'){if(db.drivers.some((x,i)=>i!==index&&String(x.username).toLowerCase()===String(obj.username).toLowerCase())){toast('Mobile Username sudah digunakan driver lain');return}}
 if(type==='routes'){obj.openTime=document.getElementById('mf-openTime')?.value||'08:00';obj.closeTime=document.getElementById('mf-closeTime')?.value||'17:00';obj.window=`${obj.openTime} - ${obj.closeTime}`;if(obj.origin===obj.destination){toast('Origin dan Destination harus berbeda');return}const a=db.hubs.find(x=>x.name===obj.origin),b=db.hubs.find(x=>x.name===obj.destination);obj.distance=haversineKm(a,b);if(!obj.distance){toast('Koordinat Hub belum lengkap, distance tidak dapat dihitung');return}obj.duration=durationText(obj.distance,obj.averageSpeed);obj.totalCost=['tollCost','fuelCost','parkingCost','otherCost'].reduce((s,k)=>s+Number(obj[k]||0),0)}
 const cfg=masterCfg[type];if(isNew){if(db[type].some(x=>x[cfg.id]===obj[cfg.id])){toast(cfg.title+' ID harus unik');return}db[type].push(obj)}else db[type][index]=obj;normalizeMasterData(db);refreshComputedStatuses();saveDB();closeModal();renderAll();toast(cfg.title+' berhasil disimpan dengan ID '+obj.id)}
function isMasterReferenced(type,obj){if(type==='hubs')return db.vehicles.some(x=>x.pool===obj.name)||db.drivers.some(x=>x.pool===obj.name)||db.routes.some(x=>x.origin===obj.name||x.destination===obj.name)||db.carriers.some(x=>x.location===obj.location)||db.contracts.some(x=>x.location===obj.location);if(type==='carriers')return db.vehicles.some(x=>x.carrier===obj.name)||db.drivers.some(x=>x.carrier===obj.name)||db.contracts.some(x=>x.carrier===obj.name);if(type==='vehicles')return db.maintenanceTasks.some(x=>x.vehicleId===obj.id)||db.plans.some(x=>x.vehicle===obj.plate);if(type==='routes')return db.contracts.some(x=>x.lane===obj.id);return false}
function deleteMaster(type,index){const obj=db[type][index];if(isMasterReferenced(type,obj)){toast('Data masih digunakan oleh master atau transaksi lain');return}if(!confirm('Delete data ini?'))return;db[type].splice(index,1);saveDB();renderAll();toast('Data berhasil dihapus')}
const IMPORT_SPECS={
 hubs:[['name','Hub Name'],['type','Hub Type'],['location','Location'],['address','Address'],['latitude','Latitude'],['longitude','Longitude'],['openTime','Open Time'],['closeTime','Close Time'],['operatingHours','Operating Hours'],['is24Hours','Open 24 Hours'],['status','Status']],
 carriers:[['name','Carrier Name'],['type','Carrier Type'],['location','Location'],['slaHours','SLA Time (hours)'],['status','Status']],
 contracts:[['carrier','Carrier'],['location','Location'],['startDate','Effective Start'],['endDate','Effective End'],['lane','Lane'],['vehicleType','Vehicle Type'],['rate','Rate Type'],['baseRate','Base Rate']],
 vehicles:[['plate','Plate Number'],['platePrefix','Plate Prefix'],['plateNumber','Plate Number Digits'],['plateSuffix','Plate Suffix'],['carrier','Carrier'],['type','Vehicle Type'],['weight','Weight Capacity (kg)'],['volume','Volume Capacity (m3)'],['pool','Base Pool'],['requiredSim','Required SIM'],['stnkExpiry','STNK Expiry'],['kirExpiry','KIR Expiry'],['status','Status']],
 maintenanceTasks:[['vehicleId','Vehicle ID'],['plate','Plate Number'],['category','Category'],['startDate','Start Date'],['endDate','End Date'],['description','Description'],['estimateCost','Estimate Cost'],['cost','Cost'],['status','Task Status']],
 drivers:[['name','Name'],['phone','Phone'],['sim','SIM Type'],['expiry','SIM Expiry'],['carrier','Courier / Carrier'],['pool','Base Pool'],['username','Mobile Username'],['status','Status']],
 routes:[['origin','Origin'],['destination','Destination'],['averageSpeed','Planning Average Speed'],['openTime','Service Window Start'],['closeTime','Service Window End'],['serviceWindow','Service Window'],['tollCost','Toll Cost'],['fuelCost','Fuel Cost'],['parkingCost','Parking Cost'],['otherCost','Other Cost'],['status','Status']]
};
function openImport(type){
 const spec=IMPORT_SPECS[type];if(!spec){toast('Import belum tersedia untuk menu ini');return}
 const title=masterCfg[type]?.title||type;
 openModal('Import '+title+' Data',`<div class="notice">Import menerima file <b>CSV</b> atau file <b>XLS</b> berbentuk tabel. ID dibuat otomatis saat data disimpan. Gunakan template agar nama kolom sesuai.</div><div class="field"><label>Choose CSV / XLS File</label><input class="input" id="import-file" type="file" accept=".csv,.xls,text/csv,application/vnd.ms-excel"></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="downloadTemplate('${type}')">Download CSV Template</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="importCSVFile('${type}')">Import Data</button>`,true)
}
function downloadTemplate(type){const spec=IMPORT_SPECS[type]||[];downloadCSV([spec.map(x=>x[1])],`${type}-import-template.csv`)}
function parseCSV(text){const rows=[];let row=[],cell='',quote=false;for(let i=0;i<text.length;i++){const c=text[i],n=text[i+1];if(c==='"'&&quote&&n==='"'){cell+='"';i++}else if(c==='"')quote=!quote;else if(c===','&&!quote){row.push(cell);cell=''}else if((c==='\n'||c==='\r')&&!quote){if(c==='\r'&&n==='\n')i++;row.push(cell);if(row.some(v=>String(v).trim()!==''))rows.push(row);row=[];cell=''}else cell+=c}row.push(cell);if(row.some(v=>String(v).trim()!==''))rows.push(row);return rows}
function parseImportTable(text){const doc=new DOMParser().parseFromString(text,'text/html');return [...doc.querySelectorAll('tr')].map(tr=>[...tr.querySelectorAll('th,td')].map(td=>td.textContent.trim())).filter(r=>r.some(v=>String(v).trim()))}
function normHeader(s){return String(s||'').toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g,'')}
function parseBooleanImport(v){return ['1','true','yes','y','ya','24 hours','24hours'].includes(String(v||'').trim().toLowerCase())}
function splitWindow(v){const m=String(v||'').match(/(\d{2}:\d{2}).*?(\d{2}:\d{2})/);return {start:m?.[1]||'',end:m?.[2]||''}}
function importCSVFile(type){
 const file=document.getElementById('import-file')?.files?.[0];if(!file){toast('Pilih file terlebih dahulu');return}
 const reader=new FileReader();reader.onload=()=>{try{
  const content=String(reader.result||''),rows=/\.xls$/i.test(file.name)?parseImportTable(content):parseCSV(content);if(rows.length<2){toast('File tidak memiliki data');return}
  const spec=IMPORT_SPECS[type],headers=rows[0].map(normHeader),indexes=Object.fromEntries(spec.map(([k,l])=>[k,headers.findIndex(h=>h===normHeader(l)||h===normHeader(k))]));let imported=0,skipped=0;
  const value=(raw,k)=>indexes[k]>=0?String(raw[indexes[k]]||'').trim():'';
  for(const raw of rows.slice(1)){try{let obj;
   if(type==='hubs'){
    const hours=splitWindow(value(raw,'operatingHours')),is24=parseBooleanImport(value(raw,'is24Hours'))||/24/.test(value(raw,'operatingHours'));
    obj={id:nextMasterId('hubs','HUB'),name:value(raw,'name'),type:value(raw,'type')||'Warehouse',location:value(raw,'location'),address:value(raw,'address'),latitude:Number(value(raw,'latitude')),longitude:Number(value(raw,'longitude')),openTime:value(raw,'openTime')||hours.start||'08:00',closeTime:value(raw,'closeTime')||hours.end||'17:00',is24Hours:is24,status:value(raw,'status')||'Active'};
    obj.hours=obj.is24Hours?'24 Hours':`${obj.openTime} - ${obj.closeTime}`;
    if(!obj.name||!obj.location||!obj.address||!Number.isFinite(obj.latitude)||!Number.isFinite(obj.longitude)||db.hubs.some(x=>x.name.toLowerCase()===obj.name.toLowerCase()))throw Error('invalid');
   }else if(type==='carriers'){
    obj={id:nextMasterId('carriers','CAR'),name:value(raw,'name'),type:value(raw,'type')||'3PL',location:value(raw,'location'),slaHours:Number(value(raw,'slaHours')||24),status:value(raw,'status')||'Active'};obj.sla=`${obj.slaHours} Hours`;
    if(!obj.name||!activeLocations().includes(obj.location)||db.carriers.some(x=>x.name.toLowerCase()===obj.name.toLowerCase()))throw Error('invalid');
   }else if(type==='contracts'){
    obj={id:nextMasterId('contracts','CTR'),carrier:value(raw,'carrier'),location:value(raw,'location'),startDate:value(raw,'startDate'),endDate:value(raw,'endDate'),lane:value(raw,'lane'),vehicleType:value(raw,'vehicleType')||'Any',rate:value(raw,'rate')||'Flat Trip',baseRate:Number(value(raw,'baseRate')||0)};
    if(!activeCarrierNames().includes(obj.carrier)||!activeLocations().includes(obj.location)||!obj.startDate||!obj.endDate||!activeLaneIds().includes(obj.lane)||obj.endDate<obj.startDate)throw Error('invalid');obj.period=`${obj.startDate} to ${obj.endDate}`;obj.status=contractAutoStatus(obj);
   }else if(type==='vehicles'){
    const full=value(raw,'plate').toUpperCase(),parsed=parsePlate(full),prefix=(value(raw,'platePrefix')||parsed.prefix).toUpperCase(),number=value(raw,'plateNumber')||parsed.number,suffix=(value(raw,'plateSuffix')||parsed.suffix).toUpperCase(),plate=`${prefix} ${number} ${suffix}`.trim();
    obj={id:nextMasterId('vehicles','VEH'),plate,carrier:value(raw,'carrier'),type:value(raw,'type'),weight:Number(value(raw,'weight')),volume:Number(value(raw,'volume')),pool:value(raw,'pool'),requiredSim:value(raw,'requiredSim').split(/[|,]/).map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean),stnkExpiry:value(raw,'stnkExpiry'),kirExpiry:value(raw,'kirExpiry'),status:value(raw,'status')||'Available'};
    if(!/^[A-Z]{1,2} \d{1,4} [A-Z]{1,3}$/.test(plate)||!activeCarrierNames().includes(obj.carrier)||!VEHICLE_TYPES.includes(obj.type)||!activeHubNames().includes(obj.pool)||!obj.requiredSim.length||!obj.stnkExpiry||!obj.kirExpiry||db.vehicles.some(x=>x.plate===plate))throw Error('invalid');obj.expiry=[obj.stnkExpiry,obj.kirExpiry].sort()[0];
   }else if(type==='maintenanceTasks'){
    const vehicleRef=value(raw,'vehicleId'),plate=value(raw,'plate').toUpperCase(),vehicle=db.vehicles.find(v=>v.id===vehicleRef)||db.vehicles.find(v=>v.plate.toUpperCase()===plate),estimateCost=Number(value(raw,'estimateCost')||value(raw,'cost')||0);
    obj={id:nextMasterId('maintenanceTasks','MNT'),vehicleId:vehicle?.id||'',category:value(raw,'category')||'Preventive Service',startDate:value(raw,'startDate'),endDate:value(raw,'endDate'),description:value(raw,'description'),estimateCost,cost:estimateCost,status:value(raw,'status')||'Scheduled'};
    if(!vehicle||!obj.startDate||!obj.endDate||obj.endDate<obj.startDate||!['Scheduled','In Progress','Completed','Cancelled'].includes(obj.status))throw Error('invalid');
   }else if(type==='drivers'){
    obj={id:nextMasterId('drivers','DRV'),name:value(raw,'name'),phone:value(raw,'phone'),sim:value(raw,'sim'),expiry:value(raw,'expiry'),carrier:value(raw,'carrier'),pool:value(raw,'pool'),username:value(raw,'username'),status:value(raw,'status')||'Available'};
    if(!obj.name||!obj.phone||!SIM_TYPES.includes(obj.sim)||!obj.expiry||!activeCarrierNames().includes(obj.carrier)||!activeHubNames().includes(obj.pool)||!obj.username||db.drivers.some(x=>String(x.username).toLowerCase()===obj.username.toLowerCase()))throw Error('invalid');
   }else if(type==='routes'){
    const win=splitWindow(value(raw,'serviceWindow'));obj={id:nextMasterId('routes','LANE'),origin:value(raw,'origin'),destination:value(raw,'destination'),averageSpeed:Number(value(raw,'averageSpeed')||40),openTime:value(raw,'openTime')||win.start||'08:00',closeTime:value(raw,'closeTime')||win.end||'17:00',tollCost:Number(value(raw,'tollCost')||0),fuelCost:Number(value(raw,'fuelCost')||0),parkingCost:Number(value(raw,'parkingCost')||0),otherCost:Number(value(raw,'otherCost')||0),status:value(raw,'status')||'Active'};
    const a=db.hubs.find(x=>x.name===obj.origin),b=db.hubs.find(x=>x.name===obj.destination);obj.distance=haversineKm(a,b);obj.duration=durationText(obj.distance,obj.averageSpeed);obj.window=`${obj.openTime} - ${obj.closeTime}`;obj.totalCost=obj.tollCost+obj.fuelCost+obj.parkingCost+obj.otherCost;
    if(!a||!b||obj.origin===obj.destination||!obj.distance||db.routes.some(x=>x.origin===obj.origin&&x.destination===obj.destination))throw Error('invalid');
   }else throw Error('unsupported');
   db[type].push(obj);if(type==='maintenanceTasks')syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(obj.vehicleId);imported++;
  }catch(e){skipped++}}
  normalizeMasterData(db);refreshComputedStatuses();saveDB();closeModal();renderAll();toast(`${imported} data imported${skipped?`, ${skipped} skipped`:''}`)
 }catch(e){console.error(e);toast('Format file tidak valid')}};reader.readAsText(file)
}
function refreshComputedStatuses(){db.contracts.forEach(x=>{x.status=contractAutoStatus(x);x.period=`${x.startDate} to ${x.endDate}`});db.maintenanceTasks.forEach(t=>syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(t.vehicleId))}
function filteredMasterRecords(type){const inputId={hubs:'hubSearch',carriers:'carrierSearch',contracts:'contractSearch',vehicles:'vehicleSearch',drivers:'driverSearch',routes:'routeSearch'}[type],q=(document.getElementById(inputId)?.value||'').toLowerCase(),st=type==='vehicles'?(document.getElementById('vehicleStatusFilter')?.value||''):'';return db[type].map((x,i)=>({x,i})).filter(o=>JSON.stringify(o.x).toLowerCase().includes(q)&&(!st||o.x.status===st))}
function renderMaster(type){refreshComputedStatuses();
 if(type==='hubs')document.getElementById('hubTbody').innerHTML=filteredMasterRecords(type).map(({x,i})=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${esc(x.name)}</td><td>${esc(x.type)}</td><td>${esc(x.location)}</td><td>${esc(x.address)}</td><td>${esc(x.hours)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td>${rowActions('hubs',i)}</td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="8" class="empty">No hub found.</td></tr>`;
 if(type==='carriers')document.getElementById('carrierTbody').innerHTML=filteredMasterRecords(type).map(({x,i})=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${esc(x.name)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.type)}</td><td>${esc(x.location)}</td><td>${esc(x.slaHours)} Hours</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td>${rowActions('carriers',i)}</td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="7" class="empty">No carrier found.</td></tr>`;
 if(type==='contracts')document.getElementById('contractTbody').innerHTML=filteredMasterRecords(type).map(({x,i})=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${esc(x.carrier)}</td><td>${esc(x.startDate)} to ${esc(x.endDate)}</td><td>${esc(x.location)}</td><td>${esc(x.lane)}</td><td>${esc(x.vehicleType)}</td><td>${esc(x.rate)}<br><span class="muted">${fmtIDR(x.baseRate)}</span></td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td>${rowActions('contracts',i)}</td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="9" class="empty">No contract found.</td></tr>`;
 if(type==='vehicles')document.getElementById('vehicleTbody').innerHTML=filteredMasterRecords(type).map(({x,i})=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${esc(x.plate)}</td><td>${esc(x.carrier)}</td><td>${esc(x.type)}</td><td>${Number(x.weight).toLocaleString()} kg / ${esc(x.volume)} m³</td><td>${esc(x.pool)}</td><td>${esc((x.requiredSim||[]).join(', '))}</td><td>${expiryHTML(x.stnkExpiry)}</td><td>${expiryHTML(x.kirExpiry)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td>${rowActions('vehicles',i,[{label:'Create Maintenance',action:`openMaintenanceForm(null,false,'${x.id}')`}])}</td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">No vehicle found.</td></tr>`;
 if(type==='drivers')document.getElementById('driverTbody').innerHTML=filteredMasterRecords(type).map(({x,i})=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${esc(x.name)}</td><td>${esc(x.phone)}</td><td>${esc(x.sim)}<br><span class="muted">${esc(x.expiry)}</span></td><td>${esc(x.carrier)}</td><td>${esc(x.pool)}</td><td>${esc(x.username)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td>${rowActions('drivers',i)}</td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="9" class="empty">No driver found.</td></tr>`;
 if(type==='routes')document.getElementById('routeTbody').innerHTML=filteredMasterRecords(type).map(({x,i})=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${esc(x.origin)}</td><td>${esc(x.destination)}</td><td>${esc(x.distance)} km</td><td>${esc(x.duration)}</td><td>${esc(x.window)}</td><td>${fmtIDR(x.tollCost)}</td><td>${fmtIDR(x.fuelCost)}</td><td>${fmtIDR(x.parkingCost)}</td><td>${fmtIDR(x.otherCost)}</td><td class="cost-total">${fmtIDR(x.totalCost)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td>${rowActions('routes',i)}</td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="13" class="empty">No lane found.</td></tr>`;
}
function closeActionMenus(except=null){document.querySelectorAll('.action-dropdown.open').forEach(x=>{if(x!==except)x.classList.remove('open')})}
function toggleActionMenu(btn,event){event.stopPropagation();const menu=btn.nextElementSibling,willOpen=!menu.classList.contains('open');closeActionMenus(menu);if(!willOpen){menu.classList.remove('open');return}menu.classList.add('open');const r=btn.getBoundingClientRect(),w=menu.offsetWidth||154,h=menu.offsetHeight||120;let left=Math.max(8,Math.min(window.innerWidth-w-8,r.right-w)),top=r.bottom+5;if(top+h>window.innerHeight-8)top=Math.max(8,r.top-h-5);menu.style.left=left+'px';menu.style.top=top+'px'}
document.addEventListener('click',()=>closeActionMenus());window.addEventListener('scroll',()=>closeActionMenus(),true);window.addEventListener('resize',()=>closeActionMenus());
function actionMenuHTML(items){return `<div class="action-menu"><button class="icon-btn action-trigger" title="Actions" aria-label="Open actions" onclick="toggleActionMenu(this,event)">⋮</button><div class="action-dropdown">${items.map(x=>`<button class="${x.danger?'danger':''}" onclick="closeActionMenus();${x.action}">${esc(x.label)}</button>`).join('')}</div></div>`}
function rowActions(type,i,extra=[]){return actionMenuHTML([{label:'Detail',action:`openMasterForm('${type}',${i},true)`},{label:'Edit',action:`openMasterForm('${type}',${i})`},...extra,{label:'Delete',action:`deleteMaster('${type}',${i})`,danger:true}])}
function exportSpec(type){return {
 hubs:{headers:['Hub ID','Hub Name','Type','Location','Address','Operating Hours','Status'],rows:x=>[x.id,x.name,x.type,x.location,x.address,x.hours,x.status]},
 carriers:{headers:['Carrier Code','Carrier Name','Carrier Type','Location','SLA Time (hours)','Status'],rows:x=>[x.id,x.name,x.type,x.location,x.slaHours,x.status]},
 contracts:{headers:['Contract Number','Carrier','Effective Start','Effective End','Location','Lane','Vehicle Type','Rate Type','Base Rate','Status'],rows:x=>[x.id,x.carrier,x.startDate,x.endDate,x.location,x.lane,x.vehicleType,x.rate,x.baseRate,x.status]},
 vehicles:{headers:['Vehicle ID','Plate Number','Carrier','Vehicle Type','Weight Capacity (kg)','Volume Capacity (m3)','Base Pool','Required SIM','STNK Expiry','KIR Expiry','Status'],rows:x=>[x.id,x.plate,x.carrier,x.type,x.weight,x.volume,x.pool,(x.requiredSim||[]).join(', '),x.stnkExpiry,x.kirExpiry,x.status]},
 drivers:{headers:['Driver ID','Name','Phone','SIM Type','SIM Expiry','Courier / Carrier','Base Pool','Mobile Username','Status'],rows:x=>[x.id,x.name,x.phone,x.sim,x.expiry,x.carrier,x.pool,x.username,x.status]},
 routes:{headers:['Lane ID','Origin','Destination','Distance (km)','Planned Duration','Service Window','Toll Cost','Fuel Cost','Parking Cost','Other Cost','Total Estimated Cost','Status'],rows:x=>[x.id,x.origin,x.destination,x.distance,x.duration,x.window,x.tollCost,x.fuelCost,x.parkingCost,x.otherCost,x.totalCost,x.status]}
 }[type]}
function excelEscape(v){return String(v??'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')}
function downloadExcelTable(headers,rows,name){const table=`<table border="1"><thead><tr>${headers.map(h=>`<th>${excelEscape(h)}</th>`).join('')}</tr></thead><tbody>${rows.map(r=>`<tr>${r.map(v=>`<td>${excelEscape(v)}</td>`).join('')}</tr>`).join('')}</tbody></table>`,html=`<html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"></head><body>${table}</body></html>`,a=document.createElement('a');a.href=URL.createObjectURL(new Blob(['\ufeff',html],{type:'application/vnd.ms-excel'}));a.download=name.endsWith('.xls')?name:name+'.xls';a.click();URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href)}
function downloadMasterExcel(type){const spec=exportSpec(type),records=filteredMasterRecords(type).map(o=>o.x);downloadExcelTable(spec.headers,records.map(spec.rows),`TMS-${type}-${todayISO()}.xls`);toast(records.length+' row downloaded')}
function syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(vehicleId){const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.id===vehicleId);if(!v)return;const active=db.maintenanceTasks.some(t=>t.vehicleId===vehicleId&&(t.status==='In Progress'||(t.status==='Scheduled'&&t.startDate<=todayISO()&&t.endDate>=todayISO())));if(active)v.status='Maintenance';else if(v.status==='Maintenance')v.status='Available'}
function openMaintenanceForm(index=null,view=false,vehicleId=''){
 const isNew=index===null,obj=isNew?{vehicleId:vehicleId||db.vehicles[0]?.id||'',category:'Preventive Service',startDate:todayISO(),endDate:addDays(todayISO(),1),description:'',estimateCost:0,cost:0,status:'Scheduled'}:{...db.maintenanceTasks[index]},ro=view?'disabled':'',estimateCost=Number(obj.estimateCost??obj.cost??0);
 const idField=isNew?'':`<div class="field"><label>Task ID</label><input class="input" value="${esc(obj.id)}" disabled></div>`;
 const body=`<div class="form-grid">${idField}<div class="field"><label>Vehicle</label><select class="select" id="mt-vehicle" ${ro}>${optionMarkup(db.vehicles.map(v=>v.id),obj.vehicleId,'Select Vehicle')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Category</label><select class="select" id="mt-category" ${ro}>${optionMarkup(['Preventive Service','Corrective Repair','Tire Service','Engine Service','Body Repair','KIR Preparation','Other'],obj.category,'Select Category')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Status</label><select class="select" id="mt-status" ${ro}>${optionMarkup(['Scheduled','In Progress','Completed','Cancelled'],obj.status,'Select Status')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Start Date</label><input class="input" id="mt-start" type="date" value="${esc(obj.startDate)}" ${view?'readonly disabled':''}></div><div class="field"><label>End Date</label><input class="input" id="mt-end" type="date" value="${esc(obj.endDate)}" ${view?'readonly disabled':''}></div><div class="field"><label>Estimate Cost</label><input class="input" id="mt-estimate-cost" type="number" min="0" value="${esc(estimateCost)}" ${view?'readonly disabled':''}></div><div class="field full"><label>Description</label><textarea class="textarea" id="mt-description" ${view?'readonly disabled':''}>${esc(obj.description||'')}</textarea></div></div>`;
 let foot=`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`;
 if(!view)foot+=`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveMaintenance(${isNew?'null':index})">${isNew?'Create':'Save Changes'}</button>`;
 openModal((view?'Detail ':'')+'Maintenance Task',body,foot)
}
function saveMaintenance(index){
 const isNew=index===null,previous=isNew?null:db.maintenanceTasks[index],estimateCost=Number(document.getElementById('mt-estimate-cost').value||0),obj={id:isNew?nextMasterId('maintenanceTasks','MNT'):previous.id,vehicleId:document.getElementById('mt-vehicle').value,category:document.getElementById('mt-category').value,startDate:document.getElementById('mt-start').value,endDate:document.getElementById('mt-end').value,description:document.getElementById('mt-description').value.trim(),estimateCost,cost:estimateCost,actualCost:previous?.actualCost,status:document.getElementById('mt-status').value};
 if(Object.values({vehicleId:obj.vehicleId,category:obj.category,startDate:obj.startDate,endDate:obj.endDate,status:obj.status}).some(v=>!v)){toast('Lengkapi seluruh field wajib');return}
 if(obj.endDate<obj.startDate){toast('End Date tidak boleh sebelum Start Date');return}
 const oldVehicle=isNew?'':previous.vehicleId;
 if(isNew)db.maintenanceTasks.push(obj);else db.maintenanceTasks[index]=obj;
 syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(oldVehicle);syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(obj.vehicleId);saveDB();closeModal();renderAll();toast('Maintenance Task berhasil disimpan dengan ID '+obj.id)
}
function filteredMaintenanceRecords(){const q=(document.getElementById('maintenanceSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),st=document.getElementById('maintenanceStatusFilter')?.value||'';return db.maintenanceTasks.map((x,i)=>({x,i})).filter(o=>(!st||o.x.status===st)&&JSON.stringify(o.x).toLowerCase().includes(q))}
function renderMaintenance(){
 const body=document.getElementById('maintenanceTbody');if(!body)return;db.vehicles.forEach(v=>syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(v.id));
 body.innerHTML=filteredMaintenanceRecords().map(({x,i})=>{const v=db.vehicles.find(z=>z.id===x.vehicleId),extra=[],displayCost=Number(x.actualCost??x.estimateCost??x.cost??0);if(x.status==='Scheduled')extra.push({label:'Start Task',action:`openStartMaintenance('${x.id}')`});if(x.status==='In Progress')extra.push({label:'Complete Task',action:`advanceMaintenance('${x.id}','Completed')`});return `<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${esc(v?.plate||x.vehicleId)}<span class="table-note">${esc(x.vehicleId)}</span></td><td>${esc(x.category)}</td><td>${esc(x.startDate)} to ${esc(x.endDate)}</td><td>${esc(x.description||'-')}</td><td>${fmtIDR(displayCost)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td>${statusBadge(v?.status||'-')}</td><td>${actionMenuHTML([{label:'Detail',action:`openMaintenanceForm(${i},true)`},{label:'Edit',action:`openMaintenanceForm(${i})`},...extra,{label:'Delete',action:`deleteMaintenance(${i})`,danger:true}])}</td></tr>`}).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="9" class="empty">No maintenance task found.</td></tr>`
}
function downloadMaintenanceExcel(){const records=filteredMaintenanceRecords().map(o=>o.x),headers=['Task ID','Vehicle ID','Plate Number','Category','Start Date','End Date','Description','Cost','Task Status','Vehicle Status'],rows=records.map(x=>{const v=db.vehicles.find(z=>z.id===x.vehicleId),displayCost=Number(x.actualCost??x.estimateCost??x.cost??0);return [x.id,x.vehicleId,v?.plate||'',x.category,x.startDate,x.endDate,x.description,displayCost,x.status,v?.status||'']});downloadExcelTable(headers,rows,`TMS-maintenance-${todayISO()}.xls`);toast(records.length+' row downloaded')}
let pendingMaintenanceStart=null;
function openStartMaintenance(id,actualCostDraft=''){
 const x=db.maintenanceTasks.find(t=>t.id===id);if(!x)return;
 if(x.status!=='Scheduled'){toast('Hanya task berstatus Scheduled yang dapat dimulai');return}
 const v=db.vehicles.find(z=>z.id===x.vehicleId),estimateCost=Number(x.estimateCost??x.cost??0),body=`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Task ID</label><input class="input" value="${esc(x.id)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle</label><input class="input" value="${esc(v?`${v.plate} — ${x.vehicleId}`:x.vehicleId)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Category</label><input class="input" value="${esc(x.category)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Status</label><input class="input" value="${esc(x.status)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Start Date</label><input class="input" type="date" value="${esc(x.startDate)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>End Date</label><input class="input" type="date" value="${esc(x.endDate)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Estimate Cost</label><input class="input" type="number" value="${esc(estimateCost)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Actual Cost</label><input class="input" id="mt-start-actual-cost" type="number" min="0" step="1" value="${esc(actualCostDraft)}" placeholder="Input actual cost"></div><div class="field full"><label>Description</label><textarea class="textarea" disabled>${esc(x.description||'')}</textarea></div></div>`;
 openModal('Start Maintenance',body,`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="submitStartMaintenance('${x.id}')">Submit</button>`)
}
function submitStartMaintenance(id){
 const x=db.maintenanceTasks.find(t=>t.id===id),input=document.getElementById('mt-start-actual-cost');if(!x||!input)return;
 const raw=input.value.trim(),actualCost=Number(raw);
 if(raw===''||!Number.isFinite(actualCost)||actualCost<0){toast('Actual Cost wajib diisi dengan nilai yang valid');input.focus();return}
 pendingMaintenanceStart={id,actualCost};
 openModal('Are you sure?',`<div style="font-size:13px;color:#535b64">Start this maintenance task?</div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="cancelStartMaintenanceConfirmation()">No</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="confirmStartMaintenance()">Yes</button>`,true)
}
function cancelStartMaintenanceConfirmation(){
 const pending=pendingMaintenanceStart;if(!pending){closeModal();return}
 openStartMaintenance(pending.id,pending.actualCost)
}
function confirmStartMaintenance(){
 const pending=pendingMaintenanceStart;if(!pending)return;
 const x=db.maintenanceTasks.find(t=>t.id===pending.id);if(!x){pendingMaintenanceStart=null;closeModal();return}
 x.estimateCost=Number(x.estimateCost??x.cost??0);x.actualCost=pending.actualCost;x.status='In Progress';if(x.startDate>todayISO())x.startDate=todayISO();syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(x.vehicleId);saveDB();pendingMaintenanceStart=null;closeModal();renderAll();toast('Maintenance status updated to In Progress')
}
function advanceMaintenance(id,status){const x=db.maintenanceTasks.find(t=>t.id===id);if(!x)return;x.status=status;if(status==='In Progress'&&x.startDate>todayISO())x.startDate=todayISO();if(status==='Completed'&&x.endDate<todayISO())x.endDate=todayISO();syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(x.vehicleId);saveDB();renderAll();toast('Maintenance status updated to '+status)}
function deleteMaintenance(index){const x=db.maintenanceTasks[index];if(x.status==='In Progress'){toast('Task In Progress harus diselesaikan atau dibatalkan dahulu');return}if(!confirm('Delete maintenance task ini?'))return;db.maintenanceTasks.splice(index,1);syncVehicleMaintenanceStatus(x.vehicleId);saveDB();renderAll();toast('Maintenance Task berhasil dihapus')}

function renderDocuments(){const q=(document.getElementById('docSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),t=document.getElementById('docTypeFilter')?.value||'';const rows=db.documents.filter(x=>x.status==='Need Planning').filter(x=>(!t||x.type===t)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q));document.getElementById('documentTbody').innerHTML=rows.map(x=>`<tr><td><input type="checkbox" ${selectedDocs.has(x.id)?'checked':''} onchange="selectDoc('${x.id}',this.checked)"></td><td>${esc(x.alert)}</td><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}<br><span class="muted">${x.type==='DO'?'Delivery Order':'Stock Transfer Out'}</span></td><td>${esc(x.customer)}</td><td>${esc(x.origin)}</td><td>${esc(x.destination)}</td><td>${x.weight.toLocaleString()} kg</td><td>${x.volume} m³</td><td>${statusBadge(x.priority)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td><button class="icon-btn" onclick="documentDetail('${x.id}')">Detail</button></td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">No documents need planning.</td></tr>`;updateSelectedInfo()}
function selectDoc(id,check){check?selectedDocs.add(id):selectedDocs.delete(id);updateSelectedInfo()}
function toggleAllDocs(v){selectedDocs.clear();if(v)db.documents.filter(x=>x.status==='Need Planning').forEach(x=>selectedDocs.add(x.id));renderDocuments()}
function updateSelectedInfo(){const docs=db.documents.filter(x=>selectedDocs.has(x.id)),w=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.weight,0),v=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.volume,0);document.getElementById('selectedDocInfo').textContent=`${docs.length} selected • ${w.toLocaleString()} kg • ${v.toFixed(1)} m³`}

</div><input type="hidden" id="sw-docs" value="${ids.join('|')}">`;
