function activeExpeditionCarriers(){
  return (db.carriers||[]).filter(x=>['3PL','Contracted Carrier'].includes(x.type)&&x.status==='Active');
}
function activeCarrierContracts(carrier,shipmentDate){
  const effectiveDate=shipmentDate||document.getElementById('sw-date')?.value||todayISO();
  return (db.contracts||[]).filter(x=>
    x.carrier===carrier&&
    x.status==='Active'&&
    (!x.startDate||x.startDate<=effectiveDate)&&
    (!x.endDate||x.endDate>=effectiveDate)
  );
}
function syncContract(){
  const supplier=document.getElementById('sw-supplier');
  const contract=document.getElementById('sw-contract');
  if(!contract)return;
  const carrier=supplier?.value||'';
  if(!carrier){
    contract.innerHTML='<option value="">No expedition carrier available</option>';
    contract.disabled=true;
    return;
  }
  const contracts=activeCarrierContracts(carrier);
  contract.innerHTML=contracts.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.id)}">${esc(x.id)} — ${esc(x.rate||'Contract Rate')} — ${fmtIDR(x.baseRate)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No active contract</option>';
  contract.disabled=!contracts.length;
}
function calculateWizardUtil(){const ids=document.getElementById('sw-docs').value.split('|'),docs=db.documents.filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id)),v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-vehicle')?.value);if(!v)return;const w=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.weight,0),vol=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.volume,0),wu=Math.round(w/v.weight*100),vu=Math.round(vol/v.volume*100),u=Math.max(wu,vu);document.getElementById('sw-util').innerHTML=`<div class="notice ${u>100?'danger':u>90?'warn':''}"><b>Capacity Validation:</b> Weight ${wu}% • Volume ${vu}% • Primary Utilization ${u}% ${u>100?'— BLOCKED, choose another vehicle or split shipment.':''}</div>`}
function createShipmentPlan(){const ids=document.getElementById('sw-docs').value.split('|'),docs=db.documents.filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id)),src=document.getElementById('sw-source').value;let vehicle='-',driver='-',supplier='-',contract='-',route='Direct to '+document.getElementById('sw-stop').value,wu=0,vu=0,u=0;if(src==='Fleet Company'){const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-vehicle').value),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-driver').value),r=db.routes.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-route').value);const w=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.weight,0),vol=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.volume,0);wu=Math.round(w/v.weight*100);vu=Math.round(vol/v.volume*100);u=Math.max(wu,vu);if(u>100){toast('Shipment melebihi kapasitas kendaraan');return}vehicle=v.plate;driver=d.name;supplier=v.carrier;route=r.origin+' → '+r.destination}else{supplier=document.getElementById('sw-supplier').value;contract=document.getElementById('sw-contract').value;if(!supplier||!contract){toast('Carrier wajib memiliki kontrak aktif');return}}
const num='PL/'+String(Math.max(0,...db.plans.map(x=>Number(x.id.replace(/\D/g,''))))+1).padStart(5,'0');const p={id:num,docs:ids,docType:[...new Set(docs.map(x=>x.type))].map(x=>x==='DO'?'Delivery Order':'Stock Transfer Out').join(' + '),source:src,supplier,contract,vehicle,driver,shipmentDate:document.getElementById('sw-date').value,eta:document.getElementById('sw-eta').value,origin:docs[0].origin,destination:[...new Set(docs.map(x=>x.destination))].join(' / '),route,weight:docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.weight,0),volume:Number(docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.volume,0).toFixed(1)),weightUtil:wu,volumeUtil:vu,util:u,status:'Planned',health:'On Schedule',plannedCost:Number(document.getElementById('sw-cost').value||0),actualCost:0,lastUpdate:'just now',stops:docs.map(x=>({doc:x.id,customer:x.customer,status:'On Going',arrival:'-',pod:false})),loadedDocs:[]};db.plans.push(p);docs.forEach(x=>x.status='Done Planning');if(src==='Fleet Company'){const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===vehicle),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===driver);if(v)v.status='Reserved';if(d)d.status='Assigned'}saveDB();selectedDocs.clear();closeModal();renderAll();planningTab(document.querySelector('#page-planning .tab:nth-child(2)'),'planPanel');toast('Plan Number berhasil dibuat: '+num)}
function renderPlans(){const q=(document.getElementById('planSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),st=document.getElementById('planStatusFilter')?.value||'';document.getElementById('planTbody').innerHTML=db.plans.filter(x=>(!st||x.status===st)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map((p,i)=>`<tr><td class="mono">${p.id}</td><td>${esc(p.docType)}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.source)}</td><td>${p.shipmentDate}</td><td>${p.eta}</td><td>${esc(p.route)}<br><span class="muted">${esc(p.destination)}</span></td><td>${p.source==='Fleet Company'?esc(p.vehicle)+' / '+esc(p.driver):esc(p.supplier)}</td><td>${p.source==='Fleet Company'?`W ${p.weightUtil}% / V ${p.volumeUtil}%<br>${statusBadge(p.util>100?'Over Capacity':p.util>90?'High Utilization':'Valid')}`:'Contract rate'}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.status)}</td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')">Detail</button><button class="icon-btn" onclick="goSchedulePlan('${p.id}')">Schedule</button>${p.status==='Planned'?`<button class="icon-btn" onclick="setLoadingPlan('${p.id}')">Loading</button>`:''}<button class="icon-btn" onclick="deletePlan('${p.id}')">Delete</button></div></td></tr>`).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="10" class="empty">No plan found.</td></tr>`}
function planDetail(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id),fo=db.fleetOrders.find(x=>x.planId===id);const stopRows=p.stops.map(s=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(s.doc)}</td><td>${esc(s.customer)}</td><td>${statusBadge(s.status)}</td><td>${esc(s.arrival)}</td><td>${s.pod?'<button class="icon-btn" onclick="toast(\'POD preview opened\')">View Photo / Signature</button>':'No Data'}</td></tr>`).join('');const syncEvents=db.syncLogs.filter(x=>x.ref===id||x.ref===fo?.id||p.docs.includes(x.ref)).slice(0,5);openModal('Detail '+id,`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Shipment Option</label><div>${statusBadge(p.source)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Status</label><div>${statusBadge(p.status)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Fleet Order Number</label><div class="mono">${fo?fo.id:'Not Created'}</div></div><div class="field"><label>McEasy Sync</label><div>${fo?statusBadge(fo.sync):statusBadge('Pending')}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Shipment Date</label><div>${p.shipmentDate}</div></div><div class="field"><label>ETA</label><div>${p.eta}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle / Supplier</label><div>${esc(p.source==='Fleet Company'?p.vehicle+' / '+p.driver:p.supplier)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Planned Cost</label><div>${fmtIDR(p.plannedCost)}</div></div><div class="field full"><label>Shipment Route</label><div>${esc(p.route)}</div></div></div><div class="section-title">Document / Stop List</div><div class="table-wrap"><table class="tbl"><thead><tr><th>Document</th><th>Customer</th><th>Status</th><th>Arrival</th><th>Attachment</th></tr></thead><tbody>${stopRows}</tbody></table></div><div class="section-title">Integration Timeline</div><div class="timeline">${syncEvents.length?syncEvents.map(e=>`<div class="timeline-item"><b>${esc(e.event)} • ${statusBadge(e.status)}</b><p>${esc(e.time)} — ${esc(e.direction)} — ${esc(e.message)}</p></div>`).join(''):'<div class="timeline-item"><b>No integration event</b><p>Create or sync Fleet Order to start the timeline.</p></div>'}</div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>${fo?`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal();fleetOrderDetail('${fo.id}')">Open Fleet Order</button>`:`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="closeModal();openFleetOrderForm('${p.id}')">Create Fleet Order</button>`}`)}
function deletePlan(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!p||['Loading','In Transit','Completed'].includes(p.status)){toast('Plan dengan proses aktif/selesai tidak dapat dihapus');return}if(!confirm('Delete '+id+'?'))return;p.docs.forEach(id=>{const d=db.documents.find(x=>x.id===id);if(d)d.status='Need Planning'});db.plans=db.plans.filter(x=>x.id!==id);saveDB();renderAll();toast('Plan deleted')}
function goSchedulePlan(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);scheduleStart=dateISO(new Date(isoDate(p.shipmentDate).setDate(isoDate(p.shipmentDate).getDate()-isoDate(p.shipmentDate).getDay()+1)));goPage('schedule')}
function setLoadingPlan(id){activeLoadingPlan=id;goPage('loading');document.getElementById('loadingPlanSelect').value=id;selectLoadingPlan(id)}
function generateRecommendations(){const docs=db.documents.filter(x=>x.status==='Need Planning'),groups={};docs.forEach(d=>{const zone=d.destination.includes('Bandung')?'Bandung':d.destination.includes('Jakarta')||d.destination.includes('Tangerang')?'Jabodetabek':'Other';const k=d.origin+'|'+zone+'|'+d.priority;(groups[k]??=[]).push(d)});const box=document.getElementById('recommendations');box.innerHTML=Object.values(groups).map((g,i)=>{const w=g.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.weight,0),v=g.reduce((a,b)=>a+b.volume,0);return `<div class="reco-card"><h3>Recommendation ${i+1} ${g[0].priority==='High'?'<span class="badge b-red">High Priority</span>':''}</h3><p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted);margin-bottom:8px">${esc(g[0].origin)} → ${esc(g.map(x=>x.destination).join(', '))}</p>${g.map(x=>`<div class="check-row"><input type="checkbox" checked disabled><span class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</span></div>`).join('')}<div class="notice" style="margin-top:10px">${g.length} docs • ${w.toLocaleString()} kg • ${v.toFixed(1)} m³</div><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick='openShipmentWizard(${JSON.stringify(g.map(x=>x.id))})'>Accept & Plan</button></div>`}).join('')||'<div class="empty">No documents available for recommendation.</div>'}

function scheduleShift(n){scheduleStart=addDays(scheduleStart,n);renderSchedule()}
function renderSchedule(){const start=isoDate(scheduleStart),days=[...Array(7)].map((_,i)=>dateISO(new Date(start.getTime()+i*86400000)));document.getElementById('scheduleRange').textContent=`${days[0]} — ${days[6]}`;const sf=document.getElementById('scheduleSourceFilter')?.value||'';const resources=[...new Set(db.plans.filter(p=>!sf||p.source===sf).map(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company'?(p.vehicle+' • '+p.driver):('EXP • '+p.supplier)))];let html='<div class="schedule-grid"><div class="sch-cell sch-head">Resource</div>'+days.map(d=>`<div class="sch-cell sch-head">${new Date(d+'T00:00').toLocaleDateString('id-ID',{weekday:'short',day:'2-digit',month:'short'})}</div>`).join('');resources.forEach(r=>{html+=`<div class="sch-cell sch-resource">${esc(r)}<small>${r.startsWith('EXP')?'Contracted carrier':'Internal fleet'}</small></div>`;days.forEach(d=>{const cards=db.plans.filter(p=>(p.source==='Fleet Company'?(p.vehicle+' • '+p.driver):('EXP • '+p.supplier))===r&&p.shipmentDate===d);html+=`<div class="sch-cell sch-day" ondragover="event.preventDefault();this.classList.add('dragover')" ondragleave="this.classList.remove('dragover')" ondrop="dropPlan(event,'${d}')">${cards.map(p=>`<div class="ship-card ${p.health==='Exception'?'exception':p.status==='Loading'||p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'?'loading':p.source==='Fleet Company'?'internal':'expedition'}" draggable="${['Planned','Draft'].includes(p.status)}" ondragstart="event.dataTransfer.setData('text','${p.id}')" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')"><b>${p.id}</b><span>${esc(p.destination)} • ${p.util||'-'}%</span></div>`).join('')}</div>`});});html+='</div>';document.getElementById('scheduleBoard').innerHTML=html}
function dropPlan(e,date){e.currentTarget.classList.remove('dragover');const id=e.dataTransfer.getData('text'),p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!p)return;if(!['Planned','Draft'].includes(p.status)){toast('Only Draft/Planned shipment can be rescheduled');return}const conflict=db.plans.some(x=>x.id!==id&&x.source==='Fleet Company'&&p.source==='Fleet Company'&&x.vehicle===p.vehicle&&x.shipmentDate===date&&!['Completed'].includes(x.status));if(conflict){toast('Vehicle schedule conflict. Choose another day/resource.');return}p.shipmentDate=date;p.eta=date;p.lastUpdate='rescheduled just now';saveDB();renderSchedule();renderPlans();toast(id+' rescheduled to '+date)}

function renderLoading(){const plans=db.plans.filter(p=>['Planned','Loading','Ready to Dispatch'].includes(p.status));const sel=document.getElementById('loadingPlanSelect');sel.innerHTML=plans.map(p=>`<option value="${p.id}">${p.id} — ${p.source} — ${p.status}</option>`).join('')||'<option>No plan available</option>';if(!activeLoadingPlan||!plans.some(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan))activeLoadingPlan=plans[0]?.id||'';sel.value=activeLoadingPlan;selectLoadingPlan(activeLoadingPlan)}
function selectLoadingPlan(id){activeLoadingPlan=id;const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!p){document.getElementById('loadingContent').innerHTML='<div class="empty">No shipment waiting for loading.</div>';return}const steps=['Planned','Loading','Ready to Dispatch','In Transit'];const current=steps.indexOf(p.status);document.getElementById('loadingFlow').innerHTML=`<div class="flow">${steps.map((s,i)=>`${i?'<span class="flow-arrow">→</span>':''}<span class="flow-step ${i<current?'done':i===current?'current':''}">${s}</span>`).join('')}</div>`;const loaded=p.loadedDocs||[];document.getElementById('loadingContent').innerHTML=`<div class="grid-2"><div><div class="notice"><b>${p.id}</b> • ${p.vehicle} • ${p.driver}<br>${p.route}</div><div class="scan-box"><input class="input" id="scanDocInput" placeholder="Scan / input DO or STO number"><button class="btn btn-cyan" onclick="scanLoadingDoc()">Scan Document</button></div><div class="load-list">${p.docs.map(id=>`<div class="load-row"><div class="name"><b class="mono">${id}</b><small>${loaded.includes(id)?'Validated for this shipment':'Waiting for scan'}</small></div><div>${statusBadge(loaded.includes(id)?'Fully Loaded':'Not Loaded')}</div><div class="qty">${loaded.includes(id)?'100%':'0%'}</div></div>`).join('')}</div></div><div><div class="card"><div class="card-head">Loading Summary</div><div class="card-body"><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Document Loaded</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${loaded.length/p.docs.length*100}%"></span></div><b>${loaded.length}/${p.docs.length}</b></div><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Item Verification</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${loaded.length/p.docs.length*100}%"></span></div><b>${loaded.length===p.docs.length?'100%':'0%'}</b></div><div class="notice ${p.util>90?'warn':''}">Vehicle capacity utilization: <b>${p.util}%</b></div>${p.status==='Planned'?`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="startLoading()">Start Loading</button>`:p.status==='Loading'?`<button class="btn btn-success" ${loaded.length!==p.docs.length?'disabled':''} onclick="completeLoading()">Complete Loading</button>`:`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="dispatchPlan()">Gate-Out / Dispatch</button>`}</div></div></div></div>`}
function startLoading(){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);p.status='Loading';p.lastUpdate='loading started now';saveDB();renderLoading();renderDashboard();toast('Loading started')}
function scanLoadingDoc(){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(p.status!=='Loading'){toast('Start Loading terlebih dahulu');return}const val=document.getElementById('scanDocInput').value.trim();if(!p.docs.includes(val)){toast('Wrong shipment: document tidak terdaftar pada plan ini');return}p.loadedDocs??=[];if(p.loadedDocs.includes(val)){toast('Duplicate scan ditolak');return}p.loadedDocs.push(val);p.lastUpdate='scan just now';saveDB();renderLoading();toast(val+' verified')}
function completeLoading(){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);if((p.loadedDocs||[]).length!==p.docs.length){toast('Seluruh document harus fully loaded');return}p.status='Ready to Dispatch';p.lastUpdate='loading completed now';saveDB();renderLoading();renderDashboard();toast('Loading completed')}
function dispatchPlan(){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);p.status='In Transit';p.health='On Schedule';p.lastUpdate='departed just now';if(p.source==='Fleet Company'){const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver);if(v)v.status='In Transit';if(d)d.status='On Trip'}saveDB();renderAll();goPage('monitoring');toast('Gate-out recorded. Shipment In Transit.')}

function monitorPlans(){return db.plans.filter(p=>!['Completed','Draft'].includes(p.status)&&p.status!=='Planned')}
function renderMonitoring(){const ps=monitorPlans(),del=ps.reduce((a,p)=>a+p.stops.filter(s=>s.status==='Successfully Delivered').length,0),total=ps.reduce((a,p)=>a+p.stops.length,0),risk=ps.filter(p=>p.health==='At Risk'||p.health==='Exception').length;document.getElementById('monitorKpis').innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Active Shipments',v:ps.length,f:'On-going only',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Total Stops',v:total,f:'Across active plans',a:'var(--cyan-dark)'},{l:'Delivered Stops',v:del,f:`${total?Math.round(del/total*100):0}% completion`,a:'var(--green)'},{l:'At Risk / Exception',v:risk,f:'Needs dispatcher action',a:'var(--orange)'},{l:'No Update >30 min',v:ps.filter(p=>String(p.lastUpdate).includes('35')).length,f:'Stale tracking',a:'var(--red)'}]);document.getElementById('monitorCount').textContent=ps.length+' active';document.getElementById('monitorList').innerHTML=ps.map((p,i)=>`<div class="ship-item ${i===0?'active':''}" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')"><div class="top"><b>${p.id}</b>${statusBadge(p.health)}<span class="age">${p.lastUpdate}</span></div><div class="meta">${esc(p.source==='Fleet Company'?p.vehicle+' • '+p.driver:p.supplier)}<br>${esc(p.destination)}</div></div>`).join('')||'<div class="empty">No on-going shipments.</div>';renderMonitoringTable()}
function renderMonitoringTable(){const q=(document.getElementById('monitorSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),src=document.getElementById('monitorSource')?.value||'';document.getElementById('monitorTbody').innerHTML=monitorPlans().filter(p=>(!src||p.source===src)&&JSON.stringify(p).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map(p=>{const d=p.stops.filter(s=>s.status==='Successfully Delivered').length,u=p.stops.length-d,fo=db.fleetOrders.find(x=>x.planId===p.id);return `<tr><td class="mono">${p.id}</td><td class="mono">${fo?fo.id:'-'}</td><td>${fo?statusBadge(fo.sync):statusBadge('Pending')}</td><td>${p.shipmentDate}</td><td>${esc(p.docType)}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.source)}</td><td>${p.eta}</td><td>${p.stops.length}</td><td>${d}</td><td>${u}</td><td>${p.lastUpdate}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.health||p.status)}</td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')">Detail</button>${fo?`<button class="icon-btn" onclick="fleetOrderDetail('${fo.id}')">Fleet Order</button>`:''}${p.source==='Expedition'?`<button class="icon-btn" onclick="processExpedition('${p.id}')">Process</button>`:''}</div></td></tr>`}).join('')||`<tr><td colspan="13" class="empty">No on-going shipment found.</td></tr>`}
function processExpedition(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);const rows=p.stops.map((s,i)=>`<tr><td class="mono">${s.doc}</td><td>${esc(s.customer)}</td><td><input class="input" type="datetime-local" id="arr-${i}" value="${s.arrival==='-'?'':s.arrival.replace(' ','T')}"></td><td><select class="select" id="st-${i}"><option ${s.status==='On Going'?'selected':''}>On Going</option><option ${s.status==='Successfully Delivered'?'selected':''}>Successfully Delivered</option><option ${s.status==='Unsuccessfully Delivered'?'selected':''}>Unsuccessfully Delivered</option><option ${s.status==='Partially Delivered'?'selected':''}>Partially Delivered</option></select></td><td><input class="input" type="file" id="pod-${i}"></td></tr>`).join('');openModal('Process '+id,`<div class="notice">Expedition diproses per DO. Shipment hilang dari Monitoring ketika seluruh stop tidak lagi On Going.</div><div class="table-wrap"><table class="tbl"><thead><tr><th>DO Number</th><th>Customer</th><th>Date to Arrival</th><th>Shipment Status</th><th>POD</th></tr></thead><tbody>${rows}</tbody></table></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveExpedition('${id}')">Save Process</button>`)}
function saveExpedition(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);p.stops.forEach((s,i)=>{s.status=document.getElementById('st-'+i).value;s.arrival=document.getElementById('arr-'+i).value.replace('T',' ')||'-';s.pod=document.getElementById('pod-'+i).files.length>0||s.status==='Successfully Delivered'});if(p.stops.every(s=>s.status!=='On Going')){p.status='Completed';p.health='Completed';p.actualCost=Math.round(p.plannedCost*(.95+Math.random()*.15));p.lastUpdate='Completed'}else{p.health=p.stops.some(s=>s.status.includes('Unsuccess')||s.status.includes('Partial'))?'Exception':'On Schedule';p.lastUpdate='just now'}saveDB();closeModal();renderAll();toast('Shipment process saved')}

const driverSteps=['Assigned','Trip Accepted','Pre-Trip Check','Loading Confirmed','Dispatched / Start Trip','Arrived at Stop','Delivery Result & ePOD','Return to Origin','Trip Closed'];
function driverPlan(){return db.plans.find(p=>p.id===db.driverState.planId)||db.plans.find(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company'&&!['Completed'].includes(p.status))}
function renderDriverMobile(){const p=driverPlan(),s=db.driverState.step;document.getElementById('driverStepper').innerHTML=driverSteps.map((x,i)=>`<div class="step-line ${i<s?'done':i===s?'active':''}"><div class="step-circle">${i<s?'✓':i+1}</div><div class="step-content"><b>${x}</b><p>${i<s?'Completed':i===s?'Current action':'Waiting previous step'}</p></div></div>`).join('');if(!p){document.getElementById('phoneBody').innerHTML='<div class="empty">No trip assigned.</div>';return}document.getElementById('driverTripSummary').innerHTML=`<div class="phone-row"><span>Plan</span><b>${p.id}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Vehicle</span><b>${p.vehicle}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Route</span><b>${esc(p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Status</span><span>${statusBadge(p.status)}</span></div>`;let html='';if(s===0)html=`${tripCard(p)}<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('accept')">Accept Trip</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverAction('reject')">Reject with Reason</button>`;else if(s===1)html=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Pre-Trip Vehicle Check</h4>${['Odometer & fuel','Tyre','Brake','Lights','Body condition','STNK / KIR'].map(x=>`<label class="check-row" style="padding:5px 0"><input type="checkbox" class="precheck">${x}</label>`).join('')}</div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('check')">Submit Checklist</button>`;else if(s===2)html=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Loading Confirmation</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Documents</span><b>${p.docs.length}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Packages</span><b>${p.docs.length*8}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Seal No.</span><b>SEAL-260625</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('loading')">Confirm Load Received</button>`;else if(s===3)html=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="notice" style="margin:10px 13px">Waiting gate operator to dispatch. Prototype allows simulation.</div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('start')">Start Trip</button>`;else if(s===4)html=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Next Stop</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(p.stops[0].customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>ETA</span><b>${p.eta} 14:30</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('arrive')">Arrived at Stop</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverException()">Report Exception</button>`;else if(s===5)html=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Delivery Result</h4><select class="select" id="mobileResult" style="width:100%"><option>Successfully Delivered</option><option>Partially Delivered</option><option>Failed Delivery</option></select><input class="input" id="receiverName" placeholder="Receiver Name" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><input class="input" placeholder="OTP / Signature reference" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('pod')">Submit ePOD</button>`;else if(s===6)html=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>All Stops Completed</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Return Destination</span><b>${p.origin}</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('return')">Start Return</button>`;else if(s===7)html=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Vehicle Handover</h4><input class="input" placeholder="Odometer End" style="width:100%"><input class="input" placeholder="Fuel End %" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><textarea class="textarea" placeholder="Damage / expense note" style="margin-top:8px"></textarea></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('close')">Close Trip</button>`;else html=`<div class="phone-card" style="text-align:center;margin-top:60px"><div style="font-size:44px;color:var(--green)">✓</div><h4>Trip Completed</h4><p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted)">${p.id} has been closed.</p></div><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverAction('reset')">Back to My Trips</button>`;document.getElementById('phoneBody').innerHTML=html}
function tripCard(p){return `<div class="phone-card"><h4>${p.id} ${statusBadge(p.status)}</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Vehicle</span><b>${p.vehicle}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Origin</span><b>${p.origin}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Planned Time</span><b>${p.shipmentDate}</b></div></div>`}
function driverAction(a){const p=driverPlan(),st=db.driverState;if(a==='reject'){toast('Reject reason required — simulation cancelled');return}if(a==='check'&&[...document.querySelectorAll('.precheck')].some(x=>!x.checked)){toast('Seluruh checklist wajib diisi');return}if(a==='accept')st.step=1;else if(a==='check')st.step=2;else if(a==='loading')st.step=3;else if(a==='start'){st.step=4;p.status='In Transit';p.health='On Schedule';p.lastUpdate='Driver started trip'}else if(a==='arrive'){st.step=5;p.lastUpdate='Arrived at stop'}else if(a==='pod'){const r=document.getElementById('mobileResult').value;if(!document.getElementById('receiverName').value.trim()){toast('Receiver Name wajib');return}p.stops[0].status=r;p.stops[0].pod=true;p.stops[0].arrival=new Date().toISOString().slice(0,16).replace('T',' ');p.health=r==='Successfully Delivered'?'On Schedule':'Exception';st.step=6}else if(a==='return'){st.step=7;p.status='Returning';p.lastUpdate='Returning to origin'}else if(a==='close'){st.step=8;p.status='Completed';p.health='Completed';p.actualCost=Math.round(p.plannedCost*1.04);p.lastUpdate='Completed';const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver);if(v)v.status='Available';if(d)d.status='Available'}else if(a==='reset'){st.step=0}saveDB();/* initialization moved to modular override */toast('Driver status updated')}
function driverException(){const p=driverPlan();openModal('Report Delivery Exception',`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Exception Type</label><select class="select" id="exType"><option>Traffic Delay</option><option>Customer Closed</option><option>Rejected by Customer</option><option>Vehicle Breakdown</option><option>Damage</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Photo Evidence</label><input class="input" type="file"></div><div class="field full"><label>Notes</label><textarea class="textarea" id="exNote"></textarea></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-danger" onclick="saveDriverException('${p.id}')">Submit Exception</button>`)}
function saveDriverException(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);p.health='Exception';p.lastUpdate='Exception just now';closeModal();saveDB();/* initialization moved to modular override */toast('Dispatcher notified')}


let activeMapping='address';
function syncClass(s){return s==='Synced'?'ok':s==='Failed'?'fail':'pending'}
function renderIntegration(){const logs=db.syncLogs||[],q=(document.getElementById('syncSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),f=document.getElementById('syncStatusFilter')?.value||'',synced=logs.filter(x=>x.status==='Synced').length,failed=logs.filter(x=>x.status==='Failed').length,pending=logs.filter(x=>x.status==='Pending').length;const el=document.getElementById('integrationKpis');if(!el)return;el.innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Connection',v:db.mceasyConfig.status,f:`${db.mceasyConfig.environment} • ${db.mceasyConfig.latency}`,a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Synced Events',v:synced,f:'Successful exchange',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Pending Queue',v:pending,f:'Waiting API response',a:'var(--orange)'},{l:'Failed Events',v:failed,f:'Needs retry or correction',a:'var(--red)'},{l:'Webhook',v:db.mceasyConfig.webhook,f:`Last sync ${db.mceasyConfig.lastSync}`,a:'var(--purple)'}]);document.getElementById('mceasyConnectionBadge').innerHTML=statusBadge(db.mceasyConfig.status);document.getElementById('mceasyConnectionInfo').innerHTML=[['Environment',db.mceasyConfig.environment],['Company',db.mceasyConfig.company],['API Version',db.mceasyConfig.apiVersion],['Webhook',db.mceasyConfig.webhook],['Last Successful Sync',db.mceasyConfig.lastSync],['Average Latency',db.mceasyConfig.latency]].map(x=>`<div class="info-row"><span>${x[0]}</span><b>${esc(x[1])}</b></div>`).join('');document.getElementById('syncLogTbody').innerHTML=logs.filter(x=>(!f||x.status===f)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map(x=>`<tr><td>${x.time}</td><td>${esc(x.direction)}</td><td>${esc(x.object)}</td><td class="mono">${esc(x.ref)}</td><td>${esc(x.event)}</td><td><span class="sync-log-status"><i class="sync-dot ${syncClass(x.status)}"></i>${statusBadge(x.status)}</span></td><td>${x.retry}</td><td>${esc(x.message)}</td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" onclick="syncLogDetail('${x.id}')">Detail</button>${x.status==='Failed'?`<button class="icon-btn" onclick="retrySync('${x.id}')">Retry</button>`:''}</div></td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="9" class="empty">No sync event found.</td></tr>'}
function testMcEasyConnection(){db.mceasyConfig.status='Connected';db.mceasyConfig.latency=(140+Math.floor(Math.random()*90))+' ms';db.mceasyConfig.lastSync=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16);saveDB();renderIntegration();toast('Connection successful')}
function syncAllMcEasy(){db.syncLogs.filter(x=>x.status==='Pending').forEach(x=>{x.status='Synced';x.message='Synchronized manually';x.time=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)});db.mceasyConfig.lastSync=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16);saveDB();renderIntegration();renderFleetOrders();toast('All pending data synchronized')}
function simulateWebhook(){const fo=db.fleetOrders.find(x=>!['Delivered','Failed'].includes(x.status))||db.fleetOrders[0];const next={Confirm:'Dijadwalkan',Dijadwalkan:'Loading',Loading:'Dijalankan',Dijalankan:'OTW Tujuan','OTW Tujuan':'Unloading',Unloading:'Delivered'}[fo.status]||fo.status;fo.status=next;fo.updated='just now';db.syncLogs.unshift({id:uid('SYNC'),time:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),direction:'McEasy → Prieds',object:'Fleet Order',ref:fo.id,event:'order.status.updated',status:'Synced',retry:0,message:'Webhook status updated to '+next});applyFleetOrderToPlan(fo);saveDB();renderIntegration();toast('Webhook received: '+next)}
function retrySync(id){const x=db.syncLogs.find(v=>v.id===id);x.retry=(x.retry||0)+1;if(x.object==='Address'){const a=db.addressMappings.find(v=>v.id===x.ref);if(a&&!a.lat){toast('Retry failed: coordinate still incomplete');x.message='Latitude and longitude are required';saveDB();renderIntegration();return}}x.status='Synced';x.message='Retry successful';x.time=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16);saveDB();renderIntegration();toast('Sync retry successful')}
function syncLogDetail(id){const x=db.syncLogs.find(v=>v.id===id);openModal('Sync Event '+id,`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Direction</label><div>${esc(x.direction)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Status</label><div>${statusBadge(x.status)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Object</label><div>${esc(x.object)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Reference</label><div class="mono">${esc(x.ref)}</div></div><div class="field full"><label>Event</label><div>${esc(x.event)}</div></div><div class="field full"><label>Response / Message</label><div class="notice ${x.status==='Failed'?'danger':''}">${esc(x.message)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Attempt</label><div>${x.retry+1}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Timestamp</label><div>${x.time}</div></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>${x.status==='Failed'?`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="closeModal();retrySync('${x.id}')">Retry Sync</button>`:''}`)}

function mappingTab(btn,type){activeMapping=type;btn.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(x=>x.classList.toggle('active',x===btn));renderMapping()}
function mappingData(){return activeMapping==='address'?db.addressMappings:activeMapping==='product'?db.productMappings:activeMapping==='fleet'?db.fleetMappings:db.statusMappings}

min</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" onclick="editAddressMapping('${x.id}')">Edit</button><button class="icon-btn" onclick="validateMapping('address','${x.id}')">Validate</button></div></td></tr>`).join('')}else if(activeMapping==='product'){head='<tr><th>SKU</th><th>Product</th><th>UOM</th><th>Weight</th><th>Volume</th><th>Temperature</th><th>Readiness</th><th>Action</th></tr>';rows=data.map(x=>`<tr><td class="mono">${x.id}</td><td>${esc(x.name)}</td><td>${x.uom}</td><td>${x.weight!==''?x.weight+' kg':'-'}</td><td>${x.volume!==''?x.volume+' m³':'-'}</td><td>${x.tempMin==='-'?'-':x.tempMin+' to '+x.tempMax+' °C'}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" onclick="editProductMapping('${x.id}')">Edit</button><button class="icon-btn" onclick="validateMapping('product','${x.id}')">Validate</button></div></td></tr>`).join('')}else if(activeMapping==='fleet'){head='<tr><th>Plate Number</th><th>Category / Type</th><th>Odometer</th><th>Volume</th><th>Main / Backup Driver</th><th>GPS / IMEI</th><th>Operating Hours</th><th>Sync</th><th>Action</th></tr>';rows=data.map(x=>`<tr><td ${esc(x.backup)}</div></td><td>${esc(x.gps)}</td><td>${x.hours}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" Status</th><th>McEasy Status</th><th>Trigger</th><th>Direction</th><th>Action</th></tr>';rows=data.map((x,i)=>`<tr><td>${statusBadge(x.prieds)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.mceasy)}</td><td>${esc(x.trigger)}</td><td>${esc(x.direction)}</td><td><button class="icon-btn" onclick="editStatusMapping(${i})">Edit</button></td></tr>`).join('')}wrap.innerHTML=`<table class="tbl"><thead>${head}</thead><tbody>${rows||'<tr><td colspan="9" class="empty">No mapping found.</td></tr>'}</tbody></table>`}
function openMappingForm(){if(activeMapping==='address')editAddressMapping('');else if(activeMapping==='product')editProductMapping('');else if(activeMapping==='fleet')editFleetMapping('');else editStatusMapping(-1)}
function editAddressMapping(id){const x=db.addressMappings.find(v=>v.id===id)||{id:'',customer:'',location:'',address:'',lat:'',lng:'',radius:100,open:'08:00',close:'17:00',unload:30,contact:'',status:'Invalid Coordinate'};openModal(id?'Edit Address Mapping':'Add Address Mapping',`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Customer ID</label><input class="input" id="am-id" value="${esc(x.id)}" ${id?'readonly':''}></div><div class="field"><label>Customer Name</label><input class="input" id="am-customer" value="${esc(x.customer)}"></div><div class="field"><label>Location Name</label><input class="input" id="am-location" value="${esc(x.location)}"></div><div class="field"><label>Contact</label><input class="input" id="am-contact" value="${esc(x.contact)}"></div><div class="field full"><label>Address</label><textarea class="textarea" id="am-address">${esc(x.address)}</textarea></div><div class="field"><label>Latitude</label><input class="input" id="am-lat" type="number" step="any" value="${x.lat}"></div><div class="field"><label>Longitude</label><input class="input" id="am-lng" type="number" step="any" value="${x.lng}"></div><div class="field"><label>Geofence Radius (m)</label><input class="input" id="am-radius" type="number" value="${x.radius}"></div><div class="field"><label>Unload Duration (min)</label><input class="input" id="am-unload" type="number" value="${x.unload}"></div><div class="field"><label>Opening Time</label><input class="input" id="am-open" type="time" value="${x.open}"></div><div class="field"><label>Closing Time</label><input class="input" id="am-close" type="time" value="${x.close}"></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveAddressMapping('${id}')">Save Mapping</button>`)}
function saveAddressMapping(oldId){const id=document.getElementById('am-id').value.trim();if(!id||!document.getElementById('am-customer').value.trim()){toast('Customer ID dan Name wajib');return}const x={id,customer:document.getElementById('am-customer').value.trim(),location:document.getElementById('am-location').value.trim(),address:document.getElementById('am-address').value.trim(),contact:document.getElementById('am-contact').value.trim(),lat:document.getElementById('am-lat').value===''?'':Number(document.getElementById('am-lat').value),lng:document.getElementById('am-lng').value===''?'':Number(document.getElementById('am-lng').value),radius:Number(document.getElementById('am-radius').value||100),unload:Number(document.getElementById('am-unload').value||30),open:document.getElementById('am-open').value,close:document.getElementById('am-close').value,status:'Invalid Coordinate'};x.status=x.lat!==''&&x.lng!==''&&x.address?'Valid':'Invalid Coordinate';const i=db.addressMappings.findIndex(v=>v.id===oldId);if(i>=0)db.addressMappings[i]=x;else db.addressMappings.push(x);saveDB();closeModal();renderMapping();toast('Address mapping saved')}
function editProductMapping(id){const x=db.productMappings.find(v=>v.id===id)||{id:'',name:'',uom:'PCS',weight:'',volume:'',tempMin:'-',tempMax:'-',status:'Incomplete'};openModal(id?'Edit Product Mapping':'Add Product Mapping',`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>SKU</label><input class="input" id="pm-id" value="${esc(x.id)}" ${id?'readonly':''}></div><div class="field"><label>Product Name</label><input class="input" id="pm-name" value="${esc(x.name)}"></div><div class="field"><label>UOM</label><input class="input" id="pm-uom" value="${esc(x.uom)}"></div><div class="field"><label>Weight per UOM (kg)</label><input class="input" id="pm-weight" type="number" step="any" value="${x.weight}"></div><div class="field"><label>Volume per UOM (m³)</label><input class="input" id="pm-volume" type="number" step="any" value="${x.volume}"></div><div class="field"><label>Min Temperature</label><input class="input" id="pm-tmin" value="${x.tempMin}"></div><div class="field"><label>Max Temperature</label><input class="input" id="pm-tmax" value="${x.tempMax}"></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveProductMapping('${id}')">Save Mapping</button>`)}
function saveProductMapping(oldId){const id=document.getElementById('pm-id').value.trim(),name=document.getElementById('pm-name').value.trim(),w=document.getElementById('pm-weight').value,v=document.getElementById('pm-volume').value;if(!id||!name){toast('SKU dan Product Name wajib');return}const x={id,name,uom:document.getElementById('pm-uom').value.trim(),weight:w===''?'':Number(w),volume:v===''?'':Number(v),tempMin:document.getElementById('pm-tmin').value,tempMax:document.getElementById('pm-tmax').value,status:w!==''&&v!==''?'Valid':'Incomplete'};const i=db.productMappings.findIndex(z=>z.id===oldId);if(i>=0)db.productMappings[i]=x;else db.productMappings.push(x);saveDB();closeModal();renderMapping();toast('Product mapping saved')}
function editFleetMapping(id){const x=db.fleetMappings.find(v=>v.id===id)||{id:'',category:'Truck',type:'CDD',odometer:0,volume:0,driver:'',backup:'-',gps:'-',tempMin:'-',tempMax:'-',hours:'06:00 - 22:00',status:'Pending'};openModal(id?'Edit Fleet Mapping':'Add Fleet Mapping',`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Plate Number</label><input class="input" id="fm-id" value="${esc(x.id)}" ${id?'readonly':''}></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle Category</label><input class="input" id="fm-category" value="${esc(x.category)}"></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle Type</label><input class="input" id="fm-type" value="${esc(x.type)}"></div><div class="field"><label>Odometer</label><input class="input" id="fm-odo" type="number" value="${x.odometer}"></div><div class="field"><label>Volume Capacity</label><input class="input" id="fm-volume" type="number" value="${x.volume}"></div><div class="field"><label>Main Driver</label><input class="input" id="fm-driver" value="${esc(x.driver)}"></div><div class="field"><label>Backup Driver</label><input class="input" id="fm-backup" value="${esc(x.backup)}"></div><div class="field"><label>GPS Vendor / IMEI</label><input class="input" id="fm-gps" value="${esc(x.gps)}"></div><div class="field full"><label>Operating Hours</label><input class="input" id="fm-hours" value="${esc(x.hours)}"></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveFleetMapping('${id}')">Save & Sync</button>`)}
function saveFleetMapping(oldId){const id=document.getElementById('fm-id').value.trim(),driver=document.getElementById('fm-driver').value.trim();if(!id||!driver){toast('Plate dan Main Driver wajib');return}const x={id,category:document.getElementById('fm-category').value.trim(),type:document.getElementById('fm-type').value.trim(),odometer:Number(document.getElementById('fm-odo').value||0),volume:Number(document.getElementById('fm-volume').value||0),driver,backup:document.getElementById('fm-backup').value.trim(),gps:document.getElementById('fm-gps').value.trim(),tempMin:'-',tempMax:'-',hours:document.getElementById('fm-hours').value.trim(),status:'Synced'};const i=db.fleetMappings.findIndex(z=>z.id===oldId);if(i>=0)db.fleetMappings[i]=x;else db.fleetMappings.push(x);saveDB();closeModal();renderMapping();toast('Fleet synchronized to McEasy')}
function editStatusMapping(i){const x=i>=0?db.statusMappings[i]:{prieds:'',mceasy:'',trigger:'',direction:'Two-way'};openModal(i>=0?'Edit Status Mapping':'Add Status Mapping',`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Prieds Status</label><input class="input" id="sm-prieds" value="${esc(x.prieds)}"></div><div class="field"><label>McEasy Status</label><input class="input" id="sm-mceasy" value="${esc(x.mceasy)}"></div><div class="field full"><label>Trigger</label><textarea class="textarea" id="sm-trigger">${esc(x.trigger)}</textarea></div><div class="field"><label>Direction</label><select class="select" id="sm-direction"><option ${x.direction==='Prieds → McEasy'?'selected':''}>Prieds → McEasy</option><option ${x.direction==='McEasy → Prieds'?'selected':''}>McEasy → Prieds</option><option ${x.direction==='Two-way'?'selected':''}>Two-way</option></select></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveStatusMapping(${i})">Save Mapping</button>`)}
function saveStatusMapping(i){const x={prieds:document.getElementById('sm-prieds').value.trim(),mceasy:document.getElementById('sm-mceasy').value.trim(),trigger:document.getElementById('sm-trigger').value.trim(),direction:document.getElementById('sm-direction').value};if(!x.prieds||!x.mceasy){toast('Both status fields are required');return}if(i>=0)db.statusMappings[i]=x;else db.statusMappings.push(x);saveDB();closeModal();renderMapping();toast('Status mapping saved')}
function validateMapping(type,id){let x;if(type==='address'){x=db.addressMappings.find(v=>v.id===id);x.status=x.address&&x.lat!==''&&x.lng!==''?'Valid':'Invalid Coordinate'}else if(type==='product'){x=db.productMappings.find(v=>v.id===id);x.status=x.weight!==''&&x.volume!==''?'Valid':'Incomplete'}else{x=db.fleetMappings.find(v=>v.id===id);x.status=x.driver&&x.volume>0?'Synced':'Pending'}saveDB();renderMapping();toast(x.status==='Valid'||x.status==='Synced'?'Mapping valid':'Mapping still incomplete')}
function validateAllMappings(){db.addressMappings.forEach(x=>x.status=x.address&&x.lat!==''&&x.lng!==''?'Valid':'Invalid Coordinate');db.productMappings.forEach(x=>x.status=x.weight!==''&&x.volume!==''?'Valid':'Incomplete');db.fleetMappings.forEach(x=>x.status=x.driver&&x.volume>0?'Synced':'Pending');saveDB();renderMapping();toast('All mappings validated')}
function exportMappingCSV(){const rows=[['Type','ID','Name','Status'],...db.addressMappings.map(x=>['Address',x.id,x.customer,x.status]),...db.productMappings.map(x=>['Product',x.id,x.name,x.status]),...db.fleetMappings.map(x=>['Fleet',x.id,x.type,x.status])];downloadCSV(rows,'TMS-McEasy-Data-Mapping.csv')}

function fleetStage(status){const list=['Confirm','Dijadwalkan','Loading','Dijalankan','OTW Tujuan','Unloading','Delivered'],idx=list.indexOf(status);return `<div class="fo-stage" title="${status}">${list.map((s,i)=>`<span class="${i<idx?'done':i===idx?'now':''}"></span>`).join('')}</div>`}
function renderFleetOrders(){const el=document.getElementById('fleetOrderKpis');if(!el)return;const fos=db.fleetOrders,q=(document.getElementById('fleetOrderSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),sf=document.getElementById('fleetOrderStatus')?.value||'',sy=document.getElementById('fleetOrderSync')?.value||'';el.innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Total Fleet Order',v:fos.length,f:'Integrated orders',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Scheduled / Loading',v:fos.filter(x=>['Dijadwalkan','Loading'].includes(x.status)).length,f:'Needs dispatch control',a:'var(--orange)'},{l:'On The Way',v:fos.filter(x=>['Dijalankan','OTW Tujuan'].includes(x.status)).length,f:'Live tracked',a:'var(--purple)'},{l:'Delivered',v:fos.filter(x=>x.status==='Delivered').length,f:'POD received',a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Sync Exception',v:fos.filter(x=>x.sync==='Failed').length,f:'Needs correction',a:'var(--red)'}]);document.getElementById('fleetOrderTbody').innerHTML=fos.filter(x=>(!sf||x.status===sf)&&(!sy||x.sync===sy)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map(x=>`<tr><td><b class="mono">${x.id}</b><div style="margin-top:5px">${fleetStage(x.status)}</div></td><td><span class="mono">${x.planId}</span><div class="muted">${x.docs.join(', ')}</div></td><td>${esc(x.customer)}</td><td>${x.departure}</td><td>${esc(x.vehicle)}<div class="muted">${esc(x.driver)}</div></td><td>${esc(x.origin)}<div class="muted">→ ${esc(x.destination)}</div></td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}<div class="muted">${esc(x.updated)}</div></td><td>${statusBadge(x.sync)}</td><td>${x.eta}<div>${x.tracking?`<a href="#" class="tracking-link" onclick="event.preventDefault();openTracking('${x.id}')">Open Tracking</a>`:'-'}</div></td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" onclick="fleetOrderDetail('${x.id}')">Detail</button>${fleetOrderActionButtons(x)}</div></td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="10" class="empty">No Fleet Order found.</td></tr>'}
function fleetOrderActionButtons(x){if(x.sync==='Failed')return `<button class="icon-btn" onclick="retryFleetOrder('${x.id}')">Retry</button>`;if(x.status==='Confirm')return `<button class="icon-btn" onclick="advanceFleetOrder('${x.id}','Dijadwalkan')">Schedule</button>`;if(x.status==='Dijadwalkan')return `<button class="icon-btn" onclick="advanceFleetOrder('${x.id}','Loading')">Start Loading</button>`;if(x.status==='Loading')return `<button class="icon-btn" onclick="advanceFleetOrder('${x.id}','Dijalankan')">Dispatch</button>`;if(x.status==='Dijalankan')return `<button class="icon-btn" onclick="advanceFleetOrder('${x.id}','OTW Tujuan')">Start Trip</button>`;if(x.status==='OTW Tujuan')return `<button class="icon-btn" onclick="advanceFleetOrder('${x.id}','Unloading')">Arrive</button>`;if(x.status==='Unloading')return `<button class="icon-btn" onclick="advanceFleetOrder('${x.id}','Delivered')">Receive POD</button>`;return ''}
function applyFleetOrderToPlan(x){const p=db.plans.find(v=>v.id===x.planId);if(!p)return;const map={Confirm:'Planned',Dijadwalkan:'Planned',Loading:'Loading',Dijalankan:'In Transit','OTW Tujuan':'In Transit',Unloading:'In Transit',Delivered:'Completed',Failed:'Exception'};p.status=map[x.status]||p.status;p.health=x.status==='Failed'?'Exception':x.status==='Delivered'?'Completed':'On Schedule';p.lastUpdate='McEasy: '+x.status+' • '+x.updated;if(x.status==='Delivered')p.stops.forEach(s=>{s.status='Successfully Delivered';s.pod=true;s.arrival=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)})}
function advanceFleetOrder(id,next){const x=db.fleetOrders.find(v=>v.id===id);x.status=next;x.updated='just now';if(next==='Dijalankan'&&!x.tracking)x.tracking='https://tracking.example/'+id.replaceAll('/','-');if(next==='Delivered')x.lastLocation=x.destination;db.syncLogs.unshift({id:uid('SYNC'),time:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),direction:next==='Dijadwalkan'||next==='Loading'||next==='Dijalankan'?'Prieds → McEasy':'McEasy → Prieds',object:'Fleet Order',ref:id,event:'order.status.updated',status:'Synced',retry:0,message:'Status updated to '+next});applyFleetOrderToPlan(x);saveDB();renderFleetOrders();renderAll();toast('Fleet Order updated to '+next)}
function syncFleetOrders(){db.fleetOrders.filter(x=>x.sync==='Pending').forEach(x=>x.sync='Synced');saveDB();renderFleetOrders();toast('Fleet Order status synchronized')}
function retryFleetOrder(id){const x=db.fleetOrders.find(v=>v.id===id),addr=db.addressMappings.find(a=>x.destination.includes(a.location)||x.customer.includes(a.customer));if(addr&&addr.status!=='Valid'){toast('Retry blocked: destination coordinate invalid');goPage('mapping');activeMapping='address';renderMapping();return}x.sync='Synced';x.updated='retry successful';db.syncLogs.unshift({id:uid('SYNC'),time:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),direction:'Prieds → McEasy',object:'Fleet Order',ref:id,event:'fleet_order.retry',status:'Synced',retry:1,message:'Fleet Order synchronized'});saveDB();renderFleetOrders();toast('Fleet Order sync successful')}
function openFleetOrderForm(planId=''){const candidates=db.plans.filter(p=>!db.fleetOrders.some(f=>f.planId===p.id)||p.id===planId);openModal('Create McEasy Fleet Order',`<div class="notice">Fleet Order dibuat dari shipment yang DO-nya sudah Confirm/DO Packed dan mapping alamat serta product valid.</div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Shipment Plan</label><select class="select" id="fo-plan" onchange="prefillFleetOrder()"><option value="">Select Plan</option>${db.plans.map(p=>`<option value="${p.id}" ${p.id===planId?'selected':''}>${p.id} — ${p.docs.join(', ')}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Repeat Cycle</label><select class="select" id="fo-repeat"><option>None</option><option>Daily</option><option>Weekly</option><option>Monthly</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Departure</label><input class="input" id="fo-departure" type="datetime-local" value="2026-06-28T08:00"></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle</label><select class="select" id="fo-vehicle"><option value="">Select Vehicle</option>${db.fleetMappings.filter(x=>x.status==='Synced').map(x=>`<option>${x.id}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Driver</label><select class="select" id="fo-driver"><option value="">Select Driver</option>${db.drivers.filter(x=>x.status!=='Inactive').map(x=>`<option>${esc(x.name)}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Initial Status</label><select class="select" id="fo-status"><option>Confirm</option><option>Dijadwalkan</option></select></div><div class="field full"><label>Special Instruction / Remark</label><textarea class="textarea" id="fo-remark" placeholder="Temperature, handling, unloading, access restriction..."></textarea></div></div><div id="fo-readiness"></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveFleetOrder()">Create & Sync</button>`);setTimeout(prefillFleetOrder,0)}
function prefillFleetOrder(){const id=document.getElementById('fo-plan')?.value,p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id),box=document.getElementById('fo-readiness');if(!box)return;if(!p){box.innerHTML='';return}const addr=db.addressMappings.find(a=>p.destination.includes(a.location)||p.stops.some(s=>s.customer.includes(a.customer))),addressOK=!addr||addr.status==='Valid',productsOK=db.productMappings.every(x=>x.status==='Valid'),existing=db.fleetOrders.some(x=>x.planId===p.id);box.innerHTML=`<div class="section-title">Readiness Validation</div><div class="grid-3"><div class="notice ${addressOK?'':'danger'}">${addressOK?'✓':'✕'} Address & Coordinate</div><div class="notice ${productsOK?'':'warn'}">${productsOK?'✓':'!'} Product Weight / Volume</div><div class="notice ${existing?'warn':''}">${existing?'! Existing Fleet Order':'✓ No Duplicate'}</div></div>`}
function saveFleetOrder(){const planId=document.getElementById('fo-plan').value,p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===planId);if(!p){toast('Shipment Plan wajib dipilih');return}if(db.fleetOrders.some(x=>x.planId===planId)){toast('Duplicate blocked: plan already has Fleet Order');return}const addr=db.addressMappings.find(a=>p.destination.includes(a.location)||p.stops.some(s=>s.customer.includes(a.customer)));if(addr&&addr.status!=='Valid'){toast('Address coordinate must be valid');return}const id='FO/MC/'+String(db.fleetOrders.length+1).padStart(5,'0'),dep=document.getElementById('fo-departure').value.replace('T',' '),vehicle=document.getElementById('fo-vehicle').value,driver=document.getElementById('fo-driver').value,status=document.getElementById('fo-status').value;if(status==='Dijadwalkan'&&(!vehicle||!driver)){toast('Vehicle dan Driver wajib untuk status Dijadwalkan');return}const fo={id,planId,docs:[...p.docs],customer:p.stops.map(s=>s.customer).join(' / '),departure:dep,origin:p.origin,destination:p.destination,vehicle:vehicle||'-',driver:driver||'-',status,sync:'Synced',eta:p.eta+' 17:00',tracking:'',lastLocation:'-',distancePlan:db.routes.find(r=>p.destination.includes(r.destination))?.distance||0,distanceActual:0,temp:'-',repeat:document.getElementById('fo-repeat').value,updated:'just now'};db.fleetOrders.push(fo);db.syncLogs.unshift({id:uid('SYNC'),time:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),direction:'Prieds → McEasy',object:'Fleet Order',ref:id,event:'fleet_order.create',status:'Synced',retry:0,message:'Fleet Order created from '+planId});saveDB();closeModal();renderFleetOrders();toast(id+' created')}
function fleetOrderDetail(id){const x=db.fleetOrders.find(v=>v.id===id),events=db.syncLogs.filter(e=>e.ref===id);openModal('Fleet Order '+id,`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Plan Number</label><div class="mono">${x.planId}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Sync</label><div>${statusBadge(x.sync)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>McEasy Status</label><div>${statusBadge(x.status)} ${fleetStage(x.status)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Departure</label><div>${x.departure}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle</label><div>${esc(x.vehicle)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Driver</label><div>${esc(x.driver)}</div></div><div class="field full"><label>Route</label><div>${esc(x.origin)} → ${esc(x.destination)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>ETA</label><div>${x.eta}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Last Location</label><div>${esc(x.lastLocation)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Distance</label><div>${x.distanceActual} / ${x.distancePlan} km</div></div><div class="field"><label>Temperature</label><div>${x.temp}</div></div><div class="field full"><label>Tracking URL</label><div>${x.tracking?`<a href="#" class="tracking-link" onclick="event.preventDefault();openTracking('${x.id}')">${esc(x.tracking)}</a>`:'Not available before dispatch'}</div></div></div><div class="section-title">Integration Timeline</div><div class="timeline">${events.map(e=>`<div class="timeline-item"><b>${esc(e.event)} • ${statusBadge(e.status)}</b><p>${esc(e.time)} — ${esc(e.message)}</p></div>`).join('')||'<div class="timeline-item"><b>No event</b></div>'}</div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>${fleetOrderActionButtons(x)}`)}
function openTracking(id){const x=db.fleetOrders.find(v=>v.id===id);openModal('Live Tracking '+id,`<div class="map" style="height:300px"><div class="route-line"></div><div class="pin p1"></div><div class="pin p2"></div><div class="pin p3"></div></div><div class="grid-3" style="margin-top:14px"><div class="notice"><b>Last Location</b><br>${esc(x.lastLocation)}</div><div class="notice"><b>ETA</b><br>${x.eta}</div><div class="notice"><b>Distance</b><br>${x.distanceActual} / ${x.distancePlan} km</div></div><div class="timeline"><div class="timeline-item"><b>${x.status}</b><p>${x.updated}</p></div><div class="timeline-item"><b>GPS Online</b><p>Temperature ${x.temp}</p></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`)}

function renderCostManagement(){const el=document.getElementById('costKpis');if(!el)return;const data=db.costRecords,total=data.reduce((a,x)=>a+x.amount,0),posted=data.filter(x=>['Posted','Paid'].includes(x.status)).reduce((a,x)=>a+x.amount,0),draft=data.filter(x=>['Draft','Approved'].includes(x.status)).reduce((a,x)=>a+x.amount,0),q=(document.getElementById('costSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),f=document.getElementById('costStatusFilter')?.value||'';el.innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Total Transport Cost',v:fmtIDR(total),f:'All recorded expenses',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Posted to Accurate',v:fmtIDR(posted),f:`${data.filter(x=>['Posted','Paid'].includes(x.status)).length} records`,a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Pending Posting',v:fmtIDR(draft),f:'Draft and approved',a:'var(--orange)'},{l:'Paid',v:fmtIDR(data.filter(x=>x.status==='Paid').reduce((a,x)=>a+x.amount,0)),f:'Settled expenses',a:'var(--purple)'},{l:'Posting Exception',v:data.filter(x=>x.status==='Failed').length,f:'Needs account mapping',a:'var(--red)'}]);const cats={};data.forEach(x=>cats[x.category]=(cats[x.category]||0)+x.amount);document.getElementById('costCategoryMetrics').innerHTML=Object.entries(cats).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).map(([k,v])=>`<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">${esc(k)}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${v/Math.max(1,total)*100}%;background:var(--cyan-dark)"></span></div><b style="width:120px">${fmtIDR(v)}</b></div>`).join('');document.getElementById('accurateSyncMetrics').innerHTML=`<div class="notice"><b>Posting Rule</b><br>Fleet Order, transaction date, source account, expense account, branch, plate/department, driver, amount, and proof attachment must be complete.</div><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Ready to Post</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${data.filter(x=>x.status==='Approved').length/Math.max(1,data.length)*100}%;background:var(--green)"></span></div><b>${data.filter(x=>x.status==='Approved').length}</b></div><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Posted / Paid</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${data.filter(x=>['Posted','Paid'].includes(x.status)).length/Math.max(1,data.length)*100}%;background:var(--blue)"></span></div><b>${data.filter(x=>['Posted','Paid'].includes(x.status)).length}</b></div>`;document.getElementById('costTbody').innerHTML=data.filter(x=>(!f||x.status===f)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map(x=>`<tr><td class="mono">${x.id}</td><td class="mono">${x.fleetOrder}</td><td>${x.date}</td><td>${esc(x.plate)}<div class="muted">${esc(x.driver)}</div></td><td>${esc(x.category)}</td><td>${esc(x.account)}</td><td>${esc(x.branch)}</td><td>${fmtIDR(x.amount)}</td><td>${x.proof==='-'?'-':`<button class="icon-btn" onclick="toast('Proof preview opened')">View</button>`}</td><td>${esc(x.accurateNo)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td><div class="actions"><button class="icon-btn" onclick="costDetail('${x.id}')">Detail</button>${x.status==='Draft'?`<button class="icon-btn" onclick="approveCost('${x.id}')">Approve</button>`:''}${x.status==='Approved'?`<button class="icon-btn" onclick="postCost('${x.id}')">Post</button>`:''}</div></td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="12" class="empty">No expense found.</td></tr>'}
function openCostForm(){openModal('Add Transport Expense',`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Fleet Order</label><select class="select" id="c-fo">${db.fleetOrders.map(x=>`<option>${x.id}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Transaction Date</label><input class="input" id="c-date" type="date" value="${todayISO()}"></div><div class="field"><label>Expense Category</label><select class="select" id="c-cat"><option>Fuel</option><option>Toll</option><option>Parking</option><option>Loading Fee</option><option>Waiting Charge</option><option>Maintenance</option><option>Other</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Expense Account</label><input class="input" id="c-account" placeholder="6-20xx Account Name"></div><div class="field"><label>Amount</label><input class="input" id="c-amount" type="number" min="0"></div><div class="field"><label>Branch</label><input class="input" id="c-branch" value="Bandung"></div><div class="field"><label>Proof Attachment</label><input class="input" id="c-proof" type="file"></div><div class="field"><label>Source Account</label><input class="input" id="c-source" placeholder="Cash / Bank account"></div><div class="field full"><label>Notes</label><textarea class="textarea" id="c-note"></textarea></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveCost()">Save Expense</button>`)}
function saveCost(){const fo=db.fleetOrders.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('c-fo').value),amount=Number(document.getElementById('c-amount').value||0),account=document.getElementById('c-account').value.trim();if(!amount||!account){toast('Amount dan Expense Account wajib');return}db.costRecords.push({id:'COST/'+String(db.costRecords.length+1).padStart(5,'0'),fleetOrder:fo.id,date:document.getElementById('c-date').value,plate:fo.vehicle,driver:fo.driver,category:document.getElementById('c-cat').value,account,amount,branch:document.getElementById('c-branch').value.trim(),proof:document.getElementById('c-proof').files[0]?.name||'-',accurateNo:'-',status:'Draft'});saveDB();closeModal();renderCostManagement();toast('Expense saved as Draft')}
function approveCost(id){const x=db.costRecords.find(v=>v.id===id);x.status='Approved';saveDB();renderCostManagement();toast('Expense approved')}
function postCost(id){const x=db.costRecords.find(v=>v.id===id);if(x.proof==='-'){toast('Proof attachment required before posting');return}x.status='Posted';x.accurateNo='BKK.'+new Date().getFullYear()+'.'+String(new Date().getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')+'.'+String(Math.floor(Math.random()*9999)).padStart(4,'0');saveDB();renderCostManagement();toast('Expense posted to Accurate')}
function syncCostsToAccurate(){let n=0;db.costRecords.filter(x=>x.status==='Approved'&&x.proof!=='-').forEach(x=>{x.status='Posted';x.accurateNo='BKK.'+new Date().getFullYear()+'.'+String(new Date().getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')+'.'+String(Math.floor(Math.random()*9999)).padStart(4,'0');n++});saveDB();renderCostManagement();toast(n?n+' expense(s) posted':'No approved expense ready')}
function costDetail(id){const x=db.costRecords.find(v=>v.id===id);openModal('Expense '+id,`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Fleet Order</label><div class="mono">${x.fleetOrder}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Status</label><div>${statusBadge(x.status)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Transaction Date</label><div>${x.date}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Accurate Number</label><div>${esc(x.accurateNo)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle</label><div>${esc(x.plate)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Driver</label><div>${esc(x.driver)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Category</label><div>${esc(x.category)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Account</label><div>${esc(x.account)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Branch</label><div>${esc(x.branch)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Amount</label><div><b>${fmtIDR(x.amount)}</b></div></div><div class="field full"><label>Proof</label><div>${esc(x.proof)}</div></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`)}
function downloadCSV(rows,name){const csv=rows.map(r=>r.map(v=>'"'+String(v??'').replace(/"/g,'""')+'"').join(',')).join('\n');const a=document.createElement('a');a.href=URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv],{type:'text/csv'}));a.download=name;a.click();URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href)}
function downloadCostCSV(){downloadCSV([['Expense No','Fleet Order','Date','Plate','Driver','Category','Account','Branch','Amount','Accurate No','Status'],...db.costRecords.map(x=>[x.id,x.fleetOrder,x.date,x.plate,x.driver,x.category,x.account,x.branch,x.amount,x.accurateNo,x.status])],'TMS-Transport-Cost.csv')}

function kpiCards(arr){return arr.map(x=>`<div class="kpi" style="--accent:${x.a}"><div class="label">${esc(x.l)}</div><div class="value">${esc(x.v)}</div><div class="foot">${esc(x.f)}</div></div>`).join('')}
function renderDashboard(){const active=db.plans.filter(p=>!['Completed','Draft'].includes(p.status)).length,planned=db.plans.filter(p=>p.status==='Planned').length,intransit=db.plans.filter(p=>p.status==='In Transit').length,available=db.vehicles.filter(v=>v.status==='Available').length,completion=db.plans.filter(p=>p.status==='Completed').length;document.getElementById('dashboardKpis').innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Active Shipments',v:active,f:'Planned to returning',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Need Planning',v:db.documents.filter(d=>d.status==='Need Planning').length,f:'DO / STO ready',a:'var(--orange)'},{l:'In Transit',v:intransit,f:'Live monitored',a:'var(--purple)'},{l:'Available Vehicles',v:available,f:`of ${db.vehicles.length} vehicles`,a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Completed Trips',v:completion,f:'Demo history',a:'var(--cyan-dark)'}]);const total=Math.max(1,db.plans.length);document.getElementById('statusMetrics').innerHTML=[['Planned',planned,'var(--blue)'],['Loading',db.plans.filter(p=>p.status==='Loading').length,'var(--orange)'],['In Transit',intransit,'var(--purple)'],['Completed',completion,'var(--green)']].map(x=>`<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">${x[0]}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${x[1]/total*100}%;background:${x[2]}"></span></div><b>${x[1]}</b></div>`).join('');document.getElementById('deliveryBars').innerHTML=[4,6,5,8,7,9,11].map((v,i)=>`<div class="bar" style="height:${v*9}px"><span>${['Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat','Sun'][i]}</span></div>`).join('');document.getElementById('fleetMetrics').innerHTML=['Available','Reserved','Loading','In Transit','Maintenance'].map(s=>{const n=db.vehicles.filter(v=>v.status===s).length;return `<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">${s}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${n/Math.max(1,db.vehicles.length)*100}%;background:${s==='Available'?'var(--green)':s==='Maintenance'?'var(--red)':'var(--cyan-dark)'}"></span></div><b>${n}</b></div>`}).join('');document.getElementById('upcomingList').innerHTML=db.plans.filter(p=>['Planned','Loading'].includes(p.status)).sort((a,b)=>a.shipmentDate.localeCompare(b.shipmentDate)).slice(0,3).map(p=>`<div class="ship-item" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')"><div class="top"><b>${p.id}</b>${statusBadge(p.status)}<span class="age">${p.shipmentDate}</span></div><div class="meta">${esc(p.destination)} • ${esc(p.source==='Fleet Company'?p.vehicle:p.supplier)}</div></div>`).join('')||'<div class="empty">No upcoming shipment.</div>'}
function renderReport(){const comp=db.plans.filter(p=>p.status==='Completed'),stops=comp.flatMap(p=>p.stops),success=stops.filter(s=>s.status==='Successfully Delivered').length,epod=stops.filter(s=>s.pod).length;document.getElementById('reportKpis').innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'On-Time Delivery',v:'92.4%',f:'Closed shipments',a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Delivery Success',v:(stops.length?Math.round(success/stops.length*100):0)+'%',f:`${success}/${stops.length} stops`,a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'First Attempt Rate',v:'88.1%',f:'Without reschedule',a:'var(--cyan-dark)'},{l:'ePOD Completion',v:(stops.length?Math.round(epod/stops.length*100):0)+'%',f:'Photo/signature',a:'var(--purple)'},{l:'Cost Variance',v:'+4.2%',f:'Actual vs planned',a:'var(--orange)'}]);document.getElementById('carrierPerformance').innerHTML=db.carriers.map((c,i)=>`<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">${esc(c.name)}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${[94,89,86][i]||82}%;background:${i===0?'var(--green)':'var(--cyan-dark)'}"></span></div><b>${[94,89,86][i]||82}%</b></div>`).join('');const totalP=db.plans.reduce((a,p)=>a+p.plannedCost,0),totalA=db.plans.reduce((a,p)=>a+(p.actualCost||p.plannedCost),0);document.getElementById('costPerformance').innerHTML=`<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Planned Cost</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:88%"></span></div><b style="width:120px">${fmtIDR(totalP)}</b></div><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Actual / Forecast</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:92%;background:var(--orange)"></span></div><b style="width:120px">${fmtIDR(totalA)}</b></div><div class="notice warn">Variance ${fmtIDR(totalA-totalP)} • Review toll, waiting charge, fuel, and carrier invoice.</div>`;renderReportTable()}
function renderReportTable(){const q=(document.getElementById('reportSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),src=document.getElementById('reportSource')?.value||'';document.getElementById('reportTbody').innerHTML=db.plans.filter(p=>(!src||p.source===src)&&JSON.stringify(p).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map(p=>{const result=p.stops.every(s=>s.status==='Successfully Delivered')?'Delivered':p.stops.some(s=>s.status.includes('Partial')||s.status.includes('Unsuccess')||s.status.includes('Failed'))?'Exception':p.status;const epod=p.stops.every(s=>s.pod);const act=p.actualCost||0,vr=act?p.actualCost-p.plannedCost:0;return `<tr><td class="mono">${p.id}</td><td>${p.source}</td><td>${esc(p.source==='Fleet Company'?p.vehicle+' / '+p.driver:p.supplier)}</td><td>${esc(p.destination)}</td><td>${p.shipmentDate}</td><td>${p.eta}</td><td>${statusBadge(result)}</td><td>${epod?statusBadge('Completed'):statusBadge('Draft')}</td><td>${fmtIDR(p.plannedCost)}</td><td>${act?fmtIDR(act):'-'}</td><td class="${vr>0?'text-red':'text-green'}">${act?fmtIDR(vr):'-'}</td></tr>`}).join('')}
function downloadReport(){const rows=[['Plan Number','Source','Carrier/Vehicle','Destination','Shipment Date','ETA','Status','Planned Cost','Actual Cost'],...db.plans.map(p=>[p.id,p.source,p.source==='Fleet Company'?p.vehicle:p.supplier,p.destination,p.shipmentDate,p.eta,p.status,p.plannedCost,p.actualCost])];const csv=rows.map(r=>r.map(v=>'"'+String(v).replace(/"/g,'""')+'"').join(',')).join('\n');const a=document.createElement('a');a.href=URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv],{type:'text/csv'}));a.download='TMS-Delivery-Performance.csv';a.click();URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href)}
function renderAll(){['hubs','carriers','contracts','vehicles','drivers','routes'].forEach(renderMaster);renderMaintenance();}
setInterval(()=>{const __clock=document.getElementById('clock');if(!__clock)return;__clock.textContent=new Date().toLocaleString('id-ID',{weekday:'short',day:'2-digit',month:'short',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})},1000);
