/* ===== Modular shared data + connected Driver Mobile override ===== */
const MODULE_ID = "master-operational-integrated";
const MODULE_DEFAULT_PAGE = document.body?.dataset.initialPage || "hub";
const MODULE_ROUTES = {"dashboard": "report-overview.html", "hub": "master.html", "carrier": "master.html", "vehicle": "master.html", "maintenance": "master.html", "driver": "master.html", "route": "master.html", "planning": "operational.html", "schedule": "operational.html", "loading": "operational.html", "monitoring": "operational.html", "driver-mobile": "operational.html", "integration": "integration.html", "mapping": "integration.html", "fleet-order": "integration.html", "cost": "integration.html", "report": "report-overview.html", "recommendation": "report-overview.html", "antifraud": "risk-control.html"};
let sharedChannel = null;
try { sharedChannel = new BroadcastChannel('PRIEDS_TMS_SHARED_CHANNEL_V3'); } catch(e) {}

function broadcastSharedUpdate(){
  try { if(sharedChannel) sharedChannel.postMessage({type:'db-updated',module:MODULE_ID,at:Date.now()}); } catch(e) {}
}
function saveDB(){
  try { localStorage.setItem(KEY,JSON.stringify(db)); } catch(e) { console.warn('Local storage unavailable; demo continues in memory.'); }
  broadcastSharedUpdate();
}
function reloadSharedDB(){
  const incoming=loadDB();
  db=incoming;
  ensureDriverStates();
  renderAll();
  if(document.getElementById('phoneBody')) renderDriverMobile();
}
window.addEventListener('storage',e=>{if(e.key===KEY) reloadSharedDB()});
if(sharedChannel) sharedChannel.onmessage=e=>{if(e.data?.type==='db-updated'&&e.data.module!==MODULE_ID) reloadSharedDB()};
window.addEventListener('focus',()=>reloadSharedDB());

function goPage(p){
  const target=document.getElementById('page-'+p);
  if(!target){
    const file=MODULE_ROUTES[p];
    if(file) location.href=file+'#'+p;
    return;
  }
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
  target.classList.add('active');
  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item[data-page]').forEach(x=>x.classList.toggle('active',x.dataset.page===p));
  const crumb=document.getElementById('crumb'); if(crumb) crumb.textContent=PAGE_NAMES[p]||p;
  if(p==='schedule')renderSchedule();
  if(p==='monitoring')renderMonitoring();
  if(p==='loading')renderLoading();
  if(p==='driver-mobile')renderDriverMobile();
  if(p==='report')renderReport();
  if(p==='integration')renderIntegration();
  if(p==='mapping')renderMapping();
  if(p==='fleet-order')renderFleetOrders();
  if(p==='cost')renderCostManagement();
  history.replaceState(null,'','#'+p);
  window.scrollTo(0,0);
}

function integrationEvent(object,ref,event,message,direction='Prieds → McEasy',status='Synced'){
  db.syncLogs=db.syncLogs||[];
  db.syncLogs.unshift({id:uid('SYNC'),time:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),direction,object,ref,event,status,retry:0,message});
}
function fleetOrderForPlan(planId){return (db.fleetOrders||[]).find(x=>x.planId===planId)}
function driverByUsername(username){return (db.drivers||[]).find(x=>x.username===username)}
function assignedPlansForUser(username){
  const d=driverByUsername(username);
  if(!d)return [];
  return db.plans.filter(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company'&&p.driver===d.name&&p.status!=='Draft')
    .sort((a,b)=>(a.status==='Completed')-(b.status==='Completed')||String(a.shipmentDate).localeCompare(String(b.shipmentDate)));
}
function inferDriverStep(p){
  if(!p)return 0;
  if(p.status==='Completed')return 8;
  if(p.status==='Returning')return 7;
  if(p.status==='Unloading')return 6;
  if(p.status==='In Transit')return 4;
  if(p.status==='Ready to Dispatch')return 2;
  if(p.status==='Loading')return 2;
  return 0;
}
function ensureDriverStates(){
  db.driverStates=db.driverStates||{};
  db.mobileDriverUser=db.mobileDriverUser||db.drivers?.find(x=>x.username)?.username||'asepdriver';
  db.plans.filter(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company').forEach(p=>{
    if(!db.driverStates[p.id]) db.driverStates[p.id]={planId:p.id,step:inferDriverStep(p),currentStop:0,accepted:false,preTrip:false,loadConfirmed:false,closed:false};
  });
  if(db.driverState?.planId&&!db.driverStates[db.driverState.planId]){
    db.driverStates[db.driverState.planId]={planId:db.driverState.planId,step:Number(db.driverState.step||0),currentStop:0,accepted:!!db.driverState.accepted,preTrip:!!db.driverState.checklist,loadConfirmed:!!db.driverState.loaded,closed:false};
  }
  const plans=assignedPlansForUser(db.mobileDriverUser);
  if(!db.mobileSelectedPlan||!plans.some(p=>p.id===db.mobileSelectedPlan)) db.mobileSelectedPlan=plans.find(p=>p.status!=='Completed')?.id||plans[0]?.id||'';
}
function selectedDriverState(){const p=driverPlan();if(!p)return null;ensureDriverStates();return db.driverStates[p.id]}
function driverPlan(){
  ensureDriverStates();
  const plans=assignedPlansForUser(db.mobileDriverUser);
  return plans.find(p=>p.id===db.mobileSelectedPlan)||plans.find(p=>p.status!=='Completed')||plans[0]||null;
}
function selectMobileDriver(username){db.mobileDriverUser=username;db.mobileSelectedPlan='';ensureDriverStates();saveDB();renderDriverMobile()}
function selectMobileTrip(planId){db.mobileSelectedPlan=planId;ensureDriverStates();saveDB();renderDriverMobile()}
function linkedEntitySummary(p){
  const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver),v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle);
  return `<div class="linked-state"><div>Plan Status<b>${esc(p.status)}</b></div><div>Fleet Order<b>${fo?esc(fo.status):'Not Created'}</b></div><div>Resource<b>${esc(d?.status||'-')} / ${esc(v?.status||'-')}</b></div></div>`;
}
function renderDriverMobile(){
  const userSel=document.getElementById('mobileDriverUser'),tripSel=document.getElementById('mobileTripSelect');
  if(!document.getElementById('phoneBody'))return;
  ensureDriverStates();
  if(userSel){
    userSel.innerHTML=db.drivers.filter(x=>x.username).map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.username)}" ${x.username===db.mobileDriverUser?'selected':''}>${esc(x.name)} (${esc(x.username)})</option>`).join('');
  }
  const plans=assignedPlansForUser(db.mobileDriverUser);
  if(tripSel){tripSel.innerHTML=plans.map(p=>`<option value="${p.id}" ${p.id===db.mobileSelectedPlan?'selected':''}>${p.id} — ${p.status} — ${esc(p.destination)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No assigned trip</option>';}
  const p=driverPlan();
  const label=document.getElementById('mobileUserLabel');if(label)label.textContent=db.mobileDriverUser||'-';
  const summary=document.getElementById('driverTripSummary');
  if(!p){
    document.getElementById('phoneBody').innerHTML='<div class="empty">No trip assigned to this driver. Assign driver and vehicle from Shipment Planning or Fleet Order.</div>';
    document.getElementById('driverStepper').innerHTML='';
    if(summary)summary.innerHTML='<div class="notice warn">Driver Mobile reads assignment from Shipment Plan and Fleet Order data.</div>';
    return;
  }
  const st=selectedDriverState(),s=Number(st.step||0),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),current=p.stops[Math.min(st.currentStop||0,p.stops.length-1)];
  document.getElementById('driverStepper').innerHTML=driverSteps.map((x,i)=>`<div class="step-line ${i<s?'done':i===s?'active':''}"><div class="step-circle">${i<s?'✓':i+1}</div><div class="step-content"><b>${x}</b><p>${i<s?'Completed':i===s?'Current action':'Waiting previous step'}</p></div></div>`).join('');
  if(summary)summary.innerHTML=`<div class="phone-row"><span>Plan</span><b>${p.id}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Fleet Order</span><b>${fo?.id||'-'}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Vehicle</span><b>${esc(p.vehicle)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Route</span><b>${esc(p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Status</span><span>${statusBadge(p.status)}</span></div>${linkedEntitySummary(p)}`;
  const loaded=(p.loadedDocs||[]).length,allLoaded=loaded===p.docs.length;
  let html=`<div class="phone-sync">Shared live data • last update: ${esc(p.lastUpdate||'-')}</div>`;
  if(s===0){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('accept')">Accept Trip</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverAction('reject')">Reject with Reason</button>`;}
  else if(s===1){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Pre-Trip Vehicle Check</h4>${['Odometer & fuel','Tyre','Brake','Lights','Body condition','STNK / KIR'].map(x=>`<label class="check-row" style="padding:5px 0"><input type="checkbox" class="precheck">${x}</label>`).join('')}</div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('check')">Submit Checklist</button>`;}
  else if(s===2){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Warehouse Loading Status</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Plan Status</span><b>${p.status}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Documents Loaded</span><b>${loaded}/${p.docs.length}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Gate Readiness</span><b>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'Ready':'Waiting Warehouse'}</b></div></div>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction(\'loading\')">Confirm Load Received</button>':'<button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Loading & Dispatch Module</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="reloadSharedDB()">Refresh Status</button>'}`;}
  else if(s===3){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="notice" style="margin:10px 13px">Load confirmed. Gate operator must perform Gate-Out / Dispatch from Loading & Dispatch.</div><button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Gate-Out</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="reloadSharedDB()">Refresh Status</button>`;}
  else if(s===4){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Next Stop ${Math.min((st.currentStop||0)+1,p.stops.length)} / ${p.stops.length}</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Customer</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Document</span><b>${esc(current.doc)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>ETA</span><b>${p.eta} 14:30</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('arrive')">Arrived at Stop</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverException()">Report Exception</button>`;}
  else if(s===5){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Arrival Confirmed</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Stop</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Geofence</span><b>Inside delivery radius</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('unload')">Start Unloading</button>`;}
  else if(s===6){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Delivery Result & ePOD</h4><select class="select" id="mobileResult" style="width:100%"><option>Successfully Delivered</option><option>Partially Delivered</option><option>Failed Delivery</option></select><input class="input" id="receiverName" placeholder="Receiver Name" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><input class="input" id="podReference" placeholder="OTP / Signature reference" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><input class="input" id="podPhoto" type="file" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('pod')">Submit ePOD</button>`;}
  else if(s===7){html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Return to Origin</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(p.origin)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>All Stops</span><b>${p.stops.filter(x=>x.pod).length}/${p.stops.length} ePOD</b></div><input class="input" id="odometerEnd" placeholder="Odometer End" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><input class="input" id="fuelEnd" placeholder="Fuel End %" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('close')">Arrived at Origin & Close Trip</button>`;}
  else {html+=`<div class="phone-card" style="text-align:center;margin-top:60px"><div style="font-size:44px;color:var(--green)">✓</div><h4>Trip Completed</h4><p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted)">${p.id} is closed and resources are available again.</p></div>`;}
  document.getElementById('phoneBody').innerHTML=html;
}
function tripCard(p){const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id);return `<div class="phone-card"><h4>${p.id} ${statusBadge(p.status)}</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Fleet Order</span><b>${fo?.id||'-'}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Vehicle / Driver</span><b>${esc(p.vehicle)} / ${esc(p.driver)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Origin</span><b>${esc(p.origin)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Planned Time</span><b>${p.shipmentDate}</b></div></div>`}
function driverAction(a){
  const p=driverPlan(),st=selectedDriverState();if(!p||!st)return;
  const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),driver=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver),vehicle=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle);
  if(a==='reject'){driverException('Trip Rejected');return;}
  if(a==='check'&&[...document.querySelectorAll('.precheck')].some(x=>!x.checked)){toast('Seluruh checklist wajib diisi');return;}
  if(a==='accept'){
    st.accepted=true;st.step=1;p.lastUpdate='Trip accepted by '+p.driver;if(driver)driver.status='Assigned';if(fo){fo.status='Dijadwalkan';fo.updated='Trip accepted';}
    integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'driver.trip.accepted','Driver accepted '+p.id,'McEasy → Prieds');
  }else if(a==='check'){
    st.preTrip=true;st.step=2;p.lastUpdate='Pre-trip checklist completed';integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'driver.pretrip.completed','Vehicle checklist completed','McEasy → Prieds');
  }else if(a==='loading'){
    if(p.status!=='Ready to Dispatch'||(p.loadedDocs||[]).length!==p.docs.length){toast('Loading belum selesai di modul Loading & Dispatch');return;}
    st.loadConfirmed=true;st.step=3;p.lastUpdate='Load received by driver';integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'driver.load.confirmed','Driver confirmed loaded documents','McEasy → Prieds');
  }else if(a==='arrive'){
    st.step=5;p.lastUpdate='Driver arrived at stop '+((st.currentStop||0)+1);if(fo){fo.lastLocation=p.stops[st.currentStop||0]?.customer||p.destination;fo.updated='Arrived at stop';fo.status='OTW Tujuan';}
    integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'driver.arrived','Driver arrived inside destination geofence','McEasy → Prieds');
  }else if(a==='unload'){
    st.step=6;p.status='Unloading';p.lastUpdate='Unloading started';if(fo){fo.status='Unloading';fo.updated='Unloading started';}if(driver)driver.status='On Trip';if(vehicle)vehicle.status='In Transit';
    integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.unloading.started','Unloading started at current stop','McEasy → Prieds');
  }else if(a==='pod'){
    const result=document.getElementById('mobileResult').value,receiver=document.getElementById('receiverName').value.trim(),ref=document.getElementById('podReference').value.trim(),photo=document.getElementById('podPhoto')?.files?.[0]?.name||'';
    if(!receiver){toast('Receiver Name wajib');return;}
    if(!ref&&!photo){toast('OTP/signature reference atau photo POD wajib');return;}
    const stop=p.stops[st.currentStop||0];stop.status=result;stop.pod=true;stop.receiver=receiver;stop.podRef=ref||photo;stop.arrival=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16);p.lastUpdate='ePOD submitted for '+stop.doc;
    if(result!=='Successfully Delivered')p.health='Exception';
    integrationEvent('POD',stop.doc,'delivery.pod.received',result+' • receiver '+receiver,'McEasy → Prieds');
    if((st.currentStop||0)<p.stops.length-1){st.currentStop=(st.currentStop||0)+1;st.step=4;p.status='In Transit';if(fo){fo.status='OTW Tujuan';fo.updated='Proceeding to next stop';}}
    else {st.step=7;p.status='Returning';if(driver)driver.status='Returning';if(vehicle)vehicle.status='Returning';if(fo){fo.status='Delivered';fo.updated='All stops delivered';fo.lastLocation=p.destination;}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.delivered','All stops processed and POD synchronized','McEasy → Prieds');}
  }else if(a==='close'){
    st.step=8;st.closed=true;p.status='Completed';p.health=p.stops.every(x=>x.status==='Successfully Delivered')?'Completed':'Exception';p.actualCost=p.actualCost||Math.round(p.plannedCost*1.04);p.lastUpdate='Trip closed at origin';if(driver)driver.status='Available';if(vehicle)vehicle.status='Available';if(fo){fo.status='Delivered';fo.updated='Trip closed';fo.lastLocation=p.origin;}
    integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'trip.closed','Trip closed; vehicle and driver released','McEasy → Prieds');
  }
  saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('Driver action synchronized to Operational, Integration, and Report modules');
}
function driverException(defaultType=''){
  const p=driverPlan();if(!p)return;
  openModal('Report Delivery Exception',`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Exception Type</label><select class="select" id="exType"><option ${defaultType==='Trip Rejected'?'selected':''}>Trip Rejected</option><option>Traffic Delay</option><option>Customer Closed</option><option>Rejected by Customer</option><option>Vehicle Breakdown</option><option>Damage</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Photo Evidence</label><input class="input" id="exPhoto" type="file"></div><div class="field full"><label>Notes</label><textarea class="textarea" id="exNote"></textarea></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-danger" onclick="saveDriverException('${p.id}')">Submit Exception</button>`);
}
function saveDriverException(id){
  const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(id),type=document.getElementById('exType')?.value||'Exception',note=document.getElementById('exNote')?.value||'',photo=document.getElementById('exPhoto')?.files?.[0]?.name||'-';
  p.health='Exception';p.lastUpdate=type+' just now';p.exceptions=p.exceptions||[];p.exceptions.unshift({time:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),type,note,photo});if(fo){fo.sync='Synced';fo.updated=type;}
  integrationEvent('Shipment',id,'delivery.exception.created',type+(note?' • '+note:''),'McEasy → Prieds');closeModal();saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('Exception synchronized to Monitoring and Integration Center');
}

function startLoading(){
  const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!p)return;p.status='Loading';p.lastUpdate='Loading started now';const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle);if(v)v.status='Loading';if(fo){fo.status='Loading';fo.updated='Loading started';}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.loading.started','Warehouse started loading','Prieds → McEasy');saveDB();renderAll();toast('Loading started and synchronized to Driver Mobile');
}
function scanLoadingDoc(){
  const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!p||p.status!=='Loading'){toast('Start Loading terlebih dahulu');return}const val=document.getElementById('scanDocInput').value.trim();if(!p.docs.includes(val)){toast('Wrong shipment: document tidak terdaftar pada plan ini');return}p.loadedDocs=p.loadedDocs||[];if(p.loadedDocs.includes(val)){toast('Duplicate scan ditolak');return}p.loadedDocs.push(val);p.lastUpdate=val+' verified';integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'loading.document.verified',val+' validated for loading','Prieds → McEasy');saveDB();renderAll();toast(val+' verified and visible in Driver Mobile');
}
function completeLoading(){
  const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!p)return;if((p.loadedDocs||[]).length!==p.docs.length){toast('Seluruh document harus fully loaded');return}p.status='Ready to Dispatch';p.lastUpdate='Loading completed now';const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id);if(fo){fo.status='Loading';fo.updated='Ready to dispatch';}const st=(db.driverStates||{})[p.id];if(st&&st.step<2)st.step=2;integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'loading.completed','All shipment documents fully loaded','Prieds → McEasy');saveDB();renderAll();toast('Loading completed; Driver Mobile can confirm load');
}
function dispatchPlan(){
  const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!p)return;if(p.status!=='Ready to Dispatch'){toast('Complete loading before dispatch');return}const st=(db.driverStates||{})[p.id];if(st&&!st.loadConfirmed){toast('Driver belum melakukan Confirm Load Received');return}p.status='In Transit';p.health='On Schedule';p.lastUpdate='Gate-out recorded just now';const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver);if(v)v.status='In Transit';if(d)d.status='On Trip';if(st)st.step=4;if(fo){fo.status='Dijalankan';fo.updated='Gate-out / dispatched';fo.tracking=fo.tracking||'https://tracking.example/'+fo.id.replaceAll('/','-');fo.lastLocation=p.origin;}
  integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.dispatched','Gate-out confirmed; trip started','Prieds → McEasy');saveDB();renderAll();goPage('monitoring');toast('Dispatch synchronized to Driver Mobile, Monitoring, and McEasy Fleet Order');
}
function applyFleetOrderToPlan(x){
  const p=db.plans.find(v=>v.id===x.planId);if(!p)return;if(x.vehicle&&x.vehicle!=='-')p.vehicle=x.vehicle;if(x.driver&&x.driver!=='-')p.driver=x.driver;
  const map={Confirm:'Planned',Dijadwalkan:'Planned',Loading:'Loading',Dijalankan:'In Transit','OTW Tujuan':'In Transit',Unloading:'Unloading',Delivered:p.status==='Returning'?'Returning':'Completed',Failed:'Exception'};p.status=map[x.status]||p.status;p.health=x.status==='Failed'?'Exception':x.status==='Delivered'?'Completed':'On Schedule';p.lastUpdate='McEasy: '+x.status+' • '+x.updated;ensureDriverStates();const st=db.driverStates[p.id];if(st){if(['Dijalankan','OTW Tujuan'].includes(x.status))st.step=Math.max(st.step,4);if(x.status==='Unloading')st.step=Math.max(st.step,6);if(x.status==='Delivered'&&p.status!=='Completed')st.step=Math.max(st.step,7);if(x.status==='Delivered'&&p.status==='Completed')st.step=8;}
  if(x.status==='Delivered'&&p.status==='Completed')p.stops.forEach(s=>{s.status='Successfully Delivered';s.pod=true;s.arrival=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)});
}
function saveFleetOrder(){
  const planId=document.getElementById('fo-plan').value,p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===planId);if(!p){toast('Shipment Plan wajib dipilih');return}if(db.fleetOrders.some(x=>x.planId===planId)){toast('Duplicate blocked: plan already has Fleet Order');return}const addr=db.addressMappings.find(a=>p.destination.includes(a.location)||p.stops.some(s=>s.customer.includes(a.customer)));if(addr&&addr.status!=='Valid'){toast('Address coordinate must be valid');return}const id='FO/MC/'+String(db.fleetOrders.length+1).padStart(5,'0'),dep=document.getElementById('fo-departure').value.replace('T',' '),vehicle=document.getElementById('fo-vehicle').value,driver=document.getElementById('fo-driver').value,status=document.getElementById('fo-status').value;if(status==='Dijadwalkan'&&(!vehicle||!driver)){toast('Vehicle dan Driver wajib untuk status Dijadwalkan');return}const fo={id,planId,docs:[...p.docs],customer:p.stops.map(s=>s.customer).join(' / '),departure:dep,origin:p.origin,destination:p.destination,vehicle:vehicle||p.vehicle||'-',driver:driver||p.driver||'-',status,sync:'Synced',eta:p.eta+' 17:00',tracking:'',lastLocation:'-',distancePlan:db.routes.find(r=>p.destination.includes(r.destination))?.distance||0,distanceActual:0,temp:'-',repeat:document.getElementById('fo-repeat').value,updated:'just now'};db.fleetOrders.push(fo);if(fo.vehicle!=='-')p.vehicle=fo.vehicle;if(fo.driver!=='-')p.driver=fo.driver;const d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver),v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle);if(d)d.status='Assigned';if(v)v.status='Reserved';ensureDriverStates();integrationEvent('Fleet Order',id,'fleet_order.create','Fleet Order created from '+planId,'Prieds → McEasy');saveDB();closeModal();renderAll();toast(id+' created and assigned trip is available in Driver Mobile');
}
function advanceFleetOrder(id,next){
  const x=db.fleetOrders.find(v=>v.id===id);if(!x)return;x.status=next;x.updated='just now';if(next==='Dijalankan'&&!x.tracking)x.tracking='https://tracking.example/'+id.replaceAll('/','-');if(next==='Delivered')x.lastLocation=x.destination;integrationEvent('Fleet Order',id,'order.status.updated','Status updated to '+next,next==='Dijadwalkan'||next==='Loading'||next==='Dijalankan'?'Prieds → McEasy':'McEasy → Prieds');applyFleetOrderToPlan(x);saveDB();renderAll();toast('Fleet Order, shipment, and Driver Mobile synchronized to '+next);
}

function renderAll(){
  ensureDriverStates();
  if(document.getElementById('dashboardKpis'))renderDashboard();
  if(document.getElementById('hubTbody'))renderMaster('hubs');
  if(document.getElementById('carrierTbody'))renderMaster('carriers');
  if(document.getElementById('contractTbody'))renderMaster('contracts');
  if(document.getElementById('vehicleTbody'))renderMaster('vehicles');
  if(document.getElementById('maintenanceTbody'))renderMaintenance();
  if(document.getElementById('driverTbody'))renderMaster('drivers');
  if(document.getElementById('routeTbody'))renderMaster('routes');
  if(document.getElementById('documentTbody'))renderDocuments();
  if(document.getElementById('planTbody'))renderPlans();
  if(document.getElementById('scheduleBoard'))renderSchedule();
  if(document.getElementById('loadingPlanSelect'))renderLoading();
  if(document.getElementById('monitorKpis'))renderMonitoring();
  if(document.getElementById('integrationKpis'))renderIntegration();
  if(document.getElementById('mappingTableWrap'))renderMapping();
  if(document.getElementById('fleetOrderKpis'))renderFleetOrders();
  if(document.getElementById('costKpis'))renderCostManagement();
  if(document.getElementById('reportKpis'))renderReport();
  if(document.getElementById('phoneBody'))renderDriverMobile();
}
