function ensureOperationalEnhancements(){
  db.documents=db.documents||[];
  const rename={'Customer A':'PT Sinar Pangan Nusantara','Customer B':'PT Mitra Retail Indonesia','Customer C':'PT Cipta Elektronik Abadi','Customer Z':'PT Nusantara Distribution Center'};
  db.documents.forEach(d=>{if(rename[d.customer])d.customer=rename[d.customer];d.source=d.source||'System Document';});
  db.plans.forEach(p=>{p.stops=(p.stops||[]).map(st=>{if(rename[st.customer])st.customer=rename[st.customer];return st;});});
  DOCUMENT_IMPORT_SAMPLE.forEach(row=>{if(!db.documents.some(d=>d.id===row.id))db.documents.push(deep(row));});
  const completed=db.plans.find(p=>p.status==='Completed'&&p.stops?.length);
  if(completed){completed.stops.forEach((st,i)=>{if(st.pod){st.receiver=st.receiver||'Rina Warehouse';st.podRef=st.podRef||'SIGN-'+completed.id.replace(/\D/g,'')+'-'+(i+1);st.podPhotoName=st.podPhotoName||'POD-'+completed.id.replaceAll('/','-')+'-'+(i+1)+'.jpg';}});}
  db.driverStates=db.driverStates||{};
  try{localStorage.setItem(KEY,JSON.stringify(db))}catch(e){}
}
function populateReadyHubFilter(){
  const el=document.getElementById('readyHubFilter');if(!el)return;
  const current=el.value;
  el.innerHTML='<option value="">All Hub</option>'+db.hubs.filter(h=>h.status==='Active').map(h=>`<option value="${esc(h.name)}">${esc(h.name)}</option>`).join('');
  if([...el.options].some(o=>o.value===current))el.value=current;
}
function updateReadyFleetOptions(){
  const src=document.getElementById('readyShippingOption')?.value||'Fleet Company',el=document.getElementById('readyFleetSelect');if(!el)return;
  const old=el.value;
  if(src==='Fleet Company')el.innerHTML=db.vehicles.filter(v=>!['Maintenance','Inactive'].includes(v.status)).map(v=>`<option value="${esc(v.id)}">${esc(v.plate)} — ${esc(v.type)} — ${esc(v.status)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No fleet available</option>';
  else el.innerHTML=activeExpeditionCarriers().map(c=>`<option value="${esc(c.name)}">${esc(c.name)} — ${esc(c.sla)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No expedition carrier available</option>';
  if([...el.options].some(o=>o.value===old))el.value=old;
}
function filteredReadyDocuments(){
  const q=(document.getElementById('docSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),t=document.getElementById('docTypeFilter')?.value||'',hub=document.getElementById('readyHubFilter')?.value||'';
  return db.documents.filter(x=>x.status==='Need Planning').filter(x=>(!t||x.type===t)&&(!hub||x.origin===hub||x.destination===hub)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q));
}
function renderDocuments(){
  populateReadyHubFilter();updateReadyFleetOptions();
  const rows=filteredReadyDocuments(),tbody=document.getElementById('documentTbody');if(!tbody)return;
  tbody.innerHTML=rows.map(x=>`<tr><td><input type="checkbox" ${selectedDocs.has(x.id)?'checked':''} onchange="selectDoc('${esc(x.id)}',this.checked)"></td><td>${esc(x.alert)}</td><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}<br><span class="muted">${x.type==='DO'?'Delivery Order':'Stock Transfer Out'} • ${esc(x.source||'System')}</span></td><td>${esc(x.customer)}</td><td>${esc(x.origin)}</td><td>${esc(x.destination)}</td><td>${Number(x.weight).toLocaleString()} kg</td><td>${x.volume} m³</td><td>${statusBadge(x.priority)}</td><td>${statusBadge(x.status)}</td><td><button class="action-dot" aria-label="Open actions" onclick="openActionMenu(event,'document','${esc(x.id)}')">⋮</button></td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">No documents need planning.</td></tr>';
  updateSelectedInfo();
}
function toggleAllDocs(v){selectedDocs.clear();if(v)filteredReadyDocuments().forEach(x=>selectedDocs.add(x.id));renderDocuments();}
function openDocumentImport(){
  const rows=DOCUMENT_IMPORT_SAMPLE.map(x=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${x.type}</td><td>${esc(x.customer)}</td><td>${esc(x.origin)}</td><td>${esc(x.destination)}</td><td>${x.weight}</td><td>${x.volume}</td><td>${x.priority}</td></tr>`).join('');
  openModal('Import Ready Documents from Excel',`<div class="notice">Template Excel sudah berisi contoh data customer, DO, dan STO. Upload kembali file <b>.xls</b> hasil template atau file <b>.csv</b> dengan kolom yang sama.</div><div class="field"><label>Choose Excel / CSV File</label><input class="input" id="documentImportFile" type="file" accept=".xls,.csv,text/csv,application/vnd.ms-excel"><small>Jika file tidak dipilih, tombol Import akan memasukkan seluruh sample data di bawah.</small></div><div class="section-title">Filled Sample Data</div><div class="import-preview"><table class="tbl"><thead><tr><th>Document Number</th><th>Type</th><th>Customer</th><th>Origin</th><th>Destination</th><th>Weight</th><th>Volume</th><th>Priority</th></tr></thead><tbody>${rows}</tbody></table></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="downloadFilledDocumentTemplate()">Download Filled Excel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="importReadyDocuments()">Import Data</button>`);
}
function documentTemplateRows(){return DOCUMENT_IMPORT_SAMPLE.map(x=>[x.id,x.type,x.customer,x.origin,x.destination,x.weight,x.volume,x.priority,x.alert,x.items]);}
function downloadFilledDocumentTemplate(){
  const headers=['Document Number','Type','Customer','Origin','Destination','Weight','Volume','Priority','Alert Time','Item Lines'];
  const table=`<table><thead><tr>${headers.map(h=>`<th>${h}</th>`).join('')}</tr></thead><tbody>${documentTemplateRows().map(r=>`<tr>${r.map(v=>`<td>${esc(v)}</td>`).join('')}</tr>`).join('')}</tbody></table>`;
  const html=`<html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"></head><body>${table}</body></html>`,blob=new Blob([html],{type:'application/vnd.ms-excel'}),a=document.createElement('a');a.href=URL.createObjectURL(blob);a.download='TMS_Ready_Documents_Filled_Template.xls';a.click();URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href);
}
function normalizeImportedRows(matrix){
  if(!matrix.length)return[];const head=matrix[0].map(x=>String(x).trim().toLowerCase());
  const find=(...keys)=>head.findIndex(h=>keys.some(k=>h===k||h.includes(k)));
  const idx={id:find('document number','document','doc number'),type:find('type'),customer:find('customer'),origin:find('origin'),destination:find('destination'),weight:find('weight'),volume:find('volume'),priority:find('priority'),alert:find('alert'),items:find('item lines','items')};
  return matrix.slice(1).filter(r=>r.some(v=>String(v).trim())).map(r=>({id:String(r[idx.id]||'').trim(),type:String(r[idx.type]||'DO').trim().toUpperCase(),customer:String(r[idx.customer]||'').trim(),origin:String(r[idx.origin]||'').trim(),destination:String(r[idx.destination]||'').trim(),weight:Number(r[idx.weight]||0),volume:Number(r[idx.volume]||0),priority:String(r[idx.priority]||'Normal').trim(),alert:String(r[idx.alert]||new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)).trim(),status:'Need Planning',items:Number(r[idx.items]||1),source:'Excel Import'})).filter(x=>x.id&&x.customer&&x.origin&&x.destination);
}
function parseCsv(text){
  const rows=[];let row=[],cell='',quote=false;
  for(let i=0;i<text.length;i++){const c=text[i],n=text[i+1];if(c==='"'&&quote&&n==='"'){cell+='"';i++;}else if(c==='"')quote=!quote;else if(c===','&&!quote){row.push(cell);cell='';}else if((c==='\n'||c==='\r')&&!quote){if(c==='\r'&&n==='\n')i++;row.push(cell);if(row.some(v=>v.trim()))rows.push(row);row=[];cell='';}else cell+=c;}
  row.push(cell);if(row.some(v=>v.trim()))rows.push(row);return rows;
}
function parseExcelHtml(text){const doc=new DOMParser().parseFromString(text,'text/html');return [...doc.querySelectorAll('tr')].map(tr=>[...tr.querySelectorAll('th,td')].map(td=>td.textContent.trim()));}
function applyImportedDocuments(rows){let added=0,updated=0;rows.forEach(x=>{const i=db.documents.findIndex(d=>d.id===x.id);if(i>=0){db.documents[i]=Object.assign({},db.documents[i],x);updated++;}else{db.documents.push(x);added++;}});saveDB();closeModal();renderDocuments();toast(`${added} document imported, ${updated} document updated`);}
function importReadyDocuments(){
  const file=document.getElementById('documentImportFile')?.files?.[0];if(!file){applyImportedDocuments(DEMO_IMPORT_CLONE());return;}
  const reader=new FileReader();reader.onload=()=>{try{const text=String(reader.result||''),matrix=text.toLowerCase().includes('<table')?parseExcelHtml(text):parseCsv(text),rows=normalizeImportedRows(matrix);if(!rows.length){toast('Tidak ada baris valid pada file import');return;}applyImportedDocuments(rows);}catch(e){console.error(e);toast('File import tidak dapat dibaca');}};reader.readAsText(file);
}
function DEMO_IMPORT_CLONE(){return DOCUMENT_IMPORT_SAMPLE.map(x=>deep(x));}

function detectedHubOptions(docs){
  const names=db.hubs.filter(h=>h.status==='Active').map(h=>h.name),detected=[];
  docs.forEach(d=>{if(names.includes(d.origin))detected.push(d.origin);if(names.includes(d.destination))detected.push(d.destination);});
  return [...new Set([...detected,...names])];
}
function openShipmentWizard(prefillDocs=null){
  const ids=prefillDocs||[...selectedDocs],docs=db.documents.filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id));if(!docs.length){toast('Pilih minimal satu DO/STO terlebih dahulu');return;}
  const hubs=detectedHubOptions(docs),commonOrigin=docs.every(d=>d.origin===docs[0].origin)?docs[0].origin:'',toolbarHub=document.getElementById('readyHubFilter')?.value||'',defaultHub=commonOrigin||toolbarHub||hubs[0]||'';
  const defaultSource=document.getElementById('readyShippingOption')?.value||'Fleet Company',defaultFleet=document.getElementById('readyFleetSelect')?.value||'';
  const docRows=docs.map(d=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(d.id)}</td><td>${d.type}</td><td>${esc(d.customer)}</td><td>${esc(d.origin)}</td><td>${esc(d.destination)}</td></tr>`).join('');
  const body=`<div class="notice">Selected ${docs.length} document(s). DO dan STO dengan origin berbeda dapat dikonsolidasikan melalui pilihan Dispatch Hub.</div><div class="doc-selection-table"><table class="tbl"><thead><tr><th>Document</th><th>Type</th><th>Customer / Recipient</th><th>Original Hub</th><th>Destination</th></tr></thead><tbody>${docRows}</tbody></table></div><div class="form-grid" style="margin-top:14px"><div class="field"><label>Total Load</label><div><b>${docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0).toLocaleString()} kg</b> / <b>${docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0).toFixed(1)} m³</b></div></div><div class="field"><label>Dispatch / Consolidation Hub</label><select class="select" id="sw-hub" onchange="wizardDynamic()">${hubs.map(h=>`<option ${h===defaultHub?'selected':''}>${esc(h)}</option>`).join('')}</select><small>Select HUB untuk kombinasi DO dan STO.</small></div><div class="field"><label>Shipping Option</label><select class="select" id="sw-source" onchange="wizardDynamic()"><option ${defaultSource==='Fleet Company'?'selected':''}>Fleet Company</option><option ${defaultSource==='Expedition'?'selected':''}>Expedition</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Stop Category</label><select class="select" id="sw-stop" onchange="wizardDynamic()"><option>End Customer</option><option>Hub</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Shipment Date</label><input class="input" type="date" id="sw-date" value="${todayISO()}" onchange="syncContract()"></div><div class="field"><label>Estimate Date to Arrival</label><input class="input" type="date" id="sw-eta" value="${addDays(todayISO(),1)}"></div><div id="sw-dynamic" class="field full"></div><div class="field full"><label>Remark</label><textarea class="textarea" id="sw-remark" placeholder="Transport notes, special handling, temperature, seal, etc."></textarea></div></div><input type="hidden" id="sw-docs" value="${ids.join('|')}"><input type="hidden" id="sw-readyFleet" value="${esc(defaultFleet)}">`;
  openModal('Create Shipment Plan',body,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="createShipmentPlan()">Create Plan</button>`);wizardDynamic();
}
function wizardDynamic(){
  const src=document.getElementById('sw-source')?.value||'Fleet Company',stop=document.getElementById('sw-stop')?.value||'End Customer',hub=document.getElementById('sw-hub')?.value||'',box=document.getElementById('sw-dynamic'),preferred=document.getElementById('sw-readyFleet')?.value||'';if(!box)return;
  if(src==='Fleet Company'){
    const vehicles=db.vehicles.filter(x=>!['Maintenance','Inactive'].includes(x.status)),drivers=db.drivers.filter(x=>!['Leave','Inactive'].includes(x.status)),routes=db.routes.filter(x=>x.status==='Active'&&(!hub||x.origin===hub));
    box.innerHTML=`<div class="section-title">Internal Fleet Assignment</div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Fleet / Vehicle</label><select class="select" id="sw-vehicle" onchange="calculateWizardUtil()">${vehicles.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.id)}" ${x.id===preferred?'selected':''}>${esc(x.plate)} — ${esc(x.type)} (${x.weight}kg / ${x.volume}m³)</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Driver</label><select class="select" id="sw-driver">${drivers.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.id)}">${esc(x.name)} — ${esc(x.status)}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Route / Lane</label><select class="select" id="sw-route">${routes.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.id)}">${esc(x.origin)} → ${esc(x.destination)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">Auto route from selected Hub</option>'}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Planned Cost</label><input class="input" type="number" id="sw-cost" value="450000"></div><div class="field full"><div id="sw-util"></div></div></div>`;calculateWizardUtil();
  }else{
    const carriers=activeExpeditionCarriers();
    box.innerHTML=`<div class="section-title">Expedition / Contracted Carrier</div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Fleet / Carrier</label><select class="select" id="sw-supplier" onchange="syncContract()">${carriers.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.name)}" ${x.name===preferred?'selected':''}>${esc(x.name)} — ${esc(x.location||'-')} — ${esc(x.sla||((x.slaHours||'-')+' Hours'))}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No expedition carrier available</option>'}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Active Contract</label><select class="select" id="sw-contract"></select></div><div class="field"><label>Fee Delivery</label><input class="input" type="number" id="sw-cost" value="500000"></div><div class="field"><label>POD Rule</label><select class="select" id="sw-pod"><option>Photo + Signature</option><option>Photo + OTP</option><option>Signature Only</option></select></div><div class="field full"><div class="notice warn">Carrier mengambil shipment dari <b>${esc(hub)}</b>. ${stop==='End Customer'?'ETA dapat diatur berdasarkan SLA setiap delivery.':'Destination menggunakan Hub tujuan.'}</div></div></div>`;syncContract();
  }
}
function createShipmentPlan(){
  const ids=document.getElementById('sw-docs').value.split('|'),docs=db.documents.filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id)),src=document.getElementById('sw-source').value,hub=document.getElementById('sw-hub').value;if(!hub){toast('Dispatch Hub wajib dipilih');return;}
  let vehicle='-',driver='-',supplier='-',contract='-',route=hub+' → '+[...new Set(docs.map(x=>x.destination))].join(' / '),wu=0,vu=0,u=0;
  if(src==='Fleet Company'){
    const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-vehicle')?.value),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-driver')?.value),r=db.routes.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-route')?.value);if(!v||!d){toast('Fleet dan Driver wajib dipilih');return;}
    const w=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),vol=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0);wu=Math.round(w/v.weight*100);vu=Math.round(vol/v.volume*100);u=Math.max(wu,vu);if(u>100){toast('Shipment melebihi kapasitas kendaraan');return;}vehicle=v.plate;driver=d.name;supplier=v.carrier;if(r)route=r.origin+' → '+r.destination;
  }else{supplier=document.getElementById('sw-supplier')?.value||'';contract=document.getElementById('sw-contract')?.value||'';if(!supplier||!contract){toast('Carrier wajib memiliki kontrak aktif');return;}}
  const num='PL/'+String(Math.max(0,...db.plans.map(x=>Number(x.id.replace(/\D/g,''))))+1).padStart(5,'0');
  const p={id:num,docs:ids,docType:[...new Set(docs.map(x=>x.type))].map(x=>x==='DO'?'Delivery Order':'Stock Transfer Out').join(' + '),source:src,supplier,contract,vehicle,driver,shipmentDate:document.getElementById('sw-date').value,eta:document.getElementById('sw-eta').value,origin:hub,dispatchHub:hub,destination:[...new Set(docs.map(x=>x.destination))].join(' / '),route,weight:docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),volume:Number(docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0).toFixed(1)),weightUtil:wu,volumeUtil:vu,util:u,status:'Planned',health:'On Schedule',plannedCost:Number(document.getElementById('sw-cost').value||0),actualCost:0,remark:document.getElementById('sw-remark').value.trim(),lastUpdate:'just now',stops:docs.map(x=>({doc:x.id,customer:x.customer,hub,status:'On Going',arrival:'-',pod:false})),loadedDocs:[]};
  db.plans.push(p);docs.forEach(x=>x.status='Done Planning');if(src==='Fleet Company'){const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===vehicle),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===driver);if(v)v.status='Reserved';if(d)d.status='Assigned';}ensureDriverStates();saveDB();selectedDocs.clear();closeModal();renderAll();planningTab(document.querySelector('#page-planning .tab:nth-child(2)'),'planPanel');toast('Plan Number berhasil dibuat: '+num);
}

function closeActionMenu(){document.querySelectorAll('.action-popover').forEach(x=>x.remove());}
function actionList(kind,id){
  if(kind==='document')return[{label:'View Detail',run:()=>documentDetail(id)},{label:selectedDocs.has(id)?'Remove from Selection':'Add to Selection',run:()=>{selectDoc(id,!selectedDocs.has(id));renderDocuments();}}];
  if(kind==='plan'){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id),list=[{label:'View Detail',run:()=>planDetail(id)},{label:'Edit Plan',run:()=>editPlan(id)},{label:'Open Schedule',run:()=>goSchedulePlan(id)}];if(p?.status==='Planned')list.push({label:'Start Loading',run:()=>setLoadingPlan(id)});list.push({label:'Delete Plan',danger:true,run:()=>deletePlan(id)});return list;}
  if(kind==='monitor'){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(id),list=[{label:'View Shipment Detail',run:()=>planDetail(id)}];if(fo)list.push({label:'Open Fleet Order',run:()=>fleetOrderDetail(fo.id)});if(p?.source==='Expedition')list.push({label:'Process Delivery',run:()=>processExpedition(id)});return list;}
  return[];
}
function openActionMenu(e,kind,id){
  e.preventDefault();e.stopPropagation();closeActionMenu();const actions=actionList(kind,id),menu=document.createElement('div');menu.className='action-popover';actions.forEach(a=>{const b=document.createElement('button');b.textContent=a.label;if(a.danger)b.classList.add('danger');b.onclick=ev=>{ev.stopPropagation();closeActionMenu();a.run();};menu.appendChild(b);});document.body.appendChild(menu);const r=e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect(),w=menu.offsetWidth,h=menu.offsetHeight;menu.style.left=Math.max(8,Math.min(window.innerWidth-w-8,r.right-w))+'px';menu.style.top=Math.max(8,Math.min(window.innerHeight-h-8,r.bottom+4))+'px';
}
document.addEventListener('click',closeActionMenu);window.addEventListener('resize',closeActionMenu);window.addEventListener('scroll',closeActionMenu,true);
function renderPlans(){
  const q=(document.getElementById('planSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),st=document.getElementById('planStatusFilter')?.value||'',el=document.getElementById('planTbody');if(!el)return;
  el.innerHTML=db.plans.filter(x=>(!st||x.status===st)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map(p=>`<tr><td class="mono">${p.id}</td><td>${esc(p.docType)}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.source)}</td><td>${p.shipmentDate}</td><td>${p.eta}</td><td>${esc(p.route)}<br><span class="muted">Hub: ${esc(p.dispatchHub||p.origin)} • ${esc(p.destination)}</span></td><td>${p.source==='Fleet Company'?esc(p.vehicle)+' / '+esc(p.driver):esc(p.supplier)}</td><td>${p.source==='Fleet Company'?`W ${p.weightUtil}% / V ${p.volumeUtil}%<br>${statusBadge(p.util>100?'Over Capacity':p.util>90?'High Utilization':'Valid')}`:'Contract rate'}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.status)}</td><td><button class="action-dot" aria-label="Open actions" onclick="openActionMenu(event,'plan','${esc(p.id)}')">⋮</button></td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="10" class="empty">No plan found.</td></tr>';
}
function editPlan(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!p)return;if(['In Transit','Completed','Returning'].includes(p.status)){toast('Plan aktif atau selesai tidak dapat diedit');return;}openModal('Edit '+id,`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Plan Number</label><input class="input" value="${esc(p.id)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Dispatch Hub</label><select class="select" id="ep-hub">${db.hubs.filter(h=>h.status==='Active').map(h=>`<option ${h.name===(p.dispatchHub||p.origin)?'selected':''}>${esc(h.name)}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Shipment Date</label><input class="input" id="ep-date" type="date" value="${p.shipmentDate}"></div><div class="field"><label>ETA</label><input class="input" id="ep-eta" type="date" value="${p.eta}"></div><div class="field"><label>Planned Cost</label><input class="input" id="ep-cost" type="number" value="${p.plannedCost}"></div><div class="field full"><label>Remark</label><textarea class="textarea" id="ep-remark">${esc(p.remark||'')}</textarea></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="savePlanEdit('${esc(id)}')">Save Changes</button>`);}
function savePlanEdit(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);p.dispatchHub=document.getElementById('ep-hub').value;p.origin=p.dispatchHub;p.shipmentDate=document.getElementById('ep-date').value;p.eta=document.getElementById('ep-eta').value;p.plannedCost=Number(document.getElementById('ep-cost').value||0);p.remark=document.getElementById('ep-remark').value.trim();p.lastUpdate='Plan edited just now';saveDB();closeModal();renderAll();toast(id+' updated');}
function renderMonitoringTable(){
  const q=(document.getElementById('monitorSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),src=document.getElementById('monitorSource')?.value||'',el=document.getElementById('monitorTbody');if(!el)return;
  el.innerHTML=monitorPlans().filter(p=>(!src||p.source===src)&&JSON.stringify(p).toLowerCase().includes(q)).map(p=>{const d=p.stops.filter(s=>s.status==='Successfully Delivered').length,u=p.stops.length-d,fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id);return `<tr><td class="mono">${p.id}</td><td class="mono">${fo?fo.id:'-'}</td><td>${fo?statusBadge(fo.sync):statusBadge('Pending')}</td><td>${p.shipmentDate}</td><td>${esc(p.docType)}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.source)}</td><td>${p.eta}</td><td>${p.stops.length}</td><td>${d}</td><td>${u}</td><td>${esc(p.lastUpdate)}</td><td>${statusBadge(p.health||p.status)}</td><td><button class="action-dot" aria-label="Open actions" onclick="openActionMenu(event,'monitor','${esc(p.id)}')">⋮</button></td></tr>`;}).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="13" class="empty">No on-going shipment found.</td></tr>';
}

function goToScheduleDate(){const value=document.getElementById('scheduleDatePicker')?.value;if(!value){toast('Pilih tanggal schedule');return;}const d=isoDate(value),day=d.getDay(),diff=day===0?-6:1-day;d.setDate(d.getDate()+diff);scheduleStart=dateISO(d);renderSchedule();}
function renderSchedule(){
  const start=isoDate(scheduleStart),days=[...Array(7)].map((_,i)=>dateISO(new Date(start.getTime()+i*86400000))),picker=document.getElementById('scheduleDatePicker');if(picker)picker.value=days[0];document.getElementById('scheduleRange').textContent=`${days[0]} — ${days[6]}`;
  const sf=document.getElementById('scheduleSourceFilter')?.value||'',resources=[...new Set(db.plans.filter(p=>!sf||p.source===sf).map(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company'?(p.vehicle+' • '+p.driver):('EXP • '+p.supplier)))];let html='<div class="schedule-grid"><div class="sch-cell sch-head">Resource</div>'+days.map(d=>`<div class="sch-cell sch-head">${new Date(d+'T00:00').toLocaleDateString('id-ID',{weekday:'short',day:'2-digit',month:'short'})}</div>`).join('');resources.forEach(r=>{html+=`<div class="sch-cell sch-resource">${esc(r)}<small>${r.startsWith('EXP')?'Contracted carrier':'Internal fleet'}</small></div>`;days.forEach(d=>{const cards=db.plans.filter(p=>(p.source==='Fleet Company'?(p.vehicle+' • '+p.driver):('EXP • '+p.supplier))===r&&p.shipmentDate===d);html+=`<div class="sch-cell sch-day" ondragover="event.preventDefault();this.classList.add('dragover')" ondragleave="this.classList.remove('dragover')" ondrop="dropPlan(event,'${d}')">${cards.map(p=>`<div class="ship-card ${p.health==='Exception'?'exception':p.status==='Loading'||p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'?'loading':p.source==='Fleet Company'?'internal':'expedition'}" draggable="${['Planned','Draft'].includes(p.status)}" ondragstart="event.dataTransfer.setData('text','${p.id}')" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')"><b>${p.id}</b><span>${esc(p.destination)} • ${p.util||'-'}%</span></div>`).join('')}</div>`;});});html+='</div>';document.getElementById('scheduleBoard').innerHTML=html;
}
function podPlaceholderData(stop,p){const receiver=esc(stop.receiver||stop.customer||'Receiver'),doc=esc(stop.doc),time=esc(stop.arrival||'-');const svg=`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="720" height="430"><defs><linearGradient id="g" x1="0" y1="0" x2="1" y2="1"><stop stop-color="#dff2fa"/><stop offset="1" stop-color="#f7fbfc"/></linearGradient></defs><rect width="720" height="430" fill="url(#g)"/><rect x="36" y="34" width="648" height="362" rx="18" fill="#fff" stroke="#b8dce9"/><text x="65" y="90" font-family="Arial" font-size="30" font-weight="700" fill="#2f93b0">Proof of Delivery</text><text x="65" y="138" font-family="Arial" font-size="20" fill="#34404a">${doc}</text><text x="65" y="181" font-family="Arial" font-size="18" fill="#68747c">Shipment: ${esc(p.id)}</text><text x="65" y="220" font-family="Arial" font-size="18" fill="#68747c">Receiver: ${receiver}</text><text x="65" y="259" font-family="Arial" font-size="18" fill="#68747c">Arrival: ${time}</text><path d="M438 306 C480 250 505 350 548 286 S616 335 650 266" fill="none" stroke="#34404a" stroke-width="4"/><text x="470" y="365" font-family="cursive" font-size="20" fill="#34404a">Digital Signature</text></svg>`;return 'data:image/svg+xml;charset=UTF-8,'+encodeURIComponent(svg);}
function viewPodAttachment(planId,stopIndex){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===planId),stop=p?.stops?.[stopIndex];if(!p||!stop||!stop.pod){toast('Attachment POD belum tersedia');return;}const photo=stop.podPhotoData||podPlaceholderData(stop,p),signature=stop.signatureRef||stop.podRef||stop.receiver||'Digital Signature';openModal('POD Attachment • '+stop.doc,`<div class="pod-preview"><div class="pod-photo"><img src="${photo}" alt="POD Photo ${esc(stop.doc)}"></div><div><div class="notice"><b>${esc(stop.status)}</b><br>${esc(stop.doc)} • ${esc(p.id)}</div><div class="info-list"><div class="info-row"><span>Receiver</span><b>${esc(stop.receiver||'-')}</b></div><div class="info-row"><span>Arrival</span><b>${esc(stop.arrival||'-')}</b></div><div class="info-row"><span>Photo File</span><b>${esc(stop.podPhotoName||'Generated POD Preview')}</b></div><div class="info-row"><span>Reference</span><b>${esc(stop.podRef||'-')}</b></div></div><div class="section-title">Photo / Signature Result</div><div class="signature-box">${esc(signature)}</div></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`);}
function planDetail(id){
  const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(id);if(!p)return;const stopRows=p.stops.map((s,i)=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(s.doc)}</td><td>${esc(s.customer)}</td><td>${statusBadge(s.status)}</td><td>${esc(s.arrival)}</td><td>${s.pod?`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="viewPodAttachment('${esc(p.id)}',${i})">View Photo / Signature</button>`:'No Data'}</td></tr>`).join(''),syncEvents=db.syncLogs.filter(x=>x.ref===id||x.ref===fo?.id||p.docs.includes(x.ref)).slice(0,5);
  openModal('Detail '+id,`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Shipment Option</label><div>${statusBadge(p.source)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Status</label><div>${statusBadge(p.status)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Dispatch Hub</label><div>${esc(p.dispatchHub||p.origin)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Fleet Order Number</label><div class="mono">${fo?fo.id:'Not Created'}</div></div><div class="field"><label>McEasy Sync</label><div>${fo?statusBadge(fo.sync):statusBadge('Pending')}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Shipment Date / ETA</label><div>${p.shipmentDate} / ${p.eta}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Vehicle / Supplier</label><div>${esc(p.source==='Fleet Company'?p.vehicle+' / '+p.driver:p.supplier)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Planned Cost</label><div>${fmtIDR(p.plannedCost)}</div></div><div class="field full"><label>Shipment Route</label><div>${esc(p.route)}</div></div></div><div class="section-title">Document / Stop List</div><div class="table-wrap"><table class="tbl"><thead><tr><th>Document</th><th>Customer</th><th>Status</th><th>Arrival</th><th>Attachment</th></tr></thead><tbody>${stopRows}</tbody></table></div><div class="section-title">Integration Timeline</div><div class="timeline">${syncEvents.length?syncEvents.map(e=>`<div class="timeline-item"><b>${esc(e.event)} • ${statusBadge(e.status)}</b><p>${esc(e.time)} — ${esc(e.direction)} — ${esc(e.message)}</p></div>`).join(''):'<div class="timeline-item"><b>No integration event</b><p>Create or sync Fleet Order to start the timeline.</p></div>'}</div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>${fo?`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal();fleetOrderDetail('${fo.id}')">Open Fleet Order</button>`:`<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="closeModal();openFleetOrderForm('${p.id}')">Create Fleet Order</button>`}`);
}

function inferDriverStep(p){if(!p)return 0;if(p.status==='Completed')return 8;if(p.status==='Returning')return 7;if(p.status==='Unloading')return 6;if(p.status==='In Transit')return 4;if(['Loading','Ready to Dispatch'].includes(p.status))return 2;return 0;}
function ensureDriverStates(){
  db.driverStates=db.driverStates||{};db.mobileDriverUser=db.mobileDriverUser||db.drivers?.find(x=>x.username)?.username||'asepdriver';
  db.plans.filter(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company').forEach(p=>{const existing=db.driverStates[p.id]||{planId:p.id,step:0,currentStop:0,accepted:false,preTrip:false,loadConfirmed:false,closed:false};const inferred=inferDriverStep(p);existing.step=p.status==='Completed'?8:Math.max(Number(existing.step||0),inferred);existing.planId=p.id;if(p.preLoadingCheck?.status==='Passed'&&p.preLoadingCheck?.checkerName){existing.checkerName=p.preLoadingCheck.checkerName;existing.checkerSource='Loading & Dispatch';existing.checkerSyncedAt=p.preLoadingCheck.completedAt||existing.checkerSyncedAt||'';}db.driverStates[p.id]=existing;});
  if(db.driverState?.planId&&!db.driverStates[db.driverState.planId])db.driverStates[db.driverState.planId]={planId:db.driverState.planId,step:Number(db.driverState.step||0),currentStop:0,accepted:!!db.driverState.accepted,preTrip:!!db.driverState.checklist,loadConfirmed:!!db.driverState.loaded,closed:false};
  const plans=assignedPlansForUser(db.mobileDriverUser);if(!db.mobileSelectedPlan||!plans.some(p=>p.id===db.mobileSelectedPlan))db.mobileSelectedPlan=plans.find(p=>p.status!=='Completed')?.id||plans[0]?.id||'';
}
function refreshDriverMobile(){reloadSharedDB();renderDriverMobile();toast('Driver Mobile refreshed from shared Operational data');}
function renderDriverMobile(){
  const userSel=document.getElementById('mobileDriverUser'),tripSel=document.getElementById('mobileTripSelect');if(!document.getElementById('phoneBody'))return;ensureDriverStates();
  if(userSel)userSel.innerHTML=db.drivers.filter(x=>x.username).map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.username)}" ${x.username===db.mobileDriverUser?'selected':''}>${esc(x.name)} (${esc(x.username)})</option>`).join('');
  const plans=assignedPlansForUser(db.mobileDriverUser);if(tripSel)tripSel.innerHTML=plans.map(p=>`<option value="${p.id}" ${p.id===db.mobileSelectedPlan?'selected':''}>${p.id} — ${p.status} — ${esc(p.destination)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No assigned trip</option>';
  const p=driverPlan(),label=document.getElementById('mobileUserLabel');if(label)label.textContent=db.mobileDriverUser||'-';const summary=document.getElementById('driverTripSummary');
  if(!p){document.getElementById('phoneBody').innerHTML='<div class="empty">No trip assigned to this driver.</div>';document.getElementById('driverStepper').innerHTML='';if(summary)summary.innerHTML='<div class="notice warn">Driver Mobile reads assignment from Shipment Plan and Fleet Order data.</div>';return;}
  const st=selectedDriverState(),s=Number(st.step||0),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),current=p.stops[Math.min(st.currentStop||0,p.stops.length-1)],vehicle=db.vehicles.find(v=>v.plate===p.vehicle),fleetMap=db.fleetMappings?.find(v=>v.id===p.vehicle),currentOdo=Number(st.odometerStart||fleetMap?.odometer||vehicle?.odometer||0);
  document.getElementById('driverStepper').innerHTML=driverSteps.map((x,i)=>`<div class="step-line ${i<s?'done':i===s?'active':''}"><div class="step-circle">${i<s?'✓':i+1}</div><div class="step-content"><b>${x}</b><p>${i<s?'Completed':i===s?'Current action':'Waiting previous step'}</p></div></div>`).join('');
  if(summary)summary.innerHTML=`<div class="phone-row"><span>Plan</span><b>${p.id}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Fleet Order</span><b>${fo?.id||'-'}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Vehicle</span><b>${esc(p.vehicle)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Route</span><b>${esc(p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Status</span><span>${statusBadge(p.status)}</span></div>${linkedEntitySummary(p)}`;
  const loaded=(p.loadedDocs||[]).length,allLoaded=loaded===p.docs.length;let html=`<div class="refresh-strip"><span>Shared live data • ${esc(p.lastUpdate||'-')}</span><button onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">↻ Refresh</button></div>`;
  if(s===0)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('accept')">Accept Trip</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverAction('reject')">Reject with Reason</button>`;
  else if(s===1)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Check Vehicle Validity</h4><input class="input" id="odometerStart" type="number" min="0" value="${currentOdo||''}" placeholder="First Odometer / Odometer Start" style="width:100%;margin-bottom:8px"><input class="input" id="fuelStart" type="number" min="0" max="100" value="${st.fuelStart||''}" placeholder="Fuel Start %" style="width:100%;margin-bottom:8px">${['Tyre','Brake','Lights','Body condition','STNK / KIR validity'].map(x=>`<label class="check-row" style="padding:5px 0"><input type="checkbox" class="precheck">${x}</label>`).join('')}</div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('check')">Submit Validity Check</button>`;
  else if(s===2)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Warehouse Loading Status</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Plan Status</span><b>${p.status}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Documents Loaded</span><b>${loaded}/${p.docs.length}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Gate Readiness</span><b>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'Ready':'Waiting Warehouse'}</b></div></div>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction(\'loading\')">Confirm Load Received</button>':'<button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Loading & Dispatch Module</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">Refresh Status</button>'}`;
  else if(s===3)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="notice" style="margin:10px 13px">Load confirmed. Gate operator must perform Gate-Out / Dispatch from Loading & Dispatch.</div><button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Gate-Out</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">Refresh Status</button>`;
  else if(s===4)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Next Stop ${Math.min((st.currentStop||0)+1,p.stops.length)} / ${p.stops.length}</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Customer</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Document</span><b>${esc(current.doc)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>ETA</span><b>${p.eta} 14:30</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('arrive')">Arrived at Stop</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverException()">Report Exception</button>`;
  else if(s===5)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Arrival Confirmed</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Stop</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Geofence</span><b>Inside delivery radius</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('unload')">Start Unloading</button>`;
  else if(s===6)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Delivery Result & ePOD</h4><select class="select" id="mobileResult" style="width:100%"><option>Successfully Delivered</option><option>Unsuccessfully Delivered</option></select><input class="input" id="receiverName" placeholder="Receiver Name" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><input class="input" id="podReference" placeholder="OTP / Signature reference" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><label style="display:block;font-size:10px;color:var(--muted);margin-top:9px">Attach POD Photo</label><input class="input" id="podPhoto" type="file" accept="image/*" style="width:100%;margin-top:4px"></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('pod')">Submit ePOD</button>`;
  else if(s===7)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Return to Origin & Final Odometer</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(p.origin)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>All Stops</span><b>${p.stops.filter(x=>x.pod).length}/${p.stops.length} ePOD</b></div><input class="input" value="${st.odometerStart||''}" disabled placeholder="First Odometer" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><input class="input" id="odometerEnd" type="number" min="0" value="${st.odometerEnd||''}" placeholder="End Odometer" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"><input class="input" id="fuelEnd" type="number" min="0" max="100" value="${st.fuelEnd||''}" placeholder="Fuel End %" style="width:100%;margin-top:8px"></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('close')">Arrived at Origin & Close Trip</button>`;
  else html+='<div class="phone-card" style="text-align:center;margin-top:60px"><div style="font-size:44px;color:var(--green)">✓</div><h4>Trip Completed</h4><p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted)">'+esc(p.id)+' is closed and resources are available again.</p></div>';
  document.getElementById('phoneBody').innerHTML=html;
}
function finishDriverPod(p,st,fo,driver,vehicle,result,receiver,ref,photoName,photoData){
  const stop=p.stops[st.currentStop||0];stop.status=result;stop.pod=true;stop.receiver=receiver;stop.podRef=ref||photoName;stop.signatureRef=ref;stop.podPhotoName=photoName||'No photo file';stop.podPhotoData=photoData||'';stop.arrival=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16);p.lastUpdate='ePOD submitted for '+stop.doc;if(result!=='Successfully Delivered')p.health='Exception';integrationEvent('POD',stop.doc,'delivery.pod.received',result+' • receiver '+receiver,'McEasy → Prieds');
  if((st.currentStop||0)<p.stops.length-1){st.currentStop=(st.currentStop||0)+1;st.step=4;p.status='In Transit';if(fo){fo.status='OTW Tujuan';fo.updated='Proceeding to next stop';}}else{st.step=7;p.status='Returning';if(driver)driver.status='Returning';if(vehicle)vehicle.status='Returning';if(fo){fo.status='Delivered';fo.updated='All stops processed';fo.lastLocation=p.destination;}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.delivered','All stops processed and POD synchronized','McEasy → Prieds');}
  saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('ePOD saved and attachment is available in Shipment Schedule detail');
}
function driverAction(a){
  const p=driverPlan(),st=selectedDriverState();if(!p||!st)return;const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),driver=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver),vehicle=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle);
  if(a==='reject'){driverException('Trip Rejected');return;}
  if(a==='accept'){st.accepted=true;st.step=1;p.lastUpdate='Trip accepted by '+p.driver;if(driver)driver.status='Assigned';if(fo){fo.status='Dijadwalkan';fo.updated='Trip accepted';}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'driver.trip.accepted','Driver accepted '+p.id,'McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='check'){
    if([...document.querySelectorAll('.precheck')].some(x=>!x.checked)){toast('Seluruh validity checklist wajib diisi');return;}const odo=Number(document.getElementById('odometerStart')?.value||0),fuel=Number(document.getElementById('fuelStart')?.value||0);if(odo<=0){toast('First Odometer wajib diisi');return;}if(fuel<0||fuel>100){toast('Fuel Start harus 0-100%');return;}st.odometerStart=odo;st.fuelStart=fuel;st.preTrip=true;st.step=2;p.lastUpdate='Validity check completed at '+odo.toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km';integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'driver.pretrip.completed','Vehicle validity and first odometer recorded','McEasy → Prieds');
  }else if(a==='loading'){
    if(p.status!=='Ready to Dispatch'||(p.loadedDocs||[]).length!==p.docs.length){toast('Loading belum selesai di modul Loading & Dispatch');return;}st.loadConfirmed=true;st.step=3;p.lastUpdate='Load received by driver';integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'driver.load.confirmed','Driver confirmed loaded documents','McEasy → Prieds');
  }else if(a==='arrive'){st.step=5;p.lastUpdate='Driver arrived at stop '+((st.currentStop||0)+1);if(fo){fo.lastLocation=p.stops[st.currentStop||0]?.customer||p.destination;fo.updated='Arrived at stop';fo.status='OTW Tujuan';}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'driver.arrived','Driver arrived inside destination geofence','McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='unload'){st.step=6;p.status='Unloading';p.lastUpdate='Unloading started';if(fo){fo.status='Unloading';fo.updated='Unloading started';}if(driver)driver.status='On Trip';if(vehicle)vehicle.status='In Transit';integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.unloading.started','Unloading started at current stop','McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='pod'){
    const result=document.getElementById('mobileResult').value,receiver=document.getElementById('receiverName').value.trim(),ref=document.getElementById('podReference').value.trim(),file=document.getElementById('podPhoto')?.files?.[0];if(!receiver){toast('Receiver Name wajib');return;}if(!ref&&!file){toast('Signature reference atau file POD wajib dilampirkan');return;}if(file){const reader=new FileReader();reader.onload=()=>finishDriverPod(p,st,fo,driver,vehicle,result,receiver,ref,file.name,String(reader.result||''));reader.onerror=()=>toast('File POD tidak dapat dibaca');reader.readAsDataURL(file);return;}finishDriverPod(p,st,fo,driver,vehicle,result,receiver,ref,'', '');return;
  }else if(a==='close'){
    const end=Number(document.getElementById('odometerEnd')?.value||0),fuelEnd=Number(document.getElementById('fuelEnd')?.value||0);if(end<=0){toast('End Odometer wajib diisi');return;}if(st.odometerStart&&end<Number(st.odometerStart)){toast('End Odometer tidak boleh lebih kecil dari First Odometer');return;}if(fuelEnd<0||fuelEnd>100){toast('Fuel End harus 0-100%');return;}st.odometerEnd=end;st.fuelEnd=fuelEnd;st.step=8;st.closed=true;p.status='Completed';p.health=p.stops.every(x=>x.status==='Successfully Delivered')?'Completed':'Exception';p.actualCost=p.actualCost||Math.round(p.plannedCost*1.04);p.lastUpdate='Trip closed at origin • '+end.toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km';if(driver)driver.status='Available';if(vehicle){vehicle.status='Available';vehicle.odometer=end;}const fm=db.fleetMappings?.find(x=>x.id===p.vehicle);if(fm)fm.odometer=end;if(fo){fo.status='Delivered';fo.updated='Trip closed';fo.lastLocation=p.origin;}integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'trip.closed','Trip closed; end odometer '+end,'McEasy → Prieds');
  }
  saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('Driver action synchronized to Loading, Monitoring, Integration, and Report');
}


/* ===== OPERATIONAL REVISION V4 LOGIC ===== */
let operationalMobileView='trips';
let mobilePodDraft={key:'',fileName:'',photoData:'',signatureData:'',receiverName:'',deliveryResult:'Successfully Delivered',deliveryReason:''};

function wizardSelectedDocuments(){
  const ids=(document.getElementById('sw-docs')?.value||'').split('|').filter(Boolean);
  return db.documents.filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id));
}
function uniqueValues(arr){return [...new Set(arr.filter(Boolean))]}
function normalizeRouteName(v){return String(v||'').toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim()}
function wizardAutoRoute(docs,stopCategory,hub){
  const origins=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin)),destinations=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.destination));
  const start=origins.length===1?origins[0]:origins.join(' + ');
  const segments=[start];if(stopCategory==='Hub'&&hub&&normalizeRouteName(hub)!==normalizeRouteName(start))segments.push(hub);destinations.forEach(d=>{if(normalizeRouteName(d)!==normalizeRouteName(segments[segments.length-1]))segments.push(d);});
  return segments.join(' → ');
}
function wizardRouteCandidates(docs,stopCategory,hub){
  const origins=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin)),destinations=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.destination));
  const referenceOrigin=stopCategory==='Hub'?hub:(origins.length===1?origins[0]:'');
  const active=(db.routes||[]).filter(r=>r.status==='Active'),matches=active.filter(r=>{const ro=normalizeRouteName(r.origin),rd=normalizeRouteName(r.destination),originMatch=!referenceOrigin||ro===normalizeRouteName(referenceOrigin),destinationMatch=destinations.some(d=>rd===normalizeRouteName(d)||rd.includes(normalizeRouteName(d))||normalizeRouteName(d).includes(rd));return originMatch&&destinationMatch;});
  if(matches.length)return matches;
  return active.filter(r=>!referenceOrigin||normalizeRouteName(r.origin)===normalizeRouteName(referenceOrigin));
}
function toggleRouteEdit(){
  const input=document.getElementById('sw-route-text'),btn=document.getElementById('sw-route-edit');if(!input)return;
  input.disabled=!input.disabled;input.dataset.manual=input.disabled?'0':'1';btn.textContent=input.disabled?'Edit Route':'Use Auto Route';
  if(input.disabled)refreshWizardRoute(true);else{input.focus();input.select();}
}
function applyWizardLane(){
  const docs=wizardSelectedDocuments(),stop=document.getElementById('sw-stop')?.value||'End Customer',hub=document.getElementById('sw-hub')?.value||'',sel=document.getElementById('sw-route-select'),input=document.getElementById('sw-route-text');if(!sel||!input)return;
  if(sel.value==='AUTO')input.value=wizardAutoRoute(docs,stop,hub);else{const route=(db.routes||[]).find(r=>r.id===sel.value);input.value=route?`${route.origin} → ${route.destination}`:wizardAutoRoute(docs,stop,hub);}
  input.disabled=true;input.dataset.manual='0';const b=document.getElementById('sw-route-edit');if(b)b.textContent='Edit Route';
}
function refreshWizardRoute(force=false){
  const docs=wizardSelectedDocuments(),stop=document.getElementById('sw-stop')?.value||'End Customer',hub=document.getElementById('sw-hub')?.value||'',select=document.getElementById('sw-route-select'),input=document.getElementById('sw-route-text'),summary=document.getElementById('sw-route-summary');if(!select||!input)return;
  const old=select.value,candidates=wizardRouteCandidates(docs,stop,hub);
  select.innerHTML=`<option value="AUTO">Auto Route — follow selected documents</option>`+candidates.map(r=>`<option value="${esc(r.id)}">${esc(r.id)} • ${esc(r.origin)} → ${esc(r.destination)} (${r.distance||'-'} km)</option>`).join('');
  if([...select.options].some(o=>o.value===old))select.value=old;else select.value='AUTO';
  if(force||input.dataset.manual!=='1')applyWizardLane();
  const origins=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin)),destinations=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.destination));
  if(summary)summary.innerHTML=`${docs.length} document • ${origins.length} origin • ${destinations.length} destination${stop==='Hub'&&hub?` • transit via <b>${esc(hub)}</b>`:''}`;
}
function wizardStopChanged(){
  const stop=document.getElementById('sw-stop')?.value||'End Customer',wrap=document.getElementById('sw-hub-wrap'),docs=wizardSelectedDocuments(),warning=document.getElementById('sw-route-warning');
  if(wrap)wrap.classList.toggle('hidden',stop!=='Hub');
  const origins=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin));
  if(warning)warning.innerHTML=stop==='Hub'?'Hub menjadi titik transit/konsolidasi. Final destination tetap mengikuti setiap dokumen.':origins.length>1?'Dokumen memiliki origin berbeda. Pilih Stop Category <b>Hub</b> agar ada titik konsolidasi sebelum delivery.':'Direct delivery menggunakan origin dokumen dan seluruh destination terpilih.';
  wizardDynamic();refreshWizardRoute(true);
}
function openShipmentWizard(prefillDocs=null){
  const ids=prefillDocs||[...selectedDocs],docs=db.documents.filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id));if(!docs.length){toast('Pilih minimal satu DO/STO terlebih dahulu');return;}
  const hubs=detectedHubOptions(docs),commonOrigin=docs.every(d=>d.origin===docs[0].origin)?docs[0].origin:'',hubNames=(db.hubs||[]).map(h=>h.name),preferredHub=docs.find(d=>hubNames.includes(d.destination))?.destination||hubs.find(h=>h!==commonOrigin)||hubs[0]||'',defaultSource=document.getElementById('readyShippingOption')?.value||'Fleet Company',defaultFleet=document.getElementById('readyFleetSelect')?.value||'';
  const docRows=docs.map(d=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(d.id)}</td><td>${d.type}</td><td>${esc(d.customer)}</td><td>${esc(d.origin)}</td><td>${esc(d.destination)}</td></tr>`).join('');
  const destinations=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.destination));
  const body=`<div class="notice">Tentukan jenis stop terlebih dahulu. Field Hub hanya muncul untuk perjalanan melalui titik transit atau konsolidasi.</div><div class="doc-selection-table"><table class="tbl"><thead><tr><th>Document</th><th>Type</th><th>Customer / Recipient</th><th>Origin</th><th>Destination</th></tr></thead><tbody>${docRows}</tbody></table></div><div class="wizard-context"><div>Total Load<b>${docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0).toLocaleString()} kg / ${docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0).toFixed(1)} m³</b></div><div>Origin<b>${esc(commonOrigin||uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin)).join(' + '))}</b></div><div>Destination<b>${esc(destinations.join(' / '))}</b></div></div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Shipping Option</label><select class="select" id="sw-source" onchange="wizardDynamic()"><option ${defaultSource==='Fleet Company'?'selected':''}>Fleet Company</option><option ${defaultSource==='Expedition'?'selected':''}>Expedition</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Stop Category</label><select class="select" id="sw-stop" onchange="wizardStopChanged()"><option>End Customer</option><option>Hub</option></select><small>Hub dipakai sebagai transit/consolidation stop.</small></div><div class="field hidden" id="sw-hub-wrap"><label>Dispatch / Consolidation Hub</label><select class="select" id="sw-hub" onchange="wizardDynamic();refreshWizardRoute(true)">${hubs.map(h=>`<option ${h===preferredHub?'selected':''}>${esc(h)}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Shipment Date</label><input class="input" type="date" id="sw-date" value="${todayISO()}" onchange="syncContract()"></div><div class="field"><label>Estimate Date to Arrival</label><input class="input" type="date" id="sw-eta" value="${addDays(todayISO(),1)}"></div><div id="sw-dynamic" class="field full"></div><div class="field full"><div class="route-builder"><div class="route-builder-head"><b>Route / Lane</b><span id="sw-route-summary"></span></div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Lane Source</label><select class="select" id="sw-route-select" onchange="applyWizardLane()"></select></div><div class="field"><label>Generated Route</label><div style="display:flex;gap:7px"><input class="input" id="sw-route-text" disabled style="flex:1;min-width:0"><button class="btn btn-outline" type="button" id="sw-route-edit" onclick="toggleRouteEdit()">Edit Route</button></div></div></div><div class="route-preview"><span class="route-icon">⌁</span><div><b>Auto routing follows selected destinations</b><p>Master Lane ditampilkan jika origin/destination cocok. User tetap dapat mengubah route secara manual.</p></div></div><div class="route-warning" id="sw-route-warning"></div></div></div><div class="field full"><label>Remark</label><textarea class="textarea" id="sw-remark" placeholder="Transport notes, special handling, temperature, seal, etc."></textarea></div></div><input type="hidden" id="sw-docs" value="${ids.join('|')}"><input type="hidden" id="sw-readyFleet" value="${esc(defaultFleet)}">`;
  openModal('Create Shipment Plan',body,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="createShipmentPlan()">Create Plan</button>`);wizardStopChanged();
}
function wizardDynamic(){
  const src=document.getElementById('sw-source')?.value||'Fleet Company',stop=document.getElementById('sw-stop')?.value||'End Customer',hub=document.getElementById('sw-hub')?.value||'',box=document.getElementById('sw-dynamic'),preferred=document.getElementById('sw-readyFleet')?.value||'';if(!box)return;
  if(src==='Fleet Company'){
    const vehicles=db.vehicles.filter(x=>!['Maintenance','Inactive'].includes(x.status)),drivers=db.drivers.filter(x=>!['Leave','Inactive'].includes(x.status));
    box.innerHTML=`<div class="section-title">Internal Fleet Assignment</div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Fleet / Vehicle</label><select class="select" id="sw-vehicle" onchange="calculateWizardUtil()">${vehicles.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.id)}" ${x.id===preferred?'selected':''}>${esc(x.plate)} — ${esc(x.type)} (${x.weight}kg / ${x.volume}m³)</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Driver</label><select class="select" id="sw-driver">${drivers.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.id)}">${esc(x.name)} — ${esc(x.status)}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Planned Cost</label><input class="input" type="number" id="sw-cost" value="450000"></div><div class="field"><label>Stop Handling</label><input class="input" value="${stop==='Hub'?'Transit via '+esc(hub||'selected Hub'):'Direct to selected customers'}" disabled></div><div class="field full"><div id="sw-util"></div></div></div>`;calculateWizardUtil();
  }else{
    const carriers=activeExpeditionCarriers();
    box.innerHTML=`<div class="section-title">Expedition / Contracted Carrier</div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Fleet / Carrier</label><select class="select" id="sw-supplier" onchange="syncContract()">${carriers.map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.name)}" ${x.name===preferred?'selected':''}>${esc(x.name)} — ${esc(x.location||'-')} — ${esc(x.sla||((x.slaHours||'-')+' Hours'))}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No expedition carrier available</option>'}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Active Contract</label><select class="select" id="sw-contract"></select></div><div class="field"><label>Fee Delivery</label><input class="input" type="number" id="sw-cost" value="500000"></div><div class="field"><label>POD Rule</label><select class="select" id="sw-pod"><option>Photo + Signature</option><option>Signature Only</option></select></div></div>`;syncContract();
  }
}
function createShipmentPlan(){
  const ids=(document.getElementById('sw-docs')?.value||'').split('|').filter(Boolean),docs=db.documents.filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id)),src=document.getElementById('sw-source')?.value||'Fleet Company',stopCategory=document.getElementById('sw-stop')?.value||'End Customer',origins=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin)),hub=stopCategory==='Hub'?(document.getElementById('sw-hub')?.value||''):'';
  if(stopCategory==='Hub'&&!hub){toast('Dispatch / Consolidation Hub wajib dipilih');return;}if(stopCategory==='End Customer'&&origins.length>1){toast('Origin dokumen berbeda. Gunakan Stop Category Hub untuk konsolidasi.');return;}
  let vehicle='-',driver='-',supplier='-',contract='-',wu=0,vu=0,u=0;
  if(src==='Fleet Company'){
    const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-vehicle')?.value),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.id===document.getElementById('sw-driver')?.value);if(!v||!d){toast('Fleet dan Driver wajib dipilih');return;}
    const w=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),vol=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0);wu=Math.round(w/v.weight*100);vu=Math.round(vol/v.volume*100);u=Math.max(wu,vu);if(u>100){toast('Shipment melebihi kapasitas kendaraan');return;}vehicle=v.plate;driver=d.name;supplier=v.carrier;
  }else{supplier=document.getElementById('sw-supplier')?.value||'';contract=document.getElementById('sw-contract')?.value||'';if(!supplier||!contract){toast('Carrier wajib memiliki kontrak aktif');return;}}
  const route=(document.getElementById('sw-route-text')?.value||'').trim();if(!route){toast('Route / Lane wajib tersedia');return;}
  const num='PL/'+String(Math.max(0,...db.plans.map(x=>Number(x.id.replace(/\D/g,''))))+1).padStart(5,'0'),destination=uniqueValues(docs.map(x=>x.destination)).join(' / '),origin=origins.length===1?origins[0]:origins.join(' / ');
  const p={id:num,docs:ids,docType:uniqueValues(docs.map(x=>x.type)).map(x=>x==='DO'?'Delivery Order':'Stock Transfer Out').join(' + '),source:src,supplier,contract,vehicle,driver,shipmentDate:document.getElementById('sw-date').value,eta:document.getElementById('sw-eta').value,origin,dispatchHub:hub||origin,transitHub:hub,stopCategory,destination,route,routeLane:document.getElementById('sw-route-select')?.value||'AUTO',weight:docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),volume:Number(docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0).toFixed(1)),weightUtil:wu,volumeUtil:vu,util:u,status:'Planned',health:'On Schedule',plannedCost:Number(document.getElementById('sw-cost')?.value||0),actualCost:0,remark:document.getElementById('sw-remark')?.value.trim()||'',lastUpdate:'just now',stops:docs.map(x=>({doc:x.id,customer:x.customer,category:'End Customer',viaHub:hub||'',destination:x.destination,status:'On Going',arrival:'-',pod:false})),loadedDocs:[]};
  db.plans.push(p);docs.forEach(x=>x.status='Done Planning');if(src==='Fleet Company'){const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===vehicle),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===driver);if(v)v.status='Reserved';if(d)d.status='Assigned';}ensureDriverStates();saveDB();selectedDocs.clear();closeModal();renderAll();planningTab(document.querySelector('#page-planning .tab:nth-child(2)'),'planPanel');toast('Plan Number berhasil dibuat: '+num);
}
function recommendationScore(group){
  const priorityMap={Urgent:60,High:50,Normal:25,Low:10},maxPriority=Math.max(...group.map(d=>priorityMap[d.priority]||25));
  const now=Date.now(),alerts=group.map(d=>Date.parse(String(d.alert).replace(' ','T'))).filter(Number.isFinite),earliest=alerts.length?Math.min(...alerts):now+86400000,minutes=(earliest-now)/60000;
  const urgency=minutes<=0?30:minutes<=240?25:minutes<=720?15:5,consolidation=Math.min(20,Math.max(0,(group.length-1)*10));
  return {total:maxPriority+urgency+consolidation,document:maxPriority,urgency,consolidation,minutes};
}
function recommendationLabel(score){return score>=85?['Critical','b-red']:score>=65?['High','b-orange']:score>=45?['Medium','b-blue']:['Normal','b-gray']}
function generateRecommendations(){
  const docs=db.documents.filter(x=>x.status==='Need Planning'),groups={};docs.forEach(d=>{const key=normalizeRouteName(d.destination);(groups[key]??=[]).push(d)});
  const recommendations=Object.values(groups).map(group=>({group,score:recommendationScore(group)})).sort((a,b)=>b.score.total-a.score.total||String(a.group[0].destination).localeCompare(String(b.group[0].destination)));
  const box=document.getElementById('recommendations');if(!box)return;
  const intro=`<div class="reco-card" style="grid-column:1/-1"><h3>How recommendation priority is calculated</h3><div class="recommend-explain"><div><b>Document Priority — max 60</b>Urgent/High from DO or STO contributes the largest score.</div><div><b>Alert Urgency — max 30</b>Earlier or overdue Alert Time receives a higher score.</div><div><b>Consolidation Benefit — max 20</b>More documents with the exact same destination receive an efficiency bonus.</div></div><div class="notice" style="margin:0">Primary grouping rule: <b>exact same destination</b>. Different origins remain in one recommendation, but the wizard will require Hub consolidation before the plan can be created.</div></div>`;
  box.innerHTML=intro+recommendations.map((r,i)=>{const g=r.group,s=r.score,[label,cls]=recommendationLabel(s.total),origins=uniqueValues(g.map(x=>x.origin)),w=g.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),v=g.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0),highest=g.sort((a,b)=>(Date.parse(a.alert)-Date.parse(b.alert)))[0];return `<div class="reco-card"><h3>Group ${i+1} <span class="badge ${cls}">${label} • ${s.total}</span></h3><div class="destination-chip">${esc(g[0].destination)}</div><p style="font-size:10.5px;color:var(--muted);margin:5px 0 8px">${g.length} document with the same destination • ${origins.length} origin</p>${g.map(x=>`<div class="check-row" style="margin:5px 0"><input type="checkbox" checked disabled><span class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</span><span style="margin-left:auto">${statusBadge(x.priority)}</span></div>`).join('')}<div style="border-top:1px solid var(--line);margin-top:9px;padding-top:7px"><div class="score-row"><span>Document priority</span><b>+${s.document}</b></div><div class="score-row"><span>Alert urgency (${esc(highest.alert)})</span><b>+${s.urgency}</b></div><div class="score-row"><span>Same-destination benefit</span><b>+${s.consolidation}</b></div></div><div class="notice" style="margin:9px 0">${w.toLocaleString()} kg • ${v.toFixed(1)} m³${origins.length>1?' • Hub consolidation required':''}</div><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick='openShipmentWizard(${JSON.stringify(g.map(x=>x.id))})'>Accept & Plan</button></div>`;}).join('');
}

}

function ensurePodDraft(p,st){const key=p.id+':'+Number(st.currentStop||0);if(mobilePodDraft.key!==key)mobilePodDraft={key,fileName:'',photoData:'',signatureData:'',receiverName:'',deliveryResult:'Successfully Delivered',deliveryReason:''};}

}

}
