}
function renderDriverTripWorkflow(p,st){
  const s=Number(st.step||0),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),current=p.stops[Math.min(st.currentStop||0,p.stops.length-1)],vehicle=db.vehicles.find(v=>v.plate===p.vehicle),fleetMap=db.fleetMappings?.find(v=>v.id===p.vehicle),currentOdo=Number(st.odometerStart||fleetMap?.odometer||vehicle?.odometer||0),loaded=(p.loadedDocs||[]).length,allLoaded=loaded===p.docs.length;let html=`<div class="refresh-strip"><span>Shared live data • ${esc(p.lastUpdate||'-')}</span><button onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">↻ Refresh</button></div>`;
  if(s===0)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('accept')">Accept Trip</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverAction('reject')">Reject with Reason</button>`;
  else if(s===1)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Check Vehicle Validity</h4><label class="field-label-mobile">First Odometer (km)</label><input class="input" id="odometerStart" type="number" min="0" value="${currentOdo||''}" placeholder="Input starting odometer" style="width:100%"><label class="field-label-mobile">First Fuel (%)</label><input class="input" id="fuelStart" type="number" min="0" max="100" value="${st.fuelStart??''}" placeholder="Input starting fuel percentage" style="width:100%;margin-bottom:8px">${['Tyre','Brake','Lights','Body condition','STNK / KIR validity'].map(x=>`<label class="check-row" style="padding:5px 0"><input type="checkbox" class="precheck">${x}</label>`).join('')}</div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('check')">Submit Validity Check</button>`;
  else if(s===2)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Warehouse Loading Status</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Plan Status</span><b>${p.status}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Documents Loaded</span><b>${loaded}/${p.docs.length}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Gate Readiness</span><b>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'Ready':'Waiting Warehouse'}</b></div></div>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction(\'loading\')">Confirm Load Received</button>':'<button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Loading & Dispatch Module</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">Refresh Status</button>'}`;
  else if(s===3)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="notice" style="margin:10px 13px">Load confirmed. Gate operator must perform Gate-Out / Dispatch from Loading & Dispatch.</div><button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Gate-Out</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">Refresh Status</button>`;
  else if(s===4)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Next Stop ${Math.min((st.currentStop||0)+1,p.stops.length)} / ${p.stops.length}</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Customer</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Document</span><b>${esc(current.doc)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(current.destination||p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>ETA</span><b>${p.eta} 14:30</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('arrive')">Arrived at Stop</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="setMobileView('route')">View Route</button>`;
  else if(s===5)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Arrival Confirmed</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Stop</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Geofence</span><b>Inside delivery radius</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('unload')">Start Unloading</button>`;
  else if(s===6)html+=renderPodForm(p,st);
  else if(s===7)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Return to Origin & Final Odometer</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(p.origin)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>All Stops</span><b>${p.stops.filter(x=>x.pod).length}/${p.stops.length} ePOD</b></div><label class="field-label-mobile">First Odometer</label><input class="input" value="${st.odometerStart||''}" disabled style="width:100%"><label class="field-label-mobile">End Odometer</label><input class="input" id="odometerEnd" type="number" min="0" value="${st.odometerEnd||''}" placeholder="End Odometer" style="width:100%"><label class="field-label-mobile">End Fuel (%)</label><input class="input" id="fuelEnd" type="number" min="0" max="100" value="${st.fuelEnd??''}" placeholder="Fuel End %" style="width:100%"></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('close')">Arrived at Origin & Close Trip</button>`;
  else html+='<div class="phone-card" style="text-align:center;margin-top:60px"><div style="font-size:44px;color:var(--green)">✓</div><h4>Trip Completed</h4><p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted)">'+esc(p.id)+' is closed and resources are available again.</p></div>';
  return {html,needsSignature:s===6};
}
function renderDriverMobile(){
  const userSel=document.getElementById('mobileDriverUser'),tripSel=document.getElementById('mobileTripSelect');if(!document.getElementById('phoneBody'))return;ensureDriverStates();
  if(userSel)userSel.innerHTML=db.drivers.filter(x=>x.username).map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x.username)}" ${x.username===db.mobileDriverUser?'selected':''}>${esc(x.name)} (${esc(x.username)})</option>`).join('');
  const plans=assignedPlansForUser(db.mobileDriverUser);if(tripSel)tripSel.innerHTML=plans.map(p=>`<option value="${p.id}" ${p.id===db.mobileSelectedPlan?'selected':''}>${p.id} — ${p.status} — ${esc(p.destination)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No assigned trip</option>';
  const p=driverPlan(),label=document.getElementById('mobileUserLabel');if(label)label.textContent=db.mobileDriverUser||'-';const summary=document.getElementById('driverTripSummary'),body=document.getElementById('phoneBody');updateMobileFooter();
  if(!p){body.innerHTML=operationalMobileView==='profile'?renderMobileProfile(null,null):'<div class="empty">No trip assigned to this driver.</div>';document.getElementById('driverStepper').innerHTML='';if(summary)summary.innerHTML='<div class="notice warn">Driver Mobile reads assignment from Shipment Plan and Fleet Order data.</div>';return;}
  const st=selectedDriverState(),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),s=Number(st.step||0);document.getElementById('driverStepper').innerHTML=driverSteps.map((x,i)=>`<div class="step-line ${i<s?'done':i===s?'active':''}"><div class="step-circle">${i<s?'✓':i+1}</div><div class="step-content"><b>${x}</b><p>${i<s?'Completed':i===s?'Current action':'Waiting previous step'}</p></div></div>`).join('');
  if(summary)summary.innerHTML=`<div class="phone-row"><span>Plan</span><b>${p.id}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Fleet Order</span><b>${fo?.id||'-'}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Vehicle</span><b>${esc(p.vehicle)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Route</span><b>${esc(p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Status</span><span>${statusBadge(p.status)}</span></div>${linkedEntitySummary(p)}`;
  let html='',needsSignature=false;if(operationalMobileView==='route')html=renderMobileRoute(p,st);else if(operationalMobileView==='exception')html=renderMobileExceptions(p);else if(operationalMobileView==='profile')html=renderMobileProfile(p,st);else{const r=renderDriverTripWorkflow(p,st);html=r.html;needsSignature=r.needsSignature;}body.innerHTML=html;updateMobileFooter();if(needsSignature)requestAnimationFrame(initSignaturePad);
}
function handlePodFile(input){
  mobilePodDraft.receiverName=document.getElementById('receiverName')?.value||mobilePodDraft.receiverName||'';
  mobilePodDraft.deliveryResult=document.getElementById('mobileResult')?.value||mobilePodDraft.deliveryResult||'Successfully Delivered';
  mobilePodDraft.deliveryReason=document.getElementById('unsuccessNote')?.value||mobilePodDraft.deliveryReason||'';
  const file=input.files?.[0];if(!file)return;if(!file.type.startsWith('image/')){toast('POD attachment harus berupa gambar');input.value='';return;}if(file.size>10*1024*1024){toast('Ukuran file maksimal 10 MB');input.value='';return;}
  const reader=new FileReader();reader.onerror=()=>toast('File POD tidak dapat dibaca');reader.onload=()=>{const img=new Image();img.onload=()=>{const max=1100,scale=Math.min(1,max/Math.max(img.width,img.height)),c=document.createElement('canvas');c.width=Math.max(1,Math.round(img.width*scale));c.height=Math.max(1,Math.round(img.height*scale));c.getContext('2d').drawImage(img,0,0,c.width,c.height);mobilePodDraft.fileName=file.name;mobilePodDraft.photoData=c.toDataURL('image/jpeg',.78);const status=document.getElementById('podUploadStatus'),preview=document.getElementById('podPhotoPreview'),receiver=document.getElementById('receiverName');if(status)status.textContent=file.name+' • '+Math.round(file.size/1024)+' KB';if(preview){preview.src=mobilePodDraft.photoData;preview.style.display='block';}if(receiver&&receiver.value!==mobilePodDraft.receiverName)receiver.value=mobilePodDraft.receiverName;toast('POD photo attached');};img.onerror=()=>toast('Gambar POD tidak valid');img.src=String(reader.result||'');};reader.readAsDataURL(file);
}
function initSignaturePad(){
  const canvas=document.getElementById('signatureCanvas');if(!canvas)return;const rect=canvas.getBoundingClientRect(),ratio=Math.max(1,window.devicePixelRatio||1);canvas.width=Math.round(rect.width*ratio);canvas.height=Math.round(rect.height*ratio);const ctx=canvas.getContext('2d');ctx.scale(ratio,ratio);ctx.fillStyle='#fff';ctx.fillRect(0,0,rect.width,rect.height);ctx.strokeStyle='#26343d';ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.lineCap='round';ctx.lineJoin='round';
  if(mobilePodDraft.signatureData){const img=new Image();img.onload=()=>ctx.drawImage(img,0,0,rect.width,rect.height);img.src=mobilePodDraft.signatureData;}
  let drawing=false,last=null;const point=e=>{const r=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();return{x:e.clientX-r.left,y:e.clientY-r.top}};canvas.onpointerdown=e=>{drawing=true;last=point(e);canvas.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);};canvas.onpointermove=e=>{if(!drawing)return;const p=point(e);ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(last.x,last.y);ctx.lineTo(p.x,p.y);ctx.stroke();last=p;};const end=()=>{if(!drawing)return;drawing=false;mobilePodDraft.signatureData=canvas.toDataURL('image/png');};canvas.onpointerup=end;canvas.onpointercancel=end;canvas.onpointerleave=end;
}
function clearSignature(){mobilePodDraft.signatureData='';initSignaturePad();}
function finishDriverPod(p,st,fo,driver,vehicle,result,receiver,signatureData,photoName,photoData,reason=''){
  const stop=p.stops[st.currentStop||0];stop.status=result;stop.pod=true;stop.receiver=receiver;stop.podRef=photoName||'Receiver Signature';stop.signatureRef='Receiver Signature';stop.signatureData=signatureData;stop.podPhotoName=photoName||'No photo file';stop.podPhotoData=photoData||'';stop.deliveryReason=reason;stop.arrival=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16);p.lastUpdate='ePOD submitted for '+stop.doc;if(result!=='Successfully Delivered')p.health='Exception';integrationEvent('POD',stop.doc,'delivery.pod.received',result+' • receiver '+receiver,'McEasy → Prieds');
  mobilePodDraft={key:'',fileName:'',photoData:'',signatureData:'',receiverName:'',deliveryResult:'Successfully Delivered',deliveryReason:''};if((st.currentStop||0)<p.stops.length-1){st.currentStop=(st.currentStop||0)+1;st.step=4;p.status='In Transit';if(fo){fo.status='OTW Tujuan';fo.updated='Proceeding to next stop';}}else{st.step=7;p.status='Returning';if(driver)driver.status='Returning';if(vehicle)vehicle.status='Returning';if(fo){fo.status='Delivered';fo.updated='All stops processed';fo.lastLocation=p.destination;}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.delivered','All stops processed and POD synchronized','McEasy → Prieds');}saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('ePOD, photo, and signature saved');
}
function driverAction(a){
  const p=driverPlan(),st=selectedDriverState();if(!p||!st)return;const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),driver=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver),vehicle=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle);
  if(a==='reject'){driverException('Trip Rejected');return;}if(a==='accept'){st.accepted=true;st.step=1;p.lastUpdate='Trip accepted by '+p.driver;if(driver)driver.status='Assigned';if(fo){fo.status='Dijadwalkan';fo.updated='Trip accepted';}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'driver.trip.accepted','Driver accepted '+p.id,'McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='check'){if([...document.querySelectorAll('.precheck')].some(x=>!x.checked)){toast('Seluruh validity checklist wajib diisi');return;}const odoRaw=document.getElementById('odometerStart')?.value||'',fuelRaw=document.getElementById('fuelStart')?.value||'';if(odoRaw===''){toast('First Odometer wajib diisi');return;}if(fuelRaw===''){toast('First Fuel wajib diisi');return;}const odo=Number(odoRaw),fuel=Number(fuelRaw);if(odo<0){toast('First Odometer tidak valid');return;}if(fuel<0||fuel>100){toast('First Fuel harus 0-100%');return;}st.odometerStart=odo;st.fuelStart=fuel;st.preTrip=true;st.step=2;p.lastUpdate='Validity check completed at '+odo.toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km / fuel '+fuel+'%';integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'driver.pretrip.completed','Vehicle validity, first odometer, and first fuel recorded','McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='loading'){if(p.status!=='Ready to Dispatch'||(p.loadedDocs||[]).length!==p.docs.length){toast('Loading belum selesai di modul Loading & Dispatch');return;}st.loadConfirmed=true;st.step=3;p.lastUpdate='Load received by driver';integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'driver.load.confirmed','Driver confirmed loaded documents','McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='arrive'){st.step=5;p.lastUpdate='Driver arrived at stop '+((st.currentStop||0)+1);if(fo){fo.lastLocation=p.stops[st.currentStop||0]?.customer||p.destination;fo.updated='Arrived at stop';fo.status='OTW Tujuan';}integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'driver.arrived','Driver arrived inside destination geofence','McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='unload'){st.step=6;p.status='Unloading';p.lastUpdate='Unloading started';if(fo){fo.status='Unloading';fo.updated='Unloading started';}if(driver)driver.status='On Trip';if(vehicle)vehicle.status='In Transit';integrationEvent('Fleet Order',fo?.id||p.id,'order.unloading.started','Unloading started at current stop','McEasy → Prieds');}
  else if(a==='pod'){const result=document.getElementById('mobileResult')?.value||'Successfully Delivered',receiver=document.getElementById('receiverName')?.value.trim()||'',reason=document.getElementById('unsuccessNote')?.value.trim()||'';if(!receiver){toast('Receiver Name wajib');return;}if(result==='Unsuccessfully Delivered'&&!reason){toast('Reason wajib untuk unsuccessful delivery');return;}if(!mobilePodDraft.signatureData){toast('Receiver Signature wajib diisi');return;}finishDriverPod(p,st,fo,driver,vehicle,result,receiver,mobilePodDraft.signatureData,mobilePodDraft.fileName,mobilePodDraft.photoData,reason);return;}
  else if(a==='close'){const endRaw=document.getElementById('odometerEnd')?.value||'',fuelRaw=document.getElementById('fuelEnd')?.value||'';if(endRaw===''){toast('End Odometer wajib diisi');return;}if(fuelRaw===''){toast('End Fuel wajib diisi');return;}const end=Number(endRaw),fuelEnd=Number(fuelRaw);if(st.odometerStart!==undefined&&end<Number(st.odometerStart)){toast('End Odometer tidak boleh lebih kecil dari First Odometer');return;}if(fuelEnd<0||fuelEnd>100){toast('End Fuel harus 0-100%');return;}st.odometerEnd=end;st.fuelEnd=fuelEnd;st.step=8;st.closed=true;p.status='Completed';p.health=p.stops.every(x=>x.status==='Successfully Delivered')?'Completed':'Exception';p.actualCost=p.actualCost||Math.round(p.plannedCost*1.04);p.lastUpdate='Trip closed at origin • '+end.toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km';if(driver)driver.status='Available';if(vehicle){vehicle.status='Available';vehicle.odometer=end;}const fm=db.fleetMappings?.find(x=>x.id===p.vehicle);if(fm)fm.odometer=end;if(fo){fo.status='Delivered';fo.updated='Trip closed';fo.lastLocation=p.origin;}integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'trip.closed','Trip closed; end odometer '+end,'McEasy → Prieds');}
  saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('Driver action synchronized to all related menus');
}
function viewPodAttachment(planId,stopIndex){
  const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===planId),stop=p?.stops?.[stopIndex];if(!p||!stop||!stop.pod){toast('Attachment POD belum tersedia');return;}const photo=stop.podPhotoData||podPlaceholderData(stop,p),signature=stop.signatureData||'';
  openModal('POD Attachment • '+stop.doc,`<div class="pod-preview"><div><div class="pod-photo"><img src="${photo}" alt="POD Photo ${esc(stop.doc)}"></div><div class="section-title">Receiver Signature</div>${signature?`<img class="signature-image" src="${signature}" alt="Receiver signature">`:`<div class="signature-box">${esc(stop.signatureRef||'Signature not available')}</div>`}</div><div><div class="notice"><b>${esc(stop.status)}</b><br>${esc(stop.doc)} • ${esc(p.id)}</div><div class="info-list"><div class="info-row"><span>Receiver</span><b>${esc(stop.receiver||'-')}</b></div><div class="info-row"><span>Arrival</span><b>${esc(stop.arrival||'-')}</b></div><div class="info-row"><span>Photo File</span><b>${esc(stop.podPhotoName||'Generated POD Preview')}</b></div><div class="info-row"><span>Signature</span><b>${signature?'Captured':'Reference only'}</b></div>${stop.deliveryReason?`<div class="info-row"><span>Delivery Reason</span><b>${esc(stop.deliveryReason)}</b></div>`:''}</div></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`);
}

  3:[['ANOMALY_DETECTION','Anomaly detection','Statistical and pattern-based operational anomaly','pilot'],['PHOTO_DUPLICATION','Photo duplication detection','Perceptual similarity across POD images','pilot'],['BEHAVIOUR_PROFILE','Behaviour profiling','Driver, dispatcher, and approver baseline deviation','pilot'],['CARRIER_NETWORK','Carrier network analysis','Shared bank, address, device, and contact links','pilot'],['COLLUSION','User-carrier collusion detection','Repeated preferential assignment and shared identifiers','pilot'],['CARGO_THEFT','Predictive cargo theft','Route, dwell, GPS, cargo value, and hotspot signals','pilot'],['CROSS_SHIPMENT','Cross-shipment fraud pattern','Repeated pattern across documents and shipment cycles','pilot'],['ML_RISK_SCORE','Machine-learning risk score','Prototype ensemble score with explainable features','pilot']]
};
let antiFraudSeeded=false;
const FRAUD_DOC_REF_PATTERN=/(?:DO\/[A-Z0-9._/-]+|STO-[A-Z0-9._/-]+|FO\/[A-Z0-9._/-]+|PL\/[A-Z0-9._/-]+)/gi;
function fraudReferenceParts(value){
  const raw=Array.isArray(value)?value.join(' / '):String(value||'');
  return [...new Set((raw.match(FRAUD_DOC_REF_PATTERN)||[]).map(x=>x.toUpperCase()))];
}
function fraudPlanReferenceByCarrier(carrier){
  const exact=(db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.supplier===carrier);
  if(exact)return exact.id;
  if(carrier==='Prieds Internal Fleet')return (db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company')?.id||'PL/00002';
  if(carrier==='JNE Logistics')return 'PL/00001';
  if(carrier==='Trans Kargo')return 'PL/00004';
  return '';
}
function fraudReferenceExists(ref){
  if(ref.startsWith('DO/')||ref.startsWith('STO-'))return (db.documents||[]).some(x=>x.id===ref);
  if(ref.startsWith('PL/'))return (db.plans||[]).some(x=>x.id===ref);
  if(ref.startsWith('FO/'))return (db.fleetOrders||[]).some(x=>x.id===ref);
  return false;
}
function fraudDocumentReference(value,context={}){
  const candidates=[value,context.documentRef,context.reference,context.ref,context.fleetOrder,context.planId,...(Array.isArray(context.docs)?context.docs:[])];
  const refs=[];candidates.forEach(v=>fraudReferenceParts(v).forEach(r=>{if(fraudReferenceExists(r)&&!refs.includes(r))refs.push(r)}));
  if(refs.length)return refs.join(' / ');
  if(context.carrier){const p=fraudPlanReferenceByCarrier(context.carrier);if(p)return p;}
  if(context.vehicle){const fo=(db.fleetOrders||[]).find(x=>x.vehicle===context.vehicle);if(fo)return fo.id;}
  if(context.driver){const p=(db.plans||[]).find(x=>x.driver===context.driver);if(p)return p.id;}
  const raw=String(value||'');
  if(raw==='CUST-003')return 'DO/BENEDIT/220900013';
  if(raw.startsWith('CUST-'))return 'DO/BENEDIT/220900011';
  if(raw.startsWith('SKU-'))return 'DO/BENEDIT/220900011';
  return (db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.id==='PL/00003')?.id||(db.plans||[])[0]?.id||'PL/00001';
}
function fraudReferenceHTML(value){
  const refs=fraudReferenceParts(value);if(!refs.length)return '<span class="muted">No linked document</span>';
  return `<span class="fraud-ref-list">${refs.map((r,i)=>`${i?'<span class="fraud-ref-sep">/</span>':''}<button type="button" class="fraud-ref-link" title="Open ${esc(r)}" onclick="openFraudDocumentReference('${encodeURIComponent(r)}')">${esc(r)}</button>`).join('')}</span>`;
}
let fraudSourceContext={ref:'',source:'',returnTab:'alerts'};
function clearSourceNavigationBanner(){document.getElementById('sourceNavigationBanner')?.remove();}
function showSourceNavigationBanner(ref,source){
  clearSourceNavigationBanner();
  const page=document.querySelector('.page.active');if(!page)return;
  const banner=document.createElement('div');banner.id='sourceNavigationBanner';banner.className='source-nav-banner';
  banner.innerHTML=`<span>↗</span><span>Opened from <b>Risk & Anti-Fraud</b>: <span class="mono">${esc(ref)}</span> in ${esc(source)}</span><span class="spacer"></span><button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="returnToFraudControl()">Back to Anti-Fraud</button>`;
  const head=page.querySelector('.page-head');if(head)head.insertAdjacentElement('afterend',banner);else page.prepend(banner);
}
function returnToFraudControl(){
  clearSourceNavigationBanner();goPage('antifraud');
  const tab=document.querySelector('[data-fraud-tab="alerts"]');if(tab)fraudTab(tab,'alerts');
  setTimeout(()=>{const q=document.getElementById('fraudSearch');if(q&&fraudSourceContext.ref){q.value=fraudSourceContext.ref;renderFraudAlertsTable();}window.scrollTo({top:0,behavior:'smooth'});},30);
}
function highlightSourceReference(ref){
  const rows=[...document.querySelectorAll('.page.active table tbody tr')];
  const row=rows.find(x=>x.textContent.includes(ref));if(!row)return;
  row.classList.remove('source-row-highlight');void row.offsetWidth;row.classList.add('source-row-highlight');
  row.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'center'});
}
function openFraudDocumentReference(encoded){
  const ref=decodeURIComponent(String(encoded||''));closeActionMenu?.();closeModal?.();
  const openAfterNavigation=(source,exists,detailFn)=>{
    fraudSourceContext={ref,source,returnTab:'alerts'};
    showSourceNavigationBanner(ref,source);
    setTimeout(()=>{highlightSourceReference(ref);if(exists){detailFn(ref);toast(ref+' opened from '+source);}else toast(ref+' tidak ditemukan di '+source);},90);
  };
  if(ref.startsWith('DO/')||ref.startsWith('STO-')){
    goPage('planning');const tab=document.querySelector('#page-planning .tab:nth-child(1)');planningTab(tab,'candidatePanel');
    const q=document.getElementById('docSearch');if(q)q.value=ref;renderDocuments();
    return openAfterNavigation('Shipment Planning • Ready Documents',(db.documents||[]).some(x=>x.id===ref),documentDetail);
  }
  if(ref.startsWith('PL/')){
    goPage('planning');const tab=document.querySelector('#page-planning .tab:nth-child(2)');planningTab(tab,'planPanel');
    const q=document.getElementById('planSearch');if(q)q.value=ref;renderPlans();
    return openAfterNavigation('Shipment Planning • Plan Number List',(db.plans||[]).some(x=>x.id===ref),planDetail);
  }
  if(ref.startsWith('FO/')){
    goPage('fleet-order');const q=document.getElementById('fleetOrderSearch');if(q)q.value=ref;renderFleetOrders();
    return openAfterNavigation('Integration • Fleet Order',(db.fleetOrders||[]).some(x=>x.id===ref),fleetOrderDetail);
  }
  toast('Reference '+ref+' tidak didukung');
}
function normalizeAntiFraudDocumentReferences(){
  const auditMap={'AUD-0001':'PL/00003','AUD-0002':'FO/MC/00003','AUD-0003':'PL/00004'};
  (db.auditTrail||[]).forEach((x,i)=>x.entity=auditMap[x.id]||fraudDocumentReference(x.entity,{planId:i===0?'PL/00003':'PL/00004'}));
  const sodMap={'SOD-001':'FO/MC/00003','SOD-002':'PL/00001'};
  (db.sodEvents||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=sodMap[x.id]||fraudDocumentReference(x.reference));
  (db.fuelTransactions||[]).forEach(x=>x.documentRef=fraudDocumentReference(x.fleetOrder,x));
  (db.carrierInvoices||[]).forEach(x=>x.documentRef=x.carrier==='Trans Kargo'?'PL/00004':x.carrier==='JNE Logistics'?'PL/00001':fraudDocumentReference('',x));
  (db.carrierVerification||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=fraudPlanReferenceByCarrier(x.carrier)||'PL/00003');
  (db.bankChangeRequests||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=fraudPlanReferenceByCarrier(x.carrier)||'PL/00003');
  const caseMap={'CASE-0001':'PL/00004','CASE-0002':'FO/MC/00003'};
  (db.fraudCases||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=caseMap[x.id]||fraudDocumentReference(x.reference,x));
  const blacklistMap={'BL-001':'PL/00004','BL-002':'PL/00004','BL-003':'FO/MC/00003'};
  (db.fraudBlacklist||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=blacklistMap[x.id]||fraudDocumentReference('',x));
  const evidenceMap={'EVD-0001':'PL/00004','EVD-0002':'PL/00004','EVD-0003':'FO/MC/00003'};
  (db.fraudEvidence||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=evidenceMap[x.id]||fraudDocumentReference('',x));
  const signalMap={'SIG-001':'FO/MC/00003','SIG-002':'DO/BENEDIT/220900011 / PL/00004','SIG-003':'PL/00003','SIG-004':'PL/00004','SIG-005':'PL/00004','SIG-006':'FO/MC/00003','SIG-007':'PL/00001 / PL/00003','SIG-008':'FO/MC/00003'};
  (db.advancedFraudSignals||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=signalMap[x.id]||fraudDocumentReference(x.reference,x));
  const behaviourMap={'Asep Driver':'FO/MC/00001','Budi Driver':'FO/MC/00003','carrier.admin':'PL/00004'};
  (db.behaviourProfiles||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference=behaviourMap[x.entity]||fraudDocumentReference('',x));
  (db.carrierNetworkLinks||[]).forEach(x=>x.reference='PL/00004');
}

}
function fraudReviewStore(){db.fraudReviews=db.fraudReviews||{};return db.fraudReviews;}
function fraudSeverityScore(risk){return({Critical:95,High:78,Medium:55,Low:30})[risk]||20;}
function fraudKey(type,ref,reason){return(type+'|'+ref+'|'+reason).replace(/\s+/g,' ').slice(0,240);}
function fraudRiskScore(alert){const base=fraudSeverityScore(alert.risk),conf=Number(alert.confidence||70),exposure=Math.min(15,Math.round(Number(alert.exposure||0)/1000000*3)),repeat=Math.min(10,Number(alert.recurrence||0)*2);return Math.min(100,Math.round(base*.58+conf*.27+exposure+repeat));}
function makeFraudAlert(type,risk,module,ref,title,reason,detected='Live detection',extra={}){const docRef=fraudDocumentReference(ref,extra),key=fraudKey(type,docRef,reason),review=fraudReviewStore()[key]||{};const a={key,type,risk,module,ref:docRef,title,reason,detected,status:review.status||'Open',note:review.note||'',owner:review.owner||'',reviewedAt:review.reviewedAt||'',phase:extra.phase||1,control:extra.control||type,confidence:extra.confidence||75,exposure:extra.exposure||0,recurrence:extra.recurrence||0,evidence:extra.evidence||[],source:extra.source||module,negativeCase:extra.negativeCase||reason,expectedCondition:extra.expectedCondition||'Transaction follows the configured control and threshold.',actualCondition:extra.actualCondition||reason,sourceRecord:extra.sourceRecord||((extra.evidence||[]).join(' • ')||docRef)};a.score=fraudRiskScore(a);return a;}
function fraudDetectionReasonHTML(a){return `<div class="detection-reason"><div class="negative-case-box"><b>Negative Case</b><span>${esc(a.negativeCase||a.reason)}</span></div><div class="condition-compare"><div class="condition-box"><small>Expected</small><span>${esc(a.expectedCondition||'-')}</span></div><div class="condition-box actual"><small>Actual</small><span>${esc(a.actualCondition||a.reason)}</span></div></div><div class="detection-result"><b>Detection Result:</b> ${esc(a.reason)}</div><div class="source-record">Source: ${esc(a.sourceRecord||a.source||a.ref)}</div></div>`;}
function collectFraudAlerts(){
  ensureAntiFraudData();const alerts=[];const activePlans=(db.plans||[]).filter(p=>!['Completed','Draft'].includes(p.status));
  (db.auditTrail||[]).filter(x=>!x.validHash).forEach(x=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('IMMUTABLE_AUDIT','Critical','Audit Trail',x.entity,'Audit trail integrity failure',`${x.id} has an invalid hash chain after action “${x.action}”.`,x.timestamp,{phase:1,control:'Immutable audit trail',confidence:99,evidence:[x.entity],negativeCase:`Audit event ${x.id} was stored with hash ${x.hash}, but the chain validation against previous hash ${x.prevHash} failed after “${x.action}”.`,expectedCondition:'Every audit event has a valid immutable hash chain.',actualCondition:`Hash ${x.hash} is invalid for ${x.id}.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id} • ${x.entity} • ${x.timestamp}`})));
  (db.sodEvents||[]).filter(x=>x.status==='Violation'||x.maker===x.checker).forEach(x=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('SEGREGATION_DUTIES','Critical','Access Control',x.reference,'Segregation of duties violation',`${x.maker} acted as both maker and checker for ${x.action}.`,'Access event',{phase:1,control:'Role & segregation of duties',confidence:98,evidence:[x.id],negativeCase:`User ${x.maker} created and also approved the same transaction action: ${x.action}.`,expectedCondition:'Maker and checker must be different authorized users.',actualCondition:`Maker = checker = ${x.maker}.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id} • ${x.reference}`})));
  (db.geofenceEvents||[]).filter(x=>x.status==='Outside'||Number(x.distance)>Number(x.radius)).forEach(x=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('GEOFENCE_CONTROL','High','Monitoring Shipment',x.fleetOrder,'Pickup or delivery outside geofence',`${x.type} event was ${x.distance} m from location while allowed radius is ${x.radius} m.`,x.timestamp,{phase:1,control:'Geofence pickup/delivery',confidence:96,evidence:[x.id],negativeCase:`The ${x.type.toLowerCase()} event for ${x.fleetOrder} was submitted ${x.distance} m from ${x.location}.`,expectedCondition:`Event location must be within ${x.radius} m of ${x.location}.`,actualCondition:`Recorded distance ${x.distance} m; status ${x.status}.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id} • ${x.fleetOrder} • ${x.timestamp}`})));
  // Source documents may be reused across multiple active shipment plans.
  // This condition is allowed and must not create a fraud alert or block Loading & Dispatch.
  const resourceUse={};activePlans.filter(p=>p.shipmentDate&&p.vehicle&&p.vehicle!=='-').forEach(p=>{const k=p.shipmentDate+'|'+p.vehicle;(resourceUse[k]=resourceUse[k]||[]).push(p.id)});Object.entries(resourceUse).filter(([,plans])=>plans.length>1).forEach(([key,plans])=>{const [date,vehicle]=key.split('|');alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('DOUBLE_BOOKING','High','Shipment Schedule',plans.join(' / '),'Vehicle double booking',`${vehicle} is assigned to ${plans.join(', ')} on ${date}.`,date,{phase:2,control:'Fraud rule engine',confidence:95,evidence:plans,negativeCase:`Vehicle ${vehicle} was allocated to multiple active plans on the same shipment date.`,expectedCondition:'One vehicle can only serve one overlapping active schedule.',actualCondition:`${plans.length} plans on ${date}: ${plans.join(', ')}.`,sourceRecord:`${vehicle} • ${date} • ${plans.join(' • ')}`}));});
  (db.plans||[]).forEach(p=>{const actual=Number(p.actualCost||0),planned=Number(p.plannedCost||0);if(actual&&planned&&actual>planned*1.2){const pct=Math.round((actual-planned)/planned*100);alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('COST_VARIANCE',pct>=40?'Critical':'High','Report / Cost',p.id,'Abnormal transport cost variance',`Actual cost is ${pct}% above planned cost (${fmtIDR(actual)} vs ${fmtIDR(planned)}).`,'Cost reconciliation',{phase:2,control:'Risk scoring',confidence:90,exposure:actual-planned,evidence:[p.id],negativeCase:`Shipment ${p.id} closed with actual transport cost materially above its approved plan.`,expectedCondition:`Actual cost must not exceed 120% of planned cost (${fmtIDR(planned*1.2)}).`,actualCondition:`Actual ${fmtIDR(actual)} versus planned ${fmtIDR(planned)}; variance +${pct}%.`,sourceRecord:`${p.id} • planned ${planned} • actual ${actual}`}));}(p.stops||[]).forEach(s=>{if((p.status==='Completed'||s.pod)&&s.status==='Successfully Delivered'&&(!s.signatureData||!s.podPhotoData||!s.podHash)){const missing=[!s.podPhotoData?'photo':'',!s.signatureData?'signature':'',!s.podHash?'evidence hash':''].filter(Boolean);alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('SECURE_POD','High','Driver Mobile',s.doc,'Secure POD validation failed',`Successful delivery is missing ${missing.join(', ')}.`,s.arrival||'Delivery completion',{phase:1,control:'Secure POD',confidence:94,evidence:[s.podPhotoName||'POD record'],planId:p.id,negativeCase:`Stop ${s.doc} was marked Successfully Delivered even though mandatory secure POD components were not completed.`,expectedCondition:'Successful delivery requires POD photo, receiver signature, and evidence hash.',actualCondition:`Missing: ${missing.join(', ')}.`,sourceRecord:`${p.id} • ${s.doc} • ${s.arrival||'completion'}`}));}});if(p.routeEdited)alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('MANUAL_ROUTE','Low','Shipment Planning',p.id,'Route manually overridden',`Auto-generated route was manually edited to ${p.route||'-'}.`,'Plan update',{phase:1,control:'Route deviation',confidence:65,evidence:[p.id],negativeCase:`The generated route for ${p.id} was manually replaced after planning.`,expectedCondition:'Shipment uses the approved system-generated route or records an approved exception.',actualCondition:`Manual route: ${p.route||'-'}; exception approval not recorded.`,sourceRecord:`${p.id} • routeEdited=true`}));});
  const proofUse={};(db.costRecords||[]).filter(c=>c.proof&&c.proof!=='-').forEach(c=>(proofUse[c.proof]=proofUse[c.proof]||[]).push(c.id));Object.entries(proofUse).filter(([,ids])=>ids.length>1).forEach(([proof,ids])=>{const fos=[...new Set(ids.map(id=>(db.costRecords||[]).find(c=>c.id===id)?.fleetOrder).filter(Boolean))];alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('DUPLICATE_PROOF','Critical','Cost Management',fos.join(' / '),'Duplicate expense proof',`${proof} is attached to ${ids.join(', ')}.`,'Expense scan',{phase:2,control:'Evidence management',confidence:97,evidence:ids,negativeCase:`The same receipt file ${proof} was uploaded against multiple expense records.`,expectedCondition:'Each expense record has a unique receipt or explicitly linked shared proof.',actualCondition:`Used by ${ids.length} records: ${ids.join(', ')}.`,sourceRecord:`${proof} • ${ids.join(' • ')}`}));});
  (db.costRecords||[]).forEach(c=>{if(['Approved','Posted','Paid'].includes(c.status)&&(!c.proof||c.proof==='-'))alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('MISSING_PROOF','High','Cost Management',c.fleetOrder||'PL/00003','Expense approved without proof',`${c.id} (${fmtIDR(c.amount)}) is ${c.status} without receipt evidence.`,'Expense approval',{phase:2,control:'Evidence management',confidence:96,exposure:Number(c.amount||0),evidence:[c.id],negativeCase:`Expense ${c.id} progressed to ${c.status} even though no receipt was attached.`,expectedCondition:'Approved, posted, or paid expense must have valid proof.',actualCondition:`Proof = ${c.proof||'-'}; status = ${c.status}; amount = ${fmtIDR(c.amount)}.`,sourceRecord:`${c.id} • ${c.fleetOrder||'-'}`}));});
  (db.fleetOrders||[]).forEach(fo=>{if(Number(fo.distancePlan)>0&&Number(fo.distanceActual)>Number(fo.distancePlan)*1.25){const pct=Math.round((fo.distanceActual-fo.distancePlan)/fo.distancePlan*100);alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('ROUTE_DEVIATION',pct>=60?'Critical':'High','Monitoring Shipment',fo.id,'Abnormal route deviation',`Actual distance is ${pct}% above plan (${fo.distanceActual} km vs ${fo.distancePlan} km).`,'GPS telemetry',{phase:1,control:'Route deviation',confidence:92,evidence:[fo.id],negativeCase:`Fleet Order ${fo.id} travelled materially farther than its approved planned distance.`,expectedCondition:`Actual distance must remain within 125% of ${fo.distancePlan} km (${Math.round(fo.distancePlan*1.25)} km).`,actualCondition:`Actual ${fo.distanceActual} km; variance +${pct}%.`,sourceRecord:`${fo.id} • ${fo.vehicle} • GPS telemetry`}));}const p=(db.plans||[]).find(x=>x.id===fo.planId);if(p){const expected={Confirm:['Draft','Planned'],Dijadwalkan:['Planned'],Loading:['Loading','Ready to Dispatch'],Dijalankan:['In Transit'],'OTW Tujuan':['In Transit'],Unloading:['Unloading'],Delivered:['Completed','Returning'],Failed:['Exception']}[fo.status]||[];if(expected.length&&!expected.includes(p.status))alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('STATUS_MISMATCH','Medium','Integration',fo.id,'Plan and Fleet Order status mismatch',`Fleet Order is ${fo.status}, while ${p.id} is ${p.status}.`,'Integration scan',{phase:2,control:'Fraud rule engine',confidence:84,evidence:[fo.id,p.id],negativeCase:`The integrated Fleet Order and its source Shipment Plan show different operational stages.`,expectedCondition:`When FO status is ${fo.status}, plan status must be ${expected.join(' or ')}.`,actualCondition:`${fo.id} = ${fo.status}; ${p.id} = ${p.status}.`,sourceRecord:`${fo.id} • ${p.id}`}));}});
  (db.gpsHealthEvents||[]).filter(x=>Number(x.offlineMinutes)>=30).forEach(x=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('GPS_OFFLINE',Number(x.offlineMinutes)>=60?'Critical':'High','Monitoring Shipment',x.fleetOrder,'GPS offline threshold exceeded',`${x.vehicle} has no GPS ping for ${x.offlineMinutes} minutes.` ,x.lastPing,{phase:1,control:'GPS offline alert',confidence:97,evidence:[x.id],negativeCase:`Vehicle ${x.vehicle} stopped sending GPS pings while ${x.fleetOrder} was active.`,expectedCondition:'GPS offline duration must stay below 30 minutes.',actualCondition:`Offline ${x.offlineMinutes} minutes; last ping ${x.lastPing}; status ${x.status}.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id} • ${x.fleetOrder}`})));
  Object.entries(db.driverStates||{}).forEach(([planId,st])=>{if(st.odometerStart!==undefined&&st.odometerEnd!==undefined&&Number(st.odometerEnd)<Number(st.odometerStart))alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('ODOMETER_ROLLBACK','Critical','Driver Mobile',planId,'Odometer rollback detected',`End odometer ${st.odometerEnd} km is below first odometer ${st.odometerStart} km.`,'Trip closure',{phase:1,control:'Immutable audit trail',confidence:99,evidence:[planId],negativeCase:`The trip was closed with a lower odometer value than its starting reading.`,expectedCondition:'End odometer must be equal to or greater than start odometer.',actualCondition:`Start ${st.odometerStart} km; end ${st.odometerEnd} km.`,sourceRecord:`${planId} • Driver Mobile state`}));if(st.fuelStart!==undefined&&st.fuelEnd!==undefined){const drop=Number(st.fuelStart)-Number(st.fuelEnd),fo=(db.fleetOrders||[]).find(x=>x.planId===planId),distance=Number(fo?.distancePlan||0);if(drop>45&&distance<120)alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('FUEL_ANOMALY','High','Driver Mobile',planId,'Fuel consumption anomaly',`Fuel decreased ${drop}% for ${distance||'unknown'} km.`, 'Trip closure',{phase:3,control:'Anomaly detection',confidence:82,evidence:[planId],negativeCase:`The reported fuel level dropped sharply during a relatively short planned trip.`,expectedCondition:'Fuel drop must be proportionate to trip distance and vehicle baseline.',actualCondition:`Fuel drop ${drop}% for ${distance||'unknown'} km.`,sourceRecord:`${planId} • ${fo?.id||'driver state'}`}));}});
  (db.fuelTransactions||[]).forEach(x=>{const v=(db.vehicles||[]).find(v=>v.plate===x.vehicle),cap=Number(v?.fuelCapacity||0);if(cap&&Number(x.liters)>cap)alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('FUEL_CAPACITY','Critical','Cost / Vehicle',x.documentRef||x.fleetOrder,'Fuel volume exceeds tank capacity',`${x.liters} L was recorded for ${x.vehicle}, exceeding configured ${cap} L capacity.`,x.timestamp,{phase:1,control:'Fuel capacity validation',confidence:99,exposure:Number(x.amount||0),evidence:[x.proof,x.documentRef||x.fleetOrder],negativeCase:`Fuel transaction ${x.id} records more liters than vehicle ${x.vehicle} can physically hold.`,expectedCondition:`Recorded liters must be ≤ configured tank capacity ${cap} L.`,actualCondition:`Recorded ${x.liters} L; excess ${Number(x.liters)-cap} L.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id} • ${x.vehicle} • ${x.proof}`}));});
  const invoiceGroups={};(db.carrierInvoices||[]).forEach(x=>{const k=[x.carrier,x.invoiceNo,Number(x.amount||0)].join('|');(invoiceGroups[k]=invoiceGroups[k]||[]).push(x)});Object.values(invoiceGroups).filter(xs=>xs.length>1).forEach(xs=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('DUPLICATE_INVOICE','Critical','Carrier Invoice',[...new Set(xs.map(x=>x.documentRef).filter(Boolean))].join(' / '),'Duplicate carrier invoice detected',`${xs[0].invoiceNo} for ${xs[0].carrier} and ${fmtIDR(xs[0].amount)} appears in ${xs.map(x=>x.id).join(', ')}.`,'Invoice validation',{phase:1,control:'Duplicate invoice detection',confidence:99,exposure:Number(xs[0].amount||0),recurrence:xs.length,evidence:[...new Set(xs.map(x=>x.documentRef).filter(Boolean))],negativeCase:`The same carrier invoice number, carrier, and amount were submitted in multiple invoice records.`,expectedCondition:'Carrier + invoice number + amount combination must be unique.',actualCondition:`${xs[0].invoiceNo} / ${xs[0].carrier} / ${fmtIDR(xs[0].amount)} appears ${xs.length} times.`,sourceRecord:xs.map(x=>x.id).join(' • ')})));
  (db.carrierVerification||[]).filter(x=>x.kyc!=='Verified'||!x.bankVerified||x.permitExpiry<todayISO()).forEach(x=>{const issues=[x.kyc!=='Verified'?`KYC ${x.kyc}`:'',!x.bankVerified?'bank not verified':'',x.permitExpiry<todayISO()?`permit expired ${x.permitExpiry}`:''].filter(Boolean);alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('CARRIER_VERIFICATION',x.risk==='High'?'Critical':'High','Carrier Master',x.reference,'Carrier verification incomplete',`${x.kyc}; permit expiry ${x.permitExpiry}; bank verified: ${x.bankVerified?'Yes':'No'}.`,'Daily verification',{phase:1,control:'Carrier verification',confidence:98,evidence:[x.reference],negativeCase:`Carrier ${x.carrier} is used or available for transport while mandatory onboarding checks are incomplete.`,expectedCondition:'KYC verified, permit valid, insurance valid, and bank account verified.',actualCondition:issues.join('; ')||'Verification incomplete.',sourceRecord:`Carrier verification • ${x.carrier} • ${x.reference}`}));});
  (db.bankChangeRequests||[]).filter(x=>x.status==='Activated'&&(x.approvers||[]).length<Number(x.requiredApprovals||2)).forEach(x=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('BANK_CHANGE_APPROVAL','Critical','Carrier Contract',x.reference,'Bank account activated without dual approval',`${x.carrier} changed payment account to ${x.newAccount} with ${(x.approvers||[]).length}/${x.requiredApprovals} approvals.` ,x.requestedAt,{phase:1,control:'Bank account change approval',confidence:99,exposure:1850000,evidence:[x.reference,'Dual approval record'],negativeCase:`Payment account ${x.newAccount} for ${x.carrier} was activated before the required approval count was completed.`,expectedCondition:`At least ${x.requiredApprovals} independent approvals before activation.`,actualCondition:`${(x.approvers||[]).length}/${x.requiredApprovals} approvals; status ${x.status}.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id} • ${x.carrier} • ${x.requestedAt}`})));
  (db.fraudBlacklist||[]).filter(x=>x.status==='Active').forEach(x=>{const bankUse=(db.bankChangeRequests||[]).find(r=>r.newAccount===x.entity&&r.status==='Activated'),planUse=(db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.supplier===x.entity||p.driver===x.entity),used=bankUse||planUse;if(used)alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('BLACKLIST_MATCH','Critical','Fraud Control Center',x.reference,'Blacklisted entity used in active process',`${x.entityType} ${x.entity} is active in a transaction while blacklist status is ${x.status}.`,'Real-time blacklist match',{phase:2,control:'Blacklist',confidence:99,evidence:[x.reference],negativeCase:`An entity marked Active in the blacklist was found in an active payment, carrier, driver, or shipment process.`,expectedCondition:'Active blacklisted entities must be blocked from operational and payment transactions.',actualCondition:`${x.entityType} ${x.entity} used in ${bankUse?.id||planUse?.id||x.reference}.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id} • ${x.reference}`}));});
  (db.syncLogs||[]).filter(x=>x.status==='Failed'||Number(x.retry)>=2).forEach(x=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert('SYNC_TAMPERING','Medium','Integration',fraudDocumentReference(x.ref,x),'Repeated failed synchronization',`${x.event} is ${x.status} with ${x.retry} retries: ${x.message}`,'Integration monitor',{phase:2,control:'Alert escalation',confidence:76,evidence:[fraudDocumentReference(x.ref,x)],negativeCase:`Integration event ${x.event} repeatedly failed or retried for the same business reference.`,expectedCondition:'Synchronization completes successfully without repeated retries.',actualCondition:`Status ${x.status}; retry ${x.retry}; message: ${x.message}.`,sourceRecord:`${x.id||x.time} • ${fraudDocumentReference(x.ref,x)}`})));
  (db.advancedFraudSignals||[]).forEach(x=>alerts.push(makeFraudAlert(x.code,x.risk,'Advanced Analytics',x.reference,x.title,x.reason,'Model scan',{phase:3,control:(FRAUD_STAGE_CONTROLS[3].find(c=>c[0]===x.code)||[])[1]||x.code,confidence:x.confidence,evidence:x.features||[],recurrence:x.code==='CROSS_SHIPMENT'?3:1,negativeCase:x.negativeCase,expectedCondition:x.expectedCondition,actualCondition:x.actualCondition,sourceRecord:x.sourceRecord||x.id})));
  return alerts.sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score||fraudSeverityScore(b.risk)-fraudSeverityScore(a.risk));
}
function fraudStatusBadge(s){return statusBadge(s==='Under Review'?'Pending':s==='Escalated'?'Exception':s==='Cleared'?'Completed':'Draft').replace(/>[^<]+<\/span>/,`>${esc(s)}</span>`);}
function fraudTab(btn,id){document.querySelectorAll('[data-fraud-tab]').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));btn?.classList.add('active');document.querySelectorAll('.fraud-panel').forEach(x=>x.classList.toggle('active',x.id==='fraud-panel-'+id));if(id==='alerts')renderFraudAlertsTable();}
function stageMaturity(phase){const cs=FRAUD_STAGE_CONTROLS[phase]||[],live=cs.filter(x=>x[3]==='live').length,pilot=cs.filter(x=>x[3]==='pilot').length;return{live,pilot,total:cs.length,pct:Math.round((live+pilot*.5)/Math.max(1,cs.length)*100)};}
function renderRoadmap(){const el=document.getElementById('fraudRoadmap');if(!el)return;const names={1:['Fundamental Control','Prevention & integrity'],2:['Fraud Control Center','Investigation & response'],3:['Advanced Analytics','Pattern & predictive signals']};el.innerHTML=[1,2,3].map(p=>{const m=stageMaturity(p),items=FRAUD_STAGE_CONTROLS[p];return `<div class="stage-card"><div class="stage-card-head"><div class="stage-number">${p}</div><div><b>Tahap ${p} — ${names[p][0]}</b><p>${names[p][1]}</p></div><div class="stage-progress"><strong>${m.pct}%</strong><span>readiness</span></div></div><div class="stage-card-body"><div class="stage-control-list">${items.map(x=>`<div class="stage-control-row"><span class="control-state ${x[3]}">${x[3]==='live'?'✓':x[3]==='pilot'?'◐':'○'}</span><div><b>${esc(x[1])}</b><p>${esc(x[2])}</p></div></div>`).join('')}</div></div></div>`}).join('');}
function renderFundamentalControls(alerts){const cards=document.getElementById('fundamentalControlCards');if(cards)cards.innerHTML=FRAUD_STAGE_CONTROLS[1].map((x,i)=>{const matches=alerts.filter(a=>a.phase===1&&a.control===x[1]),state=x[3],metric=controlMetric(x[0]);return `<div class="control-card" style="--control-accent:${matches.some(a=>a.risk==='Critical')?'var(--red)':matches.length?'var(--orange)':'var(--green)'}"><div class="control-card-head"><div class="control-icon">${['▣','♙','◎','✓','⌁','◉','⛽','▤','◆','₿'][i]||'✓'}</div><div><h3>${esc(x[1])}</h3><p>${esc(x[2])}</p></div><div class="control-meta"><b>${metric}</b><span>${matches.length} alert(s)</span></div></div><div class="control-card-foot"><span class="maturity-pill maturity-${state}">${state==='live'?'Live':state==='pilot'?'Pilot':'Planned'}</span><span class="spacer"></span><span>${matches.length?'Needs review':'Control passed'}</span></div></div>`}).join('');
  const at=document.getElementById('auditTrailTbody');if(at)at.innerHTML=(db.auditTrail||[]).map(x=>`<tr><td class="mono">${x.id}</td><td>${fraudReferenceHTML(x.entity)}</td><td>${esc(x.action)}</td><td>${esc(x.user)}<div class="muted">${esc(x.role)}</div></td><td>${esc(x.timestamp)}</td><td>${x.validHash?statusBadge('Valid'):statusBadge('Failed')}</td></tr>`).join('');
  const q=document.getElementById('fundamentalQueue');if(q){const items=[...(db.sodEvents||[]).map(x=>({title:`SoD • ${x.reference}`,desc:`${x.maker} → ${x.checker} • ${x.action}`,status:x.status,risk:x.status==='Violation'?'Critical':'Low'})),...(db.carrierVerification||[]).map(x=>({title:`Carrier • ${x.carrier}`,desc:`${x.kyc} • Permit ${x.permitExpiry} • Bank ${x.bankVerified?'verified':'not verified'}`,status:x.risk==='High'?'Review':'Verified',risk:x.risk})),...(db.bankChangeRequests||[]).map(x=>({title:`Bank Change • ${x.carrier}`,desc:`${x.oldAccount} → ${x.newAccount} • ${(x.approvers||[]).length}/${x.requiredApprovals} approvals`,status:x.status,risk:x.status==='Activated'&&(x.approvers||[]).length<x.requiredApprovals?'Critical':'Low'}))];q.innerHTML=items.map(x=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><b>${esc(x.title)}</b><span class="right">${statusBadge(x.status==='Violation'?'Failed':x.status==='Verified'?'Valid':x.status)}</span></div><p>${esc(x.desc)}</p></div>`).join('');}}
function controlMetric(code){return({IMMUTABLE_AUDIT:(db.auditTrail||[]).filter(x=>x.validHash).length+'/'+(db.auditTrail||[]).length,SEGREGATION_DUTIES:(db.sodEvents||[]).filter(x=>x.status==='Passed').length+'/'+(db.sodEvents||[]).length,GEOFENCE_CONTROL:(db.geofenceEvents||[]).filter(x=>x.status==='Inside').length+'/'+(db.geofenceEvents||[]).length,SECURE_POD:(db.plans||[]).flatMap(p=>p.stops||[]).filter(s=>s.pod&&s.signatureData&&s.podPhotoData).length+' secure',ROUTE_DEVIATION:(db.fleetOrders||[]).length+' trips',GPS_OFFLINE:(db.gpsHealthEvents||[]).filter(x=>x.offlineMinutes<30).length+'/'+(db.gpsHealthEvents||[]).length,FUEL_CAPACITY:(db.fuelTransactions||[]).length+' tx',DUPLICATE_INVOICE:(db.carrierInvoices||[]).length+' invoice',CARRIER_VERIFICATION:(db.carrierVerification||[]).filter(x=>x.kyc==='Verified'&&x.bankVerified).length+'/'+(db.carrierVerification||[]).length,BANK_CHANGE_APPROVAL:(db.bankChangeRequests||[]).filter(x=>(x.approvers||[]).length>=x.requiredApprovals).length+'/'+(db.bankChangeRequests||[]).length})[code]||'Active';}
function renderFraudCenter(alerts){const rules=document.getElementById('fraudRuleEngine');if(rules)rules.innerHTML=(db.fraudRules||[]).filter(x=>x.phase<=2).map(x=>{const n=alerts.filter(a=>a.control===x.name||a.type===x.code).length;return `<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><b>${x.id} • ${esc(x.name)}</b><span class="right">${x.enabled?statusBadge('Active'):statusBadge('Inactive')}</span></div><p>${esc(x.description)} • ${esc(x.threshold)} • Last run ${esc(x.lastRun)}</p><div class="risk-meter"><span style="width:${Math.min(100,n*18)}%;background:${n?'var(--orange)':'var(--green)'}"></span></div></div>`}).join('');const rc=document.getElementById('ruleEngineCount');if(rc)rc.textContent=(db.fraudRules||[]).filter(x=>x.enabled).length+' active rules';
  const cases=document.getElementById('fraudCaseList');if(cases)cases.innerHTML=(db.fraudCases||[]).map(c=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><b>${c.id} • ${esc(c.title)}</b><div class="right"><strong>${esc(c.risk)}</strong><span>${esc(c.status)}</span></div></div><p>${fraudReferenceHTML(c.reference)} • Owner: ${esc(c.owner)} • Due ${esc(c.dueAt)}</p><div class="case-status-flow"><span class="done">Triage</span><span class="${['Investigation','Decision','Closed'].includes(c.status)?'done':'current'}">Assign</span><span class="${c.status==='Investigation'?'current':['Decision','Closed'].includes(c.status)?'done':''}">Investigate</span><span class="${c.status==='Decision'?'current':c.status==='Closed'?'done':''}">Decision</span><span class="${c.status==='Closed'?'done':''}">Close</span></div></div>`).join('');const cc=document.getElementById('fraudCaseCount');if(cc)cc.textContent=(db.fraudCases||[]).filter(c=>c.status!=='Closed').length+' open cases';
  const bl=document.getElementById('fraudBlacklist');if(bl)bl.innerHTML=(db.fraudBlacklist||[]).map(x=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><b>${esc(x.entityType)} • ${esc(x.entity)}</b><span class="blacklist-badge">${esc(x.status)}</span></div><p>${fraudReferenceHTML(x.reference)} • ${esc(x.reason)} • Added ${esc(x.addedAt)}</p></div>`).join('');
  const ev=document.getElementById('fraudEvidence');if(ev)ev.innerHTML=(db.fraudEvidence||[]).map(x=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><b>${x.id} • ${esc(x.type)}</b><div class="right"><strong>${esc(x.caseId)}</strong><span>${esc(x.capturedAt)}</span></div></div><p>${fraudReferenceHTML(x.reference)} • ${esc(x.file)} • ${esc(x.source)} • Custodian: ${esc(x.custodian)}</p><span class="evidence-chip">🔒 ${esc(x.hash)}</span></div>`).join('');}
function renderAdvancedAnalytics(alerts){const tiles=document.getElementById('advancedAnalyticsTiles');if(tiles)tiles.innerHTML=FRAUD_STAGE_CONTROLS[3].map((x,i)=>{const sigs=(db.advancedFraudSignals||[]).filter(s=>s.code===x[0]),max=Math.max(0,...sigs.map(s=>s.confidence));return `<div class="advanced-tile"><div class="signal-head"><span class="signal-icon">${['≈','▧','◉','⌘','⇄','⚠','⧉','Σ'][i]}</span><b>${esc(x[1])}</b></div><p>${esc(x[2])}</p><div class="confidence">${max||0}% <small>max confidence</small></div><div class="risk-meter"><span style="width:${max||0}%;background:var(--purple)"></span></div></div>`}).join('');
  const bs=document.getElementById('behaviourSignals');if(bs)bs.innerHTML=(db.behaviourProfiles||[]).map(x=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><b>${esc(x.type)} • ${esc(x.entity)}</b><div class="right"><strong>${x.currentScore}/100</strong><span>${esc(x.trend)}</span></div></div><p>${fraudReferenceHTML(x.reference)} • Baseline: ${esc(x.baseline)} • ${x.signals} active signal(s)</p><div class="risk-meter"><span style="width:${x.currentScore}%;background:${x.currentScore>=80?'var(--red)':x.currentScore>=60?'var(--orange)':'var(--green)'}"></span></div></div>`).join('');
  const ns=document.getElementById('carrierNetworkSignals');if(ns)ns.innerHTML=(db.carrierNetworkLinks||[]).map(x=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><b>${esc(x.source)} → ${esc(x.target)}</b><div class="right"><strong>${esc(x.risk)}</strong><span>network link</span></div></div><p>${fraudReferenceHTML(x.reference)} • ${esc(x.relation)}</p></div>`).join('');}
function renderFraudAlertsTable(){const alerts=collectFraudAlerts(),q=(document.getElementById('fraudSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),pf=document.getElementById('fraudPhaseFilter')?.value||'',rf=document.getElementById('fraudRiskFilter')?.value||'',sf=document.getElementById('fraudStatusFilter')?.value||'',rows=alerts.filter(a=>(!pf||String(a.phase)===pf)&&(!rf||a.risk===rf)&&(!sf||a.status===sf)&&JSON.stringify(a).toLowerCase().includes(q)),tb=document.getElementById('fraudTbody');if(!tb)return;tb.innerHTML=rows.map(a=>`<tr><td><span class="fraud-score ${a.risk.toLowerCase()}">${a.score}</span><div class="muted">${a.risk}</div></td><td><span class="phase-chip phase-${a.phase}">Tahap ${a.phase}</span><div style="margin-top:5px"><b>${esc(a.control)}</b></div><div class="muted">${esc(a.module)}</div></td><td><b>${esc(a.title)}</b><div class="muted">${esc(a.type)} • Confidence ${a.confidence}%</div></td><td class="mono">${fraudReferenceHTML(a.ref)}</td><td>${fraudDetectionReasonHTML(a)}</td><td>${(a.evidence||[]).slice(0,3).map(e=>`<span class="evidence-chip">${esc(e)}</span>`).join('')||'<span class="muted">No attachment</span>'}</td><td>${fraudStatusBadge(a.status)}${a.owner?`<div class="muted">${esc(a.owner)}</div>`:''}</td><td><button class="action-dot" onclick="openFraudActionMenu(event,'${encodeURIComponent(a.key)}')">⋮</button></td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="8" class="empty">No risk alert found for this filter.</td></tr>';}
function renderAntiFraud(){ensureAntiFraudData();const alerts=collectFraudAlerts(),open=alerts.filter(a=>a.status!=='Cleared'),nav=document.getElementById('fraudNavCount');if(nav)nav.textContent=open.length;const k=document.getElementById('fraudKpis');if(!k)return;const cases=(db.fraudCases||[]).filter(c=>c.status!=='Closed'),nowKey=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),overdue=cases.filter(c=>c.dueAt&&c.dueAt<nowKey).length;k.innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Open Alerts',v:open.length,f:'Across 3 implementation stages',a:'var(--red)'},{l:'Critical Risk',v:open.filter(a=>a.risk==='Critical').length,f:'Immediate escalation',a:'var(--red)'},{l:'Open Cases',v:cases.length,f:`${overdue} past SLA`,a:'var(--orange)'},{l:'Control Coverage',v:Math.round(Object.values(FRAUD_STAGE_CONTROLS).flat().filter(x=>x[3]!=='planned').length/Object.values(FRAUD_STAGE_CONTROLS).flat().length*100)+'%',f:'Live and pilot controls',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Evidence Secured',v:(db.fraudEvidence||[]).length,f:'Hashed chain of custody',a:'var(--green)'}]);
  ['1','2','3'].forEach(p=>{const el=document.getElementById('stage'+p+'AlertCount');if(el)el.textContent=open.filter(a=>String(a.phase)===p).length});const all=document.getElementById('allFraudAlertCount');if(all)all.textContent=open.length;const metrics=document.getElementById('fraudRiskMetrics');if(metrics)metrics.innerHTML=['Critical','High','Medium','Low'].map(r=>`<div class="risk-tile"><b>${open.filter(a=>a.risk===r).length}</b><span>${r} alerts</span></div>`).join('');const mm=document.getElementById('fraudMaturityMetrics');if(mm)mm.innerHTML=[1,2,3].map(p=>{const m=stageMaturity(p);return `<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Tahap ${p}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${m.pct}%;background:${p===1?'var(--green)':p===2?'var(--cyan-dark)':'var(--purple)'}"></span></div><b>${m.pct}%</b></div>`}).join('');const top=document.getElementById('topFraudSignals');if(top)top.innerHTML=open.slice(0,5).map(a=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><span class="fraud-score ${a.risk.toLowerCase()}" style="width:32px;height:32px">${a.score}</span><div><b>${esc(a.title)}</b><p>Tahap ${a.phase} • ${fraudReferenceHTML(a.ref)} • ${esc(a.control)}</p></div><div class="right"><strong>${a.confidence}%</strong><span>confidence</span></div></div></div>`).join('');renderRoadmap();renderFundamentalControls(alerts);renderFraudCenter(alerts);renderAdvancedAnalytics(alerts);renderFraudAlertsTable();}
function runFraudDetection(){ensureAntiFraudData();(db.fraudRules||[]).forEach(r=>r.lastRun=new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16));saveDB();renderAntiFraud();toast('Fraud detection completed across all three stages');}
function fraudAlertByKey(encoded){const key=decodeURIComponent(encoded);return collectFraudAlerts().find(a=>a.key===key);}
function openFraudActionMenu(ev,encoded){ev.stopPropagation();closeActionMenu();const a=fraudAlertByKey(encoded);if(!a)return;const menu=document.createElement('div');menu.className='action-popover';menu.id='globalActionMenu';menu.innerHTML=`<button onclick="viewFraudAlert('${encoded}')">View Detail</button><button onclick="createFraudCase('${encoded}')">Create / Open Case</button><button onclick="setFraudStatus('${encoded}','Under Review')">Mark Under Review</button><button onclick="setFraudStatus('${encoded}','Escalated')">Escalate Alert</button><button onclick="setFraudStatus('${encoded}','Cleared')">Clear Alert</button>`;document.body.appendChild(menu);const r=ev.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();menu.style.left=Math.min(r.left,window.innerWidth-210)+'px';menu.style.top=Math.min(r.bottom+5,window.innerHeight-menu.offsetHeight-10)+'px';}
function viewFraudAlert(encoded){closeActionMenu();const a=fraudAlertByKey(encoded);if(!a)return;openModal('Risk Alert Detail',`<div class="notice ${a.risk==='Critical'||a.risk==='High'?'danger':'warn'}"><b>${esc(a.risk)} Risk • Score ${a.score}/100 • ${esc(a.title)}</b><br>${esc(a.reason)}</div><div class="negative-case-detail"><h4>Negative Case / Trigger Data</h4><p>${esc(a.negativeCase||a.reason)}</p><div class="condition-compare" style="margin-top:8px"><div class="condition-box"><small>Expected</small><span>${esc(a.expectedCondition||'-')}</span></div><div class="condition-box actual"><small>Actual</small><span>${esc(a.actualCondition||a.reason)}</span></div></div><div class="case-source">Source: ${esc(a.sourceRecord||a.source||a.ref)}</div></div><div class="alert-detail"><div><span>Implementation Stage</span><b>Tahap ${a.phase}</b></div><div><span>Control</span><b>${esc(a.control)}</b></div><div><span>Module / Reference</span><div><b>${esc(a.module)}</b><br>${fraudReferenceHTML(a.ref)}</div></div><div><span>Confidence / Exposure</span><b>${a.confidence}% • ${fmtIDR(a.exposure||0)}</b></div><div><span>Review Status</span><b>${esc(a.status)}</b></div><div><span>Detected</span><b>${esc(a.detected)}</b></div></div><div class="score-breakdown"><div>Severity<b>${fraudSeverityScore(a.risk)}</b></div><div>Confidence<b>${a.confidence}%</b></div><div>Recurrence<b>${a.recurrence||0}</b></div><div>Final Score<b>${a.score}</b></div></div><div class="section-title">Evidence</div><div>${(a.evidence||[]).map(e=>`<span class="evidence-chip">🔒 ${esc(e)}</span>`).join('')||'<span class="muted">No evidence attachment.</span>'}</div><div class="field" style="margin-top:14px"><label>Investigation Note</label><textarea class="textarea" id="fraudNote">${esc(a.note||'')}</textarea></div><div class="field" style="margin-top:10px"><label>Owner / Reviewer</label><input class="input" id="fraudOwner" value="${esc(a.owner||'Transport Control')}"/></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button><button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="createFraudCase('${encoded}')">Create Case</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveFraudReview('${encoded}')">Save Review</button>`);}
function saveFraudReview(encoded){const a=fraudAlertByKey(encoded);if(!a)return;const s=fraudReviewStore();s[a.key]={...(s[a.key]||{}),note:document.getElementById('fraudNote')?.value||'',owner:document.getElementById('fraudOwner')?.value||'',status:s[a.key]?.status||'Under Review',reviewedAt:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)};saveDB();closeModal();renderAntiFraud();toast('Investigation review saved');}
function setFraudStatus(encoded,status){closeActionMenu();const a=fraudAlertByKey(encoded);if(!a)return;const s=fraudReviewStore();s[a.key]={...(s[a.key]||{}),status,owner:s[a.key]?.owner||'Transport Control',reviewedAt:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)};saveDB();renderAntiFraud();toast('Alert status updated to '+status);}
function createFraudCase(encoded){closeActionMenu();const a=fraudAlertByKey(encoded);if(!a)return;let c=(db.fraudCases||[]).find(c=>(c.alertKeys||[]).includes(a.key));if(!c){const seq=Math.max(0,...(db.fraudCases||[]).map(x=>Number(String(x.id).match(/\d+/)?.[0]||0)))+1;c={id:'CASE-'+String(seq).padStart(4,'0'),title:a.title,alertTypes:[a.type],alertKeys:[a.key],risk:a.risk,owner:a.owner||'Fraud Analyst',status:'Triage',openedAt:new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),slaHours:a.risk==='Critical'?4:a.risk==='High'?8:24,dueAt:'',reference:a.ref};db.fraudCases.push(c);const s=fraudReviewStore();s[a.key]={...(s[a.key]||{}),status:'Under Review',owner:c.owner,caseId:c.id};saveDB();}closeModal();renderAntiFraud();toast(`${c.id} is ready for investigation`);}
function downloadFraudAlerts(){const data=collectFraudAlerts(),head=['Score','Risk','Stage','Control','Type','Module','Reference','Alert','Negative Case','Expected Condition','Actual Condition','Detection Reason','Source Record','Confidence','Exposure','Evidence','Review Status'];downloadCSV([head,...data.map(a=>[a.score,a.risk,a.phase,a.control,a.type,a.module,a.ref,a.title,a.negativeCase,a.expectedCondition,a.actualCondition,a.reason,a.sourceRecord,a.confidence,a.exposure,(a.evidence||[]).join(' | '),a.status])],'tms-anti-fraud-alerts.csv');}
function downloadFraudControlData(){const rows=[['Dataset','ID / Entity','Type / Control','Status / Score','Description'],...(db.auditTrail||[]).map(x=>['Audit Trail',x.id,x.entity,x.validHash?'Valid':'Integrity Failed',x.action]),...(db.fraudRules||[]).map(x=>['Rule Engine',x.id,`Tahap ${x.phase} - ${x.name}`,x.enabled?'Active':'Inactive',x.description]),...(db.fraudCases||[]).map(x=>['Case',x.id,x.reference,x.status,x.title]),...(db.fraudBlacklist||[]).map(x=>['Blacklist',x.id,x.entity,x.status,x.reason]),...(db.fraudEvidence||[]).map(x=>['Evidence',x.id,x.type,x.caseId,`${x.file} • ${x.hash}`]),...(db.advancedFraudSignals||[]).map(x=>['Advanced Signal',x.id,x.code,x.confidence,x.reason])];downloadCSV(rows,'tms-risk-control-data.csv');}

/* Data-driven Overview and Report for the integrated database */
function renderDashboard(){
  const plans=db.plans||[],vehicles=db.vehicles||[],documents=db.documents||[];
  const active=plans.filter(p=>!['Completed','Draft'].includes(p.status)).length,planned=plans.filter(p=>p.status==='Planned').length,intransit=plans.filter(p=>p.status==='In Transit').length,available=vehicles.filter(v=>v.status==='Available').length,completion=plans.filter(p=>p.status==='Completed').length;
  const k=document.getElementById('dashboardKpis');if(!k)return;k.innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Active Shipments',v:active,f:'Planned to returning',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Need Planning',v:documents.filter(d=>d.status==='Need Planning').length,f:'DO / STO ready',a:'var(--orange)'},{l:'In Transit',v:intransit,f:'Live monitored',a:'var(--purple)'},{l:'Available Vehicles',v:available,f:`of ${vehicles.length} vehicles`,a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Completed Trips',v:completion,f:'Closed shipment plans',a:'var(--cyan-dark)'}]);
  const total=Math.max(1,plans.length),sm=document.getElementById('statusMetrics');if(sm)sm.innerHTML=[['Planned',planned,'var(--blue)'],['Loading',plans.filter(p=>['Loading','Ready to Dispatch'].includes(p.status)).length,'var(--orange)'],['In Transit',intransit,'var(--purple)'],['Completed',completion,'var(--green)']].map(x=>`<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">${x[0]}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${x[1]/total*100}%;background:${x[2]}"></span></div><b>${x[1]}</b></div>`).join('');
  const validDates=plans.map(p=>p.shipmentDate).filter(Boolean).sort(),anchor=validDates.at(-1)||todayISO(),start=addDays(anchor,-6),daily=Array.from({length:7},(_,i)=>addDays(start,i)),counts=daily.map(d=>plans.filter(p=>p.shipmentDate===d).length),max=Math.max(1,...counts),bars=document.getElementById('deliveryBars');if(bars)bars.innerHTML=daily.map((d,i)=>`<div class="bar" title="${d}: ${counts[i]} shipment" style="height:${Math.max(8,counts[i]/max*105)}px"><span>${new Date(d+'T00:00:00').toLocaleDateString('en-US',{weekday:'short'})}</span></div>`).join('');
  const fm=document.getElementById('fleetMetrics');if(fm)fm.innerHTML=['Available','Reserved','Loading','In Transit','Maintenance'].map(st=>{const n=vehicles.filter(v=>v.status===st).length;return `<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">${st}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${n/Math.max(1,vehicles.length)*100}%;background:${st==='Available'?'var(--green)':st==='Maintenance'?'var(--red)':'var(--cyan-dark)'}"></span></div><b>${n}</b></div>`}).join('');
  const up=document.getElementById('upcomingList');if(up)up.innerHTML=plans.filter(p=>['Planned','Loading','Ready to Dispatch'].includes(p.status)).sort((a,b)=>(a.shipmentDate||'').localeCompare(b.shipmentDate||'')).slice(0,5).map(p=>`<div class="ship-item" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')"><div class="top"><b>${p.id}</b>${statusBadge(p.status)}<span class="age">${p.shipmentDate}</span></div><div class="meta">${esc(p.destination)} • ${esc(p.source==='Fleet Company'?p.vehicle:p.supplier)}</div></div>`).join('')||'<div class="empty">No upcoming shipment.</div>';
}
function reportCarrierRows(){
  const groups={};(db.plans||[]).forEach(p=>{const name=p.source==='Fleet Company'?(p.supplier||'Internal Fleet'):(p.supplier||'Expedition');const g=groups[name]||(groups[name]={stops:0,success:0});(p.stops||[]).forEach(s=>{g.stops++;if(s.status==='Successfully Delivered')g.success++;});});return Object.entries(groups).map(([name,g])=>({name,pct:g.stops?Math.round(g.success/g.stops*100):0,stops:g.stops})).sort((a,b)=>b.pct-a.pct);
}
function renderReport(){
  const plans=db.plans||[],completed=plans.filter(p=>p.status==='Completed'),stops=completed.flatMap(p=>(p.stops||[]).map(s=>({s,p}))),success=stops.filter(x=>x.s.status==='Successfully Delivered').length,firstAttempt=stops.filter(x=>!x.s.deliveryReason).length,epod=stops.filter(x=>x.s.pod&&x.s.signatureData&&x.s.podPhotoData).length,onTime=stops.filter(x=>x.s.arrival&&x.p.eta&&String(x.s.arrival).slice(0,10)<=x.p.eta).length;
  const plannedCost=plans.reduce((a,p)=>a+Number(p.plannedCost||0),0),actualCost=plans.reduce((a,p)=>a+Number(p.actualCost||p.plannedCost||0),0),variancePct=plannedCost?Math.round((actualCost-plannedCost)/plannedCost*1000)/10:0;
  const k=document.getElementById('reportKpis');if(!k)return;k.innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'On-Time Delivery',v:(stops.length?Math.round(onTime/stops.length*100):0)+'%',f:`${onTime}/${stops.length} completed stops`,a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Delivery Success',v:(stops.length?Math.round(success/stops.length*100):0)+'%',f:`${success}/${stops.length} stops`,a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'First Attempt Rate',v:(stops.length?Math.round(firstAttempt/stops.length*100):0)+'%',f:'Without unsuccessful reason',a:'var(--cyan-dark)'},{l:'ePOD Completion',v:(stops.length?Math.round(epod/stops.length*100):0)+'%',f:'Photo and receiver signature',a:'var(--purple)'},{l:'Cost Variance',v:(variancePct>=0?'+':'')+variancePct+'%',f:'Actual / forecast vs planned',a:variancePct>10?'var(--red)':'var(--orange)'}]);
  const cp=document.getElementById('carrierPerformance'),rows=reportCarrierRows();if(cp)cp.innerHTML=rows.map((x,i)=>`<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">${esc(x.name)}</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${x.pct}%;background:${x.pct>=90?'var(--green)':x.pct>=75?'var(--cyan-dark)':'var(--orange)'}"></span></div><b>${x.pct}%</b></div>`).join('')||'<div class="empty">No carrier performance data.</div>';
  const cost=document.getElementById('costPerformance');if(cost)cost.innerHTML=`<div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Planned Cost</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${plannedCost/Math.max(1,actualCost,plannedCost)*100}%"></span></div><b style="width:120px">${fmtIDR(plannedCost)}</b></div><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Actual / Forecast</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${actualCost/Math.max(1,actualCost,plannedCost)*100}%;background:${actualCost>plannedCost?'var(--orange)':'var(--green)'}"></span></div><b style="width:120px">${fmtIDR(actualCost)}</b></div><div class="notice ${actualCost>plannedCost?'warn':''}">Variance ${fmtIDR(actualCost-plannedCost)} • calculated from synchronized shipment and expense data.</div>`;
  renderReportTable();
}

const integratedGoPageBase=goPage;goPage=function(p){integratedGoPageBase(p);if(p==='dashboard')renderDashboard();if(p==='report')renderReport();if(p==='integration')renderIntegration();if(p==='mapping')renderMapping();if(p==='fleet-order')renderFleetOrders();if(p==='cost')renderCostManagement();location.hash=p;};


/* ===== Shared Risk Control Runtime V5 ===== */
const RC_VERSION='5.0';
function rcNow(){return new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)}
function rcToday(){return typeof todayISO==='function'?todayISO():new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}
function rcDateExpired(v){return !!v&&String(v)<rcToday()}
function rcSeverityRank(v){return ({Low:1,Medium:2,High:3,Critical:4})[v]||0}
function rcSeverityClass(v){return String(v||'Low').toLowerCase()}
function rcScore(severity='Medium',confidence=70,exposure=0,recurrence=1){const s=({Low:20,Medium:45,High:75,Critical:95})[severity]||45,e=Math.min(100,Math.round(Number(exposure||0)/10000000*100));return Math.min(100,Math.round(s*.4+Number(confidence||0)*.3+e*.15+Math.min(100,Number(recurrence||0)*20)*.15))}
function rcEnsureData(){
 db.riskEvents=Array.isArray(db.riskEvents)?db.riskEvents:[];db.approvalRequests=Array.isArray(db.approvalRequests)?db.approvalRequests:[];db.controlAudit=Array.isArray(db.controlAudit)?db.controlAudit:[];db.dispatchControls=db.dispatchControls||{};
 (db.hubs||[]).forEach((x,i)=>Object.assign(x,{geofenceRadius:Number(x.geofenceRadius||150),verificationStatus:x.verificationStatus||'Verified',highRiskLocation:x.highRiskLocation||'No',authorizedGate:x.authorizedGate||'Gate '+(i+1)}));
 (db.carriers||[]).forEach((x,i)=>Object.assign(x,{kycStatus:x.kycStatus||(String(x.name).includes('Trans Kargo')?'Pending Review':'Verified'),permitExpiry:x.permitExpiry||(i===2?'2026-06-20':'2027-12-31'),insuranceExpiry:x.insuranceExpiry||(i===2?'2026-07-10':'2027-12-31'),insuranceCoverage:Number(x.insuranceCoverage||1000000000),bankVerificationStatus:x.bankVerificationStatus||(i===2?'Pending Approval':'Verified'),riskStatus:x.riskStatus||(i===2?'High':'Low'),officialEmail:x.officialEmail||('ops@'+String(x.name||'carrier').toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g,'')+'.co.id')}));
 (db.contracts||[]).forEach((x,i)=>Object.assign(x,{approvalStatus:x.approvalStatus||'Approved',subcontractingAllowed:x.subcontractingAllowed||'No',liabilityLimit:Number(x.liabilityLimit||1000000000),podRequirement:x.podRequirement||'Photo + Signature + OTP',contractVersion:x.contractVersion||'v1.'+(i+1)}));
 (db.vehicles||[]).forEach((x,i)=>Object.assign(x,{vin:x.vin||('VIN-'+String(i+1).padStart(6,'0')),engineNumber:x.engineNumber||('ENG-'+String(i+1).padStart(6,'0')),gpsDeviceId:x.gpsDeviceId||('GPS-'+String(i+1).padStart(4,'0')),fuelType:x.fuelType||'Diesel',tankCapacity:Number(x.tankCapacity||80),odometer:Number(x.odometer||40000+i*12000),identityVerification:x.identityVerification||'Verified',riskStatus:x.riskStatus||'Low'}));
 (db.maintenanceTasks||[]).forEach((x,i)=>Object.assign(x,{vendor:x.vendor||'Authorized Workshop',workOrderNo:x.workOrderNo||('WO-'+String(i+1).padStart(5,'0')),invoiceNo:x.invoiceNo||'',odometerBefore:Number(x.odometerBefore||0),odometerAfter:Number(x.odometerAfter||0),warrantyStatus:x.warrantyStatus||'Checked',evidenceStatus:x.evidenceStatus||'Complete',approvalStatus:x.approvalStatus||'Approved'}));
 (db.drivers||[]).forEach((x,i)=>Object.assign(x,{identityStatus:x.identityStatus||'Verified',deviceId:x.deviceId||('DEVICE-'+String(i+1).padStart(4,'0')),employmentStatus:x.employmentStatus||'Active',watchlistStatus:x.watchlistStatus||'Clear',maxWorkingHours:Number(x.maxWorkingHours||12),riskStatus:x.riskStatus||'Low'}));
 (db.routes||[]).forEach((x,i)=>Object.assign(x,{deviationToleranceKm:Number(x.deviationToleranceKm||10),highRiskZone:x.highRiskZone||'No',secureParkingRequired:x.secureParkingRequired||'No',approvalStatus:x.approvalStatus||'Approved',routeVersion:x.routeVersion||'v1.'+(i+1)}));
 (db.plans||[]).forEach(x=>Object.assign(x,{screeningStatus:x.screeningStatus||'Not Screened',riskLevel:x.riskLevel||'Low',riskScore:Number(x.riskScore||0),riskIssues:Array.isArray(x.riskIssues)?x.riskIssues:[],screenedAt:x.screenedAt||''}));
}
function rcAudit(entity,ref,action,oldValue='',newValue='',reason=''){rcEnsureData();db.controlAudit.unshift({id:'AUD-RC-'+String(Date.now()),entity,ref,action,oldValue,newValue,reason,user:'Admin TEST SNACKBAR',timestamp:rcNow()});db.controlAudit=db.controlAudit.slice(0,300)}
function rcEmit(o){rcEnsureData();const evt={id:o.id||('RSK-'+String(Date.now())+'-'+Math.floor(Math.random()*999)),rule:o.rule||'CONTROL_EXCEPTION',sourceModule:o.sourceModule||'Unknown',sourceType:o.sourceType||'',sourceRef:o.sourceRef||'-',relatedRefs:o.relatedRefs||[],title:o.title||o.rule||'Risk event',negativeCase:o.negativeCase||o.title||'',expectedCondition:o.expectedCondition||'',actualCondition:o.actualCondition||'',threshold:o.threshold||'',severity:o.severity||'Medium',confidence:Number(o.confidence||75),exposure:Number(o.exposure||0),recurrence:Number(o.recurrence||1),evidence:o.evidence||[],recommendedAction:o.recommendedAction||'Review source transaction',blocking:!!o.blocking,status:o.status||'Open',detectedAt:o.detectedAt||rcNow(),sourceRecord:o.sourceRecord||o.sourceRef||'-'};evt.score=rcScore(evt.severity,evt.confidence,evt.exposure,evt.recurrence);const key=[evt.rule,evt.sourceModule,evt.sourceRef,evt.actualCondition].join('|');const found=db.riskEvents.find(x=>x.key===key&&x.status!=='Cleared');if(found){Object.assign(found,evt,{key,id:found.id,detectedAt:found.detectedAt,lastDetectedAt:rcNow(),recurrence:Number(found.recurrence||1)+1});return found}evt.key=key;db.riskEvents.unshift(evt);return evt}
function rcClearScope(scope){rcEnsureData();db.riskEvents.filter(x=>x.sourceModule===scope&&x.status==='Open').forEach(x=>x.status='Cleared')}
function rcOpenEvents(filter='',ref=''){rcEnsureData();const rows=db.riskEvents.filter(x=>x.status!=='Cleared'&&(!filter||x.sourceModule===filter||x.sourceType===filter)&&(!ref||x.sourceRef===ref||x.relatedRefs?.includes(ref)));openModal('Risk Control Events',`<div class="notice">Negative case ditampilkan bersama expected, actual, source record, dan recommended action.</div><div class="compact-list">${rows.map(x=>`<div class="compact-item"><div class="top"><span class="rc-chip ${rcSeverityClass(x.severity)}">${esc(x.severity)} • ${x.score}</span><b>${esc(x.title)}</b><div class="right"><strong>${esc(x.sourceRef)}</strong><span>${esc(x.detectedAt)}</span></div></div><p><b>Negative Case:</b> ${esc(x.negativeCase)}</p><p><b>Expected:</b> ${esc(x.expectedCondition||'-')}</p><p><b>Actual:</b> ${esc(x.actualCondition||'-')}</p><p class="rc-source">Source: ${esc(x.sourceRecord||x.sourceRef)}</p></div>`).join('')||'<div class="empty">No open risk event for this source.</div>'}</div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`)}
function rcEventsFor(source,ref=''){rcEnsureData();return db.riskEvents.filter(x=>x.status!=='Cleared'&&(x.sourceModule===source||x.sourceType===source)&&(!ref||x.sourceRef===ref||x.relatedRefs?.includes(ref)))}
function rcHighest(events){return events.reduce((a,b)=>rcSeverityRank(b.severity)>rcSeverityRank(a)?b.severity:a,'Low')}
function rcBadge(events){const level=rcHighest(events);return `<span class="rc-chip ${rcSeverityClass(level)}">${esc(level)}${events.length?' • '+events.length:''}</span>`}
function rcBannerHTML(source,title,buttons=''){const ev=rcEventsFor(source),blocked=ev.filter(x=>x.blocking).length,level=rcHighest(ev);return `<div class="rc-banner" data-rc-source="${esc(source)}"><span>🛡️</span><div><strong>${esc(title)}</strong><div>Control point aktif: validation, evidence, approval, audit trail, dan negative-case detection.</div></div><div class="rc-stats"><span class="rc-chip ${rcSeverityClass(level)}">${esc(level)} Risk</span><span class="rc-chip">${ev.length} Open</span><span class="rc-chip critical">${blocked} Blocking</span></div><div class="rc-actions">${buttons}<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="rcOpenEvents('${esc(source)}')">View Alerts</button></div></div>`}
function rcInstallBanner(pageId,source,title,buttons=''){const page=document.getElementById('page-'+pageId);if(!page)return;let old=page.querySelector('.rc-banner[data-rc-source="'+source+'"]');const html=rcBannerHTML(source,title,buttons);if(old)old.outerHTML=html;else page.querySelector('.page-head')?.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend',html)}
function rcRequestApproval(type,ref,reason,severity='High'){rcEnsureData();let a=db.approvalRequests.find(x=>x.type===type&&x.ref===ref&&x.status==='Pending');if(!a){a={id:'APR-'+String(Date.now()),type,ref,reason,severity,status:'Pending',requestedBy:'Admin TEST SNACKBAR',requestedAt:rcNow(),requiredApprovers:2,approvers:[]};db.approvalRequests.unshift(a)}return a}
rcEnsureData();


/* ===== Master Risk Controls V5 ===== */
function rcEnsureMasterFields(){rcEnsureData()}
const rcBaseMasterFields=masterFields;
