 hubs:[{k:'geofenceRadius',l:'Geofence Radius (meter)',t:'number',min:50},{k:'verificationStatus',l:'Location Verification',t:'select',o:['Verified','Pending Review','Rejected']},{k:'highRiskLocation',l:'High-Risk Location',t:'select',o:['No','Yes']},{k:'authorizedGate',l:'Authorized Gate'}],
 carriers:[{k:'kycStatus',l:'KYC Status',t:'select',o:['Verified','Pending Review','Rejected']},{k:'permitExpiry',l:'Transport Permit Expiry',t:'date'},{k:'insuranceExpiry',l:'Insurance Expiry',t:'date'},{k:'insuranceCoverage',l:'Insurance Coverage',t:'number',min:0},{k:'bankVerificationStatus',l:'Bank Account Verification',t:'select',o:['Verified','Pending Approval','Rejected']},{k:'riskStatus',l:'Carrier Risk Level',t:'select',o:['Low','Medium','High','Critical']},{k:'officialEmail',l:'Official Email'}],
 contracts:[{k:'contractVersion',l:'Contract Version'},{k:'approvalStatus',l:'Contract Approval',t:'select',o:['Approved','Pending Approval','Rejected']},{k:'subcontractingAllowed',l:'Subcontracting Allowed',t:'select',o:['No','Yes']},{k:'liabilityLimit',l:'Liability Limit',t:'number',min:0},{k:'podRequirement',l:'POD Requirement',t:'select',o:['Photo + Signature + OTP','Photo + Signature','Signature Only']}],
 vehicles:[{k:'vin',l:'VIN / Chassis Number'},{k:'engineNumber',l:'Engine Number'},{k:'gpsDeviceId',l:'GPS Device ID'},{k:'fuelType',l:'Fuel Type',t:'select',o:['Diesel','Gasoline','Electric','Hybrid']},{k:'tankCapacity',l:'Tank Capacity (liter)',t:'number',min:1},{k:'odometer',l:'Verified Odometer (km)',t:'number',min:0},{k:'identityVerification',l:'Vehicle Identity Verification',t:'select',o:['Verified','Pending Review','Rejected']},{k:'riskStatus',l:'Vehicle Risk Level',t:'select',o:['Low','Medium','High','Critical']}],
 drivers:[{k:'identityStatus',l:'Identity Verification',t:'select',o:['Verified','Pending Review','Rejected']},{k:'deviceId',l:'Registered Device ID'},{k:'employmentStatus',l:'Employment Status',t:'select',o:['Active','Suspended','Terminated']},{k:'watchlistStatus',l:'Watchlist Status',t:'select',o:['Clear','Watchlist','Blacklisted']},{k:'maxWorkingHours',l:'Maximum Working Hours',t:'number',min:1},{k:'riskStatus',l:'Driver Risk Level',t:'select',o:['Low','Medium','High','Critical']}],
 routes:[{k:'routeVersion',l:'Route Version'},{k:'deviationToleranceKm',l:'Deviation Tolerance (km)',t:'number',min:1},{k:'highRiskZone',l:'High-Risk Zone',t:'select',o:['No','Yes']},{k:'secureParkingRequired',l:'Secure Parking Required',t:'select',o:['No','Yes']},{k:'approvalStatus',l:'Route Approval',t:'select',o:['Approved','Pending Approval','Rejected']}]
 }[type]||[];return [...base,...extra]}
const rcBaseSaveMaster=saveMaster;

 if(type==='vehicles'){const vin=document.getElementById('mf-vin')?.value.trim(),gps=document.getElementById('mf-gpsDeviceId')?.value.trim();if(db.vehicles.some((x,i)=>i!==index&&vin&&x.vin===vin)){toast('VIN / Chassis Number harus unik');return}if(db.vehicles.some((x,i)=>i!==index&&gps&&x.gpsDeviceId===gps)){toast('GPS Device ID hanya boleh terpasang pada satu kendaraan aktif');return}}
 if(type==='drivers'){const device=document.getElementById('mf-deviceId')?.value.trim();if(db.drivers.some((x,i)=>i!==index&&device&&x.deviceId===device)){toast('Registered Device ID sudah digunakan driver lain');return}}
 rcBaseSaveMaster(type,index);if(!document.getElementById('modalMask')?.classList.contains('open')){rcEnsureMasterFields();rcAudit(type,index===null?'NEW':String(index),'SAVE','','','Master risk fields saved');runMasterRiskValidation(type);saveDB();renderAll()}}
const rcBaseOpenMaintenance=openMaintenanceForm;

obj=index===null?{}:db.maintenanceTasks[index]||{},grid=document.querySelector('#modalBody .form-grid');if(!grid)return;const dis=view?'disabled':'';grid.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend',`<div value="${esc(obj.invoiceNo||'')}" ${dis}></div><div class="field"><label>Warranty Status</label><select class="select" id="mt-warranty" ${dis}><option ${obj.warrantyStatus==='Checked'?'selected':''}>Checked</option><option ${obj.warrantyStatus==='Not Checked'?'selected':''}>Not Checked</option><option value="${esc(obj.odometerBefore||0)}" ${dis}></div><div class="field"><label>Odometer After</label><input class="input" id="mt-odo-after" type="number" min="0" value="${esc(obj.odometerAfter||0)}" ${dis}></div><div class="field"><label>Evidence Status</label><select class="select" id="mt-evidence" ${dis}><option ${obj.evidenceStatus==='Complete'?'selected':''}>Complete</option><option ${obj.evidenceStatus==='Pending'?'selected':''}>Pending</option><option ${obj.evidenceStatus==='Missing'?'selected':''}>Missing</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Approval Review'?'selected':''}>Pending Review</option><option ${obj.approvalStatus==='Rejected'?'selected':''}>Rejected</option></select></div>`)}
const rcBaseSaveMaintenance=saveMaintenance;
saveMaintenance=function(index){const before=db.maintenanceTasks.length,extras={vendor:document.getElementById('mt-vendor')?.value.trim(),workOrderNo:document.getElementById('mt-workorder')?.value.trim(),invoiceNo:document.getElementById('mt-invoice')?.value.trim(),warrantyStatus:document.getElementById('mt-warranty')?.value,odometerBefore:Number(document.getElementById('mt-odo-before')?.value||0),odometerAfter:Number(document.getElementById('mt-odo-after')?.value||0),evidenceStatus:document.getElementById('mt-evidence')?.value,approvalStatus:document.getElementById('mt-approval')?.value};if(extras.odometerAfter&&extras.odometerAfter<extras.odometerBefore){toast('Odometer After tidak boleh lebih kecil dari Odometer Before');return}if(extras.invoiceNo&&db.maintenanceTasks.some((x,i)=>i!==index&&x.invoiceNo===extras.invoiceNo)){toast('Vendor Invoice Number sudah digunakan maintenance task lain');return}rcBaseSaveMaintenance(index);if(!document.getElementById('modalMask')?.classList.contains('open')){const obj=index===null&&db.maintenanceTasks.length>before?db.maintenanceTasks.at(-1):db.maintenanceTasks[index];if(obj)Object.assign(obj,extras);runMasterRiskValidation('maintenanceTasks');saveDB();renderAll()}}
const rcBaseConfirmStartMaintenance=confirmStartMaintenance;
confirmStartMaintenance=function(){const p=pendingMaintenanceStart,task=p&&db.maintenanceTasks.find(x=>x.id===p.id),estimate=Number(task?.estimateCost||0),variance=estimate?((Number(p.actualCost)-estimate)/estimate*100):0;rcBaseConfirmStartMaintenance();if(task&&variance>20){task.approvalStatus='Pending Review';rcRequestApproval('MAINTENANCE_COST_VARIANCE',task.id,'Actual cost '+variance.toFixed(1)+'% above estimate');rcEmit({rule:'MAINTENANCE_COST_VARIANCE',sourceModule:'Maintenance Task',sourceType:'maintenanceTasks',sourceRef:task.id,title:'Maintenance cost exceeds estimate',negativeCase:`${task.id} dimulai dengan Actual Cost ${variance.toFixed(1)}% di atas Estimate Cost.`,expectedCondition:'Actual Cost berada dalam toleransi maksimal 20% dari Estimate Cost.',actualCondition:`Estimate ${estimate}; Actual ${p.actualCost}; Variance ${variance.toFixed(1)}%.`,threshold:'20%',severity:variance>50?'Critical':'High',confidence:95,exposure:Math.max(0,Number(p.actualCost)-estimate),blocking:variance>50,sourceRecord:task.id,recommendedAction:'Fleet Manager approval and invoice review.'});saveDB();renderAll()}}
function rcMasterRecordEvents(type,ref){const label={hubs:'Hub Management',carriers:'Carrier & Contract',contracts:'Carrier & Contract',vehicles:'Vehicle Master',maintenanceTasks:'Maintenance Task',drivers:'Driver Master',routes:'Route & Lane Master'}[type]||type;return rcEventsFor(label,ref)}
function rcDecorateMasterTable(type){const map={hubs:['hubTbody','Hub Management'],carriers:['carrierTbody','Carrier & Contract'],contracts:['contractTbody','Carrier & Contract'],vehicles:['vehicleTbody','Vehicle Master'],drivers:['driverTbody','Driver Master'],routes:['routeTbody','Route & Lane Master']},cfg=map[type];if(!cfg)return;const tb=document.getElementById(cfg[0]);if(!tb)return;const table=tb.closest('table'),head=table?.querySelector('thead tr');if(head&&!head.querySelector('[data-rc-risk]'))head.lastElementChild?.insertAdjacentHTML('beforebegin','<th data-rc-risk class="rc-table-risk">Risk Control</th>');const records=filteredMasterRecords(type);[...tb.querySelectorAll('tr')].forEach((tr,i)=>{if(tr.querySelector('.empty')){const td=tr.querySelector('td');if(td)td.colSpan=Number(td.colSpan||1)+1;return}const rec=records[i]?.x;if(!rec||tr.querySelector('[data-rc-risk]'))return;tr.lastElementChild?.insertAdjacentHTML('beforebegin',`<td data-rc-risk>${rcBadge(rcMasterRecordEvents(type,rec.id))}</td>`)});}
const rcBaseRenderMaster=renderMaster;
renderMaster=function(type){rcBaseRenderMaster(type);rcDecorateMasterTable(type);const source={hubs:'Hub Management',carriers:'Carrier & Contract',contracts:'Carrier & Contract',vehicles:'Vehicle Master',drivers:'Driver Master',routes:'Route & Lane Master'}[type];if(source)rcInstallBanner({hubs:'hub',carriers:'carrier',contracts:'carrier',vehicles:'vehicle',drivers:'driver',routes:'route'}[type],source,source,`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runMasterRiskValidation('${type}')">Run Validation</button>`)}
const rcBaseRenderMaintenance=renderMaintenance;
renderMaintenance=function(){rcBaseRenderMaintenance();const tb=document.getElementById('maintenanceTbody'),head=tb?.closest('table')?.querySelector('thead tr');if(head&&!head.querySelector('[data-rc-risk]'))head.lastElementChild?.insertAdjacentHTML('beforebegin','<th data-rc-risk>Risk Control</th>');const rows=filteredMaintenanceRecords();[...(tb?.querySelectorAll('tr')||[])].forEach((tr,i)=>{if(tr.querySelector('.empty')){const td=tr.querySelector('td');if(td)td.colSpan=Number(td.colSpan||1)+1;return}const rec=rows[i]?.x;if(rec&&!tr.querySelector('[data-rc-risk]'))tr.lastElementChild?.insertAdjacentHTML('beforebegin',`<td data-rc-risk>${rcBadge(rcMasterRecordEvents('maintenanceTasks',rec.id))}</td>`)});rcInstallBanner('maintenance','Maintenance Task','Maintenance Risk Control',`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runMasterRiskValidation('maintenanceTasks')">Run Validation</button>`)}
function runMasterRiskValidation(type='all',silent=false){
 rcEnsureMasterFields();const scopes=type==='all'?['hubs','carriers','contracts','vehicles','maintenanceTasks','drivers','routes']:[type];
 const mod={hubs:'Hub Management',carriers:'Carrier & Contract',contracts:'Carrier & Contract',vehicles:'Vehicle Master',maintenanceTasks:'Maintenance Task',drivers:'Driver Master',routes:'Route & Lane Master'};scopes.forEach(s=>rcClearScope(mod[s]));
 if(scopes.includes('hubs'))(db.hubs||[]).forEach(x=>{if(x.status==='Active'&&(!Number.isFinite(Number(x.latitude))||!Number.isFinite(Number(x.longitude))))rcEmit({rule:'HUB_COORDINATE_MISSING',sourceModule:mod.hubs,sourceType:'hubs',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Active hub has invalid coordinate',negativeCase:`${x.name} aktif tetapi koordinat lokasi belum valid.`,expectedCondition:'Hub aktif memiliki latitude, longitude, dan geofence terverifikasi.',actualCondition:`Latitude ${x.latitude||'-'}; Longitude ${x.longitude||'-'}.`,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id});if(x.status==='Active'&&x.verificationStatus!=='Verified')rcEmit({rule:'HUB_NOT_VERIFIED',sourceModule:mod.hubs,sourceType:'hubs',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Hub location not verified',negativeCase:`${x.name} digunakan sebagai hub aktif saat verification status ${x.verificationStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'Location Verification = Verified.',actualCondition:x.verificationStatus,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id})});
 if(scopes.includes('carriers'))(db.carriers||[]).forEach(x=>{if(x.status==='Active'&&x.kycStatus!=='Verified')rcEmit({rule:'CARRIER_KYC_INCOMPLETE',sourceModule:mod.carriers,sourceType:'carriers',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Carrier KYC incomplete',negativeCase:`${x.name} aktif tetapi KYC berstatus ${x.kycStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'KYC Status = Verified sebelum carrier dapat menerima shipment.',actualCondition:x.kycStatus,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id});if(rcDateExpired(x.permitExpiry))rcEmit({rule:'CARRIER_PERMIT_EXPIRED',sourceModule:mod.carriers,sourceType:'carriers',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Carrier permit expired',negativeCase:`Izin angkutan ${x.name} telah kedaluwarsa.`,expectedCondition:'Permit aktif pada tanggal assignment.',actualCondition:`Permit expiry ${x.permitExpiry}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id});if(rcDateExpired(x.insuranceExpiry))rcEmit({rule:'CARRIER_INSURANCE_EXPIRED',sourceModule:mod.carriers,sourceType:'carriers',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Carrier insurance expired',negativeCase:`Polis asuransi ${x.name} telah kedaluwarsa.`,expectedCondition:'Insurance aktif selama periode shipment.',actualCondition:`Insurance expiry ${x.insuranceExpiry}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id});if(x.bankVerificationStatus!=='Verified')rcEmit({rule:'CARRIER_BANK_UNVERIFIED',sourceModule:mod.carriers,sourceType:'carriers',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Carrier bank account awaiting verification',negativeCase:`Rekening pembayaran ${x.name} berstatus ${x.bankVerificationStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'Bank Account Verification = Verified melalui maker-checker.',actualCondition:x.bankVerificationStatus,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id})});
 if(scopes.includes('contracts'))(db.contracts||[]).forEach(x=>{if(x.status!=='Active'||x.approvalStatus!=='Approved')rcEmit({rule:'CONTRACT_NOT_ELIGIBLE',sourceModule:mod.contracts,sourceType:'contracts',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Contract is not eligible for assignment',negativeCase:`${x.id} berstatus ${x.status} dan approval ${x.approvalStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'Contract Active dan Approved pada tanggal shipment.',actualCondition:`${x.status} / ${x.approvalStatus}.`,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id})});
 if(scopes.includes('vehicles')){const gps={},vin={};(db.vehicles||[]).forEach(x=>{(gps[x.gpsDeviceId]??=[]).push(x);(vin[x.vin]??=[]).push(x);if(rcDateExpired(x.stnkExpiry)||rcDateExpired(x.kirExpiry))rcEmit({rule:'VEHICLE_DOCUMENT_EXPIRED',sourceModule:mod.vehicles,sourceType:'vehicles',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Vehicle document expired',negativeCase:`${x.plate} memiliki STNK/KIR yang kedaluwarsa.`,expectedCondition:'STNK dan KIR aktif pada tanggal trip.',actualCondition:`STNK ${x.stnkExpiry}; KIR ${x.kirExpiry}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id});if(x.identityVerification!=='Verified')rcEmit({rule:'VEHICLE_IDENTITY_UNVERIFIED',sourceModule:mod.vehicles,sourceType:'vehicles',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Vehicle identity not verified',negativeCase:`${x.plate} berstatus ${x.identityVerification}.`,expectedCondition:'Vehicle Identity Verification = Verified.',actualCondition:x.identityVerification,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id})});Object.values(gps).filter(a=>a.length>1).forEach(a=>a.forEach(x=>rcEmit({rule:'GPS_DEVICE_DUPLICATE',sourceModule:mod.vehicles,sourceType:'vehicles',sourceRef:x.id,title:'GPS device used by multiple vehicles',negativeCase:`GPS Device ${x.gpsDeviceId} terhubung ke ${a.map(v=>v.plate).join(', ')}.`,expectedCondition:'Satu GPS Device ID hanya untuk satu kendaraan aktif.',actualCondition:a.map(v=>v.plate).join(', '),severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.gpsDeviceId})));Object.values(vin).filter(a=>a.length>1).forEach(a=>a.forEach(x=>rcEmit({rule:'VIN_DUPLICATE',sourceModule:mod.vehicles,sourceType:'vehicles',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Duplicate vehicle identity',negativeCase:`VIN ${x.vin} digunakan oleh lebih dari satu kendaraan.`,expectedCondition:'VIN unik per vehicle master.',actualCondition:a.map(v=>v.plate).join(', '),severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.vin}))) }
 if(scopes.includes('maintenanceTasks')){const invoices={};(db.maintenanceTasks||[]).forEach(x=>{if(x.invoiceNo)(invoices[x.invoiceNo]??=[]).push(x);const est=Number(x.estimateCost||0),act=Number(x.actualCost||0),variance=est&&act?(act-est)/est*100:0;if(variance>20)rcEmit({rule:'MAINTENANCE_COST_VARIANCE',sourceModule:mod.maintenanceTasks,sourceType:'maintenanceTasks',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Maintenance cost variance above threshold',negativeCase:`${x.id} memiliki Actual Cost ${variance.toFixed(1)}% di atas Estimate Cost.`,expectedCondition:'Cost variance maksimal 20%.',actualCondition:`Estimate ${est}; Actual ${act}; Variance ${variance.toFixed(1)}%.`,severity:variance>50?'Critical':'High',blocking:variance>50,exposure:Math.max(0,act-est),sourceRecord:x.id});if(x.status==='Completed'&&x.evidenceStatus!=='Complete')rcEmit({rule:'MAINTENANCE_EVIDENCE_MISSING',sourceModule:mod.maintenanceTasks,sourceType:'maintenanceTasks',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Completed maintenance without complete evidence',negativeCase:`${x.id} Completed dengan evidence status ${x.evidenceStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'Evidence before/after dan invoice lengkap sebelum completion.',actualCondition:x.evidenceStatus,severity:'High',blocking:false,sourceRecord:x.id})});Object.entries(invoices).filter(([,a])=>a.length>1).forEach(([inv,a])=>a.forEach(x=>rcEmit({rule:'DUPLICATE_MAINTENANCE_INVOICE',sourceModule:mod.maintenanceTasks,sourceType:'maintenanceTasks',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Duplicate maintenance invoice',negativeCase:`Invoice ${inv} digunakan pada ${a.map(v=>v.id).join(', ')}.`,expectedCondition:'Invoice vendor unik per maintenance task.',actualCondition:a.map(v=>v.id).join(', '),severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:inv}))) }
 if(scopes.includes('drivers')){const devices={};(db.drivers||[]).forEach(x=>{(devices[x.deviceId]??=[]).push(x);if(rcDateExpired(x.expiry))rcEmit({rule:'DRIVER_LICENSE_EXPIRED',sourceModule:mod.drivers,sourceType:'drivers',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Driver license expired',negativeCase:`SIM ${x.name} telah kedaluwarsa pada ${x.expiry}.`,expectedCondition:'SIM aktif pada tanggal trip.',actualCondition:x.expiry,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id});if(x.identityStatus!=='Verified'||x.watchlistStatus!=='Clear'||x.employmentStatus!=='Active')rcEmit({rule:'DRIVER_NOT_ELIGIBLE',sourceModule:mod.drivers,sourceType:'drivers',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Driver identity or employment restriction',negativeCase:`${x.name} memiliki Identity ${x.identityStatus}, Employment ${x.employmentStatus}, Watchlist ${x.watchlistStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'Verified, Active, dan Clear.',actualCondition:`${x.identityStatus} / ${x.employmentStatus} / ${x.watchlistStatus}.`,severity:x.watchlistStatus==='Blacklisted'?'Critical':'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id})});Object.values(devices).filter(a=>a.length>1).forEach(a=>a.forEach(x=>rcEmit({rule:'DRIVER_DEVICE_SHARED',sourceModule:mod.drivers,sourceType:'drivers',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Driver device shared by multiple identities',negativeCase:`Device ${x.deviceId} digunakan oleh ${a.map(v=>v.name).join(', ')}.`,expectedCondition:'Satu registered device untuk satu driver aktif.',actualCondition:a.map(v=>v.name).join(', '),severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.deviceId}))) }
 if(scopes.includes('routes'))(db.routes||[]).forEach(x=>{if(x.status==='Active'&&x.approvalStatus!=='Approved')rcEmit({rule:'ROUTE_NOT_APPROVED',sourceModule:mod.routes,sourceType:'routes',sourceRef:x.id,title:'Active route has no approval',negativeCase:`${x.id} aktif tetapi approval ${x.approvalStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'Route aktif harus Approved sebelum digunakan.',actualCondition:x.approvalStatus,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:x.id});if(x.highRiskZone==='Yes'&&x.secureParkingRequired!=='Yes')rcEmit({rule:'HIGH_RISK_ROUTE_NO_SECURE_PARKING',sourceModule:mod.routes,sourceType:'routes',sourceRef:x.id,title:'High-risk lane lacks secure parking control',negativeCase:`${x.id} ditandai High-Risk Zone tetapi Secure Parking Required = No.`,expectedCondition:'High-risk lane mewajibkan secure parking.',actualCondition:'Secure Parking Required = No.',severity:'High',blocking:false,sourceRecord:x.id})});
 rcAudit('Risk Control',type,'RUN_VALIDATION','','',`Validated ${scopes.join(', ')}`);saveDB();renderAll();if(!silent)toast('Master risk validation completed');return db.riskEvents}

function v6QualityScore(){

function v6Cascade(type,before,after){if(!before||!after)return;const replace=(arr,key,oldV,newV)=>v6Array(arr).forEach(x=>{if(x[key]===oldV)x[key]=newV});

 if(type==='carriers'&&before.name!==after.name){replace(db.contracts,'carrier',before.name,after.name);replace(db.vehicles,'carrier',before.name,after.name);replace(db.drivers,'carrier',before.name,after.name);replace(db.plans,'supplier',before.name,after.name);}
 if(type==='vehicles'&&before.plate!==after.plate){replace(db.plans,'vehicle',before.plate,after.plate);replace(db.fleetOrders,'plate',before.plate,after.plate);replace(db.costRecords,'plate',before.plate,after.plate);}
 if(type==='drivers'&&before.name!==after.name){replace(db.plans,'driver',before.name,after.name);replace(db.fleetOrders,'driver',before.name,after.name);replace(db.costRecords,'driver',before.name,after.name);v6Array(db.plans).forEach(p=>v6Array(p.stops).forEach(s=>{if(s.driver===before.name)s.driver=after.name}));}

}

Instruction</label><textarea class="textarea" id="v6-c-instruction" ${ro}>${esc(obj.deliveryInstruction||'')}</textarea></div></div>`;

window.v6SaveCustomer=function(index){const isNew=index===null,before=isNew?null:deep(db.customers[index]),name=document.getElementById('v6-c-name').value.trim(),location=document.getElementById('v6-c-location').value.trim(),address=document.getElementById('v6-c-address').value.trim(),latRaw=document.getElementById('v6-c-lat').value,lngRaw=document.getElementById('v6-c-lng').value;if(!name||!location||!address){toast('Name, City / Area, dan Address wajib diisi');return}if(db.customers.some((x,i)=>i!==index&&v6NormalizeName(x.name)===v6NormalizeName(name))){toast('Customer / Recipient Name harus unik');return}const latitude=latRaw===''?'':Number(latRaw),longitude=lngRaw===''?'':Number(lngRaw);if((latRaw!==''&&!Number.isFinite(latitude))||(lngRaw!==''&&!Number.isFinite(longitude))){toast('Latitude atau Longitude tidak valid');return}const obj={id:isNew?v6NextCustomerId():db.customers[index].id,name,type:document.getElementById('v6-c-type').value,location,address,latitude,longitude,openTime:document.getElementById('v6-c-open').value||'08:00',closeTime:document.getElementById('v6-c-close').value||'17:00',contactName:document.getElementById('v6-c-contact').value.trim(),phone:document.getElementById('v6-c-phone').value.trim(),geofenceRadius:Number(document.getElementById('v6-c-radius').value||150),verificationStatus:document.getElementById('v6-c-verification').value,riskStatus:document.getElementById('v6-c-risk').value,status:document.getElementById('v6-c-status').value,deliveryInstruction:document.getElementById('v6-c-instruction').value.trim()};obj.window=`${obj.openTime} - ${obj.closeTime}`;if(isNew)db.customers.push(obj);else db.customers[index]=obj;v6CascadeCustomer(before,obj);saveDB();closeModal();window.v6RenderCustomers();window.v6RenderMasterOverview();toast(`Customer ${obj.id} berhasil disimpan dan disinkronkan`)};

/* ===== Original script block 3 ===== */

(function(){
 const LOCATION_OPTIONS=['Ambon','Balikpapan','Bandar Lampung','Bandung','Banjar','Banjarmasin','Batam','Bekasi','Bengkulu','Bogor','Cilegon','Cimahi','Cirebon','Denpasar','Depok','Gorontalo','Jakarta','Jakarta Barat','Jakarta Pusat','Jakarta Selatan','Jakarta Timur','Jakarta Utara','Jambi','Jayapura','Kediri','Kupang','Makassar','Malang','Manado','Mataram','Medan','Padang','Palembang','Palu','Pangkalpinang','Pekanbaru','Pontianak','Samarinda','Semarang','Serang','Solo','Surabaya','Tangerang','Tangerang Selatan','Tasikmalaya','Yogyakarta'];
 const LOCATION_ALIASES={jakrta:'Jakarta',jakata:'Jakarta',jakarata:'Jakarta',bandug:'Bandung',bandun:'Bandung',bndung:'Bandung',surabya:'Surabaya',surabaya:'Surabaya',semarng:'Semarang',tanggerang:'Tangerang',tangerng:'Tangerang',bekasih:'Bekasi',bogor:'Bogor',yogjakarta:'Yogyakarta',jogjakarta:'Yogyakarta',jogja:'Yogyakarta',makasar:'Makassar',palembng:'Palembang',pekanbaru:'Pekanbaru'};
 const originalMasterFields=window.masterFields;
 window.masterFields=function(type,obj={},isNew=false){
  let fields=originalMasterFields(type,obj,isNew).filter(f=>!['contractVersion','liabilityLimit','routeVersion','hubSchedule'].includes(f.k));
  fields=fields.map(f=>{
   const x={...f};
   if(type==='hubs'&&x.k==='location')x.locationAssist=true;
   if(type==='contracts'&&x.k==='baseRate')x.currency=true;
   if(type==='carriers'&&x.k==='insuranceCoverage')x.currency=true;
   if(type==='routes'&&x.k==='serviceWindow')x.l='Delivery Hours';
   return x;
  });
  if(type==='routes'&&!fields.some(f=>f.k==='totalActualCost')){
   const idx=fields.findIndex(f=>f.k==='totalCost');
   const actual={k:'totalActualCost',l:'Total Actual Cost',t:'computed',readonly:true,help:'Akumulasi actual cost shipment yang menggunakan lane ini.'};
   if(idx>=0)fields.splice(idx+1,0,actual);else fields.push(actual);
  }
  return fields;
 };
 const originalFieldHTML=window.fieldHTML;
 window.fieldHTML=function(f,v,obj,readonly=false){
  if(f.currency){
   const ro=readonly||f.readonly,dis=readonly||f.disabled,cls=f.full?'field full':'field';
   return `<div class="${cls}"><label>${esc(f.l)}</label><div class="currency-field"><span class="currency-prefix">Rp</span><input class="input" id="mf-${f.k}" type="number" value="${esc(v??'')}" min="${f.min??0}" step="${f.step||1}" placeholder="0" ${ro?'readonly':''} ${dis?'disabled':''} ${f.oninput?`oninput="${f.oninput}"`:''} ${f.onchange?`onchange="${f.onchange}"`:''}></div>${f.help?`<small>${esc(f.help)}</small>`:''}</div>`;
  }
  if(f.locationAssist){
   const dis=readonly||f.disabled;
   return `<div class="${f.full?'field full':'field'}"><label>${esc(f.l)}</label><input class="input" id="mf-${f.k}" list="hub-location-options" value="${esc(v??'')}" autocomplete="off" ${dis?'disabled':''} oninput="hubLocationInputChanged(this)" onblur="validateHubLocationInput(this,true)"><datalist id="hub-location-options"></datalist><div class="location-help" id="hub-location-help"><span>Ketik kota/area. Typo umum akan dikoreksi otomatis.</span></div></div>`;
  }
  if(f.t==='computed'&&f.k==='totalActualCost')return `<div class="${f.full?'field full':'field'}"><label>${esc(f.l)}</label><input class="input" id="mf-${f.k}" value="${esc(fmtIDR(routeTotalActualCost(obj)))}" disabled>${f.help?`<small>${esc(f.help)}</small>`:''}</div>`;
  return originalFieldHTML(f,v,obj,readonly);
 };
 function locationKey(v){return String(v||'').trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,' ')}
 function titleCase(v){return String(v||'').trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ').toLowerCase().replace(/(^|[\s-])\p{L}/gu,m=>m.toUpperCase())}
 function levenshtein(a,b){a=locationKey(a);b=locationKey(b);const dp=Array.from({length:b.length+1},(_,i)=>[i]);for(let j=0;j<=a.length;j++)dp[0][j]=j;for(let i=1;i<=b.length;i++)for(let j=1;j<=a.length;j++)dp[i][j]=b[i-1]===a[j-1]?dp[i-1][j-1]:1+Math.min(dp[i-1][j],dp[i][j-1],dp[i-1][j-1]);return dp[b.length][a.length]}
 function knownLocations(){return [...new Set([...LOCATION_OPTIONS,...(db.hubs||[]).map(h=>h.location).filter(Boolean)])]}
 function setLocationHelp(message,state='',allowCustom=false){const box=document.getElementById('hub-location-help');if(!box)return;box.className='location-help'+(state?' '+state:'');box.innerHTML=`<span>${esc(message)}</span>${allowCustom?'<button type="button" onclick="acceptCustomHubLocation()">Use as typed</button>':''}`}
 window.hubLocationInputChanged=function(el){el.dataset.custom='0';el.dataset.invalid='0';el.classList.remove('input-error');setLocationHelp('Ketik kota/area. Typo umum akan dikoreksi otomatis.')}
 window.validateHubLocationInput=function(el,autoCorrect=false){
  if(!el)return true;const raw=el.value.trim();el.classList.remove('input-error');el.dataset.invalid='0';if(!raw){el.dataset.invalid='1';el.classList.add('input-error');setLocationHelp('Location wajib diisi.','error');return false}
  const key=locationKey(raw),alias=LOCATION_ALIASES[key];if(alias){el.value=alias;setLocationHelp(`Auto-corrected: ${raw} → ${alias}`,'success');return true}
  const known=knownLocations(),exact=known.find(x=>locationKey(x)===key);if(exact){el.value=exact;setLocationHelp('Location dikenali.','success');return true}
  const ranked=known.map(x=>({x,d:levenshtein(key,x)})).sort((a,b)=>a.d-b.d),best=ranked[0],threshold=Math.max(1,Math.floor(key.length*.22));
  if(autoCorrect&&best&&best.d<=threshold){el.value=best.x;setLocationHelp(`Auto-corrected: ${raw} → ${best.x}`,'success');return true}
  if(el.dataset.custom==='1'){el.value=titleCase(raw);setLocationHelp('Custom location diterima.','success');return true}
  el.dataset.invalid='1';el.classList.add('input-error');setLocationHelp(best&&best.d<=Math.max(3,threshold+1)?`Location tidak dikenali. Apakah maksud Anda “${best.x}”?`:'Location tidak dikenali. Pilih suggestion atau periksa ejaan.','error',true);return false
 }

 function updateLocationDatalist(){const dl=document.getElementById('hub-location-options');if(dl)dl.innerHTML=knownLocations().map(x=>`<option value="${esc(x)}"></option>`).join('')}
 function parseGoogleCoordinate(value){const s=decodeURIComponent(String(value||'').trim());const patterns=[/@(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?),(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/,/query=(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)[,%20\s]+(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i,/[?&]q=(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)[,%20\s]+(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i,/^\s*(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*[,;]\s*(-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*$/];for(const p of patterns){const m=s.match(p);if(m)return {lat:Number(m[1]),lng:Number(m[2])}}return null}

 window.applyHubGoogleMaps=function(){const input=document.getElementById('hub-gmaps-input'),coord=parseGoogleCoordinate(input?.value);if(!coord||Math.abs(coord.lat)>90||Math.abs(coord.lng)>180){toast('Google Maps link / coordinate tidak valid');return}document.getElementById('mf-latitude').value=coord.lat;document.getElementById('mf-longitude').value=coord.lng;refreshHubMapPreview();toast('Latitude dan Longitude berhasil diisi')}

 function routeMatchesPlan(route,plan){if(plan.routeLane===route.id)return true;const text=String(plan.route||'').toLowerCase();return text.includes(String(route.origin||'').toLowerCase())&&text.includes(String(route.destination||'').toLowerCase())}

(function operationalMasterAlignmentV7(){
  'use strict';
  const DEMO_VERSION='OPERATIONAL_MASTER_ALIGNED_V7';
  const destinationGroups=[
    ['Bandung Wetan','Jl. R.E. Martadinata, Bandung'],['Bandung Kulon','Jl. Holis, Bandung'],['Cimahi Selatan','Jl. Baros, Cimahi'],['Jakarta Timur','Jl. Tuparev, Cirebon'],['Subang','Jl. Otto Iskandardinata, Subang']
  ];
  function operationalDemoRows(){
    const hubs=(db.hubs||[]).filter(h=>h.status==='Active').map(h=>h.name);const origins=hubs.length?hubs:['Hub A Bandung','Hub B Jakarta','Hub C Bintaro'];const base=new Date(todayISO()+'T08:00:00');
    return Array.from({length:120},(_,i)=>{const n=i+1,g=destinationGroups[i%destinationGroups.length],isSto=n%3===0,type=isSto?'STO':'DO',deadline=new Date(base.getTime()+((i%9)-2)*86400000+(8+(i%10))*3600000);return {id:`${type}/DEMO/2607/${String(n).padStart(4,'0')}`,type,customer:`Recipient ${String((i%45)+1).padStart(3,'0')} • ${g[0]}`,origin:origins[i%origins.length],destination:g[1],weight:650+(i%12)*275,volume:Number((2.4+(i%10)*1.15).toFixed(1)),priority:i%17===0?'Urgent':i%7===0?'High':i%11===0?'Low':'Normal',alert:deadline.toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16),status:'Need Planning',items:3+(i%18),source:'Excel Demo 120 Rows'};});
  }
  function ensureMasterAlignedData(){
    try{if(typeof rcEnsureData==='function')rcEnsureData();}catch(e){}
    (db.drivers||[]).forEach((d,i)=>Object.assign(d,{identityStatus:d.identityStatus||'Verified',deviceId:d.deviceId||('DEVICE-'+String(i+1).padStart(4,'0')),employmentStatus:d.employmentStatus||'Active',watchlistStatus:d.watchlistStatus||'Clear',maxWorkingHours:Number(d.maxWorkingHours||12),riskStatus:d.riskStatus||'Low'}));
    (db.vehicles||[]).forEach((v,i)=>Object.assign(v,{tankCapacity:Number(v.tankCapacity||([80,120,200][i%3])),odometer:Number(v.odometer||40000+i*12500),identityVerification:v.identityVerification||'Verified',fuelType:v.fuelType||'Diesel',riskStatus:v.riskStatus||'Low'}));
    (db.contracts||[]).forEach(c=>{if(String(c.podRequirement||'').includes('OTP'))c.podRequirement='Photo + Signature';});
    db.driverStates=db.driverStates||{};
    const rows=operationalDemoRows();rows.forEach(x=>{if(!(db.documents||[]).some(d=>d.id===x.id))db.documents.push(x)});db.operationalDemoVersion=DEMO_VERSION;saveDB();
  }
  ensureMasterAlignedData();

  const baseNormalizeImportedRows=window.normalizeImportedRows;
  window.normalizeImportedRows=function(matrix){
    if(!matrix.length)return[];const head=matrix[0].map(x=>String(x).trim().toLowerCase());
    const find=(...keys)=>head.findIndex(h=>keys.some(k=>h===k||h.includes(k)));
    const idx={id:find('document number','document','doc number'),type:find('type'),customer:find('customer','recipient'),origin:find('origin'),destination:find('destination'),weight:find('weight'),volume:find('volume'),priority:find('priority'),alert:find('dispatch deadline','alert time','alert','deadline'),items:find('item lines','items')};
    return matrix.slice(1).filter(r=>r.some(v=>String(v).trim())).map(r=>({id:String(r[idx.id]||'').trim(),type:String(r[idx.type]||'DO').trim().toUpperCase(),customer:String(r[idx.customer]||'').trim(),origin:String(r[idx.origin]||'').trim(),destination:String(r[idx.destination]||'').trim(),weight:Number(r[idx.weight]||0),volume:Number(r[idx.volume]||0),priority:String(r[idx.priority]||'Normal').trim(),alert:String(r[idx.alert]||new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)).trim(),status:'Need Planning',items:Number(r[idx.items]||1),source:'Excel Import'})).filter(x=>x.id&&x.customer&&x.origin&&x.destination);
  };
  window.openDocumentImport=function(){
    const sample=operationalDemoRows(),preview=sample.slice(0,30).map(x=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</td><td>${x.type}</td><td>${esc(x.customer)}</td><td>${esc(x.origin)}</td><td>${esc(x.destination)}</td><td>${x.weight}</td><td>${x.volume}</td><td>${x.priority}</td><td>${esc(x.alert)}</td></tr>`).join('');
    openModal('Import Ready Documents from Excel',`<div class="notice">Template berisi <b>120 baris</b> data DO/STO untuk pengujian.   };
  window.downloadFilledDocumentTemplate=function(){const headers=['Document Number','Type','Customer / Recipient','Origin','Destination','Weight','Volume','Priority','Dispatch Deadline','Item Lines'];const table=`<table><thead><tr>${headers.map(h=>`<th>${h}</th>`).join('')}</tr></thead><tbody>${operationalDemoRows().map(x=>`<tr>${[x.id,x.type,x.customer,x.origin,x.destination,x.weight,x.volume,x.priority,x.alert,x.items].map(v=>`<td>${esc(v)}</td>`).join('')}</tr>`).join('')}</tbody></table>`;const html=`<html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"></head><body>${table}</body></html>`;downloadBlob(html,`TMS-ready-document-120-rows-${todayISO()}.xls`,'application/vnd.ms-excel');toast('120-row Excel template downloaded');};
  window.importReadyDocuments=function(){const file=document.getElementById('documentImportFile')?.files?.[0];if(!file){applyImportedDocuments(operationalDemoRows());return;}const reader=new FileReader();reader.onload=()=>{try{const text=String(reader.result||''),matrix=text.toLowerCase().includes('<table')?parseExcelHtml(text):parseCsv(text),rows=normalizeImportedRows(matrix);if(!rows.length){toast('Tidak ada baris valid pada file import');return;}applyImportedDocuments(rows);}catch(e){console.error(e);toast('File import tidak dapat dibaca');}};reader.readAsText(file);};

  const baseDocumentDetail=window.documentDetail;
  window.documentDetail=function(id){const x=db.documents.find(d=>d.id===id);if(!x)return;openModal('Detail '+id,`<div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Customer / Recipient</label><div>${esc(x.customer)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Document Type</label><div>${x.type==='DO'?'Delivery Order':'Stock Transfer Out'}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Origin Hub</label><div>${esc(x.origin)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Destination</label><div>${esc(x.destination)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Dispatch Deadline</label><div class="mono">${esc(x.alert)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Priority</label><div>${statusBadge(x.priority)}</div></div><div class="field"><label>Weight</label><div>${Number(x.weight).toLocaleString()} kg</div></div><div class="field"><label>Volume</label><div>${x.volume} m³</div></div><div class="field"><label>SKU / Item Lines</label><div>${x.items} lines</div></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>`,true);};

  window.recommendationScore=function(group){const priorityMap={Urgent:60,High:50,Normal:25,Low:10},maxPriority=Math.max(...group.map(d=>priorityMap[d.priority]||25)),now=Date.now(),deadlines=group.map(d=>Date.parse(String(d.alert).replace(' ','T'))).filter(Number.isFinite),earliest=deadlines.length?Math.min(...deadlines):now+86400000,minutes=(earliest-now)/60000,urgency=minutes<=0?30:minutes<=240?25:minutes<=720?15:5,consolidation=Math.min(20,Math.max(0,(group.length-1)*10));return {total:maxPriority+urgency+consolidation,document:maxPriority,urgency,consolidation,minutes};};
  window.generateRecommendations=function(){
    const docs=db.documents.filter(x=>x.status==='Need Planning'),groups={};docs.forEach(d=>{const key=normalizeRouteName(d.destination);(groups[key]??=[]).push(d)});const recommendations=Object.values(groups).map(group=>({group,score:recommendationScore(group)})).sort((a,b)=>b.score.total-a.score.total||String(a.group[0].destination).localeCompare(String(b.group[0].destination))),box=document.getElementById('recommendations');if(!box)return;
    const intro=`<div class="reco-card" style="grid-column:1/-1"><h3>Auto Group Logic <span class="demo-count">${recommendations.length} groups</span></h3><div class="recommend-explain"><div><b>Document Priority — max 60</b>Urgent/High documents receive the largest score.</div><div><b>Dispatch Deadline — max 30</b>Overdue or near-deadline documents receive higher urgency.</div><div><b>Consolidation Benefit — max 20</b>More documents with the exact same destination improve efficiency.</div></div><div class="notice" style="margin:0">At least 10 recommendation groups are available from the 120-row testing dataset.</div></div>`;
    box.innerHTML=intro+recommendations.map((r,i)=>{const g=[...r.group],s=r.score,[label,cls]=recommendationLabel(s.total),origins=uniqueValues(g.map(x=>x.origin)),w=g.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),v=g.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0),highest=[...g].sort((a,b)=>Date.parse(a.alert)-Date.parse(b.alert))[0];return `<div class="reco-card"><h3>Group ${i+1} <span class="badge ${cls}">${label} • ${s.total}</span></h3><div class="destination-chip">${esc(g[0].destination)}</div><p style="font-size:10.5px;color:var(--muted);margin:5px 0 8px">${g.length} documents • ${origins.length} origin hub(s)</p>${g.slice(0,8).map(x=>`<div class="check-row" style="margin:5px 0"><input type="checkbox" checked disabled><span class="mono">${esc(x.id)}</span><span style="margin-left:auto">${statusBadge(x.priority)}</span></div>`).join('')}${g.length>8?`<div class="muted">+${g.length-8} more documents</div>`:''}<div style="border-top:1px solid var(--line);margin-top:9px;padding-top:7px"><div class="score-row"><span>Document priority</span><b>+${s.document}</b></div><div class="score-row"><span>Dispatch deadline (${esc(highest.alert)})</span><b>+${s.urgency}</b></div><div class="score-row"><span>Same-destination benefit</span><b>+${s.consolidation}</b></div></div><div class="notice" style="margin:9px 0">${w.toLocaleString()} kg • ${v.toFixed(1)} m³${origins.length>1?' • Hub consolidation required':''}</div><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick='openShipmentWizard(${JSON.stringify(g.map(x=>x.id))})'>Accept &amp; Plan</button></div>`;}).join('');
  };

  const baseActionList=window.actionList;
  window.actionList=function(kind,id){
    if(kind!=='plan')return baseActionList(kind,id);const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id),list=[{label:'View Detail',run:()=>planDetail(id)}];if(p?.status!=='Completed')list.push({label:'Edit Plan',run:()=>editPlan(id)});list.push({label:'Open Schedule',run:()=>goSchedulePlan(id)});if(p?.status==='Planned')list.push({label:'Start Loading',run:()=>setLoadingPlan(id)});if(p?.status!=='Completed')list.push({label:'Delete Plan',danger:true,run:()=>deletePlan(id)});return list;
  };
  window.editPlan=function(id){const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!p)return;if(p.status==='Completed'){toast('Completed plan bersifat read-only');return;}openModal('Edit '+id,`<div class="notice">Plan hanya dapat diedit selama status belum Completed.</div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Plan Number</label><input class="input" value="${esc(p.id)}" disabled></div><div class="field"><label>Dispatch Hub</label><select class="select" id="ep-hub">${db.hubs.filter(h=>h.status==='Active').map(h=>`<option ${h.name===(p.dispatchHub||p.origin)?'selected':''}>${esc(h.name)}</option>`).join('')}</select></div><div class="field"><label>Shipment Date</label><input class="input" id="ep-date" type="date" value="${p.shipmentDate}"></div><div class="field"><label>ETA</label><input class="input" id="ep-eta" type="date" value="${p.eta}"></div><div class="field"><label>Planned Cost</label><input class="input" id="ep-cost" type="number" value="${p.plannedCost}"></div><div class="field full"><label>Remark</label><textarea class="textarea" id="ep-remark">${esc(p.remark||'')}</textarea></div></div>`,`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="savePlanEdit('${esc(id)}')">Save Changes</button>`);};

  window.renderSchedule=function(){
    const start=isoDate(scheduleStart),days=[...Array(7)].map((_,i)=>dateISO(new Date(start.getTime()+i*86400000))),picker=document.getElementById('scheduleDatePicker');if(picker)picker.value=days[0];const range=document.getElementById('scheduleRange');if(range)range.textContent=`${days[0]} — ${days[6]}`;const sf=document.getElementById('scheduleSourceFilter')?.value||'',plans=db.plans.filter(p=>!sf||p.source===sf),resources=[];
    plans.forEach(p=>{const key=p.source==='Fleet Company'?`INT|${p.vehicle}|${p.driver}`:`EXP|${p.supplier}|${p.contract||'-'}`;if(!resources.some(r=>r.key===key))resources.push({key,source:p.source,vehicle:p.vehicle,driver:p.driver,supplier:p.supplier,contract:p.contract});});
    let html='<div class="schedule-grid"><div class="sch-cell sch-head">Resource</div>'+days.map(d=>`<div class="sch-cell sch-head">${new Date(d+'T00:00').toLocaleDateString('id-ID',{weekday:'short',day:'2-digit',month:'short'})}</div>`).join('');
    resources.forEach(r=>{let main='',sub='';if(r.source==='Fleet Company'){const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===r.vehicle);main=esc(r.vehicle);sub=`Internal Fleet • ${esc(r.driver)}${v?` • ${esc(v.type)}`:''}`;}else{main=esc(r.supplier);sub=`3PL • Contracted Carrier${r.contract&&r.contract!=='-'?` • ${esc(r.contract)}`:''}`;}html+=`<div class="sch-cell sch-resource"><span class="resource-main">${main}</span><small class="resource-sub">${sub}</small></div>`;days.forEach(d=>{const cards=plans.filter(p=>(p.source==='Fleet Company'?`INT|${p.vehicle}|${p.driver}`:`EXP|${p.supplier}|${p.contract||'-'}`)===r.key&&p.shipmentDate===d);html+=`<div class="sch-cell sch-day" ondragover="event.preventDefault();this.classList.add('dragover')" ondragleave="this.classList.remove('dragover')" ondrop="dropPlan(event,'${d}')">${cards.map(p=>`<div class="ship-card ${p.health==='Exception'?'exception':p.status==='Loading'||p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'?'loading':p.source==='Fleet Company'?'internal':'expedition'}" draggable="${['Planned','Draft'].includes(p.status)}" ondragstart="event.dataTransfer.setData('text','${p.id}')" onclick="planDetail('${p.id}')"><b>${p.id}</b><span>${esc(p.destination)} • ${p.util||'-'}%</span></div>`).join('')}</div>`;});});html+='</div>';const board=document.getElementById('scheduleBoard');if(board)board.innerHTML=html;
  };

  function driverMasterSnapshot(p,st){
    const d=currentDriverRecord(),v=p?db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle):null,route=p?(db.routes||[]).find(r=>r.id===p.routeLane||((r.origin===p.origin||r.origin===p.dispatchHub)&&String(p.destination).includes(r.destination))):null;const sim=expiryInfo(d?.expiry),stnk=expiryInfo(v?.stnkExpiry),kir=expiryInfo(v?.kirExpiry);return `<div class="master-sync-card"><h5>Master Data Snapshot</h5><div class="master-sync-grid"><div>Driver Identity<b>${esc(d?.identityStatus||'-')} • ${esc(d?.employmentStatus||'-')}</b></div><div>SIM Validity<b>${esc(d?.sim||'-')} • ${esc(d?.expiry||'-')} (${sim.days===null?'-':sim.days+' day(s)'})</b></div><div>Carrier / Pool<b>${esc(d?.carrier||'-')} • ${esc(d?.pool||'-')}</b></div><div>Registered Device<b>${esc(d?.deviceId||'-')}</b></div><div>Vehicle Identity<b>${esc(v?.identityVerification||'-')} • ${esc(v?.type||'-')}</b></div><div>STNK / KIR<b>${esc(stnk.status)} • ${esc(kir.status)}</b></div><div>Tank / Fuel Type<b>${Number(v?.tankCapacity||0)} L • ${esc(v?.fuelType||'-')}</b></div><div>Verified Odometer<b>${Number(v?.odometer||0).toLocaleString('id-ID')} km</b></div>${route?`<div>Lane / Delivery Hours<b>${esc(route.id)} • ${esc(route.window||'-')}</b></div>`:''}<div>Checker<b>${esc(st?.checkerName||p?.preLoadingCheck?.checkerName||'Not recorded')}</b><span class="table-note">Source: Loading &amp; Dispatch Pre-Loading Check</span></div></div></div>`;
  }
  window.handleIdentityEvidence=function(input){const p=driverPlan(),st=selectedDriverState(),file=input?.files?.[0];if(!p||!st||!file)return;st.identityAttachmentName=file.name;st.identityAttachmentType=file.type||'file';const status=document.getElementById('identityAttachmentStatus');if(status)status.textContent='Attached: '+file.name;if(file.size<=350000){const r=new FileReader();r.onload=()=>{st.identityAttachmentData=String(r.result||'');saveDB();};r.readAsDataURL(file);}saveDB();};
  window.updateFuelCapacityInfo=function(stage){const p=driverPlan(),v=p?db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle):null,capacity=Number(v?.tankCapacity||0),input=document.getElementById(stage==='start'?'fuelStartLiters':'fuelEndLiters'),box=document.getElementById(stage==='start'?'fuelCapacityStartInfo':'fuelCapacityEndInfo');if(!input||!box)return;const val=Number(input.value||0),pct=capacity?Math.round(val/capacity*100):0;box.className='capacity-info'+(capacity&&val>capacity?' danger':capacity&&pct>=90?' warn':'');box.innerHTML=capacity&&val>capacity?`Fuel ${val} L melebihi tank capacity ${capacity} L. Input tidak dapat disimpan.`:`Tank capacity ${capacity||'-'} L • Current fuel ${val||0} L (${pct||0}%)`;};
  window.updateTripDistance=function(){const st=selectedDriverState(),end=Number(document.getElementById('odometerEnd')?.value||0),box=document.getElementById('tripDistanceInfo');if(!box)return;const start=Number(st?.odometerStart||0),distance=end>=start?end-start:0;box.className='capacity-info'+(end&&end<start?' danger':'');box.innerHTML=end&&end<start?`End Odometer tidak boleh lebih kecil dari First Odometer ${start.toLocaleString('id-ID')} km.`:`Estimated trip distance: <span class="distance-result">${distance.toLocaleString('id-ID')} km</span>`;};

  window.linkedEntitySummary=function(p){const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver),v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle);return `<div class="linked-state"><div>Plan / Fleet Order<b>${esc(p.status)} / ${esc(fo?.status||'Not Created')}</b></div><div>Driver Master<b>${esc(d?.identityStatus||'-')} • SIM ${esc(d?.sim||'-')}</b></div><div>Vehicle Master<b>${esc(v?.identityVerification||'-')} • ${Number(v?.tankCapacity||0)} L</b></div></div>`;};

${esc(v?.fuelType||'')}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Master Odometer</span><b>${Number(v?.odometer||0).toLocaleString('id-ID')} km</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>STNK /   window.renderDriverTripWorkflow=function(p,st){const s=Number(st.step||0),fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),current=p.stops[Math.min(st.currentStop||0,p.stops.length-1)],vehicle=db.vehicles.find(v=>v.plate===p.vehicle),fleetMap=db.fleetMappings?.find(v=>v.id===p.vehicle),currentOdo=Number(st.odometerStart||fleetMap?.odometer||vehicle?.odometer||0),loaded=(p.loadedDocs||[]).length,allLoaded=loaded===p.docs.length,tank=Number(vehicle?.tankCapacity||0),startFuelLiters=st.fuelStartLiters!==undefined?st.fuelStartLiters:(st.fuelStart!==undefined&&tank?Number((Number(st.fuelStart)*tank/100).toFixed(1)):'');let html=`<div class="refresh-strip"><span>Shared live data • ${esc(p.lastUpdate||'-')}</span><button onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">↻ Refresh</button></div>`;
    if(s===0)html+=`${tripCard(p)}${driverMasterSnapshot(p,st)}<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('accept')">Accept Trip</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="driverAction('reject')">Reject with Reason</button>`;
    else if(s===1)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Pre-Trip Verification</h4><div class="identity-status-line"><span>Master Identity Status</span>${statusBadge(currentDriverRecord()?.identityStatus||'Pending Review')}</div><div class="identity-evidence"><label class="field-label-mobile">Attach Verify Identity</label><input class="input" type="file" accept="image/*,.pdf" capture="user" onchange="handleIdentityEvidence(this)"><div class="upload-status" id="identityAttachmentStatus">${st.identityAttachmentName?'Attached: '+esc(st.identityAttachmentName):'No identity evidence attached'}</div></div><input type="hidden" id="checkerName" value="${esc(st.checkerName||p.preLoadingCheck?.checkerName||'')}"><label class="field-label-mobile">First Odometer (km)</label><input class="input" id="odometerStart" type="number" min="0" value="${currentOdo||''}" placeholder="Input starting odometer" style="width:100%"><label class="field-label-mobile">First Fuel (liter)</label><input class="input" id="fuelStartLiters" type="number" min="0" max="${tank||9999}" step="0.1" value="${startFuelLiters}" placeholder="Input fuel in liter" style="width:100%" oninput="updateFuelCapacityInfo('start')"><div class="capacity-info" id="fuelCapacityStartInfo">Tank capacity ${tank||'-'} L • input fuel in liter</div>${['Tyre','Brake','Lights','Body condition','STNK / KIR validity'].map(x=>`<label class="check-row" style="padding:5px 0"><input type="checkbox" class="precheck">${x}</label>`).join('')}</div>${driverMasterSnapshot(p,st)}<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('check')">Submit Pre-Trip Verification</button>`;
    else if(s===2)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Warehouse Loading Status</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Plan Status</span><b>${p.status}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Documents Loaded</span><b>${loaded}/${p.docs.length}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Checker</span><b>${esc(st.checkerName||p.preLoadingCheck?.checkerName||'-')}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Gate Readiness</span><b>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'Ready':'Waiting Warehouse'}</b></div></div>${p.status==='Ready to Dispatch'&&allLoaded?'<button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction(\'loading\')">Confirm Load Received</button>':'<button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Loading &amp; Dispatch Module</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">Refresh Status</button>'}`;
    else if(s===3)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="notice" style="margin:10px 13px">Load confirmed. Gate operator must perform Gate-Out / Dispatch from Loading &amp; Dispatch.</div><button class="phone-btn wait" disabled>Waiting Gate-Out</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="refreshDriverMobile()">Refresh Status</button>`;
    else if(s===4)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Next Stop ${Math.min((st.currentStop||0)+1,p.stops.length)} / ${p.stops.length}</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Customer / Recipient</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Document</span><b>${esc(current.doc)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(current.destination||p.destination)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>ETA</span><b>${p.eta} 14:30</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('arrive')">Arrived at Stop</button><button class="phone-btn ghost" onclick="setMobileView('route')">View Route</button>`;
    else if(s===5)html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card phone-stop"><h4>Arrival Confirmed</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Stop</span><b>${esc(current.customer)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>Geofence</span><b>Inside delivery radius</b></div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('unload')">Start Unloading</button>`;
    else if(s===6)html+=renderPodForm(p,st);
    else if(s===7){const endFuel=st.fuelEndLiters??'';html+=`${tripCard(p)}<div class="phone-card"><h4>Return to Origin &amp; Final Odometer</h4><div class="phone-row"><span>Destination</span><b>${esc(p.origin)}</b></div><div class="phone-row"><span>All Stops</span><b>${p.stops.filter(x=>x.pod).length}/${p.stops.length} ePOD</b></div><label class="field-label-mobile">First Odometer</label><input class="input" value="${st.odometerStart??''}" disabled style="width:100%"><label class="field-label-mobile">End Odometer</label><input class="input" id="odometerEnd" type="number" min="0" value="${st.odometerEnd??''}" placeholder="End Odometer" style="width:100%" oninput="updateTripDistance()"><div class="capacity-info" id="tripDistanceInfo">End Odometer must be equal to or greater than First Odometer.</div><label class="field-label-mobile">End Fuel (liter)</label><input class="input" id="fuelEndLiters" type="number" min="0" max="${tank||9999}" step="0.1" value="${endFuel}" placeholder="Fuel at return" style="width:100%" oninput="updateFuelCapacityInfo('end')"><div class="capacity-info" id="fuelCapacityEndInfo">Tank capacity ${tank||'-'} L • input fuel in liter</div></div><button class="phone-btn" onclick="driverAction('close')">Arrived at Origin &amp; Close Trip</button>`;}
    else html+='<div class="phone-card" style="text-align:center;margin-top:60px"><div style="font-size:44px;color:var(--green)">✓</div><h4>Trip Completed</h4><p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--muted)">'+esc(p.id)+' is closed and resources are available again.</p></div>';return {html,needsSignature:s===6};
  };

  const baseDriverAction=window.driverAction;
  window.driverAction=function(a){const p=driverPlan(),st=selectedDriverState();if(!p||!st)return;const fo=fleetOrderForPlan(p.id),driver=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver),vehicle=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle),tank=Number(vehicle?.tankCapacity||0);
    if(a==='check'){
      if([...document.querySelectorAll('.precheck')].some(x=>!x.checked)){toast('Seluruh validity checklist wajib diisi');return;}const identity=currentDriverRecord()?.identityStatus||'Pending Review';if(identity==='Rejected'){toast('Driver Identity di Master berstatus Rejected');return;}if(!st.identityAttachmentName){toast('Attach Verify Identity wajib diisi');return;}const checker=st.checkerName||p.preLoadingCheck?.checkerName||document.getElementById('checkerName')?.value.trim()||'';if(!checker||p.preLoadingCheck?.status!=='Passed'){toast('Complete Checking di Loading & Dispatch terlebih dahulu agar Checker tersinkron otomatis');return;}const odoRaw=document.getElementById('odometerStart')?.value||'',fuelRaw=document.getElementById('fuelStartLiters')?.value||'';if(odoRaw===''){toast('First Odometer wajib diisi');return;}if(fuelRaw===''){toast('First Fuel wajib diisi');return;}const odo=Number(odoRaw),fuelLiters=Number(fuelRaw);if(odo<Number(vehicle?.odometer||0)){toast('First Odometer tidak boleh lebih kecil dari Verified Odometer di Vehicle Master');return;}if(fuelLiters<0||(tank&&fuelLiters>tank)){toast(`Fuel ${fuelLiters} L melebihi tank capacity ${tank} L`);return;}st.checkerName=checker;st.odometerStart=odo;st.fuelStartLiters=fuelLiters;st.fuelStart=tank?Math.round(fuelLiters/tank*100):0;st.preTrip=true;st.step=2;p.lastUpdate=`Pre-trip verified by ${checker} • ${odo.toLocaleString('id-ID')} km • ${fuelLiters} L`;integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'driver.pretrip.completed',`Identity evidence, checker ${checker}, odometer, and fuel capacity verified`,'McEasy → Prieds');saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('Pre-trip verification synchronized');return;
    }
    if(a==='close'){
      const endRaw=document.getElementById('odometerEnd')?.value||'',fuelRaw=document.getElementById('fuelEndLiters')?.value||'';if(endRaw===''){toast('End Odometer wajib diisi');return;}if(fuelRaw===''){toast('End Fuel wajib diisi');return;}const end=Number(endRaw),fuelLiters=Number(fuelRaw),start=Number(st.odometerStart||0);if(end<start){toast('End Odometer tidak boleh lebih kecil dari First Odometer');return;}if(fuelLiters<0||(tank&&fuelLiters>tank)){toast(`Fuel ${fuelLiters} L melebihi tank capacity ${tank} L`);return;}st.odometerEnd=end;st.tripDistance=end-start;st.fuelEndLiters=fuelLiters;st.fuelEnd=tank?Math.round(fuelLiters/tank*100):0;st.step=8;st.closed=true;p.status='Completed';p.health=p.stops.every(x=>x.status==='Successfully Delivered')?'Completed':'Exception';p.actualCost=p.actualCost||Math.round(p.plannedCost*1.04);p.lastUpdate=`Trip closed • ${end.toLocaleString('id-ID')} km • distance ${st.tripDistance.toLocaleString('id-ID')} km`;if(driver)driver.status='Available';if(vehicle){vehicle.status='Available';vehicle.odometer=end;}const fm=db.fleetMappings?.find(x=>x.id===p.vehicle);if(fm)fm.odometer=end;if(fo){fo.status='Delivered';fo.updated='Trip closed';fo.lastLocation=p.origin;}integrationEvent('Shipment',p.id,'trip.closed',`Trip closed; end odometer ${end}; distance ${st.tripDistance} km`,'McEasy → Prieds');saveDB();renderAll();renderDriverMobile();toast('Trip closed and odometer synchronized to Vehicle Master');return;
    }
    baseDriverAction(a);
  };

  // Ensure no OTP field is rendered in Driver Mobile. ePOD uses photo, receiver name, and signature only.
  const baseRenderPodForm=window.renderPodForm;
  window.renderPodForm=function(p,st){return baseRenderPodForm(p,st).replace(/OTP[^<\"]*/gi,'').replace(/placeholder="[^"]*OTP[^"]*"/gi,'');};

  document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item[data-page]').forEach(b=>{b.onclick=()=>goPage(b.dataset.page);});
  try{renderAll();const initialIntegratedPage=location.hash.replace('#','');goPage(document.getElementById('page-'+initialIntegratedPage)?initialIntegratedPage:(document.body.dataset.initialPage||'hub'));generateRecommendations();}catch(e){console.error('Operational alignment initialization:',e);}
})();

(function operationalRiskCompatibilityV7(){
  'use strict';
  function expiredAt(date,reference){if(!date||!reference)return false;return String(date)<String(reference)}
  window.runOperationalRiskValidation=function(scope='all',silent=false){
    if(typeof rcEnsureData==='function')rcEnsureData();
    // Migration: duplicate source-document usage is allowed. Clear legacy events so old localStorage data cannot keep Loading blocked.
    (db.riskEvents||[]).filter(event=>['DUPLICATE_SOURCE_DOCUMENT','DUPLICATE_DOCUMENT'].includes(event.rule)).forEach(event=>{event.status='Cleared';event.blocking=false;});
    const scopes=scope==='all'?['Shipment Planning','Shipment Schedule','Loading & Dispatch','Monitoring Shipment','Driver Mobile']:[scope];scopes.forEach(x=>rcClearScope(x));
    if(scopes.includes('Shipment Planning')){
      const active=(db.plans||[]).filter(p=>!['Completed','Cancelled'].includes(p.status));
      active.forEach(p=>{
        // Reusing the same DO/STO in multiple active plans is permitted.
        // Do not emit DUPLICATE_SOURCE_DOCUMENT as an issue or blocking validation.
        if(Number(p.util||0)>100)rcEmit({rule:'VEHICLE_CAPACITY_EXCEEDED',sourceModule:'Shipment Planning',sourceType:'Shipment Planning',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Vehicle capacity exceeded',negativeCase:`Utilization ${p.util}% melebihi kapasitas kendaraan.`,expectedCondition:'Weight and volume utilization must be at or below 100%.',actualCondition:`${p.util}%`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:p.vehicle||p.id});
        if(p.source==='Fleet Company'){
          const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle),d=db.drivers.find(x=>x.name===p.driver);
          if(!v||!d)rcEmit({rule:'MASTER_RESOURCE_MISSING',sourceModule:'Shipment Planning',sourceType:'Shipment Planning',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Assigned resource is missing from Master',negativeCase:'Vehicle atau Driver assignment tidak ditemukan di Master.',expectedCondition:'Assigned vehicle and driver must exist in active Master data.',actualCondition:`Vehicle ${p.vehicle}; Driver ${p.driver}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:p.id});
          if(v&&(expiredAt(v.stnkExpiry,p.shipmentDate)||expiredAt(v.kirExpiry,p.shipmentDate)))rcEmit({rule:'VEHICLE_DOCUMENT_EXPIRED',sourceModule:'Shipment Planning',sourceType:'Shipment Planning',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Vehicle document is not valid for shipment date',negativeCase:`STNK ${v.stnkExpiry}; KIR ${v.kirExpiry}; trip ${p.shipmentDate}.`,expectedCondition:'STNK and KIR must be valid on shipment date.',actualCondition:`STNK ${v.stnkExpiry}; KIR ${v.kirExpiry}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:v.id});
          if(d&&(expiredAt(d.expiry,p.shipmentDate)||d.identityStatus!=='Verified'||d.employmentStatus!=='Active'))rcEmit({rule:'DRIVER_NOT_ELIGIBLE',sourceModule:'Shipment Planning',sourceType:'Shipment Planning',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Driver is not eligible for assignment',negativeCase:`SIM ${d.expiry}; Identity ${d.identityStatus}; Employment ${d.employmentStatus}.`,expectedCondition:'SIM valid, identity verified, and employment active.',actualCondition:`${d.expiry} / ${d.identityStatus} / ${d.employmentStatus}.`,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:d.id});
        }else{
          const c=db.contracts.find(x=>x.id===p.contract),carrier=db.carriers.find(x=>x.name===p.supplier);if(!c||c.status!=='Active'||expiredAt(c.endDate,p.shipmentDate))rcEmit({rule:'CONTRACT_NOT_ACTIVE',sourceModule:'Shipment Planning',sourceType:'Shipment Planning',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Carrier contract is not active',negativeCase:`Contract ${p.contract||'-'} tidak aktif pada tanggal ${p.shipmentDate}.`,expectedCondition:'Contract must be active and cover the shipment date.',actualCondition:c?`${c.status}; ${c.startDate} to ${c.endDate}`:'Contract not found.',severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:p.contract||p.supplier});if(carrier&&(expiredAt(carrier.permitExpiry,p.shipmentDate)||expiredAt(carrier.insuranceExpiry,p.shipmentDate)))rcEmit({rule:'CARRIER_COMPLIANCE_EXPIRED',sourceModule:'Shipment Planning',sourceType:'Shipment Planning',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Carrier permit or insurance expired',negativeCase:`Permit ${carrier.permitExpiry}; Insurance ${carrier.insuranceExpiry}.`,expectedCondition:'Carrier permit and insurance must be valid.',actualCondition:`Permit ${carrier.permitExpiry}; Insurance ${carrier.insuranceExpiry}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:carrier.id});
        }
      });
    }
    if(scopes.includes('Shipment Schedule')){const active=(db.plans||[]).filter(p=>!['Completed','Cancelled'].includes(p.status));active.forEach((p,i)=>active.slice(i+1).forEach(q=>{if(p.shipmentDate===q.shipmentDate&&p.source==='Fleet Company'&&q.source==='Fleet Company'&&p.vehicle===q.vehicle)rcEmit({rule:'VEHICLE_SCHEDULE_OVERLAP',sourceModule:'Shipment Schedule',sourceType:'Shipment Schedule',sourceRef:p.id,relatedRefs:[q.id],title:'Vehicle schedule overlap',negativeCase:`${p.vehicle} digunakan oleh ${p.id} dan ${q.id} pada ${p.shipmentDate}.`,expectedCondition:'One vehicle cannot be assigned to overlapping active plans.',actualCondition:`${p.id} / ${q.id}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:p.vehicle});if(p.shipmentDate===q.shipmentDate&&p.source==='Fleet Company'&&q.source==='Fleet Company'&&p.driver===q.driver)rcEmit({rule:'DRIVER_SCHEDULE_OVERLAP',sourceModule:'Shipment Schedule',sourceType:'Shipment Schedule',sourceRef:p.id,relatedRefs:[q.id],title:'Driver schedule overlap',negativeCase:`${p.driver} digunakan oleh ${p.id} dan ${q.id} pada ${p.shipmentDate}.`,expectedCondition:'One driver cannot be assigned to overlapping active plans.',actualCondition:`${p.id} / ${q.id}.`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:p.driver});}));}
    if(scopes.includes('Loading & Dispatch'))(db.plans||[]).filter(p=>['Ready to Dispatch','In Transit'].includes(p.status)).forEach(p=>{if((p.loadedDocs||[]).length!==(p.docs||[]).length)rcEmit({rule:'INCOMPLETE_LOADING',sourceModule:'Loading & Dispatch',sourceType:'Loading & Dispatch',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Shipment status advanced with incomplete loading',negativeCase:`Loaded ${(p.loadedDocs||[]).length} of ${(p.docs||[]).length} documents.`,expectedCondition:'All shipment documents must be validated before dispatch.',actualCondition:`${(p.loadedDocs||[]).length}/${(p.docs||[]).length}`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:p.id});});
    if(scopes.includes('Monitoring Shipment'))(db.plans||[]).filter(p=>['In Transit','Unloading','Returning'].includes(p.status)&&['Exception','At Risk'].includes(p.health)).forEach(p=>rcEmit({rule:'ACTIVE_SHIPMENT_EXCEPTION',sourceModule:'Monitoring Shipment',sourceType:'Monitoring Shipment',sourceRef:p.id,title:'Active shipment requires attention',negativeCase:`${p.id} berstatus ${p.status} dengan health ${p.health}.`,expectedCondition:'Active shipment health remains On Schedule.',actualCondition:p.health,severity:'High',blocking:false,sourceRecord:p.id}));
    if(scopes.includes('Driver Mobile'))Object.entries(db.driverStates||{}).forEach(([id,st])=>{const p=db.plans.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!p)return;const v=db.vehicles.find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle),cap=Number(v?.tankCapacity||0);const syncedChecker=st.checkerName||p.preLoadingCheck?.checkerName||'';if(st.preTrip&&(!st.identityAttachmentName||!syncedChecker))rcEmit({rule:'PRETRIP_EVIDENCE_INCOMPLETE',sourceModule:'Driver Mobile',sourceType:'Driver Mobile',sourceRef:id,title:'Pre-trip identity evidence is incomplete',negativeCase:`Identity attachment ${st.identityAttachmentName?'available':'missing'}; Loading & Dispatch checker ${syncedChecker||'missing'}.`,expectedCondition:'Identity attachment is required and checker must be synchronized from a completed Pre-Loading Check.',actualCondition:`Attachment ${st.identityAttachmentName||'-'}; Checker ${syncedChecker||'-'}.`,severity:'High',blocking:true,sourceRecord:id});if(cap&&Number(st.fuelStartLiters||0)>cap)rcEmit({rule:'FUEL_CAPACITY_EXCEEDED',sourceModule:'Driver Mobile',sourceType:'Driver Mobile',sourceRef:id,title:'Fuel input exceeds vehicle tank capacity',negativeCase:`Input ${st.fuelStartLiters} L exceeds ${cap} L.`,expectedCondition:'Fuel input must not exceed Vehicle Master tank capacity.',actualCondition:`${st.fuelStartLiters} L / ${cap} L`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:v?.id||p.vehicle});if(st.odometerEnd!==undefined&&Number(st.odometerEnd)<Number(st.odometerStart||0))rcEmit({rule:'ODOMETER_SEQUENCE_INVALID',sourceModule:'Driver Mobile',sourceType:'Driver Mobile',sourceRef:id,title:'End odometer is below first odometer',negativeCase:`First ${st.odometerStart}; End ${st.odometerEnd}.`,expectedCondition:'End Odometer must be equal to or greater than First Odometer.',actualCondition:`${st.odometerStart} → ${st.odometerEnd}`,severity:'Critical',blocking:true,sourceRecord:id});});
    saveDB();installOperationalRiskBanners();if(document.getElementById('planTbody'))renderPlans();if(!silent){const count=scopes.reduce((n,x)=>n+rcEventsFor(x).length,0);toast(`${count} open operational risk event(s) found`);}return scopes.reduce((n,x)=>n+rcEventsFor(x).length,0);
  };
  window.installOperationalRiskBanners=function(){
    rcInstallBanner('planning','Shipment Planning','Master & Planning Validation',`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runOperationalRiskValidation('Shipment Planning')">Run Validation</button><button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="rcOpenEvents('Shipment Planning')">View Issues</button>`);
    rcInstallBanner('schedule','Shipment Schedule','Resource Conflict Control',`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runOperationalRiskValidation('Shipment Schedule')">Check Conflicts</button>`);
    rcInstallBanner('loading','Loading & Dispatch','Loading Completeness Control',`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runOperationalRiskValidation('Loading & Dispatch')">Run Validation</button>`);
    rcInstallBanner('monitoring','Monitoring Shipment','Active Shipment Risk Monitoring',`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runOperationalRiskValidation('Monitoring Shipment')">Run Detection</button>`);
    rcInstallBanner('driver-mobile','Driver Mobile','Identity, Fuel & Odometer Control',`<button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runOperationalRiskValidation('Driver Mobile')">Validate Mobile Controls</button>`);
  };
  const operationalRiskBaseRenderPlans=window.renderPlans;
  window.renderPlans=function(){operationalRiskBaseRenderPlans();const tb=document.getElementById('planTbody'),table=tb?.closest('table'),head=table?.querySelector('thead tr');if(!tb||!head)return;if(!head.querySelector('[data-operational-risk]'))head.lastElementChild.insertAdjacentHTML('beforebegin','<th data-operational-risk>Risk Control</th>');const q=(document.getElementById('planSearch')?.value||'').toLowerCase(),st=document.getElementById('planStatusFilter')?.value||'',rows=db.plans.filter(x=>(!st||x.status===st)&&JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q));[...tb.querySelectorAll('tr')].forEach((tr,i)=>{if(tr.querySelector('.empty')){tr.firstElementChild.colSpan=11;return;}const p=rows[i];if(!p||tr.querySelector('[data-operational-risk]'))return;const ev=rcEventsFor('Shipment Planning',p.id),td=document.createElement('td');td.setAttribute('data-operational-risk','');td.innerHTML=rcBadge(ev);tr.lastElementChild.insertAdjacentElement('beforebegin',td);});};
  try{runOperationalRiskValidation('all',true);installOperationalRiskBanners();renderPlans();}catch(e){console.warn('Operational risk compatibility:',e);}
})();

(function(){
  'use strict';
  function refreshCurrentIntegratedPage(){
    const current=document.querySelector('.page.active')?.id?.replace('page-','')||'hub';
    try{
      if(current==='hub') renderMaster('hubs');
      if(current==='carrier'){renderMaster('carriers');renderMaster('contracts');}
      if(current==='vehicle') renderMaster('vehicles');
      if(current==='maintenance') renderMaintenance();
      if(current==='driver') renderMaster('drivers');
      if(current==='route') renderMaster('routes');
      if(current==='planning'){renderDocuments();renderPlans();}
      if(current==='schedule') renderSchedule();
      if(current==='loading') renderLoading();
      if(current==='monitoring') renderMonitoring();
      if(current==='driver-mobile') renderDriverMobile();
    }catch(e){console.warn('Integrated page refresh skipped:',e);}
  }
  const originalIntegratedSaveDB=window.saveDB;
  if(typeof originalIntegratedSaveDB==='function'){
    window.saveDB=function(){
      originalIntegratedSaveDB();
      setTimeout(refreshCurrentIntegratedPage,0);
    };
  }
  document.querySelectorAll('.topbar-right').forEach(el=>{
    if(!el.querySelector('.integrated-sync-pill')){
      const pill=document.createElement('span');
      pill.className='integrated-sync-pill';
      pill.textContent='Master ↔ Operational';
      el.insertBefore(pill,el.firstChild);
    }
  });
  const requested=location.hash.replace('#','');
  try{goPage(document.getElementById('page-'+requested)?requested:(document.body.dataset.initialPage||'hub'));}catch(e){console.error('Integrated initialization:',e);}
})();
