(function(){
  const baseRenderReport=window.renderReport;
  const baseRenderIntegration=window.renderIntegration;
  const baseRenderAll=window.renderAll;
  let activeReportTab='performance';

  PAGE_NAMES.dashboard='Overview Dashboard';PAGE_NAMES.report='Report Center';PAGE_NAMES.antifraud='Risk & Anti-Fraud';

  window.reportCenterTab=function(tab,btn){
    activeReportTab=tab;
    document.querySelectorAll('.report-panel').forEach(x=>x.classList.toggle('active',x.id==='report-panel-'+tab));
    document.querySelectorAll('.report-tab').forEach(x=>x.classList.toggle('active',x.dataset.reportTab===tab));
    if(tab==='driver')renderDriverHistoryReport();
    if(tab==='delivery')renderDeliveryReport();
    if(tab==='fleet')renderFleetMaintenanceReport();
    if(tab==='cost')renderCostDetailReport();
  };

  function ensureDriverHistoryData(){
    ensureDriverStates();
    db.driverMobileHistory=db.driverMobileHistory||{};
    if(!db._suiteHistorySeeded){
      const drivers=(db.drivers||[]).filter(x=>x.username),vehicles=db.vehicles||[],routes=db.routes||[];
      for(let i=0;i<12;i++){const d=drivers[i%Math.max(1,drivers.length)]||{},v=vehicles[i%Math.max(1,vehicles.length)]||{},route=routes[i%Math.max(1,routes.length)]||{},dist=Number(route.distance||38+(i%4)*17),end=Math.max(1000,Number(v.odometer||55000)-(11-i)*dist),start=end-dist,stops=1+(i%3),success=stops-(i%5===0?1:0),tank=Number(v.tankCapacity||80),fuelStart=Math.max(20,Math.round(tank*(.65+(i%3)*.08))),fuelEnd=Math.max(5,fuelStart-Math.round(dist*.18)),day=String(8+i).padStart(2,'0'),planId='HIST/DRV/'+String(i+1).padStart(4,'0'),stopDetails=Array.from({length:stops},(_,j)=>({doc:'DO/HIST/'+String(i+1).padStart(3,'0')+'/'+String(j+1).padStart(2,'0'),customer:(route.destination||route.to||'Delivery Point')+' Stop '+(j+1),status:j<success?'Successfully Delivered':'Unsuccessfully Delivered',receiver:j<success?['Budi','Sari','Andi','Maya'][j%4]:'-',arrival:`2026-06-${day} ${String(10+j).padStart(2,'0')}:2${j}`,pod:j<success,podPhotoName:j<success?'pod-'+(i+1)+'-'+(j+1)+'.jpg':'-',signatureRef:j<success?'Receiver Signature':'-',deliveryReason:j<success?'':'Customer unavailable'}));db.driverMobileHistory[planId]={planId,shipmentDate:`2026-06-${day}`,driver:d.name||'Demo Driver',username:d.username||'driver.mobile',vehicle:v.plate||'B 9000 TMS',carrier:v.carrier||d.carrier||'-',pool:v.pool||d.pool||'-',route:route.id||'LANE-HIST',origin:route.origin||route.from||'Origin Hub',destination:route.destination||route.to||'Destination Hub',checker:['Dedi Warehouse','Rina Checker','Agus Gate'][i%3],identityAttachment:'identity-'+(d.id||String(i+1)).toLowerCase()+'.jpg',identityStatus:d.identityVerification||d.identityStatus||'Verified',odometerStart:start,odometerEnd:end,fuelStartLiters:fuelStart,fuelEndLiters:fuelEnd,tankCapacity:tank,status:'Completed',actualCost:750000+i*85000,plannedCost:700000+i*80000,health:success===stops?'Completed':'Exception',stops,success,pod:success,exceptions:stops-success,lastUpdate:'Historical trip closed from Driver Mobile',stopDetails};}
      db._suiteHistorySeeded=true;
    }
    (db.plans||[]).filter(p=>p.source==='Fleet Company').forEach((p,idx)=>{
      const st=db.driverStates[p.id]||{},v=(db.vehicles||[]).find(x=>x.plate===p.vehicle),d=(db.drivers||[]).find(x=>x.name===p.driver),route=(db.routes||[]).find(x=>x.id===p.route),completed=p.status==='Completed';
      const baseOdo=Number(v?.odometer||40000+idx*2500),distance=Number(route?.distance||Math.max(12,(p.stops||[]).length*18));
      if(completed&&st.odometerStart===undefined)st.odometerStart=Math.max(0,baseOdo-distance);
      if(completed&&st.odometerEnd===undefined)st.odometerEnd=baseOdo;
      if(completed&&st.fuelStartLiters===undefined)st.fuelStartLiters=Math.round(Number(v?.tankCapacity||80)*.78);
      if(completed&&st.fuelEndLiters===undefined)st.fuelEndLiters=Math.max(4,Math.round(Number(st.fuelStartLiters||50)-distance*.22));
      if(completed&&!st.checkerName)st.checkerName=['Dedi Warehouse','Rina Checker','Agus Gate'][idx%3];
      if(completed&&!st.identityAttachmentName)st.identityAttachmentName=`identity-${(d?.id||'driver').toLowerCase()}.jpg`;
      if(completed)st.closed=true;
      db.driverStates[p.id]=st;
      db.driverMobileHistory[p.id]={planId:p.id,shipmentDate:p.shipmentDate,driver:p.driver||'-',username:d?.username||'-',vehicle:p.vehicle||'-',carrier:v?.carrier||'-',pool:v?.pool||'-',route:p.route||p.destination,origin:p.origin,destination:p.destination,checker:st.checkerName||'-',identityAttachment:st.identityAttachmentName||'-',identityStatus:d?.identityVerification||d?.identityStatus||'Pending Review',odometerStart:st.odometerStart,odometerEnd:st.odometerEnd,fuelStartLiters:st.fuelStartLiters,fuelEndLiters:st.fuelEndLiters,tankCapacity:Number(v?.tankCapacity||0),status:p.status,actualCost:Number(p.actualCost||0),plannedCost:Number(p.plannedCost||0),health:p.health||'-',stops:(p.stops||[]).length,success:(p.stops||[]).filter(s=>s.status==='Successfully Delivered').length,pod:(p.stops||[]).filter(s=>s.pod).length,exceptions:(p.stops||[]).filter(s=>s.status&&s.status!=='Successfully Delivered').length,lastUpdate:p.lastUpdate||'-'};
    });
    saveDB();
    return Object.values(db.driverMobileHistory);
  }
  function driverRows(){return ensureDriverHistoryData().sort((a,b)=>String(b.shipmentDate).localeCompare(String(a.shipmentDate)));}
  function recordDistance(r){const a=Number(r.odometerStart),b=Number(r.odometerEnd);return Number.isFinite(a)&&Number.isFinite(b)&&b>=a?b-a:0;}
  function reportFilter(rows,q,status){q=(q||'').toLowerCase();return rows.filter(x=>(!status||x.status===status)&&(!q||JSON.stringify(x).toLowerCase().includes(q)));}

  window.renderDriverHistoryReport=function(){
    const body=document.getElementById('driverHistoryTbody');if(!body)return;
    const all=driverRows(),rows=reportFilter(all,document.getElementById('driverHistorySearch')?.value,document.getElementById('driverHistoryStatus')?.value);
    const completed=all.filter(x=>x.status==='Completed'),distance=all.reduce((a,x)=>a+recordDistance(x),0),epod=all.reduce((a,x)=>a+x.pod,0),stops=all.reduce((a,x)=>a+x.stops,0);
    document.getElementById('driverHistoryKpis').innerHTML=kpiCards([{l:'Recorded Trips',v:all.length,f:'Driver Mobile assignments',a:'var(--blue)'},{l:'Completed',v:completed.length,f:'Closed from mobile workflow',a:'var(--green)'},{l:'Recorded Distance',v:distance.toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km',f:'End minus first odometer',a:'var(--purple)'},{l:'ePOD Completion',v:(stops?Math.round(epod/stops*100):0)+'%',f:`${epod}/${stops} delivery stops`,a:'var(--cyan-dark)'},{l:'Trips with Exception',v:all.filter(x=>x.exceptions>0).length,f:'Non-success stop result',a:'var(--orange)'}]);
    body.innerHTML=rows.map(r=>{const dist=recordDistance(r),delivery=`${r.success}/${r.stops}`,pod=`${r.pod}/${r.stops}`;return `<tr><td><button class="link-cell" onclick="driverHistoryDetail('${esc(r.planId)}')">${esc(r.planId)}</button><div class="report-mini">${esc(r.lastUpdate)}</div></td><td>${esc(r.shipmentDate||'-')}</td><td><b>${esc(r.driver)}</b><div class="muted">${esc(r.username)}</div></td><td><b>${esc(r.vehicle)}</b><div class="muted">${esc(r.carrier)} • ${esc(r.pool)}</div></td><td>${esc(r.origin||'-')} → ${esc(r.destination||'-')}<div class="muted">${esc(r.route||'-')}</div></td><td>${esc(r.checker)}</td><td>${r.identityAttachment!=='-'?'<span class="badge b-green">Attached</span>':'<span class="badge b-orange">Missing</span>'}<div class="report-mini">${esc(r.identityStatus)} • ${esc(r.identityAttachment)}</div></td><td>${r.odometerStart!==undefined?Number(r.odometerStart).toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km':'-'}</td><td>${r.odometerEnd!==undefined?Number(r.odometerEnd).toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km':'-'}</td><td>${dist?dist.toLocaleString('id-ID')+' km':'-'}</td><td>${r.fuelStartLiters!==undefined?Number(r.fuelStartLiters)+' L':'-'} / ${r.fuelEndLiters!==undefined?Number(r.fuelEndLiters)+' L':'-'}<div class="report-mini">Tank ${r.tankCapacity||'-'} L</div></td><td>${delivery}<div class="report-mini">successful / stops</div></td><td>${pod}</td><td>${r.exceptions?`<span class="badge b-red">${r.exceptions}</span>`:'<span class="badge b-green">0</span>'}</td><td>${fmtIDR(r.actualCost||r.plannedCost||0)}</td><td>${statusBadge(r.status)}</td><td><button class="icon-btn" onclick="driverHistoryDetail('${esc(r.planId)}')">Detail</button></td></tr>`}).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="17" class="empty">No Driver Mobile history found.</td></tr>';
  };

<script>
/* ===== Operational Revision: Remove Plate Filter + Preserve POD Draft + First Odometer Barrier ===== */
(function operationalDriverGuardRevision(){
  function validOdometerValue(value){
    return value !== undefined && value !== null && String(value).trim() !== '' && Number.isFinite(Number(value));
  }

  window.ensureFirstOdometerState=function(plan,state){
    if(!plan||!state)return null;
    if(validOdometerValue(state.odometerStart))return Number(state.odometerStart);
    const vehicle=(db.vehicles||[]).find(x=>x.plate===plan.vehicle);
    const fleetMap=(db.fleetMappings||[]).find(x=>x.id===plan.vehicle||x.plate===plan.vehicle);
    const fallback=[fleetMap?.odometer,vehicle?.odometer].find(validOdometerValue);
    if(fallback===undefined)return null;
    state.odometerStart=Number(fallback);
    return state.odometerStart;
  };

  const baseRenderDriverTripWorkflow=window.renderDriverTripWorkflow;
  window.renderDriverTripWorkflow=function(plan,state){
    ensureFirstOdometerState(plan,state);
    return baseRenderDriverTripWorkflow(plan,state);
  };

  const baseRenderMobileProfile=window.renderMobileProfile;
  window.renderMobileProfile=function(plan,state){
    if(plan&&state)ensureFirstOdometerState(plan,state);
    return baseRenderMobileProfile(plan,state);
  };

  const baseDriverActionWithMasterValidation=window.driverAction;
  window.driverAction=function(action){
    const plan=driverPlan(),state=selectedDriverState();
    if(action==='close'){
      const first=ensureFirstOdometerState(plan,state);
      if(first===null){
        toast('First Odometer wajib tersedia sebelum trip dapat ditutup');
        return;
      }
    }
    return baseDriverActionWithMasterValidation(action);
  };

  const baseOperationalRiskValidation=window.runOperationalRiskValidation;
  window.runOperationalRiskValidation=function(scope,silent=false){
    const result=baseOperationalRiskValidation(scope,silent);
    const scopes=scope?[scope]:['Shipment Planning','Shipment Schedule','Loading & Dispatch','Monitoring Shipment','Driver Mobile'];
    if(scopes.includes('Driver Mobile')){
      Object.entries(db.driverStates||{}).forEach(([planId,state])=>{
        const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(x=>x.id===planId);
        if(!plan)return;
        const first=ensureFirstOdometerState(plan,state);
        if(state.step>=2&&first===null&&typeof rcEmit==='function'){
          rcEmit({
            rule:'FIRST_ODOMETER_MISSING',
            sourceModule:'Driver Mobile',
            sourceType:'Driver Mobile',
            sourceRef:planId,
            title:'First Odometer is mandatory',
            negativeCase:`${planId} sudah melewati Pre-Trip tetapi First Odometer kosong.`,
            expectedCondition:'First Odometer wajib tercatat sebelum Loading, Dispatch, ePOD, dan Close Trip.',
            actualCondition:'First Odometer tidak tersedia pada Driver State maupun Vehicle Master.',
            severity:'Critical',
            blocking:true,
            sourceRecord:planId
          });
        }
      });
      saveDB();
      if(typeof installOperationalRiskBanners==='function')installOperationalRiskBanners();
    }
    return result;
  };
})();
</script>

<script>
(function modularNavigation(){
  const initial = (location.hash || '').replace('#','') || document.body.dataset.initialPage;
  function openPage(page, updateHash){
    if(!page || !document.getElementById('page-'+page)) return;
    try{ if(typeof window.goPage === 'function') window.goPage(page); }catch(err){ console.warn('Navigation fallback:', err); }
    if(updateHash && location.hash !== '#'+page) history.replaceState(null,'','#'+page);
  }
  document.querySelectorAll('a.nav-item[data-page]').forEach(link=>{
    link.addEventListener('click', function(event){
      event.preventDefault(); openPage(this.dataset.page, true);
    });
  });
  window.addEventListener('hashchange', ()=>openPage(location.hash.replace('#',''), false));
  openPage(initial, false);
})();
</script>

<script>
/* ===== Shipment Planning Revision — 07 Jul 2026 ===== */
window.refreshDocumentStatus=function(){
  const activePlanDocs=new Set(
    (db.plans||[])
      .filter(p=>!['Completed','Cancelled'].includes(p.status))
      .flatMap(p=>p.docs||[])
  );
  const closedPlanDocs=new Set(
    (db.plans||[])
      .filter(p=>['Completed','Cancelled'].includes(p.status))
      .flatMap(p=>p.docs||[])
  );
  let changed=0;
  (db.documents||[]).forEach(d=>{
    const status=String(d.status||'');
    const explicitlyComplete=['Complete','Completed'].includes(status);
    const closedDonePlanning=status==='Done Planning'&&closedPlanDocs.has(d.id)&&!activePlanDocs.has(d.id);
    if(explicitlyComplete||closedDonePlanning){
      d.status='Need Planning';
      changed++;
    }
  });
  try{selectedDocs.clear()}catch(e){}
  saveDB();
  renderAll();
  toast(changed?`${changed} document status refreshed to Need Planning`:'No completed document status found');
};
</script>

<script>
/* ===== Shipment Fee Auto Calculation & Fraud Threshold — 07 Jul 2026 ===== */
(function shipmentFeeAndFraudRevision(){
  'use strict';

  const DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD = 15;

  function normalizeContractFeeConfig(contract){
    if(!contract) return contract;
    if(String(contract.rate||'').trim()==='Base + /kg') contract.rate='Per kg';
    const threshold=Number(contract.feeVarianceThreshold);
    contract.feeVarianceThreshold=Number.isFinite(threshold)&&threshold>=0?threshold:DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD;
    return contract;
  }
  (DEMO.contracts||[]).forEach(normalizeContractFeeConfig);
  (db.contracts||[]).forEach(normalizeContractFeeConfig);
  saveDB();

  const feeBaseMasterFields=window.masterFields;
  window.masterFields=masterFields=function(type,obj={},isNew=false){
    let fields=feeBaseMasterFields(type,obj,isNew);
    if(type!=='contracts') return fields;
    fields=fields.map(field=>field.k==='rate'?{
      ...field,
      l:'Rate Type',
      o:['Flat Trip','Per kg','Per km','Per drop']
    }:field);
    if(!fields.some(field=>field.k==='feeVarianceThreshold')){
      const thresholdField={
        k:'feeVarianceThreshold',
        l:'Fee Variance Threshold (%)',
        t:'number',
        min:0,
        step:'0.1',
        help:'Jika Fee Delivery melebihi nilai kontrak di atas persentase ini, shipment otomatis masuk Fraud Detection.'
      };
      const statusIndex=fields.findIndex(field=>field.k==='status');
      if(statusIndex>=0) fields.splice(statusIndex,0,thresholdField);
      else fields.push(thresholdField);
    }
    return fields;
  };

  const feeBaseOpenMasterForm=window.openMasterForm;
  window.openMasterForm=openMasterForm=function(type,index=null,view=false){
    feeBaseOpenMasterForm(type,index,view);
    if(type==='contracts'){
      const input=document.getElementById('mf-feeVarianceThreshold');
      if(input&&!input.value) input.value=String(index===null?DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD:(db.contracts[index]?.feeVarianceThreshold??DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD));
    }
  };

  function selectedWizardDocuments(){
    const ids=(document.getElementById('sw-docs')?.value||'').split('|').filter(Boolean);
    return (db.documents||[]).filter(doc=>ids.includes(doc.id));
  }
  function selectedWizardContract(){
    const id=document.getElementById('sw-contract')?.value||'';
    return (db.contracts||[]).find(contract=>contract.id===id)||null;
  }
  function wizardRouteDistance(contract){
    const selectedLane=document.getElementById('sw-route-select')?.value||'';
    const laneId=selectedLane&&selectedLane!=='AUTO'?selectedLane:(contract?.lane||'');
    const lane=(db.routes||[]).find(route=>route.id===laneId);
    return Number(lane?.distance||0);
  }
  function contractRateUnit(contract){
    const rate=String(contract?.rate||'').toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
    if(rate.includes('kg')&&rate.includes('km')) return 'kg-km';
    if(rate.includes('kg')) return 'kg';
    if(rate.includes('km')) return 'km';
    if(rate.includes('drop')) return 'drop';
    return 'trip';
  }
  function deliveryFeeReference(contract,docs=selectedWizardDocuments()){
    if(!contract) return {reference:0,unit:'trip',quantity:0,label:'No active contract selected',weight:0,distance:0,drops:0,baseRate:0};
    const baseRate=Number(contract.baseRate||0);
    const weight=docs.reduce((total,doc)=>total+Number(doc.weight||0),0);
    const distance=wizardRouteDistance(contract);
    const drops=Math.max(1,new Set(docs.map(doc=>doc.destination||doc.id)).size);
    const unit=contractRateUnit(contract);
    let quantity=1,label='1 trip';
    if(unit==='kg'){quantity=weight;label=`${weight.toLocaleString('id-ID')} kg`;}
    else if(unit==='km'){quantity=distance;label=`${distance.toLocaleString('id-ID')} km`;}
    else if(unit==='drop'){quantity=drops;label=`${drops} drop`;}
    else if(unit==='kg-km'){quantity=weight*distance;label=`${weight.toLocaleString('id-ID')} kg × ${distance.toLocaleString('id-ID')} km`;}
    const reference=Math.max(0,Math.round(baseRate*quantity));
    return {reference,unit,quantity,label,weight,distance,drops,baseRate};
  }
  function feeThresholdElement(){return document.getElementById('sw-fee-threshold-status')}
  function ensureFeeHelper(){
    const cost=document.getElementById('sw-cost');
    if(!cost) return null;
    cost.step='1000';
    cost.setAttribute('oninput','validateDeliveryFeeThreshold()');
    let helper=feeThresholdElement();
    if(!helper){
      helper=document.createElement('div');
      helper.id='sw-fee-threshold-status';
      helper.style.marginTop='6px';
      cost.insertAdjacentElement('afterend',helper);
    }
    return helper;
  }
  window.refreshDeliveryFeeFromContract=function(){
    const contract=selectedWizardContract();
    const cost=document.getElementById('sw-cost');
    if(!cost) return;
    const calc=deliveryFeeReference(contract);
    const threshold=Number(contract?.feeVarianceThreshold??DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD);
    cost.value=String(calc.reference);
    cost.dataset.referenceFee=String(calc.reference);
    cost.dataset.feeThreshold=String(threshold);
    cost.dataset.contractId=contract?.id||'';
    ensureFeeHelper();
    validateDeliveryFeeThreshold(true);
    const pod=document.getElementById('sw-pod');
    if(pod&&contract?.podRequirement&&[...pod.options].some(option=>option.value===contract.podRequirement)) pod.value=contract.podRequirement;
  };
  window.validateDeliveryFeeThreshold=function(silent=false){
    const contract=selectedWizardContract();
    const cost=document.getElementById('sw-cost');
    const helper=ensureFeeHelper();
    if(!cost||!helper) return {exceeded:false,reference:0,actual:0,threshold:DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD,variancePct:0,maxAllowed:0};
    const calc=deliveryFeeReference(contract);
    const reference=Number(cost.dataset.referenceFee||calc.reference||0);
    const actual=Number(cost.value||0);
    const threshold=Number(cost.dataset.feeThreshold||contract?.feeVarianceThreshold||DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD);
    const maxAllowed=reference*(1+threshold/100);
    const variancePct=reference?((actual-reference)/reference*100):0;
    const exceeded=reference>0&&actual>maxAllowed;
    if(!contract){
      helper.className='notice warn';
      helper.innerHTML='Pilih Active Contract untuk menghitung Fee Delivery otomatis.';
    }else if(calc.unit==='km'&&calc.distance<=0||calc.unit==='kg-km'&&calc.distance<=0){
      helper.className='notice warn';
      helper.innerHTML=`Distance pada Lane kontrak belum tersedia. Fee Delivery tetap editable, tetapi referensi tarif per km belum dapat dihitung.`;
    }else if(exceeded){
      helper.className='notice danger';
      helper.innerHTML=`<b>Fraud threshold exceeded.</b> Nilai kontrak ${fmtIDR(reference)}, batas ${threshold.toLocaleString('id-ID')}% = ${fmtIDR(Math.round(maxAllowed))}. Input ${fmtIDR(actual)} (${variancePct.toFixed(1)}% di atas referensi) akan masuk Fraud Detection saat plan dibuat.`;
      if(!silent) toast('Fee Delivery melebihi fraud threshold kontrak');
    }else{
      helper.className='notice';
      const varianceText=reference?`${variancePct>=0?'+':''}${variancePct.toFixed(1)}%`:'-';
      helper.innerHTML=`Auto calculation: <b>${calc.label} × ${fmtIDR(calc.baseRate)} = ${fmtIDR(reference)}</b>. Threshold kontrak ${threshold.toLocaleString('id-ID')}% (maks. ${fmtIDR(Math.round(maxAllowed))}). Current variance: ${varianceText}. Fee tetap dapat diedit.`;
    }
    return {exceeded,reference,actual,threshold,variancePct,maxAllowed,calc,contract};
  };

  const feeBaseSyncContract=window.syncContract;
  window.syncContract=syncContract=function(){
    const supplier=document.getElementById('sw-supplier');
    const contractSelect=document.getElementById('sw-contract');
    if(!contractSelect) return;
    const carrier=supplier?.value||'';
    const previous=contractSelect.value;
    if(!carrier){
      contractSelect.innerHTML='<option value="">No expedition carrier available</option>';
      contractSelect.disabled=true;
      const cost=document.getElementById('sw-cost');
      if(cost) cost.value='0';
      ensureFeeHelper();
      validateDeliveryFeeThreshold(true);
      return;
    }
    const contracts=activeCarrierContracts(carrier).map(normalizeContractFeeConfig);
    contractSelect.innerHTML=contracts.map(contract=>{
      const unit=contractRateUnit(contract)==='trip'?'/ trip':contractRateUnit(contract)==='drop'?'/ drop':contractRateUnit(contract)==='kg'?'/ kg':contractRateUnit(contract)==='km'?'/ km':'/ kg/km';
      return `<option value="${esc(contract.id)}">${esc(contract.id)} — ${esc(contract.rate||'Contract Rate')} — ${fmtIDR(contract.baseRate)} ${unit} — Threshold ${Number(contract.feeVarianceThreshold||DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD).toLocaleString('id-ID')}%</option>`;
    }).join('')||'<option value="">No active contract</option>';
    contractSelect.disabled=!contracts.length;
    if(contracts.some(contract=>contract.id===previous)) contractSelect.value=previous;
    contractSelect.onchange=refreshDeliveryFeeFromContract;
    refreshDeliveryFeeFromContract();
  };

  function emitDeliveryFeeFraud(plan,assessment){
    if(!plan||!assessment?.exceeded||typeof rcEmit!=='function') return;
    const exposure=Math.max(0,assessment.actual-assessment.reference);
    rcEmit({
      rule:'DELIVERY_FEE_VARIANCE',
      sourceModule:'Shipment Planning',
      sourceType:'Shipment Planning',
      sourceRef:plan.id,
      title:'Delivery fee exceeds active contract threshold',
      negativeCase:`Fee Delivery ${fmtIDR(assessment.actual)} pada ${plan.id} melebihi nilai kontrak ${fmtIDR(assessment.reference)} sebesar ${assessment.variancePct.toFixed(1)}%.`,
      expectedCondition:`Fee Delivery maksimal ${assessment.threshold}% di atas hasil kalkulasi Active Contract.`,
      actualCondition:`Contract ${plan.contract}; Reference ${fmtIDR(assessment.reference)}; Input ${fmtIDR(assessment.actual)}; Variance ${assessment.variancePct.toFixed(1)}%.`,
      threshold:`${assessment.threshold}% / maksimum ${fmtIDR(Math.round(assessment.maxAllowed))}`,
      severity:assessment.variancePct>50?'Critical':'High',
      confidence:99,
      exposure,
      recurrence:1,
      evidence:[plan.contract,...(plan.docs||[])],
      recommendedAction:'Review contract rate, supporting quotation, and fee approval before dispatch.',
      blocking:false,
      sourceRecord:`${plan.id} • ${plan.contract}`
    });
    plan.feeReference=assessment.reference;
    plan.feeThresholdPct=assessment.threshold;
    plan.feeVariancePct=Number(assessment.variancePct.toFixed(2));
    plan.fraudStatus='Flagged';
    plan.health=plan.health==='On Schedule'?'At Risk':plan.health;
  }

  const feeBaseCreateShipmentPlan=window.createShipmentPlan;
  window.createShipmentPlan=createShipmentPlan=function(){
    const isExpedition=document.getElementById('sw-source')?.value==='Expedition';
    const assessment=isExpedition?validateDeliveryFeeThreshold(true):null;
    const before=(db.plans||[]).length;
    feeBaseCreateShipmentPlan();
    if((db.plans||[]).length<=before) return;
    const plan=db.plans[db.plans.length-1];
    if(isExpedition&&assessment){
      plan.feeReference=assessment.reference;
      plan.feeThresholdPct=assessment.threshold;
      plan.feeVariancePct=Number(assessment.variancePct.toFixed(2));
      emitDeliveryFeeFraud(plan,assessment);
      saveDB();
      if(typeof installOperationalRiskBanners==='function') installOperationalRiskBanners();
      renderAll();
      if(assessment.exceeded) toast(`Plan ${plan.id} dibuat dan ditandai pada Fraud Detection`);
    }
  };

  function scanExistingDeliveryFeeVariance(){
    (db.plans||[]).filter(plan=>plan.source==='Expedition'&&plan.contract).forEach(plan=>{
      const contract=(db.contracts||[]).find(item=>item.id===plan.contract);
      if(!contract) return;
      const reference=Number(plan.feeReference||0);
      const actual=Number(plan.plannedCost||0);
      const threshold=Number(plan.feeThresholdPct??contract.feeVarianceThreshold??DEFAULT_FEE_THRESHOLD);
      if(!reference) return;
      const variancePct=(actual-reference)/reference*100;
      const assessment={reference,actual,threshold,variancePct,maxAllowed:reference*(1+threshold/100),exceeded:actual>reference*(1+threshold/100)};
      emitDeliveryFeeFraud(plan,assessment);
    });
  }

  const feeBaseRunOperationalRiskValidation=window.runOperationalRiskValidation;
  if(typeof feeBaseRunOperationalRiskValidation==='function'){
    window.runOperationalRiskValidation=function(scope='all',silent=false){
      feeBaseRunOperationalRiskValidation(scope,true);
      if(scope==='all'||scope==='Shipment Planning') scanExistingDeliveryFeeVariance();
      saveDB();
      if(typeof installOperationalRiskBanners==='function') installOperationalRiskBanners();
      const scopes=scope==='all'?['Shipment Planning','Shipment Schedule','Loading & Dispatch','Monitoring Shipment','Driver Mobile']:[scope];
      const total=scopes.reduce((sum,item)=>sum+(typeof rcEventsFor==='function'?rcEventsFor(item).length:0),0);
      if(!silent) toast(`${total} open operational risk event(s) found`);
      return total;
    };
  }

  const feeBaseResetDemo=window.resetDemo;
  window.resetDemo=resetDemo=function(){
    feeBaseResetDemo();
    (DEMO.contracts||[]).forEach(normalizeContractFeeConfig);
    (db.contracts||[]).forEach(normalizeContractFeeConfig);
    saveDB();
  };
})();
</script>


<script>
/* ===== Shipment Planning Revision V9: status refresh, full edit wizard, toolbar alignment ===== */
(function shipmentPlanningRevisionV9(){
  'use strict';

  function normalizeText(value){return String(value||'').trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,' ')}
  function activeHubRows(){return (db.hubs||[]).filter(h=>h.status==='Active')}
  function optionExists(select,value){return !!select&&[...select.options].some(option=>option.value===value)}
  function setValueIfAvailable(select,value){if(select&&optionExists(select,value))select.value=value}

  /* Dispatch / Consolidation Hub is derived from the selected Ready Documents rows.
     Unrelated Master hubs are not offered unless no table-derived hub can be found. */
  window.detectedHubOptions=detectedHubOptions=function(docs){
    const active=activeHubRows(),activeByName=new Map(active.map(h=>[normalizeText(h.name),h.name])),result=[];
    const add=value=>{const raw=String(value||'').trim();if(!raw)return;const masterName=activeByName.get(normalizeText(raw));const candidate=masterName||(/\bhub\b/i.test(raw)?raw:'');if(candidate&&!result.some(x=>normalizeText(x)===normalizeText(candidate)))result.push(candidate)};
    (docs||[]).forEach(doc=>{add(doc.origin);add(doc.destination)});
    if(!result.length)active.forEach(h=>add(h.name));
    return result;
  };

  function wizardDocumentRows(docs){
    return docs.map(d=>`<tr><td class="mono">${esc(d.id)}</td><td>${esc(d.type)}</td><td>${esc(d.customer)}</td><td>${esc(d.origin)}</td><td>${esc(d.destination)}</td></tr>`).join('');
  }

  function buildPlanWizard(prefillDocs=null,editId=''){
    const plan=editId?(db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.id===editId):null;
    if(editId&&!plan){toast('Shipment Plan tidak ditemukan');return}
    if(plan&&plan.status!=='Planned'){toast('Edit Plan hanya tersedia untuk status Planned');return}
    const ids=prefillDocs||(plan?.docs||[...selectedDocs]),docs=(db.documents||[]).filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id));
    if(!docs.length){toast('Pilih minimal satu DO/STO terlebih dahulu');return}

    const tableHubs=detectedHubOptions(docs),currentHub=plan?.transitHub||plan?.dispatchHub||'';
    if(plan&&currentHub&&!tableHubs.some(h=>normalizeText(h)===normalizeText(currentHub)))tableHubs.unshift(currentHub);
    const commonOrigin=docs.every(d=>d.origin===docs[0].origin)?docs[0].origin:'',destinations=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.destination));
    const defaultHub=plan?currentHub:(tableHubs.find(h=>normalizeText(h)!==normalizeText(commonOrigin))||tableHubs[0]||commonOrigin);
    const defaultSource=plan?.source||document.getElementById('readyShippingOption')?.value||'Fleet Company';
    const defaultFleet=plan?(plan.source==='Fleet Company'?((db.vehicles||[]).find(v=>v.plate===plan.vehicle)?.id||''):plan.supplier):(document.getElementById('readyFleetSelect')?.value||'');
    const defaultStop=plan?.stopCategory||(plan?.transitHub?'Hub':'End Customer');
    const title=plan?`Edit ${esc(plan.id)}`:'Create Shipment Plan';
    const info=plan?'Edit menggunakan field dan validasi yang sama seperti Create Plan. Hanya plan berstatus Planned yang dapat diubah.':'Tentukan jenis stop terlebih dahulu. Field Hub hanya muncul untuk perjalanan melalui titik transit atau konsolidasi.';
    const body=`<div class="notice">${info}</div><div class="doc-selection-table"><table class="tbl"><thead><tr><th>Document</th><th>Type</th><th>Customer / Recipient</th><th>Origin</th><th>Destination</th></tr></thead><tbody>${wizardDocumentRows(docs)}</tbody></table></div><div class="wizard-context">${plan?`<div>Plan Number<b>${esc(plan.id)}</b></div>`:''}<div>Total Load<b>${docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0).toLocaleString()} kg / ${docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0).toFixed(1)} m³</b></div><div>Origin<b>${esc(commonOrigin||uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin)).join(' + '))}</b></div><div>Destination<b>${esc(destinations.join(' / '))}</b></div></div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Shipping Option</label><select class="select" id="sw-source" onchange="wizardDynamic()"><option ${defaultSource==='Fleet Company'?'selected':''}>Fleet Company</option><option ${defaultSource==='Expedition'?'selected':''}>Expedition</option></select></div><div class="field"><label>Stop Category</label><select class="select" id="sw-stop" onchange="wizardStopChanged()"><option ${defaultStop==='End Customer'?'selected':''}>End Customer</option><option ${defaultStop==='Hub'?'selected':''}>Hub</option></select><small>Hub dipakai sebagai transit/consolidation stop.</small></div><div class="field ${defaultStop==='Hub'?'':'hidden'}" id="sw-hub-wrap"><label>Dispatch / Consolidation Hub</label><select class="select" id="sw-hub" onchange="wizardDynamic();refreshWizardRoute(true)">${tableHubs.map(h=>`<option value="${esc(h)}" ${normalizeText(h)===normalizeText(defaultHub)?'selected':''}>${esc(h)}</option>`).join('')}</select><small>Option mengikuti Origin/Destination pada document yang dipilih.</small></div><div class="field"><label>Shipment Date</label><input class="input" type="date" id="sw-date" value="${esc(plan?.shipmentDate||todayISO())}" onchange="syncContract()"></div><div class="field"><label>Estimate Date to Arrival</label><input class="input" type="date" id="sw-eta" value="${esc(plan?.eta||addDays(todayISO(),1))}"></div><div id="sw-dynamic" class="field full"></div><div class="field full"><div class="route-builder"><div class="route-builder-head"><b>Route / Lane</b><span id="sw-route-summary"></span></div><div class="form-grid"><div class="field"><label>Lane Source</label><select class="select" id="sw-route-select" onchange="applyWizardLane()"></select></div><div class="field"><label>Generated Route</label><div style="display:flex;gap:7px"><input class="input" id="sw-route-text" disabled style="flex:1;min-width:0"><button class="btn btn-outline" type="button" id="sw-route-edit" onclick="toggleRouteEdit()">Edit Route</button></div></div></div><div class="route-preview"><span class="route-icon">⌁</span><div><b>Auto routing follows selected destinations</b><p>Master Lane ditampilkan jika origin/destination cocok. User tetap dapat mengubah route secara manual.</p></div></div><div class="route-warning" id="sw-route-warning"></div></div></div><div class="field full"><label>Remark</label><textarea class="textarea" id="sw-remark" placeholder="Transport notes, special handling, temperature, seal, etc.">${esc(plan?.remark||'')}</textarea></div></div><input type="hidden" id="sw-docs" value="${ids.join('|')}"><input type="hidden" id="sw-readyFleet" value="${esc(defaultFleet)}"><input type="hidden" id="sw-edit-plan" value="${esc(editId)}">`;
    const footer=plan?`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveShipmentPlanEdit('${esc(plan.id)}')">Save Changes</button>`:`<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Close</button><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="createShipmentPlan()">Create Plan</button>`;
    openModal(title,body,footer);
    wizardStopChanged();

    if(!plan)return;
    document.getElementById('sw-source').value=plan.source||'Fleet Company';
    document.getElementById('sw-stop').value=defaultStop;
    setValueIfAvailable(document.getElementById('sw-hub'),defaultHub);
    wizardStopChanged();
    document.getElementById('sw-date').value=plan.shipmentDate||todayISO();
    document.getElementById('sw-eta').value=plan.eta||addDays(todayISO(),1);
    document.getElementById('sw-remark').value=plan.remark||'';

    if(plan.source==='Fleet Company'){
      const vehicle=(db.vehicles||[]).find(v=>v.plate===plan.vehicle),driver=(db.drivers||[]).find(d=>d.name===plan.driver);
      setValueIfAvailable(document.getElementById('sw-vehicle'),vehicle?.id||'');
      setValueIfAvailable(document.getElementById('sw-driver'),driver?.id||'');
      const cost=document.getElementById('sw-cost');if(cost)cost.value=Number(plan.plannedCost||0);
      if(typeof calculateWizardUtil==='function')calculateWizardUtil();
    }else{
      setValueIfAvailable(document.getElementById('sw-supplier'),plan.supplier||'');
      if(typeof syncContract==='function')syncContract();
      setValueIfAvailable(document.getElementById('sw-contract'),plan.contract||'');
      const cost=document.getElementById('sw-cost');if(cost)cost.value=Number(plan.plannedCost||0);
    }

    if(typeof refreshWizardRoute==='function')refreshWizardRoute(true);
    const lane=document.getElementById('sw-route-select'),routeInput=document.getElementById('sw-route-text');
    if(lane&&plan.routeLane&&optionExists(lane,plan.routeLane)){lane.value=plan.routeLane;if(typeof applyWizardLane==='function')applyWizardLane()}
    if(routeInput&&plan.route){routeInput.value=plan.route;routeInput.disabled=true;routeInput.dataset.manual='1'}
  }

  window.openShipmentWizard=openShipmentWizard=function(prefillDocs=null,editId=''){return buildPlanWizard(prefillDocs,editId)};
  window.editPlan=editPlan=function(id){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.id===id);if(!plan)return;
    if(plan.status!=='Planned'){toast('Edit Plan hanya tersedia untuk status Planned');return}
    buildPlanWizard(plan.docs||[],id);
  };

  function releaseResourceIfUnused(source,vehiclePlate,driverName,excludePlanId){
    if(source!=='Fleet Company')return;
    const activePlans=(db.plans||[]).filter(p=>p.id!==excludePlanId&&p.source==='Fleet Company'&&!['Completed','Cancelled'].includes(p.status));
    const vehicleStillUsed=activePlans.some(p=>p.vehicle===vehiclePlate),driverStillUsed=activePlans.some(p=>p.driver===driverName);
    const vehicle=(db.vehicles||[]).find(v=>v.plate===vehiclePlate),driver=(db.drivers||[]).find(d=>d.name===driverName);
    if(!vehicleStillUsed&&vehicle&&vehicle.status==='Reserved')vehicle.status='Available';
    if(!driverStillUsed&&driver&&driver.status==='Assigned')driver.status='Available';
  }

  window.saveShipmentPlanEdit=function(id){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.id===id);if(!plan)return;
    if(plan.status!=='Planned'){toast('Perubahan ditolak. Status plan bukan Planned');return}
    const ids=(document.getElementById('sw-docs')?.value||'').split('|').filter(Boolean),docs=(db.documents||[]).filter(x=>ids.includes(x.id));
    const source=document.getElementById('sw-source')?.value||'Fleet Company',stopCategory=document.getElementById('sw-stop')?.value||'End Customer',origins=uniqueValues(docs.map(d=>d.origin)),hub=stopCategory==='Hub'?(document.getElementById('sw-hub')?.value||''):'';
    if(stopCategory==='Hub'&&!hub){toast('Dispatch / Consolidation Hub wajib dipilih');return}
    if(stopCategory==='End Customer'&&origins.length>1){toast('Origin dokumen berbeda. Gunakan Stop Category Hub untuk konsolidasi.');return}

    let vehicle='-',driver='-',supplier='-',contract='-',weightUtil=0,volumeUtil=0,overallUtil=0;
    if(source==='Fleet Company'){
      const vehicleRow=(db.vehicles||[]).find(v=>v.id===document.getElementById('sw-vehicle')?.value),driverRow=(db.drivers||[]).find(d=>d.id===document.getElementById('sw-driver')?.value);
      if(!vehicleRow||!driverRow){toast('Fleet dan Driver wajib dipilih');return}
      const weight=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),volume=docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0);
      weightUtil=Math.round(weight/Number(vehicleRow.weight||1)*100);volumeUtil=Math.round(volume/Number(vehicleRow.volume||1)*100);overallUtil=Math.max(weightUtil,volumeUtil);
      if(overallUtil>100){toast('Shipment melebihi kapasitas kendaraan');return}
      vehicle=vehicleRow.plate;driver=driverRow.name;supplier=vehicleRow.carrier;
    }else{
      supplier=document.getElementById('sw-supplier')?.value||'';contract=document.getElementById('sw-contract')?.value||'';
      if(!supplier||!contract||contract==='No active contract'){toast('Carrier wajib memiliki kontrak aktif');return}
    }

    const route=(document.getElementById('sw-route-text')?.value||'').trim();if(!route){toast('Route / Lane wajib tersedia');return}
    const oldSource=plan.source,oldVehicle=plan.vehicle,oldDriver=plan.driver;
    Object.assign(plan,{
      docs:ids,
      docType:uniqueValues(docs.map(x=>x.type)).map(x=>x==='DO'?'Delivery Order':'Stock Transfer Out').join(' + '),
      source,supplier,contract,vehicle,driver,
      shipmentDate:document.getElementById('sw-date')?.value||plan.shipmentDate,
      eta:document.getElementById('sw-eta')?.value||plan.eta,
      origin:origins.length===1?origins[0]:origins.join(' / '),
      dispatchHub:hub||(origins.length===1?origins[0]:origins.join(' / ')),
      transitHub:hub,
      stopCategory,
      destination:uniqueValues(docs.map(x=>x.destination)).join(' / '),
      route,
      routeLane:document.getElementById('sw-route-select')?.value||'AUTO',
      weight:docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.weight),0),
      volume:Number(docs.reduce((a,b)=>a+Number(b.volume),0).toFixed(1)),
      weightUtil,volumeUtil,util:overallUtil,
      plannedCost:Number(document.getElementById('sw-cost')?.value||0),
      remark:document.getElementById('sw-remark')?.value.trim()||'',
      health:'On Schedule',
      lastUpdate:'Plan edited just now',
      loadedDocs:[],
      stops:docs.map(x=>({doc:x.id,customer:x.customer,category:'End Customer',viaHub:hub||'',destination:x.destination,status:'On Going',arrival:'-',pod:false}))
    });
    releaseResourceIfUnused(oldSource,oldVehicle,oldDriver,id);
    if(source==='Fleet Company'){
      const newVehicle=(db.vehicles||[]).find(v=>v.plate===vehicle),newDriver=(db.drivers||[]).find(d=>d.name===driver);
      if(newVehicle)newVehicle.status='Reserved';if(newDriver)newDriver.status='Assigned';
    }
    docs.forEach(doc=>doc.status='Done Planning');
    saveDB();closeModal();renderAll();planningTab(document.querySelector('#page-planning .tab:nth-child(2)'),'planPanel');toast(id+' updated');
  };

  /* Re-open completed demo plans as Planned so the plan can be corrected through the edit wizard. */
  window.refreshPlanDocumentStatus=function(){
    const eligible=(db.plans||[]).filter(plan=>['Complete','Completed'].includes(plan.status));
    if(!eligible.length){toast('Tidak ada plan berstatus Complete / Completed');return}
    if(!window.confirm(`Ubah ${eligible.length} plan Complete / Completed menjadi Planned? Loading, POD, dan execution progress pada plan tersebut akan di-reset.`))return;
    eligible.forEach(plan=>{
      plan.status='Planned';plan.health='On Schedule';plan.loadedDocs=[];plan.lastUpdate='Document status refreshed to Planned';
      plan.stops=(plan.stops||[]).map(stop=>Object.assign({},stop,{status:'On Going',arrival:'-',pod:false,signature:false,receiver:''}));
      (plan.docs||[]).forEach(id=>{const doc=(db.documents||[]).find(d=>d.id===id);if(doc)doc.status='Done Planning'});
      const state=(db.driverStates||{})[plan.id];if(state){state.step=0;state.currentStop=0;state.loadConfirmed=false;state.startOdo=null;state.endOdo=null}
      const order=(db.fleetOrders||[]).find(item=>item.planId===plan.id);if(order){order.status='Dijadwalkan';order.updated='Status refreshed to Planned'}
      if(plan.source==='Fleet Company'){
        const vehicle=(db.vehicles||[]).find(v=>v.plate===plan.vehicle),driver=(db.drivers||[]).find(d=>d.name===plan.driver);
        if(vehicle)vehicle.status='Reserved';if(driver)driver.status='Assigned';
      }
    });
    saveDB();renderAll();renderPlans();toast(`${eligible.length} plan berhasil diubah menjadi Planned`);
  };

  const baseActionList=window.actionList;
  window.actionList=actionList=function(kind,id){
    if(kind!=='plan')return typeof baseActionList==='function'?baseActionList(kind,id):[];
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(p=>p.id===id),items=[{label:'View Detail',run:()=>planDetail(id)}];
    if(plan?.status==='Planned')items.push({label:'Edit Plan',run:()=>editPlan(id)});
    items.push({label:'Open Schedule',run:()=>goSchedulePlan(id)});
    if(plan?.status==='Planned')items.push({label:'Start Loading',run:()=>setLoadingPlan(id)});
    items.push({label:'Delete Plan',danger:true,run:()=>deletePlan(id)});
    return items;
  };
})();
</script>

<script>
(function loadingDispatchPreCheckV2(){
  'use strict';
  const SCHEMA_VERSION=2;
  const baseStartLoading=window.startLoading;
  const baseStatusBadge=window.statusBadge;
  const legacyAdvancedStatuses=['Loading','Ready to Dispatch','In Transit','Unloading','Returning','Completed'];
  const manualDefinitions={
    staging:{label:'Barang tersedia di staging area',description:'Petugas memastikan barang sudah dipisahkan, diberi label, dan siap dimuat.'},
    vehicleCondition:{label:'Kondisi kendaraan layak',description:'Petugas memeriksa kebersihan, bak, pintu, ban, dan kondisi fisik kendaraan.'},
    seal:{label:'Seal tersedia dan sesuai',description:'Petugas memastikan seal atau alat pengaman tersedia dan sesuai kebutuhan shipment.'}
  };
  function nowText(){return new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').slice(0,16)}
  function safe(value){return typeof esc==='function'?esc(value):String(value??'')}
  function checkBadge(status){
    const normalized=status==='Pass'?'Passed':status;
    const cls={Passed:'b-green',Pending:'b-orange',Failed:'b-red','Not Applicable':'b-gray','Not Started':'b-gray','In Progress':'b-orange','Checking Passed':'b-checking-passed'}[normalized]||'b-gray';
    const label=normalized==='Not Applicable'?'N/A':normalized;
    return `<span class="badge ${cls}">${safe(label)}</span>`;
  }
  function createManualValue(result='Pending'){
    const normalized=result==='Passed'?'Pass':result;
    return {result:['Pass','Fail','Not Applicable','Pending'].includes(normalized)?normalized:'Pending',note:'',evidenceName:''};
  }
  function newCheckState(plan,legacyPassed=false){
    return {
      schemaVersion:SCHEMA_VERSION,
      status:legacyPassed?'Passed':'Not Started',
      validationRunAt:'',startedAt:legacyPassed?'Migrated from existing loading status':'',savedAt:'',completedAt:legacyPassed?'Migrated from existing loading status':'',
      checkerName:legacyPassed?'System Migration':'',notes:legacyPassed?'Existing shipment was already beyond the checking stage.':'',
      automatic:{},
      manual:{
        staging:createManualValue(legacyPassed?'Pass':'Pending'),
        vehicleCondition:createManualValue(legacyPassed?'Pass':'Pending'),
        seal:createManualValue(legacyPassed?'Pass':'Pending')
      }
    };
  }
  function ensureCheckState(plan){
    const legacyPassed=legacyAdvancedStatuses.includes(plan.status);
    let c=plan.preLoadingCheck;
    if(!c||c.schemaVersion!==SCHEMA_VERSION){
      const old=c||{};
      c=newCheckState(plan,legacyPassed);
      if(!legacyPassed&&plan.status==='Checking'){
        c.status=old.status==='Completed'||old.status==='Passed'?'Passed':'In Progress';
        c.startedAt=old.startedAt||nowText();c.completedAt=old.completedAt||'';c.checkerName=old.checkerName||'';c.notes=old.notes||'';
        const oldManual=old.manual||{};
        c.manual.staging=createManualValue(oldManual.staging||'Pending');
        c.manual.vehicleCondition=createManualValue(oldManual.vehicle||oldManual.vehicleCondition||'Pending');
        c.manual.seal=createManualValue(oldManual.seal||'Pending');
      }
      plan.preLoadingCheck=c;
    }
    c.automatic=c.automatic||{};c.manual=c.manual||{};
    Object.keys(manualDefinitions).forEach(key=>{
      const value=c.manual[key];
      if(!value||typeof value!=='object')c.manual[key]=createManualValue(value||'Pending');
      c.manual[key].result=c.manual[key].result==='Passed'?'Pass':(c.manual[key].result||'Pending');
      c.manual[key].note=c.manual[key].note||'';c.manual[key].evidenceName=c.manual[key].evidenceName||'';
    });
    c.status=c.status||'Not Started';c.checkerName=c.checkerName||'';c.notes=c.notes||'';
    return c;
  }
  function openBlockingEvents(plan){
    const allowedNonBlockingRules=['DUPLICATE_SOURCE_DOCUMENT','DUPLICATE_DOCUMENT'];
    const rows=(db.riskEvents||[]).filter(event=>
      event&&
      event.status!=='Cleared'&&
      event.blocking&&
      !allowedNonBlockingRules.includes(event.rule)&&
      (event.sourceRef===plan.id||(event.relatedRefs||[]).includes(plan.id))
    );
    return rows;
  }
  function contractIsValid(plan){
    if(plan.source!=='Expedition')return true;
    const contract=(db.contracts||[]).find(item=>item.id===plan.contract);
    return !!contract&&contract.status==='Active'&&(!contract.endDate||contract.endDate>=plan.shipmentDate);
  }
  function computeAutomaticChecks(plan){
    const docs=(plan.docs||[]).filter(Boolean);
    const knownDocs=docs.filter(id=>(db.documents||[]).some(doc=>doc.id===id));
    const vehicle=(db.vehicles||[]).find(item=>item.plate===plan.vehicle);
    const driver=(db.drivers||[]).find(item=>item.name===plan.driver);
    const isInternal=plan.source==='Fleet Company';
    const contractValid=contractIsValid(plan);
    const blockers=openBlockingEvents(plan);
    const capacityPassed=isInternal?Number(plan.util||0)<=100:contractValid;
    const driverPassed=isInternal?!!driver:!!plan.supplier&&contractValid;
    const vehiclePassed=isInternal?!!vehicle&&vehicle.status!=='Maintenance':contractValid;
    const docsPassed=docs.length>0&&(knownDocs.length===docs.length||docs.every(id=>/^(DO|STO)[\/-]/i.test(id)));
    const blockingPassed=blockers.length===0&&contractValid;
    return {
      shipmentDocs:{label:'Shipment Plan dan DO/STO sesuai',result:docsPassed?'Passed':'Failed',description:docsPassed?`${docs.length} dokumen DO/STO sesuai dengan shipment plan.`:'Dokumen shipment belum lengkap atau tidak terhubung ke shipment plan.',corrective:'Tambahkan DO/STO yang valid ke Shipment Plan, lalu klik Run Validation.'},
      driver:{label:'Driver sudah ditentukan',result:driverPassed?'Passed':'Failed',description:driverPassed?(isInternal?`${plan.driver} terhubung ke Master Driver.`:`PIC driver dikelola oleh carrier ${plan.supplier}.`):'Driver aktif belum ditentukan pada shipment plan.',corrective:'Pilih driver aktif dari Master Driver atau pastikan carrier dan kontraknya aktif.'},
      vehicle:{label:'Kendaraan sesuai shipment plan',result:vehiclePassed?'Passed':'Failed',description:vehiclePassed?(isInternal?`${plan.vehicle} sesuai dengan resource pada shipment plan.`:'Kendaraan dikelola oleh carrier sesuai kontrak aktif.'):'Kendaraan tidak ditemukan, tidak sesuai, atau sedang Maintenance.',corrective:'Pilih kendaraan valid yang sesuai pada Shipment Planning, lalu jalankan validasi ulang.'},
      capacity:{label:'Kapasitas kendaraan mencukupi',result:capacityPassed?'Passed':'Failed',description:capacityPassed?(isInternal?`Utilization ${Number(plan.util||0)}% masih dalam kapasitas kendaraan.`:'Kapasitas dikonfirmasi melalui kontrak carrier aktif.'):`Utilization ${Number(plan.util||0)}% melebihi kapasitas kendaraan.`,corrective:'Gunakan kendaraan berkapasitas lebih besar atau pecah shipment menjadi lebih dari satu plan.'},
      documentBlocking:{label:'Dokumen tidak memiliki blocking',result:blockingPassed?'Passed':'Failed',description:blockingPassed?'Dokumen, fraud alert, kontrak, dan data master tidak memiliki blocking aktif.':`${blockers.length+(contractValid?0:1)} blocking aktif ditemukan dari Risk & Control / kontrak.`,corrective:'Buka View Alerts, perbaiki source record atau kontrak, clear blocking, lalu klik Run Validation.'}
    };
  }
  function applyAutomaticValidation(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);
    c.automatic=computeAutomaticChecks(plan);
    c.validationRunAt=nowText();
    return c.automatic;
  }
  function automaticList(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);
    if(!c.validationRunAt||!Object.keys(c.automatic||{}).length)applyAutomaticValidation(plan);
    const a=c.automatic;
    return [a.shipmentDocs,a.driver,a.vehicle,a.capacity,a.documentBlocking].filter(Boolean);
  }
  function manualResolved(item){return item.result==='Pass'||item.result==='Not Applicable'}
  function allChecksResolved(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);
    return automaticList(plan).every(item=>item.result==='Passed')&&Object.values(c.manual).every(manualResolved);
  }
  function failedCount(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);
    return automaticList(plan).filter(item=>item.result==='Failed').length+Object.values(c.manual).filter(item=>item.result==='Fail').length;
  }
  function passedCount(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);
    return automaticList(plan).filter(item=>item.result==='Passed').length+Object.values(c.manual).filter(manualResolved).length;
  }
  function captureVisibleDraft(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);
    const checker=document.getElementById('preloadCheckerName');if(checker)c.checkerName=checker.value.trim();
    const notes=document.getElementById('preloadOverallNotes');if(notes)c.notes=notes.value.trim();
    Object.keys(manualDefinitions).forEach(key=>{
      const status=document.getElementById(`preload-status-${key}`);if(status)c.manual[key].result=status.value;
      const note=document.getElementById(`preload-note-${key}`);if(note)c.manual[key].note=note.value.trim();
    });
    return c;
  }
  function renderAutomaticCard(item){
    const passed=item.result==='Passed';
    return `<div class="preload-check ${passed?'is-passed':'is-failed'}"><div class="preload-check-head"><b>${safe(item.label)}</b>${checkBadge(item.result)}</div><p>${safe(item.description)}</p>${passed?'':`<div class="corrective"><b>Corrective action:</b> ${safe(item.corrective)}</div>`}</div>`;
  }
  function renderManualCard(key,plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan),item=c.manual[key],definition=manualDefinitions[key],editable=c.status==='In Progress'&&plan.status==='Checking';
    const css=item.result==='Pass'?'is-passed':item.result==='Fail'?'is-failed':item.result==='Not Applicable'?'is-na':'is-pending';
    const badgeStatus=item.result==='Pass'?'Passed':item.result==='Fail'?'Failed':item.result;
    return `<div class="preload-check ${css}"><div class="preload-check-head"><b>${safe(definition.label)}</b>${checkBadge(badgeStatus)}</div><p>${safe(definition.description)}</p><div class="preload-manual-fields"><select class="select" id="preload-status-${key}" ${editable?'':'disabled'} onchange="setPreLoadingManualStatus('${key}',this.value)"><option value="Pending" ${item.result==='Pending'?'selected':''}>Select status</option><option value="Pass" ${item.result==='Pass'?'selected':''}>Pass</option><option value="Fail" ${item.result==='Fail'?'selected':''}>Fail</option><option value="Not Applicable" ${item.result==='Not Applicable'?'selected':''}>Not Applicable</option></select><input class="input" id="preload-note-${key}" ${editable?'':'disabled'} value="${safe(item.note)}" placeholder="Catatan pemeriksaan (optional)"><div class="preload-evidence">${editable?`<input type="file" accept="image/*" onchange="setPreLoadingEvidence('${key}',this)">`:''}<small>${item.evidenceName?`Evidence: ${safe(item.evidenceName)}`:'Evidence foto belum ditambahkan.'}</small></div></div>${item.result==='Fail'?'<div class="corrective"><b>Corrective action:</b> Selesaikan temuan operasional, tambahkan catatan/evidence, lalu ubah status menjadi Pass.</div>':''}</div>`;
  }
  function renderPreLoadingCard(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan),passed=passedCount(plan),total=8,progress=Math.round(passed/total*100);
    const canComplete=c.status==='In Progress'&&allChecksResolved(plan)&&!!c.checkerName;
    const locked=c.status==='Passed'||legacyAdvancedStatuses.includes(plan.status);
    const stateLabel=c.status==='Passed'?'Checking Passed':c.status;
    return `<div class="preload-card"><div class="preload-card-head"><span class="preload-card-icon">✓</span><div class="preload-card-title"><b>Pre-Loading Check</b><span>Pemeriksaan sistem dan operasional wajib selesai sebelum loading dimulai.</span></div><div class="preload-state">${checkBadge(stateLabel)}</div></div><div class="preload-body"><div class="preload-validation-note"><div><b>Run Validation</b>Validasi otomatis untuk dokumen, kapasitas, fraud alert, kontrak, dan data master.</div><div><b>Pre-Loading Check</b>Pemeriksaan langsung untuk barang staging, kondisi kendaraan, seal, dan kondisi fisik.</div></div><div class="preload-progress"><span>Checking progress</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${progress}%"></span></div><b>${passed}/${total}</b></div><div class="preload-check-grid">${renderAutomaticCard(automaticList(plan)[0])}${renderAutomaticCard(automaticList(plan)[1])}${renderAutomaticCard(automaticList(plan)[2])}${renderAutomaticCard(automaticList(plan)[3])}${renderManualCard('staging',plan)}${renderAutomaticCard(automaticList(plan)[4])}${renderManualCard('vehicleCondition',plan)}${renderManualCard('seal',plan)}</div><div class="preload-footer-form"><div class="field"><label>Checker Name <span class="text-red">*</span></label><input class="input" id="preloadCheckerName" ${locked?'disabled':''} value="${safe(c.checkerName)}" placeholder="Nama petugas pemeriksa" oninput="refreshPreLoadingCompleteButton()"></div><div class="field"><label>Completed At</label><div class="readonly-value">${safe(c.completedAt||'Not completed')}</div></div><div class="field full"><label>Overall Notes (optional)</label><textarea class="textarea" id="preloadOverallNotes" ${locked?'disabled':''} placeholder="Tambahkan catatan umum pemeriksaan bila diperlukan">${safe(c.notes)}</textarea></div></div><div class="preload-actions"><span class="preload-time">${c.startedAt?`Started: ${safe(c.startedAt)}`:'Checking belum dimulai.'}${c.savedAt?` • Saved: ${safe(c.savedAt)}`:''}</span><button class="btn btn-primary" ${c.status==='Not Started'&&plan.status==='Planned'?'':'disabled'} onclick="startPreLoadingCheck()">Start Checking</button><button class="btn btn-outline" ${c.status==='In Progress'?'':'disabled'} onclick="savePreLoadingCheck()">Save Check</button><button class="btn btn-success" id="completePreLoadingButton" ${canComplete?'':'disabled'} onclick="completePreLoadingCheck()">Complete Checking</button></div></div></div>`;
  }
  function renderLoadingDocuments(plan){
    if(!['Loading','Ready to Dispatch'].includes(plan.status))return '';
    const loaded=plan.loadedDocs||[],editable=plan.status==='Loading';
    return `<div class="loading-work-area"><div class="scan-box"><input class="input" id="scanDocInput" ${editable?'':'disabled'} placeholder="Scan / input DO or STO number"><button class="btn btn-cyan" ${editable?'':'disabled'} onclick="scanLoadingDoc()">Scan Document</button></div><div class="load-list">${(plan.docs||[]).map(id=>`<div class="load-row"><div class="name"><b class="mono">${safe(id)}</b><small>${loaded.includes(id)?'Validated for this shipment':'Waiting for scan'}</small></div><div>${checkBadge(loaded.includes(id)?'Passed':'Pending')}</div><div class="qty">${loaded.includes(id)?'100%':'0%'}</div></div>`).join('')}</div></div>`;
  }
  function flowStage(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);
    if(plan.status==='Planned'&&c.status!=='Not Started')return 'Checking';
    return plan.status;
  }
  function loadingGateMessage(plan){
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan),failures=failedCount(plan);
    if(failures>0){
      const noun=failures===1?'check requires':'checks require';
      return `<div class="notice danger loading-summary-message">Loading cannot be started because ${failures} ${noun} corrective action.</div>`;
    }
    if(c.status!=='Passed')return '<div class="notice warn loading-summary-message">Complete the pre-loading check before starting the loading process.</div>';
    return '<div class="notice loading-summary-message">Pre-loading check passed. Loading can now be started.</div>';
  }
  function patchValidationBanner(plan){
    const page=document.getElementById('page-loading');if(!page)return;
    let banner=page.querySelector('.rc-banner[data-rc-source="Loading & Dispatch"]');
    if(!banner){
      const head=page.querySelector('.page-head');
      if(head){head.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend','<div class="rc-banner" data-rc-source="Loading & Dispatch"></div>');banner=page.querySelector('.rc-banner[data-rc-source="Loading & Dispatch"]')}
    }
    if(!banner)return;
    const failures=plan?automaticList(plan).filter(item=>item.result==='Failed').length:0;
    banner.innerHTML=`<span>🛡️</span><div><strong>Loading Readiness Validation</strong><div>Run Validation mengisi checklist otomatis dari dokumen, kapasitas, fraud alert, kontrak, dan data master.</div></div><div class="rc-stats"><span class="rc-chip ${failures?'high':'low'}">${failures?'Attention':'Low Risk'}</span><span class="rc-chip">${failures} Validation Issue</span><span class="rc-chip ${failures?'critical':''}">${failures} Blocking</span></div><div class="rc-actions"><button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="runPreLoadingValidation()">Run Validation</button>${typeof rcOpenEvents==='function'?'<button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="rcOpenEvents(\'Loading & Dispatch\')">View Alerts</button>':''}</div>`;
  }
  window.renderLoading=function(){
    const plans=(db.plans||[]).filter(plan=>['Planned','Checking','Loading','Ready to Dispatch'].includes(plan.status));
    const select=document.getElementById('loadingPlanSelect');if(!select)return;
    select.innerHTML=plans.map(plan=>`<option value="${safe(plan.id)}">${safe(plan.id)} — ${safe(plan.source)} — ${safe(plan.status==='Checking'&&ensureCheckState(plan).status==='Passed'?'Checking Passed':plan.status)}</option>`).join('')||'<option value="">No plan available</option>';
    if(!activeLoadingPlan||!plans.some(plan=>plan.id===activeLoadingPlan))activeLoadingPlan=plans[0]?.id||'';
    select.value=activeLoadingPlan;
    window.selectLoadingPlan(activeLoadingPlan);
  };
  window.selectLoadingPlan=function(id){
    activeLoadingPlan=id;
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===id),flow=document.getElementById('loadingFlow'),content=document.getElementById('loadingContent');
    if(!plan){if(flow)flow.innerHTML='';if(content)content.innerHTML='<div class="empty">No shipment waiting for checking or loading.</div>';patchValidationBanner(null);return}
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);if(!c.validationRunAt)applyAutomaticValidation(plan);
    const steps=['Planned','Checking','Loading','Ready to Dispatch','In Transit'];
    const current=Math.max(0,steps.indexOf(flowStage(plan)));
    flow.innerHTML=`<div class="flow">${steps.map((step,index)=>`${index?'<span class="flow-arrow">→</span>':''}<span class="flow-step ${index<current?'done':index===current?'current':''}">${step}</span>`).join('')}</div>`;
    const loaded=plan.loadedDocs||[],docCount=(plan.docs||[]).length,docDenominator=Math.max(1,docCount),preloadPercent=Math.round(passedCount(plan)/8*100);
    let primaryButton='';
    if(plan.status==='Planned'||plan.status==='Checking')primaryButton=`<button class="btn btn-primary" ${c.status==='Passed'?'':'disabled'} onclick="startLoading()">Start Loading</button>`;
    else if(plan.status==='Loading')primaryButton=`<button class="btn btn-success" ${loaded.length===docCount&&docCount>0?'':'disabled'} onclick="completeLoading()">Complete Loading</button>`;
    else if(plan.status==='Ready to Dispatch')primaryButton='<button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="dispatchPlan()">Gate-Out / Dispatch</button>';
    content.innerHTML=`<div class="loading-check-layout"><div><div class="notice"><b>${safe(plan.id)}</b> • ${safe(plan.vehicle&&plan.vehicle!=='-'?plan.vehicle:plan.supplier||'-')} • ${safe(plan.driver&&plan.driver!=='-'?plan.driver:plan.supplier||'-')}<br>${safe(plan.route||'-')}</div>${renderPreLoadingCard(plan)}${renderLoadingDocuments(plan)}</div><div><div class="card"><div class="card-head">Loading Summary</div><div class="card-body"><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Pre-Loading Check</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${preloadPercent}%"></span></div><b>${preloadPercent}%</b></div><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Document Loaded</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${loaded.length/docDenominator*100}%"></span></div><b>${loaded.length}/${docCount}</b></div><div class="metric-row"><span class="name">Item Verification</span><div class="progress"><span style="width:${loaded.length/docDenominator*100}%"></span></div><b>${loaded.length===docCount&&docCount>0?'100%':'0%'}</b></div><div class="notice ${Number(plan.util||0)>90?'warn':''}">Vehicle capacity utilization: <b>${Number(plan.util||0)}%</b></div>${primaryButton}${(plan.status==='Planned'||plan.status==='Checking')?loadingGateMessage(plan):''}</div></div></div></div>`;
    patchValidationBanner(plan);
  };
  window.runPreLoadingValidation=function(){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!plan)return;
    captureVisibleDraft(plan);applyAutomaticValidation(plan);saveDB();window.renderLoading();toast('System validation completed and automatic checklist updated');
  };
  window.startPreLoadingCheck=function(){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!plan||plan.status!=='Planned')return;
    const c=ensureCheckState(plan);applyAutomaticValidation(plan);c.status='In Progress';c.startedAt=nowText();c.savedAt='';c.completedAt='';plan.status='Checking';plan.lastUpdate='Pre-loading checking started';saveDB();window.renderLoading();toast('Pre-Loading Check started');
  };
  window.setPreLoadingManualStatus=function(key,value){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!plan)return;
    const c=captureVisibleDraft(plan);if(c.status!=='In Progress'){toast('Klik Start Checking terlebih dahulu');return}
    if(c.manual[key])c.manual[key].result=value;saveDB();window.renderLoading();
  };
  window.setPreLoadingEvidence=function(key,input){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!plan)return;
    const c=captureVisibleDraft(plan);if(c.status!=='In Progress')return;
    if(c.manual[key])c.manual[key].evidenceName=input.files?.[0]?.name||'';saveDB();window.renderLoading();toast(c.manual[key].evidenceName?'Evidence photo attached':'Evidence photo removed');
  };
  window.refreshPreLoadingCompleteButton=function(){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan),button=document.getElementById('completePreLoadingButton');if(!plan||!button)return;
    const c=captureVisibleDraft(plan);button.disabled=!(c.status==='In Progress'&&allChecksResolved(plan)&&!!c.checkerName);
  };
  window.savePreLoadingCheck=function(){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!plan)return;
    const c=captureVisibleDraft(plan);if(c.status!=='In Progress'){toast('Klik Start Checking terlebih dahulu');return}
    c.savedAt=nowText();saveDB();window.renderLoading();toast('Pre-loading check saved');
  };
  window.completePreLoadingCheck=function(){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!plan)return;
    const c=captureVisibleDraft(plan);const failures=failedCount(plan);
    if(!c.checkerName){toast('Checker Name wajib diisi');return}
    if(failures>0){toast(`Loading cannot be started because ${failures} ${failures===1?'check requires':'checks require'} corrective action.`);return}
    if(!allChecksResolved(plan)){toast('Semua checklist manual harus Pass atau Not Applicable');return}
    c.status='Passed';c.completedAt=nowText();c.savedAt=nowText();plan.status='Checking';plan.lastUpdate='Pre-loading checking passed';
    db.driverStates=db.driverStates||{};
    const driverState=db.driverStates[plan.id]||(db.driverStates[plan.id]={planId:plan.id,step:0,currentStop:0,accepted:false,preTrip:false,loadConfirmed:false,closed:false});
    driverState.checkerName=c.checkerName;
    driverState.checkerSource='Loading & Dispatch';
    driverState.checkerSyncedAt=c.completedAt;
    saveDB();window.renderLoading();if(typeof window.renderDriverMobile==='function'&&document.querySelector('.page.active')?.id==='page-driver-mobile')window.renderDriverMobile();toast('Checking Passed. Checker synchronized to Driver Mobile and Start Loading is now active');
  };
  window.startLoading=function(){
    const plan=(db.plans||[]).find(item=>item.id===activeLoadingPlan);if(!plan)return;
    const c=captureVisibleDraft(plan),failures=failedCount(plan);
    if(c.status!=='Passed'||!allChecksResolved(plan)){
      toast(failures>0?`Loading cannot be started because ${failures} ${failures===1?'check requires':'checks require'} corrective action.`:'Complete the pre-loading check before starting the loading process.');return;
    }
    if(typeof baseStartLoading==='function')baseStartLoading();
  };
  window.statusBadge=function(status){
    if(status==='Checking')return '<span class="badge b-checking">Checking</span>';
    if(status==='Checking Passed')return '<span class="badge b-checking-passed">Checking Passed</span>';
    return typeof baseStatusBadge==='function'?baseStatusBadge(status):checkBadge(status);
  };
  const pageText=document.querySelector('#page-loading .page-head p');if(pageText)pageText.textContent='Validasi sistem, pre-loading checking, konfirmasi loading, driver handover, dan gate-out.';
  setTimeout(()=>{if(document.querySelector('.page.active')?.id==='page-loading')window.renderLoading()},0);
})();
</script>

</body>
</html>
